Ayssi comensan las paraulas de Albucasim .	The words of Albucaisim begin here.
O, filhs, pus yeu he a vos complit aquest libre, le qual es le derier de la sciencia de medicina, per le compliment de lu so consequit la fi en lu, e per las exposicios de lu, e per las declaracios de lu, es a mi vist que yeu complesca aquel a vos am aquest tractat, le qual es partida de la operacio am ma, so es cyrurgia.	Oh, sons, since I have now completed this book for you, which is the final part of the science of medicine, and since its completion has reached its end, and through its explanations and declarations, it appears to me that you should understand and possess this treatise, which is a part of my operation, namely surgery.
Quar la operacio am ma es prostrada en nostre regio e en nostre temps de tot privada, entro que fort leu peric la sciencia de lu, e le vistigi de lu es ostat; e no romasero de lu sino alcunas petitas descripcios en les libres dels Antics, les quals mudero las mas e endevenc ad aquels error e heyssitacio entro que son clausas las entencios de lu e es elonguada la forsa de lu e l’art.	Therefore, my operation is now laid to waste in our region and in our time, completely private, so that little by little the science of it has been forgotten, and its vestige remains hidden; and there remained no more than some small descriptions in the books of the Ancients, which have been corrupted and distorted through errors and obscurity, until the intentions of it are closed up and its force and art are elongated.
E es vist a mi que yeu vivifique aquela am ordenacio de aquest tractat en aquela segon la via de exposicio e de declaracio e de abreviacio; e per que vengua am las formas dels ferramentz de cautheri e dels autres instrumentz de la obra cum sia per addicio de la declaracio, e per preparacio de lu, la qual causa es necessaria.	And it seems to me that you should revitalize that ancient order of this treatise according to the way of exposition and declaration and abbreviation; and in order that I may show you the forms of the instruments of cauterization and other tools of the work as they should be used, adding explanation and preparing them, which is a necessary cause.
Mays la causa per la qual no es atrobat bo artifex am la sieua ma en aquest nostre temps, es quar la art de medicina es longua, e que cove le sieu actor denant aquo esser excercitat en la sciencia de anotomia la qual recontec Gualia entro que sapia les juvament dels membres e las formas de aquels, e la conjunctio e la separacio de lor; e haia la conoyssensa dels osses, dels nervis e dels lacertz, e·l nombre de aquels, e la egrecio de lor; e de las venas pulsatils e de las quietas, e dels locs del eyssiment de lor.	But the reason why no good craftsman is found who has his own hand in this our time, is because the art of medicine is long, and it requires the one who will act in front to be exercised in the science of anatomy, which Galen knew well, so that he could know the joints of the members and their shapes, and their conjunction and separation; and have knowledge of bones, nerves, and ligaments, and their number, and their arrangement; and of pulsing veins and quiet ones, and the locations of their effluent.
E per aquo ditz Ypocras que am u nom es mot, mays en l’obra petit, e majorment en la art de la ma.	And therefore Hippocrates says that with no name is a movement, but in the work small, and most of all in the art of hand.
Mays nos ja avem dit de aquel en l’introit de aquest libre; quar qui no es scient aquo que li avem dit de anotomia, no es evacuat que no caia en error per la qual siran mortz les homes, ayssi cum yeu he vist trops de aquels, quar alscus son formatz en esta sciencia e gettan se de aquela ses sciencia e ses experiment.	But we have already said about this in the introduction to this book; for one who is not knowledgeable in anatomy, as we have told you, will not be exempt from falling into error which will cause men's deaths, just as I have seen many of them, because some are formed in this science and seek to get ahead without true knowledge or experiment.
Quar yeu vi un metge folh e enperit aver incidit un apostema escrophilos en le colh de una femna, e incidic alcunas arterias del colh per que fluic gran sanc entro que la femna cazec morta entre las mas de lu.	For I saw a foolish and inexperienced doctor who had inflicted an abscess on the throat of a woman, and he had cut some arteries in her throat so that great blood flowed and the woman died between those present.
E vi un autre metge que pres que el traguera una peyra d’un home le qual avia procesit en sa etat, e la peyra era gran, e venguet a lu e trayssec aquela peyra am un tros de la vesiqua, per que aquel home al tertz dia es mort.	And I saw another doctor who took out an abscess from a man whose state he had examined, and the abscess was large, and it came to him and removed that abscess with a piece of his bladder, so that that man died on the third day.
E yeu ja apelat fuy a estrayre aquela, e vi que per la grandesa de la peyra e per la disposicio del malaute conogui subre lu que morira.	And you yourself had predicted that it would be fatal to remove it, and I saw that due to the greatness of the abscess and the patient's condition, he knew it would kill him.
E vi un autre metge le qual prenia stipendic de un duc de nostra terra per cyrurgia, e endeven a un crastrat negre le qual era deves lu fractura en la coyssa de lu; e perparec le metge am la sua ignorancia, estrayssec la fractura, sobre la plagua, am pulvinas e astelas am forta strectura, e no layssec a la plagua espiracio.	And I saw another doctor who received pay from a duke of our land for surgery, and he undertook to suture the wound on a blacksmith's leg which had been fractured; and the doctor, with his ignorance, removed the fracture, placing it above the wound, with splints and sticks under strong tension, and did not allow the wound to breathe.
E aprop le desliet segons los sieus desiriers, e aprop le relieg, e aprop le leyssec per alcus jorns e comandec que nos deslies le liament; e estec ayssi entro que la coyssa e·l pe foro apostematz, e pervenguet a perdicio.	And then he loosened the stitches according to his own desires, and then he removed the splints, and then he allowed it to be left for some days and commanded that we loosen the bandage; and thus it became so that the leg and foot were apostemated, and it led to perdition.
E yeu fuy apelat a lu, e aparelhegui a desliar le liament, e conseguida es tranquilitat e enayssi amermet de sas dolors.	And you were called to him, and he was prepared to loosen the bandage, and as a result, there was calmness and an end to his pains.
Mays empero ja corrupcio era confermada en le membre, per que no pogui refrenar aquela, e no cessec perambular la corrupcio en le membre entro que·l malaute peric.	But meanwhile corruption had already been confirmed in the member, so that it could not be restrained and ceased to walk, spreading corruption in the member until the patient perished.
E vi un autre metge le qual perforec un apostema cancros, e fo ulcerat aprop alscus dias, entro que foc magnificada la malicia de lu am lo senhor de lu.	And I saw another doctor who pierced a cancerous abscess and caused it to ulcerate within a few days, until the malice of it magnified with its lord.
La qual causa es quar le cranc caut es pur de humor melencolic, lahoras no cove que pervengua a lu am ferr de tot, sino que sia an membre le qual suffertes que de tot fos hostat.	The cause is that the cancerous part is pure of melancholic humor, therefore it does not need to be removed completely, but rather it should be left in the member which suffers and is fully hostile.
E per aquo, filhs, necessari es a vos que la operacio am ma sia devisada en dos devesios: so es en operacio a lu qual es associada salut, e en obra am la qual es perilh en las majors disposicios.	And therefore, sons, it is necessary for you that my operation be divided into two parts: one is in the operation associated with health, and the other is in the work where there is danger in the greater dispositions.
E yeu ja he exsitat aquo en tot loc de aquest libre en le qual venc opperacio en la qual es error e temor; per que necessari es a vos que guardetz aquo e layssetz aquel, per que les folhs no atrobo via a parlar e a vos desonestar.	And you have already existed in this place throughout this book, where I described the operation in which there is error and fear; therefore it is necessary for you that you guard this and avoid that, so that foolish ones do not find a way to speak and deceive you.
E donc prenetz las vostras armas am sollicitut e am proteccio de Dieu , e les vostres malautes am falicitat e am fermetat.	And therefore, take up your own arms with solicitude and protection of God, and your own patients with felicity and firmness.
E usatz de la milhor via per la gracia de Dieu perdusent a salut e a lausabla successio, e laysatz las malautias terriblas de difficil sanacio, e ostatz las vostras armas de aquo que vos fa temer, per so que ysitatio en vostra fe e en le vostre nom no vos evasisca: quar mays es remanent a la vostra gloria, e pus aut en le mon e en derier a las vostras sanctitatz.	And use the best way with the grace of God, to preserve health and to obtain blessed success, and abandon terrible diseases that are difficult to heal, and keep your own arms from this which makes you fear, so that your situation remains in your faith and in your name does not escape: because it is more remaining at your glory, and further in the world and in eternity at your sanctity.
Gualia ja diyssec en alcunas sieuas monicios:	Galen already said this in certain of his own writings:
“No mediquetz malautia mala, per so que mals metges no siatz nompnatz”.	"Don't treat a bad disease, lest you become a bad doctor."
E yeu ja he devesit aquest libre segontz tres capitols.	And I have divided this book into three chapters.
Comensa la divisio del libre, e primier de la primieyra partida.	The division of the book begins, and first, the first part.
Le primier capitol ordenat del cap entro·s pes, en las formas dels instrumentz e en les ferrementz dels cauteris, e de aquo que necessari es en la opperacio.	The first chapter, ordered according to the head and its members, in the forms of instruments and the furnishings of cauterization, and from this it is necessary in the operation.
La divisio de la segonda partida.	The division of the second part.
Le segon capitol, de siccio e perforacio, e de ventosas, e de plaguas, e de extractio de sagetas e de semblantz ad aquelas, tot capitolat e ordenat de las formas dels instrumentz.	The second chapter, on drying and piercing, and on suction cups, and on wounds, and on the extraction of splinters and similar things, entirely chaptered and ordered according to the forms of instruments.
Divisio de la tersa partida.	Division of the third part.
Le tertz capitol, de restauracio e de dislocacio, e de curacio de torcio e de semblantz ad aquels; capitol ordenat del cap entro·s pes, e de las formas dels instrumentz.	The third chapter, on restoration and dislocation, and on the cure of torsion and similar things; a chapter ordered from head to foot, and according to the forms of instruments.
De cauteri am foc e am medicina aguda e rememoracio de la opperacio.	On cauterization with fire and acute medicine, and a reminder of the operation.
Am aquel comensa le tractat de tot le libre.	In that one begins the treatise of the entire book.
Cove que yeu digua la qualitat dels juvamentz de aquel cauteri e dels noccumentz de lu, e en qual compleccio sia prohibit cauteri.	You should know the quality of the joints of that cauterization and the inconveniences of it, and in what condition it is forbidden to cauterize.
Donc dic que·l sermo de la qualitat del juvament de cauteri e del noccument de lu es sermo lonc e prolixs, e subtil per sciensa, e secret amaguat; e ja de lu a parlat gran multitut de savis, e de lu se son desacordatz, et a mi abasta un petit dels sermons de lor, temen perlonguacio.	Therefore I say that the sermon on the quality of the joints of cauterization and its inconveniences is a long and prolix discourse, subtle by science, and secret veiled; and many wise men have spoken about it, and they have disagreed among themselves, and for me it is sufficient to draw from their sermons a small part, fearing prolongation.
E donc dic que cauteri comfereys a tota compleccio universalment la qual es am materia o ses materia, exceptat dos compleccios, las quals son compleccios caudas ses materia .	And therefore I say that cauterization conforms to all conditions universally, which is in material or its matter, except for two conditions, which are conditions contrary to their matter.
En la compleccio cauda e secca am materia se desecordero; quar alcus dyssero que cauteri es juvatiu ad aquela, e les autres dyssero le contrari de aquel, que cauteri no es convenient en malautia la qual es per qualiditat e per siccitat, quar natura del foc es qualiditat e siccitat, e enconvenient es que malautia cauda e secca am aquo que es caut e sec sia sanada.	In the dry and withered condition of material, it desiccate; for some would say that cauterization is beneficial to that, and others would say the opposite of that, that cauterization is not suitable in a disease which is due to quality and dryness, for nature of fire is quality and dryness, and it is inconvenient that a withered and dry disease, with water that is hot and dry, should be healed.
E diysec aquel que ditz le contrari de aquel, que per cauteri es fayt juvament en tota malautia cauda e secca que ve en les cors dels homes, quar quan tu comparas le cors de home e las humiditatz de lu a la compleccio del foc, atrobas le cors de home freg.	And he says that which is the opposite of that, that through cauterization it is made joint in all withered and dry disease that is found in the bodies of men, for when you compare the human body and its moistures to the condition of fire, you find the human body cold.
E yeu dic per le sermo de aquel, que esperiment aquo ja a mi alscunas vetz a descubert.	And I say through the sermon of that, that experiment is here already revealed to me several times in discovering.
Mays empero no cove que vengua sobre aquo aquel que ja es exproat e excersitat en le capitol de cauteri per derier exercici, e a conogut la diversitat de la compleccio dels homes e la disposicio de las malautias en lor meteyssas, e las causas de aquelas, e·ls accidentz de lor, e l’espasi del temps de aquelas.	But it is not necessary for me to come back on this again, since it has already been dealt with and exercised in the chapter on cauterization, and I have become acquainted with the diversity of human conditions and the disposition of diseases in their respective forms, and their causes, and the accidents that occur in them, and the span of time for those.
Mays en las autras compleccios, no es sobre vos temor, e majorment en las malautias fregas e humidas, quar ja totz les metges se son acordatz sobre aquels, e no so desecordatz en le juvament am cauteri en aquelas.	But in other conditions, there is no fear for you, and especially in cold and humid diseases, for all doctors have agreed on these, and are not discordant in the joints about cauterization in those.
E sapiatz, filhs, que del secret de curacio per cauteri am foc e de la bontat de lu, so sobre cauteri am medicina comburent, es quar le foc es simple, la accio del qual no perven sino al membre le qual es cauterizat e no notz al autre membre am lu ajustat sino am petit nocument.	And know, sons, that from the secret of healing by cauterization with fire and its goodness, it is more on cauterization with medicine combined, because the fire is simple, whose action does not extend beyond the member being cauterized, nor does it harm another member adjusted to it, only with a small drawback.
Mays la accio de medicina comburent perven ad aquel en les membres le qual de lu alunhat, e fort leu fa venir en le membre malautia de dificil sanacio e fort leu ausit.	But the action of medicine combined extends to those members which are far away from it, and very quickly brings disease with difficult healing and great suffering to that member.
Mays le foc, per la sua sublimitat e de la sua substancia bontat, no fa aquo sino que superfluisca E ja es a nos conogut per experiment e per longitut de servitut de studi am l’art sobre le veritat de las causas; e per aquo yeu so excusat de la longitut del sermo E si no fos que no es legut al mieu libre en aquest pausero a vos secret amaguat am le foc, e la qualitat de la operacio de lu en les cors e de la sieua expulcio per la qual expellis las malautias, am sermo philosophic demostratiu, le qual siria acuit en las vostras pessas.	But fire, due to its subtlety and the goodness of its substance, does not do this except that it superfluously causes; and it is already known to us through experiment and long-standing service in studying the art, based on the truth of the causes. And therefore I am excused from the length of my sermon. If it were not for the fact that this secret hidden by fire has not been read in a better book, and the quality of its operation in the body and its expulsion by which it expels diseases, with a philosophical demonstration speech, which would be sharp in your chests.
E sapiatz, filhs, que els se desacordan del temps en le qual es convenient far cauteri e pausan le milhor temps de primaveyra.	And know, sons, that they are out of accord with the time in which it is suitable to perform cauterization and pause at the best time of spring.
E yeu dic que cauteri es convenient en tot temps, per so que le nocument per le temps accident es submergit en le juvament de aquo que am le cauteri es atirat, e majorment si le cauteri es per dolors o de dolors necessaries, fortz e fistinas, las quals no suffertan tarditat per so que es temut de aquelas que vengua malicia, que es major que petit nocument entrant per lo temps.	And I say that cauterization is suitable at any time, for the harm caused by time accidents is submerged in the joint of what is attracted to the cauterization, and especially if the cauterization is for pains or necessary pains, strong and fierce, which do not suffer from tardiness because it is feared of those who come with malice, which is greater than small harm entering through the time.
E aysso no catz en vostras pessas, o, filhs, aquo no estiman sino le poble vulguar e les fols metges, so es que ad aquela malautia que es sanada per cauteri no es redicio tot temps, e pausan aquel consequen.	And thus it is not in your chests, or sons, that this is estimated by only the common people and foolish doctors, for it is true that at that disease which is cured by cauterization, there is no reduction of time, and pause from the consequence.
E la causa no es ges ayssi quo els cuydan per aquo, quar cauteri no es sino en loc de medicina la qual altera la compleccio e esicca las humiditatz las quals son causa per que veno las dolors.	And the cause is not as they think it is, for cauterization is nothing but a place of medicine that alters the condition and dries out the humors which are the cause of why pains come.
Mays empero cauteri superflueys sobre la medicina per volicitat de la sua valitut e vertut de la sua operacio e grandesa del sieu senhor.	But meanwhile, cauterization is superfluous over medicine by the will of its virtue and the greatness of its lord.
E es possible que la sua malautia retorne en alcuna hora del temps, segon la compleccio del malaute e la locacio de la sua malautia, e la vertut de lu, e aquo que es preparat en le cors de lu de la agreguacio de las superfluitatz en lu, e aquo que es pervengut a lu en la sua acquisicio en viandas e semblantz de aquelas causas; sino que la malautia en la qual sia aministrat cauteri sia malautia subtil en membre de paucas superfluitatz e humiditatz, ayssi cum cauteri de dent per dolor e semblantz ad aquel, possible es que en lu no retorne aquela dolor, mays aquo se fa en petitz.	And it is possible that his disease will return at some hour of time, according to the condition of the patient and the location of his disease, and the virtue of what is prepared in the body of what is accumulated in him from the superfluities, and what has been acquired through food and similar causes; but if the disease in which cauterization is administered is a subtle disease in a few superfluities and humors, just like cauterization for toothache and similar pains, it is possible that this pain will not return to him, but rather it will be reduced in small measure.
E mays sermo vulgar es que cauteri es le derier remezi de medicina, e es sermo dreyturier, no ad aquo que els entendo en lu, quar els crezo que no es curacio que aprofieyta am medicina ni am autra causa aprop cauteri.	And it is also said in plain speech that cauterization is the last remedy of medicine, and it is a dreadful saying, not according to what they understand in it, because I believe that there is no cure that profits by medicine or any other cause that approaches cauterization.
E la causa es en contrari de aquo; e la entencio que cauteri es le derier remezi de medicina no es sino quan administram las manieyras de curacio en alcunas malautias, e aquelas medicinas no conferieysso, e aprop en la fi de la causa aministra hom cauteri, e aprofieyta ad aquela.	And the cause is contrary to that; and I understand that cauterization is the last remedy of medicine only when one administers the methods of cure for certain diseases, and those medicines do not concur, and in the end of the cause, one administers cauterization, and it profits from that.
E lahoras de aqui cat16 que cauteri es le derier remezi de medicina, no segon la entencio la qual entendo les vulgars e trops dels fols metges.	And I conclude here that cauterization is the last remedy of medicine, not according to the understanding which I understand the common people and many foolish doctors.
E diyssero les antics que cauteri am aur es milhor que cauteri am ferr, e no diyssero aquo sino per la equalitat del aur e sublimitat de la sua sustancia.	And they said the ancients that cauterization with gold is better than cauterization with iron, and they did not say this except for the equality of gold and the subtlety of its substance.
E diyssero que le loc de cauteri no fa brac, cum aquo no sia absolutament vertat, quar yeu ja he aquo proat e he atrobat que aquel no fa aquo sino en alcus cors ses les autres, e cauteri am aquel es bo e milhor que am ferr ayssi quo els diyssero; mays empero quan tu fas cauteri am foc am de aur, no es a tu declarat, quar es egnit segon la quantitat que tu vols per la rugor de l’aur, e quar prepara a recebre freg; e si ajustas sobre lu ignicio se fon l’aur per le foc, e caso en le foc alcunas laminas per que le artifex catz per la occupacio de aquel.	And they said that the place of cauterization does not matter, as if it were absolutely true, for I have already proved and discovered that it does not matter at all, except in certain bodies, and that cauterization with gold is good and better than with iron, just as they said; but however, when you do cauterization with fire on gold, it is not declared to you, for it is hidden according to the quantity that you want by the roughness of the gold, and prepares to receive heat; and if you place over it ignition, the gold melts in the fire, and some plates are formed so that the artisan can see through the occupation of that.
E per aquo es fayt cauteri am ferr deves nos pus leugerament e pus propdanament a rectitut de operacio.	And therefore it is made necessary to perform cauterization with iron in a way that is lighter and more precisely according to the rectitude of operation.
E yeu ja he ordenat aquest capitol en le cauteri segon capitols, et he ordenat aquels del cap entro les pes, per so que aleugo le demandant aquo que vol de lu.	And I have already ordered this chapter on cauterization according to chapters, and I have ordered those from head to foot, so that the demanding person can easily get what they want from here.
De cauteri de dolor de cap per frigiditat e humiditat.	On cauterization for headaches caused by coldness and humidity.
Le capitol primier.	The first chapter.
Aquesta cauterizacio confereys a la humiditat e frigiditat sobre le servel accident de la qual so doas causas, so es causa de soda e multitut de flux raumatic, apelat corissa, del cap a las partidas dels huelhs e de las aurelhas fluent, e multitut de dormir, e de dolor de dentz e del guolayro, e universalment de tota malautia que ve per fregiditat, ayssi cum paraliticament, sodo e apoplexio, e semblantz en aquelas malautias.	This cauterization conquers the humidity and coldness in the serving of accidents which has two causes, one being the cause of soda and the multitude of rheumatic fluxes, called corissa, from the head to the parts of the eyes and ears, and flowing with sleepiness, toothaches, and yawning, and universally all disease that comes through coldness, just like paralysis, sodality, apoplexy, and similar diseases in those illnesses.
La forma de aquesta cauterizacio es aquesta, que primieyrament comandes al malaute que sia evacuat am medicina lacsativa le cap mondificant, per tres o per quatre nueytz, segon que exhigeys la vertut del malaute e la edat de lu e la sua costuma.	The form of this cauterization is this: first, I command the patient to be evacuated with lactative medicine, clearing the head, for three or four nights, according to what the disease requires and the age and habit of the patient.
E aprop comanda li que raza le sieu cap am razor, e aprop fay aquel sezer entre las tuas mas sobre una banca cayrada e que pause las suas mas sobre le pietz sieu.	And then I command him to shave his head with a razor, and then make that shape between the hairs on his back, sitting on a well-cushioned bench, and placing his hands on his feet.
E aprop pausa la razit de la tua palma aprop le pous sobre la razit del nas entre les huels sieus.	And then pause the razor's edge at the tip of your nose, between the eyes, and place it on the skin.
Mays empero, cum le tieu dit del mieg loc es pervengut, signa aquel loc am tenta, e aprop igneys le cauteri olivar del qual aquesta es la forma:	But meanwhile, when the time has come from the middle location is accomplished, mark that location with a tent, and then ignite the olive cauterization of which this is the form:
E aprop pausa aquel sobre le loc senhat am tenta, a manieyra que descent, am la qual la tieua ma sia constrengida petit a petit, e tu revolveys aquel.	And then pause that on the marked location with the tent, in a way that it descends, and by which my own hand is slightly constricted little by little, and you turn that around.
E aprop leva la tua ma leugerament e reguarda le loc, e si veses ja del os esser descubert alcuna quantitat del cap, ayssi cum la quantitat de gra de errs, lahoras eleva la tua ma, e si no torno la tua ma am aquel ferr, am autre de aquel, si es enfrigidat, entro que sia vist del os aquo que yeu he dit a tu.	And then raise your hand slightly and look at the location, and if you see already that some quantity of bone has been uncovered from the skull, like the amount of grain of errors, hours elevate your hand, and if not return your hand with that iron, with another similar to it, if it is chilled, until what I have told you is visible.
E aprop pren un petit de sal e disolveys aquel sobre le loc e leyssa aquel per tres jorns.	And then take a small amount of salt and dissolve it over the location and let it be for three days.
E aprop pausa sobre lu coto enbegut en boder e leyssa aquel sobre lu entro que sia destrusida la scara del foc.	And then pause over it with a cloth wrapped in a border and let it be over there until the scar of the fire is destroyed.
E aprop cura le loc am anguent tetrafarmacon entro que sia sanat.	And then cure the location with a four-fold medicine, until it is healed.
E ja diyssero que quant la plagua roman uberta, tant mielhs geta le brac, per que es milhor e mays juvatiu.	And they said that as long as the wound remains open, so much the better is the cauterization, because it is more effective and beneficial.
E diyssero alcus de lor que sia cauterizada la codena entro al os, e sia tengut le cauteri entro que sia adhurida alcuna partida de la specitut del os.	And some of them said that the tongue should be cauterized into the bone, and the cauterization should be kept until some part of the specificity of the bone is absorbed.
E aprop sia ras aquo que es adhust del os, e aprop sia curat.	And then it will be cleared what is adhered to the bone, and then it will be cured.
E diyssero autres que am lo cauteri pervengua al derier, entro que enprema en le os forta enprecio entro que le os caga, e aquesta es la forma de alphecati petit:	And others said that with the cauterization it will come to the last, until it presses into the bone with great force, until the bone cracks, and this is the form of little aphicate:
E estiman de aquel loc expiran la vapors del cap.	And they consider that from that location the vapors of the head will be expelled.
E sia tenguda la plagua uberta per lonc temps, e aprop sia curada entro que sia consolidada.	And it should be kept open for a long time, and then it will be cured when it is consolidated.
Mays a mi no so vistas aquestas doas specias de cauteri de tot, sino en alcus homes segon via de temor; e layssa aquel, deves mi, milhor es am salut, quan es; quar le cap es develitat per solucio de continuitat de lu ayssi cum havem testificat en les autres membres, e majorment quan le cap del malaute es de freul natura.	But to me, these two species of cauterization are not visible at all, except in some men according to the way of fear; and leaving that aside, I consider it better for health when it is; because the head has been revealed by the dissolution of continuity, just as we have testified in other members, and especially when the patient's head is of a frightful nature.
E la specia de cauteri primieyra es mays salva e milhor deves mi; e de aquela husi e am aquela obra am salut.	And the first species of cauterization is more saved and better for me; and from that house and with that work, salvation comes.
Capitol segon.	The second chapter.
Del cauteri del cap.	On the Cauterization of the Head.
Quan en tot le cap accideys dolor cronica e longua e aquo es en le malaute prolonguat, e usa de gerras e de cochias e de capipurges e de emplaustres e de guatz e de cadels e de gualinas e de semblantz, e majorment si ja es cauterizat am un cautere le qual recontam e no aprofieyta a lu deguna de aquelas causas, lahoras considera quar si le cap del malaute es de fort creacio en la sua natura; e no es freul et atroba mot gran freg, lahoras aquel cauterisa am autra cauteri dejos aquel un pauc.	When in all the head there occurs chronic and long-lasting pain, and it is prolonged in the patient, and they use various remedies such as wars and cochias and capipurges and emplausters and guats and cadels and gualinas and similar things, and especially if already cauterized with one cautery which does not respond and does not benefit at all from any of those causes, then consider that if the patient's head is of strong creation in its nature; and it is not frightful and finds no great fear, then that cauterization should be done with another cautery, leaving a little bit between.
E aprop cauterisa aquel sobre le corn del sieu cap am cauteri entro que la codena es partida.	And then cauterize that over the horn of one's head with a cautery until the tongue is parted.
Incisa la codena e sia descuberta del os la quantitat la qual havem recontat e cauteriza aquel am un cauteri en la partida deriera del cap en le loc le qual es apelat vas, — e es aquel loc en le qual es pausada ventosa.	Cut the tongue and let it be discovered the quantity which we have recounted, and then cauterize that with a cautery in the rear part of the head at the location called "vas", -- and it is that location where the windpipe is paused.
Et alleuja la tua ma en aysso, e no descobras le os, quar le malaute per aquo atroba mot gran dolor diversa de la dolor de totz les autres cauteris del cap.	And lift your hand in that way, and do not uncover the bone, because the patient through this will experience great pain of a different kind than all other head cauteries.
E yeu diyre aquest cauteri en son loc, quar cove que·l cauteri am le qual so cauterisatz les corns del cap e le occiput es pus subtil cauteri que aquel am le qual es cauterisat le mieg loc del cap; e aquesta es la forma de lu.	And you will say this cautery in its place, because it is necessary to cauterize the horns of the head and the occiput with a more subtle cautery than that which is cauterized at the middle location of the head; and this is the form of it.
Capitol ters.	The third chapter.
De cauterisacio de emigranea no-antiqua.	On Cauterization for Migraine that is not Ancient.
Quan endeve en la partida del cap dolor sodo, o es stenduda dolor entro al uelh, sia evacuat am medicinas le cap mondificantz, e sia aministrada l’autra curacio, la qual yeu he dita en las devesios de las malautias; e tot no aprofieyta, lahoras cauterisacio en lu es en dos manieyras: o cauterisacio am medicina acuta comburent, o am ferr.	When the patient in the part of the head feels a dull pain, or it is spread into the eye, let the head be evacuated with medicines that clear the mind, and let another cure be administered, which I have said in the divisions of diseases; and if none of these things help, then cauterization is done in two ways: either with medicine combined with acute remedies, or with iron.
Mays cauteri am medicina comburent es que tu prenguas una dolsa de alh, e escorgas aquela e abcindas las extremitatz de lu de amdos les caps.	But cauterization with medicine combined is that you take a piece of aloes, and scrape it off and cut off the extremities of both heads.
E aprop incideys le loc de la dolor en la templa am una lanceta lada entro que sia en lu feyt loc dejos la codena, entro que sia occultada.	And then incise the location of the pain in the temple with a well-made razor until it forms a spot behind the tongue, so that it is hidden.
E aprop strenh sobre lu am stopada per descent constreccio, e layssa aquel per le spazi de tres horas; e aprop deslia le e tratz le alh, e laysa la plagua per dos o per tres jorn, e aprop pausa sobre lu coto submergit en boder entro que le loc fassa brac.	And then press on it with a stopper for a constant constriction, and let it be for the space of three hours; and then remove the aloes and treat the wound for two or three days, and then pause over it with a cloth wrapped in a border until the spot becomes dry.
E aprop cura aquel am enguent entro que sia sanat.	And then cure that with a four-fold medicine until it is healed.
E si tu voys, fe aquo am alcunas medicinas comburentz las quals yeu he scriutas en le douse tractat de medicinas comburentz.	And if you wish, do this with some combined medicines that I have written in the two treatises on combined medicines.
Mays la cauterisacio am ferr segon aquesta manieyra: igneys per cauteri del qual aquesta es la forma:	But cauterization with iron, according to this method: ignite with the cautery of which this is the form:
e es apelat claus clavilhs, quar le cap de lu es ayssi cum forma de clavel en le qual es alcuna curvitat, e·n le mieg loc de lu es eminensia petita.	and it is called "claus clavilhs", because the head of it is thus shaped like a clove in which there is some curvature, and in the middle location of it there is a small prominence.
E aprop pausa sobre loc de la dolor, e rete la tua ma — per que no sia adhurida la arceria la qual es dejos — e revol le ferr petit a petit am velocitat.	And then pause over the location of the pain, and hold your hand - so that the iron is not too hot to be left there - and slowly turn the iron little by little with velocity.
E si la quantitat de lu que es adhurida per la specitut de la codena ayssi quo la maytat de lu, e elava la tua ma per so que la arteria no sia adhurida la qual es dejos, per so que no vengua flux de sanc.	And if the quantity of it that is absorbed by the specificity of the tongue is like the majority of it, and lift your hand in order that the artery is not absorbed which is left behind, so that a flow of blood does not come.
E aprop enbibeys coto en aygua de sal e pausa aquel sobre le loc, e layssa aquel per tres dias; e aprop pausa coto mulhat am boder, e aprop cura am enguent entro que sia sanat.	And then wrap the cloth in water and salt and pause it over the location, and let it be for three days; and then pause with a mulled cloth wrapped in border, and then cure with four-fold medicine until it is healed.
E si voys, cauterisa am la extremitat del cutellari segon cauteri, e guarda te de incisio de arteria en aquesta emigranea propriament no-antiqua.	And if you wish, cauterize at the extremity of the cutlery according to the cautery, and be careful not to incise an artery in this non-ancient migraine properly.
Capitol quart.	The fourth chapter.
De cauterizacio d’emigranea antiqua.	On Cauterization for Ancient Migraine.
Quan tu curas emigranea am aquo que havem dit de la curacio precedent, e aquo que havem dit en las divisios de las malautias, e no aprofieyta la curacio, e vezes per la malautia que no abasta a lu aquo que havem dit del primier cauteri am medicina o del cauteri am foc, lahoras cove que tu igniscas le cauteri cutellar entro que sia albificat, pus que significas sobre le loc de la dolor am linha de longuesa de la qual sia la maytat del dit, o quays aquel; e depausa la tua ma per una veguada e strenh aquela entro incidiscas la arceria e pervengua entro al os.	When you cure the migraine with that which we have said about the previous cure, and that which we have said in the divisions of diseases, and the cure does not help, and sometimes by the disease it is not enough to do what we have said about the first cauterization with medicine or with fire, then you must ignite the cutlery cautery until it becomes white, so that you mark the location of the pain with a line of length which is the majority of the finger, or where it is; and pause your hand for one moment and press that in to incise the artery and bring it into the bone.
Empero necessari es a tu que guardes de la continuacio de la mandibula, la qual es mauguda deves la masticacio, e que le lacert no sia adhurit e le nervi le qual mau aquela, e que no s’endevengua espasme.	However, it is necessary for you to beware of the continuation of the jawbone, which is disturbed by mastication, and that the ligament is not inflamed and the nerves which are connected to it are not affected, and that there is no spasmodic deviation.
E si es sobre la custodia e cautela de flux de sanc de l’arteria que es abciza, quar en la abcizio de lu es temor, e majorment ad aquel le qual ignora aquo que fa e no es studios e esproat; e layssa la operacio en lu al comensament.	And if it is on the custody and caution of the flow of blood from the artery that is cut, because in the cutting of it there is fear, and especially for him who does not know what he is doing and has no experience or skill; and leave the operation to begin.
E yeu vindre am rememoracio del regiment de flux de sanc accident de la arceria segon la sieua manieyra, en le sieu loc de aquest libre.	And you will come with a recollection of the regulation of blood flow accidental to the artery according to your own method in this book.
E si veses de aquesta malautia que no abaste aquest cauteri e veses le cors del malaute tollerable, cauteriza aquel en le mieg loc del cap ayssi cum havem recontat, e cura la plagua entro que sia sanada.	And if you see that this disease does not respond to this cautery and you see the patient's body is tolerable, then cauterize it in the middle location of the head as we have recounted, and cure the wound until it is healed.
E si voys, aministra le cauteri le qual havem dit en le capitol de streccio de arceria am cauteri havent dos cotels, e es milhor cauterizacio aquesta e mays conferent.	And if you wish, administer the cautery that we have said in the chapter on stricture of artery with two cauteries, and it is better and more convergent.
Capitol .v.	The fifth chapter.
De cauterisacio de las dolors de aurelhas.	On Cauterization for Earaches.
Quan en la aurelha ve dolor per freg e es curat am causas lacsativas e am l’autra curacio la qual he dita en la divisio, e no es remauguda la dolor, lahoras igneys le cauteri, e es aquest le qual ha nom puncta, del qual aquesta es la forma:	When in the ear there is pain due to heat and it is cured by lactative causes and by another cure which I have said in the division, and the pain does not subside, then ignite the cautery, and this is called "puncta", of which this is the form:
E aprop puncta aprop la ignicio, e sia menat al enviro de tota la aurelha ayssi cum roda es revolguda, o en le circuit de quascuna essemps si la dolor es en quascuna.	And then, the puncta is brought to the ignition, and it should be guided around the entire ear like a wheel is revolved, or in the circuit of each sample if the pain is in each one.
Alonga te am le cauteri de la razit de la aurelha pauc a pauc pus que aias senhat le loc am tenta.	Lengthen yourself with the cautery of the root of the ear little by little, so that you sense the location with intent.
E si le cauteri de detz puntz en tota aurelha, e quays aquela, e aprop cura les locz entro que sian sanatz.	And if the cautery is applied to all points in the entire ear, and each one, and then cure the locations until they are healed.
Capitol .vi.	The sixth chapter.
De cauterizacio de turtura.	On Cauterization for Torture.
Turtura la qual es curada e am cauterizacio no es sino de las specias las quals veno per flecma, segon que havem dit en las divisios de las malautias.	Torture which is cured and with cautery is not but of the species which come through flux, according to what we have said in the divisions of diseases.
Esquiva cauterizacio de la specia que endeve per siccacio o per spasme del nervi.	Avoid cauterization of the species that occurs due to dryness or spasmodic contraction of the nerve.
Quan tu curas aquela specia de turtura am jerras e capipurgi e guarguarismes, e no comfereys la tua curacio, lahoras cove que tu cauterizas le malaute am tres cauteris: la i deves la razit de la aurelha, e·l segon un petit dejos le sieu templar, e le ters deves la conjunccio de doas labias.	When you cure that species of torture with jellies and capipurgis and guarguarisms, and your cure does not provide relief, then it is necessary for you to cauterize the patient with three cauteries: one on the root of the ear, and the second a little below the temple, and the third at the conjunction of two lips.
E pausa lo tieu cauteri per le contrari de la partida malauta, quar mollificacio no ve sino en la partida que apar sana.	And pause your cautery on the contrary side of the affected part, because softening only occurs in the part that appears to be healing.
E la forma de cauterisacio es que cauterizas aquel am le cauteri en le dreyt de la extremitat de la aurelha pus sobirana un petit sobre le corn del cap, e en le templar autre, la longuesa del qual sia segon la longitut del dit pous, e depausa la tua ma am cauteri entro que sia comburida la quantitat de la maytat de la specitut de la codena.	And the form of cautery is that you cauterize with the cautery on the right side of the extremity of the ear, slightly above the horn of the head, and on the temple another one, the length of which is according to the length of the thumb, and then pause your hand with the cautery until the quantity of the majority of the specificity of the tongue has been consumed.
E aquesta es la forma del cauteri, e es specia del cutellari, la forma del qual es denant mesa.	And this is the form of the cautery, and it is a species of the cutlary, the form of which is before us.
Mays empero pus subtil es que aquel un pauc ayssi co vesas; e cove que cotel en lu de superflua groceza un pauc.	But however, more subtle is that it must be done as you see; and it is necessary to cut off in excess of superfluous gristle a little.
E aprop cura le loc am aquo que es denant procezit entro que sia sanat.	And then cure the location with water that is before us, until it is healed.
Capitol .vii.	The seventh chapter.
De cauterizacio de apoplextia antiqua.	On Cauterization for Ancient Apoplexy.
Quan apoplextia es antiquada e curas aquela am aquo que havem dit e no confereys la tua medicacio e le malaute no ha febre, lahoras cauteriza aquel am quatre cauteris: sobre totz les corn del sieu cap; e am cauteri e le mieg loc del cap, ayssi cum havem dit; e am cauteri en le coguot.	When apoplexy is ancient and you cure it with the water that we have said and your medicine does not provide relief, and the patient has no fever, then cauterize it with four cauteries: on all the horns of his head; and with one cautery in the middle location of the head, just as we have said; and with one cautery in the cranium.
E la manieyra del cauteri es fayta segon que es desus dit.	And the method of the cautery is done according to what has been said above.
E ja es cauterizat sobre la boca del estomac; e es mays derier; e aprop sia curat am aquo que procezeys.	And already it has been cauterized on the mouth of the stomach, and it is more posterior; and then it should be cured with water that proceeds.
Capitol .viii.	The eighth chapter.
De cauterizacio de obblivio fayta per flacma.	On Cauterization for Oblivion caused by Flux.
Cove que sian donatz al malaute en le comensament jerras grans e pilulas le servel mondificantz.	It is necessary to give the patient in the beginning large jellies and pills that serve as mind-clearing remedies.
E aprop ras le cap tot del malaute e pausa sus le coguot de lu emplaustre de cetre descrit en le tractat dels emplastres.	And then remove the head of the patient and pause on the cranium of it an ointment described in the treatise on ointments.
E pausa aquel alcunas veguadas, quar aquel es manieyra de cauteri.	And pause it for several times, because that is the method of cauterization.
E fay aquo segon aquel meteys orde le qual ja he dit.	And do this according to the order of the method which I have already said.
E donc si per aqueles sanat bo es; e sino, lahoras fay a lu tres cauteris en la deriera partida de sieu cap, les quals sian deysendentz de la partida pus sobirana del cap entro a la partida pus dejos del col.	And therefore, if through these he is fully healed; and otherwise, then ignite three cauteries in the rear part of his head, which are descendants of the uppermost part of the head down to the lower part of the neck.
E pausa entre quascun cauteri la grossetut del dit, e aprop cura lo cauteri am aquo que es procedit.	And pause between each cautery the length of the thumb, and then cure the cautery with water that has been proceeded.
Mays si tu vos addicio e le malaute es aquo tollerant, lahoras fay a lu cauteri en le mieg loc; e si voys major addicio, lahora cauteriza aquel sobre les dos corns.	But if you wish to add more and the patient is tolerating it well, then ignite one cautery in the middle location; and if you wish for even greater addition, then cauterize that over both horns.
Aprop cura aquel entro que sia sanat; e sia le cauteri olivar segon la forma denant donat.	And then cure that until it is healed; and be the cautery olive-shaped according to the form previously given.
Capitol .ix.	The ninth chapter.
De cauterisacio de parazili e de mollificacio de tot le cors.	On Cauterization for Paralysis and Softening of the Entire Body.
Cove que tu procesiscas en mondificacio del cap am jerras e am aquo que havem dit; e aprop ras le cap del malaute, e aprop cauteriza aquel am cauteri en le mieg loc del cap, e am cauteri sobre totz les corns del cap, e am cauteri sobre la deriera partida de lu, e am tres cauteris sobre les spondils del col.	It is necessary that you proceed with the softening of the head with jellies and water as we have said; and then remove the head of the patient, and then cauterize it with three cauteries: one in the middle location of the head, one on all the horns of the head, one on the rear part of it, and three on the vertebrae of the neck.
E si es necessari en la malautia de mollificacio del cors de trops aquel e les malautes tollerantz e la malautia es fort, lahoras cauteriza aquel am quatre cauteris sobre les spondils del dos, e dererament am cauteri entro que sia comborit de la codena mot de lu, e aleva la tieua ma.	And if it is necessary in the disease of softening of the body of many and the patients are tolerating it well, but the disease is strong, then cauterize it with four cauteries on the vertebrae of the back, and finally one cautery into the code of the tongue, and lift up your hand.
E aprop cura aquel entro que sia sanat, e aquest sia cauteri olivar.	And then cure that until it is healed, and this is olive-shaped cauterization.
Capitol .x.	The tenth chapter.
De cauterisacio de epilemcia.	On Cauterization for Epilepsy.
No es cauterizat le epilemtic sino aquella epilemcia es per flecma.	It is not cauterized the epilepsy, but that epilepsy is caused by flux.
E donc cove que mondifiques le cervel de lu al comensament de lu am yeras e am l’autra curacio la qual havem dicta en la divisio quan le malaute es gran e es tollerant la exceperacio de las medicinas.	And therefore, it is necessary to soften the brain of him at the beginning with jellies and with the other cure which we have said in the division when the patient is great and tolerates the exception of medicines.
E si es enfant le qual no sufferte las medicinas, lahoras aministra guarguarissmes e mastiguatoris le servel mondifican, denant aquo per motz dias, am bonifficacio de las viandas.	And if it is a child who does not tolerate medicines, then administer guarguarisms and mastigatories that serve as mind-clearing remedies, before this for several days, with goodification of foods.
E aprop ras le cap del malaute, e aprop cauteriza aquel am un cauteri en le mieg loc del cap segon la manieyra precedent, e am autre cauteri en le occiput de lu, e sobre quascun corn del cap sieu cauterisa.	And then remove the head of the patient, and then cauterize it with one cautery in the middle location of the head according to the previous method, and another one on the back of the head, and over each horn of the head, it is cauterized.
E si le malaute es fort e es tollerant, lahoras cauteriza aquel am cauteris les quals he ditz, en havent paraliticament e mollificacio del cors sobre les spondils del col e les spondils del dos.	And if the patient is strong and tolerates it, then cauterize it with cauteries which I say, having paralyzed and softened the body on the vertebrae of the neck and the vertebrae of the back.
E sia cauteri olivar segon qu’es precedit.	And be olive-shaped according to what has been previously said.
Mays si le malaute es enfant, lahoras pausa cauteri subtil segon aquesta manieyra.	But if the patient is a child, then pause with a subtle cautery according to this method.
Capitol .xi.	The eleventh chapter.
De cauterizacio de melencolia.	On Cauterization for Melancholy.
Quan las causas de melencolia so humiditatz corrompudas e flacma gros, lahoras cauteriza aquel am les cauteris les quals havem ditz en le havent paralisi.	When the causes of melancholy are humid and corrupted and flux is great, then cauterize it with the cauteries which we have said in having paralyzed.
E si la causa de melencolia es superfluitat declinant a melencolia, e le cors del malaute es humit, lahoras da ha beure aquo que mundifica le cervel de lu segon aquo que ha precedut en la divisio.	And if the cause of melancholy is superfluity declining into melancholy, and the body of the patient is humid, then give him to drink water that softens the brain of him according to what has proceeded in the division.
E aprop ras le cap del malaute, e aprop fay tortora decentment fayta de li sobre le cercle, e aprop depausa aquela en le mieg loc del cap.	And then remove the head of the patient, and then make a tortoise-shaped figure, done from it over the circle, and then place that in the middle location of the head.
E le malaute sia sesent cayrat, e sia tengut de tota partida.	And the patient should be seated comfortably, and held by all parts.
E aprop pausa liniment; et es pus digne de boder antic de ovelhas.	And then pause with a liniment; and it is more worthy of an old sheep's border.
E escalfa aquel sobre le foc per calefaccio temprada per mesura, le qual le dit sufferta quan es mes en lu.	And warm him over the fire by tempered heat, to his liking, which he suffered when it was more in him.
E aprop vuo’ aquel en le mieg loc del cap de lu en le cercle, e leysa lu entro que sia enfregidat.	And then place that in the middle location of his head on the circle, and let it be there until he is warmed up.
E fay aquo am le malaute en tota semmana una veguada, am le autre regiment de lu bo entro que sia sanat; o si vols, cauteriza aquel fazen petitz puntz segon lo mays de lu, sino que tenguas la ma am un cauteri ayssi ordenat: aquesta es specia de cauteri la qual humecta le cervel am equalitat.	And do this with the patient for seven days, once a day, with another regimen of it good until he is healed; or if you wish, cauterize that making small points according to what is most in him, so that you hold your hand with a cautery thus ordered: this is a species of cautery which moistens the brain with equality.
E aprop pausa aquel coto enbegut en boder o en grays de gualina.	And then pause with a cloth wrapped in linen or grey wool.
Capitol .xii.	The twelfth chapter.
De cauterisacio de aygua descendent en le huel.	On Cauterization for Water that Descends into the Veins.
Quan a tu es declarat le comensament de aygua en le huel per les senhals les quals yeu he ditz en la divisio, lahoras comensa e dona en beure al malaute aquo que mondifique le cap de lu, e guarda aquel de totas humiditatz.	When you have declared the beginning of water in the veins through the signs which I have said in the division, then begin and give to drink to the patient water that softens the head of him, and guard that from all humidity.
E fay aquel suzar en banh en degu per alcus jorns.	And make that sweat in a bath for several days.
E aprop comanda a lu que raza le sieu cap, e cauteriza aquel am cauteri en le mieg loc del cap; e aprop cauteriza aquel am dos cauteris sobre dos templas si es le comensament de ysement de aygua en dos huels, o de la un latz si es comensamen de l’aygua en un huel.	And then command him to rub his head, and cauterize it with a cautery in the middle location of the head; and then cauterize it with two cauteries on both temples if there is the beginning of water in two veins, or of one side if there is the beginning of water in one vein.
Incideys am cauteri totas las venas e arcerias las quals so dejos la codena; e sian les cauteris en aquela lonh en la latitut de las templas.	Insert with a cautery all the veins and arteries that are below the code; and be the cauteries in that length, in the latitude of the temples.
E guarda te de fluxs de sanc quan es cauterizat; e si veses de lu fluxs de sanc, osta le am alcuna medicina, la qual es a tu possible.	And be careful of blood flows when it is being cauterized; and if you see blood flows from him, stop them with some medicine that is to your ability.
E yeu vindre am savieza la qual es en extraccio de arcerias e am abscizio de aquelas e cautela de fluxs de sanc.	And you will gain wisdom, which is in the extraction of arteries and in the absorption of those and caution against blood flows.
E alcunas vetz es cauterizat en le cervitz dejos dos osses am dos cauteris dererament produzitz.	And sometimes it is cauterized in the vertebrae below two bones with two cauteries gradually produced.
Capitol .xiii.	The thirteenth chapter.
De cauterizacio de lacrimas antiquas.	On Cauterization for Old Tears.
Quan lacrimas dels huels so antiquas assuduament e per las venas e arterias las quals so en le loc manifest del cap defora e es verificat que aquo es superfluitatz frejas flecmatiquas, lahoras cauteriza aquel am cauteri le qual havem recontat en le capitol de comensament de aygua cazent en les huels, e am cauteri en le mieg loc del cap e am dos cauteris en la cervitz dejos dos templas, e am dos cauteris en la cervitz dejos dos osses.	When tears from the eyes are ancient and due to the veins and arteries which are in the manifest location of the head outside and it is verified that this is superfluous and flux-like, then cauterize it with a cautery which we have recounted in the chapter on the beginning of water flowing into the veins, and also with a cautery in the middle location of the head and two cauteries in the vertebrae below two temples, and two cauteries in the vertebrae below two bones.
E si indigeyses de addicio, lahoras cauteriza aquel en tot latz de la coa del huel sobre la extremitat del sobrecilh am petit cauteri.	And if you need additional addition, then cauterize it in the entire length of the coccyx of the spine on the extremity of the forehead with a small cautery.
Capitol .xiiii.	The fourteenth chapter.
De cauterizacio de fetor de nas.	On Cauterization for Stench of the Nose.
Quan tu medicas aquel am aquo que havem dit en la divisio e no aprofieyta la tua medicacio, lahoras tu aparelha e dona en beure al malaute las cochias per tres noytz; e aprop ras le cap de lu, e cauteriza le am cauteri migier am cauteri olivar.	When you treat him with water as we have said in the division and your treatment does not take effect, then prepare yourself and give to drink to the patient cochial root for three nights; and then remove the head of him, and cauterize it with a middle-shaped cautery and an olive-shaped cautery.
E aprop cauteriza aquel am cauteri clavelh am dos cauteris sobre les dos sobrecilhs dejos les cabels un petit.	And then cauterize it with a holly-shaped cautery, and two cauteries on both foreheads below the hair, a little.
E guarda te de la arceria que no incindas aquela.	And be careful not to cut into that artery.
E del cauteri clavilh aquesta es la forma.	And of the holly-shaped cautery, this is the form.
Capitol .xv.	The fifteenth chapter.
De cauteri de mollificacio de palpebras dels huels.	On Cauterization for Softening of Eyelids of the Eyes.
Quan la palpebra del huel es mollificada per malautia o per humiditat, lahoras cauteriza aquela palpebre1 am un cauteri am aquest cauteri lunar; e aquesta es la forma de lu:	When the eyelid of the eye is softened by disease or humidity, then cauterize that eyelid with a cautery in the shape of a crescent moon; and this is the form of it:
E si vos, cauteriza aquel sobre les dos sobrecils un petit am dos cauteris en tota partida, e sian elonguatz de las timporas.	And if you wish, cauterize that on both foreheads a little with two cauteries in all parts, and be extended from the temples.
E sia la longitut de quascun cauteri segon la quantitat del sobrecil.	And be the length of each cautery according to the quantity of the forehead.
E no premas trop la tua ma am le cauteri, mays segon la quantitat que la tersa partida de la palpebre sia adhurida.	And do not press too hard with your hand and the cautery, but according to the quantity that the third part of the eyelid is hardened.
Capitol .xvi.	The sixteenth chapter.
De cauteri de la palpebre del huel quan les pels so convertitz a las partidas dedintz e punho le huel.	On Cauterization of the Eyelid of the Eye when the hairs are converted to the inner parts and push the eye.
Quan les pels del huel son convertitz a las partidas dedintz ayssi que pungo le huel, cauteri en aquels es segon dos manieyras, quar cauteri o es am fer o es am medicina comburent.	When the hairs of the eye are converted to the inner parts in such a way that they push into the eye, cauterize them by two methods: one method is with fire or another method is with medicine which burns.
Si am cauteri de lu am foc, comanda al malaute denant aquo que leyse les sieus pels ayssi cum aquels les quals les mundan, entro que sian prolonguatz e engualhatz; e si punho aquel deves le lor naysement, lahoras tu strenh les huels de lu am una benda per so que no sia maugut entro que·ls pels sian nascutz.	If with a cautery of fire, command the patient to look before him at those hairs as if they were being cleaned, until they are prolonged and equalized; and if pushing that hurts him, then you should strengthen the eyes of him with a bandage so that it is not troubled until the hairs are born.
Donc cum siran nascutz e engualhatz, lahoras pausa le cap del malaute en le tieu se, e aprop senha sobre la palpebre dels huels de lu am tenta, am senhal le qual sia segon la figura de fulha de merta, e sia le comensament del senhal prop dels pels.	Then when they are born and equalized, pause the head of the patient in your sight, and then sign above the eyelid of the eyes of him with a tenta, with a signal which is according to the figure of a leaf of myrtle, and be the beginning of the signal near the hairs.
E aprop pausa coto enbegut en album de huou o en mucillatge de ptilli sobre le huel.	And then pause with a cloth wrapped in albumen of egg white or in a poultice of pellitory on the eye.
E aprop igneys le cauteri del qual aquesta es la forma de lu.	And then ignite the cautery which this is the form of it.
E aprop cauteriza sobre la figura la qual as senhada, petit a petit, em motas veguadas, entro que sia comburida la superficia de la codena la qual es ayssi cum fuelha de mirta, tota aparent propriament.	And then cauterize on the figure which you have signaled, little by little, in many times, until the surface of the code is burned away like a leaf of myrtle, all appearing properly.
E senhal de sanetat de la tieua obra es que tu vegus la palpebre de l’huel ja esser contrayta e·ls pels de lu esser elevatz deves la punctura del huel.	And the sign of health for this work is that you see the eyelid of the eye already contracted and the hairs of him being lifted above the point of the eye.
E donc eleva la tua ma e laysa aquel per tres jorns, e aprop pausa sobre lu coto am boder entro que sia eredicada la scara.	And then lift up your hand and leave it for three days, and then pause with a cloth wrapped in linen until the scar is healed.
E aprop cura aquela am enguent entro que sia sanat.	And then cure that with ointment until it is healed.
Mays si retorna per les pels alcuna causa aprop lor naysement e la palpebra es mollificada, lahoras fay autra vetz le cauteri sobre aquel tot ayssi cum avias fayt primieyrament.	But if some cause returns to the hairs and the eyelid is softened again, then do it again just as you did the first time.
Mays si les pels so en la palpebra dejos, lahoras cauterisa aquela entro que sia elevada al sieu loc natural e sia engualhat e que les pels no punhan le huelh.	But if the hairs are in the eyelid below, then cauterize that until it is lifted to its natural place and equalized, so that the hairs do not push into the eye.
Mays le cauteri am medicina comburent aquest es que comandes al malaute que leyse les pels entro que sian prolonguatz e engualhatz, e aprop sia fayta de carta de drap la forma de fuelha de mirtra.	But the cautery with burning medicine is what you command the patient to look at the hairs until they are prolonged and equalized, and then make a shape of a leaf of myrtle on cloth.
E aprop pren de sabo conogut e de caus viva ana unc. .i., o quays aquo, e aprop mescle3 aquelas causas be, e fay aquo am festinacio per so que no sia enfregidat; e aprop expandeys de aquo sobre la carta la qual es fayta ayssi cum forma de fulha de mirtra, e pausa aquel sobre la un huel od amdos; e pausa dejos le huel coto enbegut en album de huou, e el cap del malaute sia en le tieu se.	And then take one ounce of known saffron and fresh cause. The end! And so, and then mix those causes well, and make this with a feast to prevent it from being cooled; and then spread the water on the paper which is made in the shape of a leaf of myrtle, and pause that over one eye or both eyes; and pause below the eye cloth wrapped in albumen of egg white, and the head of the patient be in your sight.
E pausa le dit sobre le medicina e prem aquela un petit e no la mauguas entro que lo malaute senta la mordicacio de la medicina, quar mordicacio es en lu ayssi cum de foc.	And then pause the said thing on the medicine and press that a little bit and not trouble it until the patient feels the pungency of the medicine, for pungency is in him like fire.
E donc cum percevera aquo que el atrobo mordicacio, lahoras leyssa la medicina e mau aquela am le tieu dit; donc cum cessa la mordicacio, lahoras remau la medicina he lava le huel am aygua; e lahoras considera si vezes la palpebra ja es levada ayssi cum es lavada deves la costriccio am foc o am incisio, quar lahoras esta be; e si no torna sobre aquela de la medicina sobre le loc en le qual no ha empremut la medicina e no se denigra entro que sia engualhada la tua operacio e sia contrayt le huel.	And then, as he perceives that the medicine has a pungent effect, pause the medicine and trouble it with your said thing; therefore, when the pungency ceases, then removethe medicine and wash the eye with water; and then consider if the eyelid is already lifted as if it were washed away by fire or incision, for now all is well; and if not, return to that spot where you did not apply the medicine and do not despise until your operation is equalized and the eye is contracted.
E aprop pausa sobre lu coto am boder entro que sia eradicada la codena de la adhustio, e aprop cura aquel am enguent deafinicon o am autre entro que sia sanat.	And then pause with a cloth wrapped in linen until the scar of adjustment is eradicated, and then cure that with ointment or another substance until it is healed.
E es necessari a tu, deves la tua operacio que guardes am pervigil diligencia que en le huel no caia re de la medicina, e si la palpebre aprop alscus dias es mollificada e alcuna causa dels pels punh en le huel, lahoras itera la tua medicina sobre aquel loc le qual de la palpebre es mollificat, e propriamen ayssi quo as fayt al comensament, e aprop enaviro lu entro que sia sanat.	And it is necessary for you to keep a diligent vigilance that the medicine does not fall into the eye, and if the eyelid is softened after some days and some cause of the hairs pushes into the eye, then repeat your medicine on that spot where the eyelid is softened, and do it exactly as you did at the beginning, and then send the patient away until he is healed.
E aquesta es la forma de fuelha de mirtra.	And this is the form of a leaf of myrtle.
E sapias que les huels dels homes son diversificatz segon la magnitut e la parvitat, e donc segon aquo es fayta la tua contraccio.	And know that the eyes of men are diversified according to their magnitude and smallness, and therefore, according to this, is made your contraction.
E no sira amaguada la via de rectetut ad aquel al qual es studi en aquesta art.	And may not be hidden the way of rectitude to him who studies in this art.
Capitol .xvii.	The seventeenth chapter.
De cauterizacio de fistula que es en le lacrimal de l’huel.	On Cauterization of a Fistula that is in the Lachrymal Duct of the Eye.
Quan tu curas fistula am aquo que havem dit en las divisios de las malautias e no confereys la tua curacio, lahoras cove que tu cauterizas aquela segon aquesta manieyra: comanda al malaute que pause le cap sieu en le tieu se, e tengua le cap de lu alcun ministre entre las tieuas mas en tal manieyra que no sia maugut ni agitat am le sieu cap.	When you cure a fistula with the water we have said in the divisions of diseases and it does not correspond to your treatment, then cause yourself to cauterize that according to this method: command the patient to pause his head in your sight, and hold the head of him by some minister between your knees in such a way that it is not troubled or agitated with his own head.
E aprop pausa coto enfus en album de huou o en mucellage de ptilli sobre le huel de lu.	And then pause with a cloth wrapped in albumen of egg white or in a poultice of pellitory on the eye of him.
E aprop igneys le cauteri del qual aquesta es la forma:	And then ignite the cautery which this is the form:
le qual sia conquau, ayssi cum es forma de cana o de pena de voltor, de la una extremitat am la qual es fayta lo cauteri.	which is curved, like a form of cane or a pen nib of vulture, from one extremity to the other, with which the cautery is made.
E si voys, sia penetrant entro a la autra extremitat.	And if you wish, be penetrating into the other extremity.
E si vols sia sort ayssi cum tenta.	And if you want, be out like a tent.
Mays empero aquel que es concau es milhor a la tieua obra.	But meanwhile that which is curved is better for your work.
E aprop prem la fistula si es uberta, e tra de lu sania et exsicca aquela.	And then press the fistula if it is open, and draw out from it pus and dry up that.
E si no es uberta, lahoras obre aquela e extratz la poyredura de lu.	And if it is not open, then operate on it and extract the pus from it.
E aprop pausa sobre lu le cauteri le qual sia be ignit, e te am aquel la tieua ma un petit deves le cauteri del huel a la partida del nas, per so que no erre la tua ma o le malaute sia enquietat, e lahoras pausa le cauteri en le grays del huel e corrompas aquel.	And then pause with the cautery which is well ignited, and take that in your hand a little bit of the cautery from the eye to the nostril, so that you do not err or the patient be troubled, and then pause the cautery on the gray of the eye and corrupt that.
E donc si al comensament del tieu cauteri perve entro al os, bo es; e sino, lahoras itera le cauteri una veguada o dos, si mestiers era; e layssa aquel ayssi per tres jorns, e aprop pausa sobre aquel coto am boder e enviro lu am enguent exsiccatiu entro que sia sanat.	And thus if at the beginning of your cautery you pierce into the bone, it is good; and otherwise, then repeat the cautery one or two times as needed; and leave that so for three days, and then pause with a cloth wrapped in linen and surround it with an ointment to dry until it is healed.
Mays si eran passatz xi dias e no es sanat, lahoras pausa sobre lu medicina aguda corrosiva entro que l’os sia descubert e sia ras segon que conveneys en le sieu capitol.	But if it has been passed eleven days and it is not healed, then pause with the medicine acute corrosive until the bone is uncovered and scraped according to what is written in your own chapter.
E es autra manieyra de cauteri de fistula la qual alscus primiers diysero: enten al loc de la fistula e fen aquela e aprop pausa en aquela fissura camaen subtil del qual es la forma de lu: E fon en aquela la quantitat de i unc de plom fundut; e te la tua ma am camaem am bona retencio, e no sia maugut le malaute per so que le plom fundut no pervengua al huel de aquel; e cove que pausas sobre le huel del malaute coto enfus en album de huou o en aygua, quar plom adhureys le loc de la fistula e sana aquela per sanacio meravilhora.	And there is another method of cautery for a fistula which some first doctors also described: enter the location of the fistula and fill it with that; and then pause in that fissure, as subtle as the form of it: And pour into that the quantity of one ounce of melted lead; and take your hand with a camomile with good retention, and do not trouble the patient so that the melted lead does not reach the eye of him; and cause that you pause on the eye of the patient cloth wrapped in albumen of egg white or water, because lead adheres to the location of the fistula and heals it through marvelous healing.
E si la fistula es sanada am aquo que havem dit del cauteri e de la curacio, bo es; e sino, lahoras es necessari aministrar trauc del nas e reduzir la fistula al cors del nas segon que vindra en son loc propri.	And if the fistula is healed with the water we have said about the cautery and healing, it is good; and otherwise, then it is necessary to administer a cut of the nose and reduce the fistula to the body of the nose according to what will come in its own proper place.
Capitol .xviii.	The eighteenth chapter.
De cauterizacio de la fendedura des potz.	On Cauterization of the Fissure of the Lips.
Motas veguadas accideysso fissuras en las labias, e majorment en las labias dels enfantz.	Many times it happens that fissures occur on the lips, and most especially on the lips of children.
Donc cum tu curas aquelas fissuras am aquo que nos havem dit en las divisios e no aprofieyta la tua cura, lahoras igneys le cauteri petit cutellar segon aquesta forma que s’ensiec:	Therefore, as you cure those fissures with the water we have said in the divisions and it does not improve your treatment, then ignite the cautery small knife according to this form that is seen:
E sia la conquavitat de lu segon la subtilitat de cotella.	And be the curvature of it according to the subtlety of a scalpel.
Aprop pausa aquel init cuytadament en aquelas fissuras entro que·l cauteri pervengua al preon de las fissuras.	And then pause with that instrument gently in those fissures until the cautery reaches the depth of the fissures.
E aprop cura aquel am cerotz entro que sia sanat.	And then cure that with ointment until it is healed.
Capitol .xix.	The nineteenth chapter.
De cauterizacio de fistula en la boca.	On Cauterization of a Fistula in the Mouth.
Quan en la razit de uvula o en le paladar o en las razitz de las dentz endeve apostema e aprop fa brac, e aprop es rompuda, e aprop es antiquada, e corr brac e es fayta fistula, e aprop tu curas aquela e no aprofieyta a curacio, lahoras cove que tu igniscas cauteri segon la quantitat que sia receubuda en la fistula, e aprop met aquel ignit en le trauc de la fistola, e te la tua ma entro que pervengua le ferr ignit al preon de lu, e al derier de lu fazen aysso una veguada o dos; e aprop cura aquel am aquo que nos havem dit de la curacio entro que sia sanat.	When in the root of the uvula or on the palate or on the roots of the teeth an apostema forms and then breaks out, and then becomes old, and a fistula is formed, and you cure that but it does not improve with your treatment, then cause yourself to ignite the cautery according to the quantity received in the fistula, and place that ignited cauteri into the opening of the fistula, and take your hand so that the hot iron reaches the depth of it, and at the end make it so once or twice; and then cure that with the water we have said about healing until it is healed.
E donc si la sania es abscindita e es sanat, bo es; e sino, lahoras es necessari de descubrir le loc e hostar le os corrumput segon que vindra en son capitol.	And thus if the pus is discharged and healed, it is good; and otherwise, then it is necessary to discover the location and expose the corrupted bone according to what will come in its own chapter.
Capitol .xx.	The twentieth chapter.
De cauterisacio de las dentz e de mollificacio de las angivas.	On Cauterization of the Teeth and Softening of the Gums.
Quan las angivas son mollificadas per humiditat e las dentz son maugudas, e curas aquelas am medicinas e no confereys, lahoras pausa le cap del malaute en le tieu se, e aprop igneys le cauteri la forma del qual vindra aprop aysso, enayssi que tu pauses la quanula sobre la dent e entromet en aquela le cauteri ignit festinantment, e te la tieua ma un petit entro que·l malaute cente la calor del foc a la razit de la dent esser pervenguda.	When the gums are softened by humidity and the teeth are troubled, and you cure those with medicines but they do not correspond, then pause the head of the patient in your sight, and then ignite the cautery in the form which will come thus, namely that you pause the caustic on the tooth and insert into it the ignited cautery hastily, and take your hand a little bit until the patient feels the heat of the fire at the root of the tooth to be reached.
E aprop leva la tua ma, e aprop itera le cauteri alcunas veguadas segon que vols.	And then lift up your hand, and then repeat the cautery several times as you wish.
E aprop le malaute huompla la sua boca de aygua de sal e tengua aquela per una hora, e pueys stupa aquela, quar la dent mauguda es fermada e la gengiva mollificada es strenguda e la humiditat corrompuda es exsiccada.	And then the patient should fill his mouth with saltwater and keep it for an hour, and afterwards stop, because the troubled tooth is closed and the softened gum is strengthened and the corrupted humidity is dried up.
Capitol .xxi.	The twenty-first chapter.
De cauterisacio de dolor de dent.	On Cauterization of Toothache.
Quan dolor de dent es per fregiditat, o en lu es freg o verm, o no comfereys la curacio am medicina, lahoras cauteri en aquela es segon dos manieyras: o cauteri am boder de vacas, o cauteri am foc.	When toothache is caused by coldness, or in it is cold or warm, or does not correspond with the cure with medicine, then cauterize that according to two methods: either cauterization with the edge of cows, or cauterization with fire.
Cauteri am boder es que tu prenguas boder de vacas e bulhas aquel en culhe de ferr , e aprop pren coto e envolopa le sobre la extremitat de la tenta, e aprop enmergeys aquel am boder bulhit, e pausa aquel sobre la dent dolorosa festinantment entro que sia enfregidat.	Cauterization with the edge is that you take the edge of cows and boil it in a cauldron of iron, and then take a cloth and wrap it around the end of the tent, and then immerse that with boiled edge, and pause that over the painful tooth hastily until it is cooled.
E aprop itera aquela alcunas veguadas entro que la vertut del foc pervengua a la razit de la dentz.	And then repeat that several times until the virtue of fire reaches the root of the teeth.
E si voys, submergeys lana o coto en le boder desus dit, e pausa aquel sobre la dent dolent, e pausa sobre aquel ferr ignit entro que·l ferr pervengua al preon de la conquavitat de la dent.	And if you wish, immerse wool or cloth in the edge mentioned above, and pause that over the painful tooth, and pause on top of that hot iron until the iron reaches the depth of the curvature of the tooth.
Mays empero la cauterizacio am foc es que tu atendas a la quannula de eram o de ferr, e sia en le cor de lu alcuna grocesa e la acuitat del foc no pervengua a la boca del malaute.	But meanwhile the cauterization by fire is that you attend to the heat of iron or copper, and be in its core some roughness and the sharpness of the fire does not reach the mouth of the patient.
E aprop igneys le cauteri la forma del qual vindra, e pausa aquel sobre la dent e te la tua ma entro que·l cauteri sia enfregidat; e fay aquo alcunas veguadas quar la dolor sira remauguda o en aquel dia o en l’autre dia.	And then ignite the cautery in the form which will come, and pause that over the tooth and take your hand until the cautery is cooled; and do this several times because the pain is relieved or on that day or on the next day.
E cove que per empressio de aquel cauteri que·l malaute umpla la sieua boca de bon boder e tengua aquel per una hora e aprop scupa le; e aquesta es la forma del cauteri.
