And cause that by the impression of that cautery, the patient should fill his mouth with good bread and keep it for an hour, and then spit it out; and this is the form of the cautery.
E cauteriza am qual que tu voys extremittat segon que a tu es possible.	And cauterize as much as you wish at the extreme end according to what is possible for you.
E aquesta es la forma de la cannula:	And this is the form of the caustic:
Capitol .xxii.	The twenty-second chapter.
De cauterizacio de extrophulos.	On Cauterization of Hernias.
Quan extrophulos so de flecma e de humors fregas e no so hobedientz a digistio per medicinas e tu voys la digistio de aquelas leugerament, lahoras tu igneys le cauteri conquau la forma del qual es aquesta seguen, havent dos extremitatz hubertas per que yesca le fum deves le cauteri per l’autra extremitat, e pausa aquel ignit sobre aquel apostema una veguada, e autre si indigeyses de aquel, entro que pervengua al preon del apostema.	When hernias are caused by fat and cold humors and do not obey digestion by medicines, and you wish to induce digestion of those slightly, then ignite the cautery curved in the form which is this following, having two extremities broad for the smoke of the cautery to escape through one extremity, and pause that ignited over that apostema once, or another time if needed, until it reaches the depth of the apostema.
E si l’apostema es pauca, lahoras pausa le cauteri segon la quantitat del apostema, e aprop leyssa le per tres jorns e pausa sobre lu coto enfus en boder entro que sia remaugut aquo que·l foc ha comburit.	And if the apostema is small, then pause the cautery according to the quantity of the apostema, and let it be for three days and pause on top of that cloth wrapped in linen until what the fire has burned is relieved.
E aprop cura aquel am enguent e tentas e draps entro que sia sanat.	And then cure that with ointment and tents and cloths until it is healed.
E la forma de la cannula o deu cauteri a tal es comveyter.	And the form of the caustic or of the cautery to this end is to convey.
Capitol .xxiii.	The twenty-third chapter.
De cauterizacio de rauquiera de votz e de constriccio de ale.	On Cauterization of Hoarseness of Voice and Constriction of Ale.
Quan las humiditatz veno sobre le quanal del pulmo, e majorment quan aquo es am fregiditat de compleccio, lahoras cove que·l malaute sia evacuat al comensament am medicinas laxativas, e aprop cauteriza aquel deves la razit del golayro en le loc depremegut.	When the humors come out of the throat and most especially when that is caused by coldness of congestion, then it is necessary to evacuate the patient at the beginning with laxative medicines, and then cauterize that in the root of the gullet in the location affected.
E guarda te que no pervenguas am le cauteri al golayro ni no comburas de la codena de lu sino un pauc.	And beware that you do not burn too deeply with the cautery nor consume the cord of it, but only a little.
E cauteriza aquel am autra cauteri deves la junctura del col en le derier espondil de lu.	And then cauterize that with another cautery at the joint of the neck in the last vertebra of it.
E·l cauteri de lu sia clavilh sego la maniera precedent.	And the cautery of it shall be like a claw, following the previous manner.
E aprop cura aquel am aquo que es precedit entro que sia sanat.	And then cure that with water that is preceded by it until it is healed.
Capitol .xxiiii.	The twenty-fourth chapter.
De cauterizacio de malautia del pulmo e de tos.	On Cauterization of Pulmonary Disease and Cough.
Quan tos e malautia de pulmo so de humiditatz fregas e le malaute no ha febre ni tisic e es malautia antiqua, lahoras cauterisa aquel am dos cauteris sobre la furcula en les locz depremegutz leontz e buoytz; e am autra cauteri en le mieg loc del pietz entre dos mamillos; e sia le cauteri clavilh segon la forma precedent.	When cough and pulmonary disease are caused by cold humors and the patient does not have fever or sweating, but is an old illness, then cauterize that with two cauteries on the furcula in the affected locations, and with another cautery in the middle of the breast between two nipples; and let the cautery be like a claw according to the previous form.
E si vols, sia la tua cauterizacio punctan am le cauteri que es apelat puncta, la forma del qual precedeys en la ponctacio de dolor de aurelhas.	And if you wish, then make your cautery punctate with the points that are called puncture, in the form which precedes in the puncturing of earache.
E sian puntz entro cays ad aquels; e aprop cura aquel am aquo meteys que es precedit entro que sia sanat.	And make points until they reach those places; and then cure that with water that is preceded by it, until it is healed.
E ya sia le cauteri haventz tres ramps quar cauterizacio es am aquel: am una veguada podes far tres cauteris segon aquesta forma:	And now the cauteries have three bends where cauterization is done in that way: you can do three cauteries according to this form once.
Capitol .xxv.	The twenty-fifth chapter.
De cauterizacio de titillic que es le cap del ajutori.	On Cauterization of Titillation which is the Head of Assistance.
Quan le cap del ajutori es dislocat per causa de humiditatz lubricas e no es fermat en la hora del sieu retornament deves la sua dislocacio entro que sia a lu aquo costuma de retornar, e aprop per un petit movement es deslocat ayssi que s’endeve, ayssi cum nos havem testificat, lahoras cove que primieyrament redusiscas la dislocacio, e aprop le malaute sia reversat sobre le sieu dos o sobre le latz sa; e aprop eleva la codena la qual es en la partida dedintz del citillic a las partidas desus am les ditz de la tua ma sinistra, si la junctura es dislocada a las partidas dedintz.	When the head of assistance is displaced due to cause of lubricous humors and does not return to its usual place, and for a little movement it becomes displaced again as we have testified, then it is necessary to first reduce the displacement, and then let the patient be reversed onto his back or side; and then elevate the cord which is in the parting line above the citillic at the said parts with your left hand, if the juncture is dislocated above.
E aprop igneys le cauteri havent dos caps; e aquesta es la forma de lu:	And then ignite the cautery having two heads; and this is its form:
E aprop cauteriza la codena entro que penetre aquela entro al autre latz; e vindra la figura de cauterizacio lahoras de iv caps cauteris.	And then cauterize the cord so that it enters one side and penetrates into the other; and the figure of cauterization will be like this, with four heads of cautery.
e so aquel subtils segon la quantitat de tenta; e aquesta es la forma de lu:	and thus those subtleties according to the quantity of cloth; and this is its form:
E alcunas veguadas es ajustat segon aquest comte i per que son les cauteris .viii.	And sometimes it is adjusted according to this count, because there are eight cauteries.
E aprop pausa sobre le cauteri porys cuytz am sal, e aprop fay adherir le malaute a trenquilitat, e lo membre no sia maugut per alcun temps entro que sia confortat.	And then pause over the cautery with porous cloth soaked in salt, and then cause the patient to adhere to quietness, and let the member not be troubled for some time until it is comforted.
E si la dislocacio es a las partidas desus e tart es fayt aquo, lahoras cauteriza sobre le muscle am cauteri clavilh o am motz cauteris puntan, quar la junctura es confermada e la humiditat es romauguda e le malaute es sanat.	And if the displacement is above and it becomes confirmed, then cauterize on the muscle with a claw-shaped cautery or with punctate cauteries, because the juncture is confirmed, and the humidity is removed, and the patient is healed.
Capitol .xxvi.	The twenty-sixth chapter.
De cauterizacio del stomac.	On Cauterization of the Stomach.
Quan veno en l’estomac freg e motas humiditatz entro que aquel extrazo de la sua compleccio e so multiplicatz raumases a lu, e si tu continuas las manieyras de curacio e no confereyso, lahoras cove que le malaute sia sobre le sieu dos ressupinat, e extenda las suas mas e las suas coysas, e aprop cauteriza aquel am tres cauteris: an un cauteri dejos le pietz per la quantitat d’un dit am cauteri clavilh, e am dos cauteris dejos del dos costatz del cauteri, entro que vengua la figura de cauteri triangulada; e elonga entre els que no sian ajustatz que faran poyredura.	When cold humors and many fluids come out of the stomach and are expelled from its natural disposition and multiply in it, and if you continue with the methods of cure and do not conform, then it is necessary to let the patient lie on his back, and stretch out his arms and legs, and then cauterize that with three cauteries: one at the breast for the quantity of a finger with a claw-shaped cautery, and two at the sides of the cautery, so that the figure of triangular cautery appears; and elongate between them so that they are not adjusted to cause pressure.
E si la profunditat del cauteri la quantitat de les dos terses de la grocesa de la codena.	And if the depth of the cautery is the quantity of two thirds of the thickness of the cord.
E sia la figura del cauteri segon aquesta forma ses addicio, E si vols, cauteriza am gran cauteri en le mieg loc del estomac segon aquesta forma; et aquest sia un cauteri segon la forma de cercle segon aquesta forma:	And be the figure of the cautery according to this form without addition, And if you wish, then cauterize with a large cautery in the middle location of the stomach according to this form; and this is one cautery according to the form of a circle according to this form:
E sia cauterizat l’estomac punctan ad aquel que de aquest cauteri es spaventat: e es que tu senhes sobre l’estomac punt segon la quantitat que voles am tenta, e aprop cauteriza aquel am cauteri en les puntz; e aprop cura aquel am la curacio qu’es precedita entro que sia sanat.	And be the stomach punctured by that which is frightened by this cautery: and it is that you sense on the stomach point according to the quantity that you wish with cloth, and then cauterize those points with a cautery; and then cure that with the cure that precedes it until it is healed.
Capitol .xxvii.	The twenty-seventh chapter.
De cauterizacio del fietge fret.	On Cauterization of Fretful Fetter.
Quan endeve en le fietge dolor per fregiditat o per humiditat o per grossa ventositat entro que de la sieua normal compleccio sia getat per egressio superflua, e es curat le malaute am aquo que havem dit e no comfereys, lahoras cove que·l malaute sia ressupinat sobre la sua cervitz, e senhes am tenta tres cauteris segon aquesta forma et aquesta quantitat meteyssa sobre le fietge dejos dels ipocondres, la hon perve le decubit de home.	When distress arises in the fetlock due to coldness or humidity or excessive evaporation, and it is expelled from its natural disposition by superfluous egress, and the patient is cured with water as we have said and does not correspond, then it is necessary that the patient lie on his back with his head bent, and sense with cloth three cauteries according to this form and quantity placed on the fetlock left of the hip bones, where the seat of man is.
E sia l’espazi le qual es entre quascun cauteri segon la grossetut del dit, e sia le cauteri segon la longitut del cors dreyta.	And be the space which is between each cautery according to the thickness of the finger, and be the cauteries according to the length of a straight cord.
E no compremas la tua am le cauteri mot.	And do not compress your hand with the cautery motion.
E si la quantitat de aquo que es adhurit la quantitat de la maytat de la specitut de la codena, e no y sia pus ajustat; e si le malaute stant sobre les pes de lu; e si no es estant, lahoras sia jassent, le qual ja ha extendudas las suas coysas, e eleve les sieus brasses.	And if the quantity of water that is absorbed is equal to the quantity of the maturation of the cord's substance, and it is not adjusted; and if the patient stands on his feet; and if he is not standing, then let him be lying down, which has already stretched out its legs, and elevated its arms.
E es aquesta la forma del cauteri:	And this is the form of the cautery:
E a tu es possible que cauterizes aquestz cauteris am cauteri cutellar, quan es am tu subtilitat e prudencia en l’art.	And if it is possible for you to cauterize these cauteries with a knife-shaped cautery, when it is with your subtlety and prudence in the art.
E guarda te que trop no procesiscas en la cauterizacio, e sia adhurida la specitut de tota la codena per que sia adhurit tot le cors e pervengua entro als budels, quar la codena aqui es subtil; e sapias aquo.	And beware that you do not proceed too much in the cauterization, and let the substance of all the cord be absorbed so that it is absorbed throughout the body and reaches into the vessels, for the cord here is subtle; and know this.
Capitol .xxviii.	The twenty-eighth chapter.
De perforacio de apostema del fietge am cauteri.	On Perforation of Apostema of the Fetlock with a Cautery.
Quan endeve excitura o apostema en le fietge e voles saber si aquel apostema es en le carn del fietge o en la tunica de lu, lahoras si es en la carn del fietge, le malaute atrobo gravitat e dolor ses acuitat.	When a swelling or apostema arises in the fetlock and you wish to know if that apostema is in the flesh of the fetlock or in its tendon, then if it is in the flesh of the fetlock, the patient's gravity and pain become more acute.
E si es en la tunica del fietge, am la dolor es acuitat gran e vezes que ja afatiguatz les metges la cura de lu.	And if it is in the tendon of the fetlock, with great pain and many times that already fatigues the doctors to cure it.
Donc cove que·l malaute sia enversat sobre la sieua cervit; e aprop senha le loc de l’apostema am tenta; e aprop igneys le cauteri le quel es asemblat a rag, la forma del qual a precedit en l’autra pagina.	Therefore, it is necessary that the patient be turned over onto his back; and then sense the location of the apostema with cloth; and then ignite the cautery which is similar to rag, the form of which has preceded on the other page.
E cauteriza am aquel i cauteri entro que tota la codena sia comborida, entro que pervengua al ciphac, entro qu’en yesca sania.	And then cauterize with that and the cautery until all the cord is consumed, until it reaches the ciphac, until in which you escape with health.
E aprop cura aquel per curacio dels autres apostemas entro que sia sanat.	And then cure that with the cure of other apostemas until it is healed.
E no cove que de aquesta forma de cauteri use sino aquel del qual le estudi en l’art de medicina es prolonguat, e en las mas del qual motas malautias an conogut; mays aquest am esperiment alcunas veguadas sia ardit sobre aquesta operacio, mays empero leyssa aquela deves nos, e es miels.	And it is not necessary to use this form of cauterization except by that doctor who has prolonged his study in the art of medicine and has known many diseases; but this one with experience has sometimes been bold in this operation, yet nonetheless you should follow my counsel, and it will be better.
Capitol .xxix.	The twenty-ninth chapter.
De cauterizacio de plauresi.	On Cauterization of Pleurisy.
Diyssero les antics cauteri de las razitz de aristologia a plauresi frega segon aquesta manieyra esser fazedor, e es aquest que tu prenguas de las razitz de aristologia longa secca una razit pun longua que es trobada, e sia de la grossetut del dit.	They say the ancient cauteries of the roots of aristology are to be used for pleurisy in a cold manner according to this way of making, and it is that which you take from the roots of aristology long dry one root point long which is found, and it is of the thickness of a finger.
E aprop submergeys aquela en oli e eysen aquela al foc, e aprop cauteriza per un cauteri en aquel loc le qual es entre la continuacio de la furcula am le col; e am dos cauteris petitz dejos guidazi, un pauc declinans a la partida que es dejus la barba, e am dos cauteris en aquo que es declinant entre la quinta costa e la cizena, declinant un pauc a las partidas detras; e am autre cauteri en le mieg loc del pietz; et am autre sobre l’estomac, et am tres cauteris de las partidas detras; et am un cauteri en aquel loc le qual es entre las dos spallas, e am dos cauteris dels dos latz del pietz, dejos le cauteri le qual es entre doas spallas.	And then immerse that in oil and ignite that at the fire, and then cauterize with one cautery at the location which is between the continuation of the furcula and the neck; and with two small cauteries on the sides, one slightly declining towards the party that is below the beard, and with two others in that which is declining between the fifth rib and the navel, declining a little behind; and with another one in the middle location of the thigh; and with another one above the stomach, and with three others on the back; and with one cautery at the location which is between the two shoulder blades, and with two others from both sides of the thigh, leaving out the cautery which is between the two shoulder blades.
E no cove que compremas la tua ma am le cauteri, ans sia en le manifest de la codena en obra.	And it is not necessary to compress your hand with the cautery, but rather let it be in the manifestation of the cord's work.
E ja diyssero alscus antics que so alscus dels homes les quals uson de cauteri de ferr semblant a ray e igneysso aquel, e meto aquel en aquel loc le qual es entre las costas, entro que pervenguam am aquel ad aquel apostema e sia foragetada sania, ayssi cum havem dit en l’apostema del fietge.	And already some ancient ones have said that there are some men who use a cautery of iron resembling a ray and ignite it, and put it in the location which is between the ribs, so that it reaches to that apostema and expels bad blood, just as we have said in the apostema of the fetlock.
Mays en aquesta perforacio am cauteri no es ses temor, quar hu mor tantost ho accideys en le loc fistula a la qual no es sanacio.	But in this perforation with a cautery there is no fear, for too much happens soon enough in the location of the fistula to which there is no healing.
Capitol .xxx.	The thirtieth chapter.
De la cauterizacio de la melsa.	On Cauterization of the Mole.
Quan tu curas la malautia de la melsa am aquo que havem dit de la curacio en la divisio e no confereys la tua curacio, lahoras cauteri en lu es segon tres manieras, las quals totas son dreyturieras, de las quals la una es que fassas tres cauteris o quatre linhan segon la longitut de la melsa segon la figura dels cauteris del fietge, la figura dels quals ha precedit.	When you cure the disease of the mole with water as we have said in the division and do not conform your cure, then cauterize it in three ways, all of which are right, of which one is that you make three or four lines according to the length of the mole according to the figure of the cauteries of the fetlock, the figure of which has preceded.
E sia entre quascun cauteri la grossetut d’un dit o un pauc mes, e la manieyra del cauteri sia la manieyra la qual havem dita en le cauteri del fietge engualment.	And be the thickness between each cautery that of a finger or a little more, and the manner of the cautery be the manner which we have said in the cautery of the fetlock, equally.
E no compremas la tua ma am le cauteri; e le malaute sia eves sobre lo sieu dos.	And do not compress your hand with the cautery; and let the patient lie on his back.
E es autra manieyra de cauterizar, so es que tu igniscas le cauteri haventz dos vertimentz, la qual causa havem dita en le capitol de dislocacio del muscle, e elava la codena la qual es en le endreyt de la melsa la hon perve le jazer del malaute sinistre.	And it is another manner of cauterizing, so that you ignite the cautery having two handles, which we have said in the chapter on dislocation of the muscle, and elevate the cord which is at the end of the mole, where the left side of the patient's body will be.
E sia la tua elevacio am la qual elevas la codena segon la longuesa del cors, per que sian faytz cauteris segon la latitut del cos.	And let your elevation be with which you elevate the cord according to the length of the body, so that the cauteries may be made according to the latitude of the body.
E aprop entromet les dos vernimentz, ignitz mot, en aquel entro que am aquels penetres la codena de la autra part.	And then enter the two handles, ignite it, into that which with those you will penetrate the cord of the other side.
E aprop extrayt le cauteri; e donc son faytz quatre cauteris.	And then extract the cautery; and thus four cauteries are made.
E si voys, cauteriza am cauteri havent tres vernimentz.	And if you wish, cauterize with a cautery having three handles.
E aprop tu cura le cauteri pus que aia laysat de getar brac per trops jorns, quar mays es comferent que las autras causas precedentz en la curacio.	And then cure the cautery more than it has already laid down to get rid of the excess for too many days, because it is more certain that the other causes previously mentioned in the cure.
Capitol .xxxi.	The thirty-first chapter.
De cauterizacio de ydropici.	On Cauterization of Hydrocephalus.
Cauteri no catz en ydropici sino en alcinte3 propriament.	Cauteries are not used in hydrocephalus, but only in acute cases properly.
Quan tu curas le ydropic am las manieyras de curacio las quals havem ditas en la divisio e no confereys la tua curacio, lahoras cove que aquel cauterizes am quatre cauteris en le cercuit del embelic e am un cauteri sobre l’estomac, e am autre cauteri sobre le fietge, e am autre cauteri sobre la melsa, e am dos cauteris entre les spondils del dos, e un cauteri en lo dreyt del pietz, e am autre cauteri sobre l’estomac.	When you cure the hydrocephalus with the methods of cure which we have said in the division and do not conform your cure, then it is necessary to cauterize with four cauteries around the waistline and one on the stomach, and another on the thigh, and another on the mole, and two between the vertebrae of the back, and one on the right side of the leg, and another on the stomach.
E la quantitat de la profunditat del cauteri sia propdana a la spicitut de la codena.	And the quantity of the depth of the cautery be proportioned to the thickness of the cord.
E aprop layssa le cauteri ubert per so que gete brac per lonc temps.	And then let the cautery remain open for that reason so that it may get rid of excess for a long time.
E no evacuas le malaute de curacio aprop le cauteri am aquo que cove per que sian agreguadas a lu doas entencios, e sira festinada a lu am ajutori sanacio.	And do not evacuate the patient from cure near the cautery with water as is necessary for two purposes, and let it be hastened to him with the aid of healing.
La forma del cauteri am lo qual es cauterizat lo ventre sia clavilh segon que la forma de aquel es desus precedent, e es aquel am le qual es cauterizat le dos sia olivar segon qu’es precedent a la sua forma.	The form of the cautery with which the stomach is cauterized is claw-shaped according to its previous form, and that with which the back is cauterized is olive-shaped according to its previous form.
Capitol .xxxii.	The thirty-second chapter.
De cauterizacio de pes e de las coyssas.	On Cauterization of Feet and Legs.
Quan les pes so apostematz en ydropitz e so repletz de aygua sitrina, cove que cauterisas les pes sobre le dos del pe in nocrati aquo que es entre le auricular e le anular, e eleva la tua ma am le cauteri e no torses aquel; e aprop eleva la tua ma, e no retornes aquela de tot, quar l’aygua satrina rezuda.	When the feet are swollen with dropsy and filled with serous water, it is necessary to cauterize the feet above the ankle in non-irrigated water that is between the auricular and anular, and elevate your hand with the cautery and do not twist it; and then elevate your hand, and do not return it completely, because the serous water resists.
Es le cauteri segon aquesta forma: E aprop fay sobre las doas coyssas dos cauteris, e en quascuna coysa sia feyt cauteri am la extremitat del cauteri cutellar.	This is the cautery according to this form: And then make two cauteries on each leg, and in each leg be made a cautery at the extremity of the knife-shaped cautery.
E sia le cauteri segon la longitut de la coyssa: i dejos le denolh e l’autre jos le mieg loc de la coyssa; e sobre quascuna coyssa dos cauteris.	And the cauteries be according to the length of the leg: one at the top and the other at the middle location of the leg; and on each leg two cauteries.
E layssa la plagua uberta ses curacio per lonc temps per so que alcuna aygua resuda de lu.	And let the wound remain open without cure for a long time because some water may flow from it.
E aprop cura le am aquelas causas las quals havem ditas.	And then cure with those causes which we have said.
Capitol .xxxiii.	The thirty-third chapter.
De cauterizacio de cos de ventre.	On Cauterization of the Abdomen.
Quan cos de ventre es per freg e per humiditat entro que debelice las vertutz, so es la vertut digestiva e retentiva, las quals so en l’estomac e en les budels, e es curat aquo am las manieyras de curacio e no confereys, e vezes le malaute suffertan cauteri de vertut exhiberant, lahoras cauteriza aquel am gran cauteri sobre le sieu stomac segon que a precedit en la cauterizacio del estomac, am le cauteri del cercle e am quatre cauteris en le cercuit del embelic subtils, am cauteri clavilh subtil; e am cauteri sobre le alcatin sobre alozis gran, o am dos cauteris.	When the abdomen is cold and humid, causing the digestive and retentive virtues to be debilitated in the stomach and intestines, and it is cured with the methods of cure and does not conform, and sometimes the patient requires a cautery of virtue to exhibit, then cauterize that with a large cautery on his stomach according to what has preceded in the cauterization of the stomach, with the ring-shaped cautery and four subtle cauteries around the waistline, with a claw-shaped subtle cautery; and with a cautery above the navel or two.
E si vezes las humiditatz exhuberants e le malaute aquo tollerant, lahoras cauteriza aquel sobre le pentenilh e sobre les budels, e fort leu ajustant dos cauteris sobre l’estomac e prop dels inguonas, quar es curacio perficent de juvament de la qual no erras.	And if sometimes the excess of humidity and the patient's tolerance are abundant, then cauterize that on the navel and on the intestines, and firmly adjust two cauteries above the stomach and near the inguinal region, because it is a perfect cure for the juice of which you will not err.
Capitol .xxxiv.	The thirty-fourth chapter.
De cauterizacio de emorroydas antiquas.	On Cauterization of Old Hemorrhoids.
Quan so en la natura derier emorroydas antiquas o una de humors grossas fregas o de humiditatz corrompudas, e son curadas am aquo que havem dit en la divisio e no confereys la tieua curacio, lahoras cauterisa am tres cauteris sobre le pus dejos spondilh del dos petit e petit triangular, e am cauteri desus le ombelic cays per dos ditz.	When old hemorrhoids or one of the thick humors is in a state of congestion or corruption, and they are cured with water as we have said in the division and do not conform to the natural cure, then cauterize with three cauteries above the small triangular spine and the small triangle-shaped bone, and another above the navel going down by two digits.
E si doptas que l’estomac de lu sia enfregidat e la vianda de lu no sia degerida, e la cara de lu vezes apostemada, lahoras cauteriza aquel sobre l’estomac am gran cauteri segon que es precedit; e am un cauteri sobre fietge, e am autre cauteri sobre la melsa de lu am cauteri clavilh, e leyssa le cauteri per alcun temps ubert, e aprop cura lu entro que sia sanat.	And if you find that his stomach is inflamed and his food is not digested, and his face is often swollen, then cauterize that on the stomach with a large cautery according to what has preceded; and one cautery on the thigh, and another on the mole of him with a claw-shaped cautery, and let the cautery remain open for some time, and then cure him until he is healed.
Capitol .xxxv.	The thirty-fifth chapter.
De cauterizacio de atheyl aprop la abscizio de lor.	On Cauterization of Athletes' Wounds near the Abscesses of Them.
Quan tu abscindes atheyl, lahoras tu igneys le cauteri que es asemblat a ray.	When you cut away the athletes' wounds, then you ignite the cautery that is similar to a ray.
Aprop entremet aquel ignit en aquel atheyl abscis, e ultima la tieua ma entro que pervengua le cauteri al orifici de la vena de la qual ve la sanc.	And then put that ignited cautery into the athlete's wound cut away, and finally bring your hand to where the cautery reaches the opening of the vein from which blood flows.
E fay aquo una vetz o doas, quar si achieyl son trops, lahoras cauteriza quascun de lor segon que havem recontat, e aprop cura aquels am aquo que confereys a lor dels enguentz entro que sia sanat.	And make it once or twice, because if the wounds are many, then you cauterize each of them according to what we have recounted, and then cure those with water that conforms to their wounds until they are healed.
E si cauterizas am gran cauteri sobre alquatin, es mays derier en juvament.	And if you cauterize with a large cautery on someone, it is more likely to be effective.
Capitol .xxxvi.	The thirty-sixth chapter.
De cauterizacio de fistolas que son faytas en la natura derie en las partidas de lu.	On Cauterization of Fistulas that are formed in the natural openings of the body.
Quan la natura no obeziys a la obra la qual havem recomtada en son loc, e·l pacient es espaventat per aquo, sia sanat am cauteri.	When nature does not obey the work which we have recommended in its place, and the patient is frightened by that, then cure him with a cautery.
Donc quan ad alcun ve fistola en la natura derier, e es antiquada, corro sania de lu e humiditatz corrompudas, e donc aquo que es pus digne que cove es que proes aquela am tenta subtil, e aprop conoys la quantitat de la profunditat de lu am la devant dita tenta.	Therefore, when you find some fistula in the natural opening of the body that is old and corroded, filled with pus and corrupted humidity, and thus what is most worthy to do is to make an attempt on it with a subtle probe, and then know the quantity of its depth according to the aforementioned probe.
Aprop igneys le cauteri que es semblant a ray.	And then ignite the cautery that is similar to a ray.
E aprop met aquel cauteri ignit en aquesta fistula, e segon la quantitat en la qual intrec la tenta.	And then put that ignited cautery into this fistula, and according to the quantity in which the probe enters.
E itera sobre aquela le cauteri entro que sian comburitz aquels cors corrumputz tost una veguada o dos o tres, segon la quantitat de la tua necessitat.	And repeat that process with the cautery until those corrupted bodies are burned away at once or twice or three times, according to the quantity of your necessity.
E guarda te de combustio de nervi e de vena; o si fistula va al cors de la vesica o al cors del budel, lahoras guarda te de totz aquels locz; e no fassas aquo sino quan la fistula es en loc carnos e cogitas que no es penetrant.	And be careful not to burn the nerves or veins; or if the fistula goes to the bladder or to the intestines, then beware of all those places; and do not do that unless the fistula is in a place where it is not penetrating.
E aprop cura le loc entro que sia sanat.	And then cure that place until it is healed.
E si le loc es sigillat, e so abscindidas de lu las materias, e roman ayssi per lonc temps, lahoras sapias que ja es curat entierament.	And if the place is sealed, and the matters are cut away from it, and it remains like that for a long time, then know that it has been completely cured.
E si las materias no so de lu ostadas, lahoras sapias que es penetrant o en le preon de lu os corromput, o cays aquo de aquelas causas de las quals vindra rememoracio en son loc.	And if the matters are not removed from it, then know that it is penetrating or in the process of corrupting, or falling victim to those causes of which a memory will be recalled in its place.
Capitol .xxxvii.	The thirty-seventh chapter.
De cauterizacio dels ronhos.	On Cauterization of the Tonsils.
Quan en les ronhos endeve dolor per freg o per grossa ventozitat, e per aysso le coyt del malaute es amermat, lahoras cove que cauterizes aquel sobre les ronhos am cauteri sobre quascun ronho am cauteri clavilh del qual precesic la rememoracio.	When in the tonsils there is pain due to congestion or great ventilation, and because of this the patient's throat is inflamed, then it is necessary that you cauterize that on each tonsil with a claw-shaped cautery, whose memory precedes.
E fort leu cauterizam am le segon un petit dejos, per que vindran tres cauteris liniatz, e donc siran mays deriers en juvament.	And firmly cauterize with the second one a little bit away, so that three lined cauteries will be, and thus they will be more effective.
Capitol .xxxviii.	The thirty-eighth chapter.
De cauterizacio de la vesica.	On Cauterization of the Bladder.
Quan accideys en la vesica debelitat e mollificacio per freg e per humiditatz ayssi que·l malaute la urina no retengua, lahoras cauteriza aquel en la partida pus dejos sobre la vesiqua, la hon comensan les pels del pentenilh, e cauteriza am un cauteri en la partida dreyta, e am autre en la senestra de lu.	When debilitation and mollification occur in the bladder due to congestion and corrupted humidity, so that the patient's urine does not retain, then cauterize that on the part farthest from the navel, where the hairs of the navel begin, and cauterize with one cautery on the right side and another on the left.
E sia la longitut de quascun cauteri segon la cantitat dels not del pous; e cauteriza aquel am cauteri en la partida pus bassa del dos, o am dos cauteris si es necessitat.	And let the length of each cautery be according to the quantity of the nodules on the foot; and cauterize that with a cautery in the lowest part of the back, or with two cauteries if necessary.
E sia cauteri clavilh segon que es procesit.	And let it be a claw-shaped cautery according to what has been processed.
Capitol .xxxix.	The thirty-ninth chapter.
De cauterizacio de la mayra.	On Cauterization of the Mare.
Quan veno en la mayra freg e humiditatz, e per aysso es prohibida enpreignacio, e son corrompudas las mestruas de lu, e es tardada la provocacio de lor, e accideys dolor deves le haveniment de lor, lahoras cove que·l loc sia cauterizat am tres cauteris en le circuit del ombelic, ayssi cum havem dit en le cauteri de la vesica; e am cauteri sobre le loc pus dejos del dos, o am dos cauteris, e sia le cauteri clavilh.	When congestion and humidity occur in the mare, and because of this conception is prohibited, and the menstrual flows are corrupted, and the provocation of them is delayed, and there occurs pain due to the hinderance of their passage, then it is necessary that the location be cauterized with three cauteries in the circuit of the navel, just as we have said in the cauterization of the bladder; and with a cautery on the lowest part of the back, or with two cauteries, and let the cautery be claw-shaped.
Capitol .xl.	The fortieth chapter.
De cauterizacio de la dislocacio de l’anqua.	On Cauterization of the Dislocation of the Hip.
Quan humiditatz moucozas so efundudas a la partida de la anqua, e so faytas causas del yssiment del sieu loc, e senhal de lu es que la coyssa es prolonguada sobre l’autre quan so comparadas entre lor.	When corrupted humidity has flowed into the part of the hip, and causes have been formed that hinder the proper location of the joint, and the sign is that the leg is prolonged over the other when compared between them.
E le loc de la dislocacio es atrobat en lu quays boyt.	And the location of the dislocation is found in the part where the buttock is.
Adonc cove que cauterizas le malaute sobre la partida de la anqua de lu am cauteri a sercle semblant, pus que tu auras senhat am tenta en le cercuit de la partida ayssi cum es revolguda, e per so que la partida caia el mieg loc del cercle.	Then it is necessary to cauterize the patient on the part of the hip with a circle-shaped cautery, as you have signaled with a probe in the circuit of that part, and because the part falls into the middle location of the circle.
E sia le cauteri del qual precedit la forma en la cauterizacio del estomac.	And let the cautery be of the same form as that which preceded in the cauterization of the stomach.
E si aquest cauteri no es a tu present, lahoras cauteriza aquel am tres cauteris am cauteri olivar gran.	And if this cautery is not available to you, then cauterize that with three cauteries and one large olive-shaped cautery.
E sia fayt le cauteri segon la quantitat de la ispicitut de tota la codena; e aprop cura aquel entro que sia sanat.	And let the cautery be made according to the quantity of the thickness of the entire cord; and then cure that place until it is healed.
Capitol .xli.	The forty-first chapter.
De cauterizacio de la vena sciatica.	On Cauterization of the Sciatic Vein.
Quan dolor ve en la partida de anqua, e so causa de lu freg et humiditatz, le malaute es curat am aquo que havem dit e no confereys, e aquo es antiquat, lahoras cove que tu lacses le malaute de humors grosses am pillulas fetidas o am pillulas artificials o semblantz; e aprop cauteriza aquel.	When pain occurs in the part of the hip, and its cause is congestion and humidity, the patient is cured with water as we have said and does not conform, and it is old, then it is necessary to apply the patient with thick humors using fetid pills or artificial pills or similar; and then cauterize that.
E la manieyra del cauteri en aquela es segon dos manieyras: o cauteri am medicinas comburentz, o cauteri am foc.	And the method of the cautery in that is according to two methods: either a cautery with concombustive medicines, or a cautery with fire.
Sira segon dos manieyras scientas, de las quals es la una que cauterizes aquel sobre la partida de l’ancha de lu am tres cauteris triangulatz segon aquesta forma; e fay am aquels bona profunditat.	Then according to two scientific methods, one of which is that you cauterize that on the part of the hip with three triangular cauteries in this form; and make good depth.
E sia le spazi le qual es entre cascun cauteri la quantitat de la grossitut del dit e si le cauteri olivar o gran.	And let the space between each cautery be equal to the thickness of the said digit, and if it is an olive-shaped or large cautery.
Mays alcunas veguadas sia le cauteri sobre le mieg loc sobre le cap de l’anquan per que son quatre cauteris.	Sometimes there may be a cautery on the middle location on top of the hip bone, so that there are four cauteries.
E si vols, cauteriza am le cercle del qual es precesida la forma en la cauterizacio de la dislocacio de l’anqua, la i que sia cercle continent e comburey la ispicitut de tota la codena.	And if you wish, cauterize with the circle of which the form precedes in the cauterization of the hip dislocation, so that it be a continuous and burning circle that consumes the thickness of the entire cord.
E aquesta es la manieyra de cauteri in ciatiqua quan dolor es adherent al anqua e no es estenduda entro a la coyssa.	And this is the method of cauterization in sciatica when pain is attached to the hip and does not spread into the joint.
Mays si es estenduda entro a la coyssa, lahoras cauteriza aquel am dos cauteris sobre la coyssa sobre le loc al qual envireys le malaute que es la dolor; e am un cauteri sobre la cavilha per quatre ditz un pauc deves la part cilvestra.	But if it spreads into the joint, then cauterize that with two cauteries on the joint over the location where the patient feels the pain; and with one cautery on the hollow for four digits a little above the hairy part.
E si le cauteri cutellar, e sia la profunditat del cauteri segon la quantitat de la ispicitut de la codena.	And if the cautery is cut-like, and let the depth of the cautery be according to the quantity of the thickness of the cord.
E si le malaute envireys que la dolor es estenduda entro al loc prop les ditz des pes, lahoras cauteriza aquel aqui on envireys am cauteri per tres puntz o quatre o mays si indigeys de aquel.	And if the patient says that the pain is spreading into the location near the bones of the feet, then cauterize that where it says with a cautery for three or four or more points if needed.
E si le malaute envireys dolor esser dejos le donolh ves la coyssa, lahoras cauteriza aquel aqui am un cauteri cutellar.	And if the patient says that pain is below the kneecap near the joint, then cauterize that with a cut-like cautery.
E guarda te en tota cauterizacio que no ultimes am le cauteri en tant que comburas nervi o gran arceria, e que per aquo a tu es sobre le malaute mal noccument o contraccio.	And be careful in all cauterization that you do not stop the cautery until it has burned nerves or large arteries, and because of this it is bad for your patient to have bad necrosis or contraction.
E yeu ja e vist un e autre de aquels les quals cauterizero sobre la cavilha e ultimero en la cauterizacio, e la cama foc inflada entro que la tumor aconseguit lo pe, e foc perforat e corromput tot le pe.	And you have already seen one and another of those which I will cauterize on the hollow and finally in the cauterization, and the inflamed fire burns into the toe until the tumor reaches the end, and the fire perforates and corrupts all the toe.
E aprop accidic fort solucio de ventre, e aprop aquo la mort.	And then comes a strong solution of belly, and with this comes death.
E si la dolor es en dos partidas ensemps cauteriza quascuna segon aquesta manieyra.	And if the pain is in two parts together, then cauterize each one according to this method.
E diysero les savis alcus en la cauterizacio de anqua cauteri del qual aquesta es la manieyra: fay semblant a cercle de ferr del qual le cercuit sia la maytat de un palm; e sia deves le sieu orrifici segon la grossesa de un os de datil o mens un pauc.	And they say that the wise men have said in the cauterization of the hip: make it similar to a circle of iron, the circumference of which is half a palm; and let its orifice be according to the thickness of a date pit or somewhat less.
E dedintz aquel cercle sia un autre tertz; e sia le spazi le qual es entre lor la quantitat del notz del pous; e sian aquels cercles ubertz de dos partidas; e sia la longitut de aquels cays un notz o dos notz, e fay en aquels margue de ferr decentment apparelhat en les cercles; e aquesta es la forma de lu:	And within that circle be another fourth part; and let the space between them be equal to the thickness of the nodules on the foot; and let those circles be one above the other, and let their length be one nodule or two nodules, and make in those margins a ferruginous decently apparelled in the circles; and this is its form.
Aprop sia ignit en le foc entro que s’enrogesisca e gete scintillas, e aprop sia pausat sobre la partida del anqua, le malaute colcat sobre le latz sa.	And then be ignited in the fire until it blazes up and sends sparks, and then be placed on the part of the hip, with the patient lying on their side.
E donc cauteriza aquel am tres cauteris redontz en una veguada.	And therefore cauterize that with three cauteries rounded in one stroke.
E aprop layssa aquel per tres jorns; aprop emplastre aquel am boder e layssa la plagua uberta per trops dias; e aprop cura aquel am enguentz entro que sia sanat.	And then leave that alone for three days; apply a poultice to it with a border and leave the wound open for many days; and then cure that with ointments until it is healed.
Diys Albucasis : o, filhs, de aquesta specia de cauteri pauc havem usat per la terror del reguardament de lu, e per aquo que paucs havem trobatz les quals reguardan sobre lu.	Thus says Albucasis: Oh, sons, of this type of cautery we have used little, due to the fear of looking at it, and therefore few have found those who look upon it.
Mays dels bos cauteris a lu qui les sufferta, et atroba am aquel le loc de lu.	But from the good cauteries that suffered him, and found the place of him.
Mays cauteri am medicinas adhurentz es que tu fassas dos cercles haventz armula perforada en la qual deyssen le guaffo de la porta de ferr; sia la longuitut de la paretz en la nauteza de lor sian dos nozes o quays aquels.	But a cautery with concombustive medicines is one that you make two circles having an armula perforated in which the guaffo of the iron door should be placed; let the length of the walls be in the height of theirs, namely two nodules or as many as those.
E si le spazi le qual es entre quascu la quantitat de la grossitut del dit; e sian ubertz dejos e desus, e sian que contenguan se entre lor segon aquesta forma:	And if the space between each one is equal to the thickness of the said digit; and let them be above and below, and let them contain themselves within each other according to this form:
E aprop pausa sobre la partida de la anqua le malaut jasent sobre le latz sa, e comprem la tua ma sobre la partida de la anqua; e aprop pren de aygua cauda e fon la entre dos cercles, e la qualiditat de aquela sia am le foc petit a petit, e te aquela per la quantitat de una hora, e sufferta le malaute la mordicacio e la adhustio de lu — quar aquel atrobo mordicacio ayssi cum de foc — entro que cesse la mordicacio.	And then place it on the part of the hip, with the patient lying on their side, and grasp your hand over the part of the hip; and then take cold water and pour it between two circles, and let its quality be in the small fire, little by little, and keep it for the quantity of an hour, and suffer the patient to endure the mordication and the adjustment of it -- until that mordication ceases as if from fire.
E aprop eleva la tua ma am le instrument et abstergeys l’aygua cauda de tota la anqua am aygua dousa.	And then lift your hand with the instrument and wash away the cold water from all the hip with warm water.
E aprop leyssa aquel per tres jorns e pausa sobre aquel boder entro que sia la negror de la adhustio remauguda, e leyssa aquo per alcus jorns, e correra de lu poyredura; aquest es derier en juvament.	And then leave that alone for three days and place over it a border until the blackness of the adjustment is restored, and leave it so for some days, and let it be filled with blood; this is the end in healing.
E aprop cura aquel am enguentz entro que sia sanat.	And then cure that with ointments until it is healed.
E si la dolor es extenduda entro la coyssa o la camba, fay a lu estatua en lu que contengua aygua segon que es feyt en la anqua engualment.	And if the pain is spread into the joint or thigh, make it like a statue in the water, according to what is done in the hip similarly.
E aquesta es la manieyra de aygua cauda, e yeu ja he scrit aquela en le tractat de la rectificacio de medicinas.	And this is the method of cold water, and you have already written that in the treatise on the correction of medicines.
Recipe de alcali e de caus no extinta de amdos ana partida una, e trissa les e pausa en una ola nova de la qual la partida dejos sia perforada per un petit trauc, segon la quantitat que intre en lu ray.	Recipe of alkali and non-extinguished cause of both ana parts one, and crush them and place them in a new wave of which the left part is pierced by a small hole, according to the quantity that enters into it ray.

And place the bottom of one wave into another wave inverted, and pour on top of that alkali and living cause with warm water which covers them by one digit, and then you compress them with your own hand for good compression, and leave it so that the hole will descend from the sharp water in the left part to the inverted wave.
E aprop ajusta tota aquela aygua, e geta la sobre autra caus viva e autre alcali renovelatz, quar aquela lahoras sira de mot forta acuitat, la qual es aministrada en motas operacios de medicina e en cauterizacio dels autres membres, quar operacio fa de foc.	And then adjust all that water, and pour it over another living cause and other alkali renewed, because that which is already strong acuity will be administered in many operations of medicine and in the cauterization of other members, for this operation is fiery.
E so de las medicinas alcunas am las quals es cauterizat ancha, ayssi cum tezizic e mel anacrat e caus am sabo enayssi que sian mesclatz.	And some of the medicines are mixed with those which are cauterized wide, such as mezize, malanacrate, and causes with salt, so that they are blended.

And Gualia recounted the operation and cure of a man from ancient times who was cured of hip and sciatic vein pain with this method, and magnificently declared it to be very effective, saying that no other cure was needed, and thus he is healed in one stroke just like I recommended, for indeed that one entered into bath and exercise already knowing about this.
Et es que sia pres de certarragi vert, e si no es atrobat vert, sia presa figua recent; e mot sia trissada am un pauc de grays e sia pausat sus la anqua en la qual es la dolor, o en la coyssa, o en la camba, e sia liat.	And it is said that a certain quantity of greenery should be used, and if not found, a fresh fig should be taken; and it should be crushed with a little gray powder and placed on the hip where there is pain, or in the joint or thigh, and bound.
E sia layssat per la cantitat de tres horas o per la quantitat que·l malaute centa cedacio de la adhustio.	And it should be left for the quantity of three hours or for as long as the patient considers that the adjustment is giving way.
E aprop met aquel en banh e donc quan le cors de lu sia enrozat, entromet aquel en le sol, quar la dolor cessa e es sanat.	And then put it in bath, and when the body of him is heated, immerse it in the sun, because the pain ceases and he is healed.
E sapias que no cove que alcu use de cauteri am aquestas medicinas sino aprop la evacuacio del cors.	And know that you should not use cautery with these medicines except in proper evacuation of the body.
Mays ja Escorides diysec que quan am fenda de cabra la vena stretica es cauterizada, aprofieyra a lu mo be; e sia le cauteri am lu segon aquesta manieyra: sia presa lana e sia enbeguda en oli antic, e sia pausat entre le pous del pe e entre le fossil.	But already Escorides said that when the sciatic vein is cauterized with a goat's horn, it will be of great benefit to him; and let the cautery be made according to this method: take wool and soak it in old oil, and place it between the toes of the foot and between the bones.
E aprop pren fenda de cabra secca e emflasma aquela am foc entro que sia fayta carbo; e aprop pausa lu sobre la lana e leysa la entro que sia estengida. E aprop itera aquo, e no cessas far aquo entro que·l scintiment de la mordicacio pervengua entro al anqua e repausa la dolor.	And then repeat this process, and do not cease doing so until the sensation of the burning reaches into the hip and relieves the pain.
Et aquesta manieyra de cauteri es apelat cauteri de vaquas.	And this method of cautery is called the "cauterization of oxen".

De cauterizacio de dolor de dos.	Chapter 42: On the Cauterization of Two-Pain Dolor.
Alcunas veguadas dolor es en le dos per tropas causas, cum per cazement o per percucio o per superflua evacuacio, e per causas ad aquelas semblantz, per infusio de materia frega e humida. E cauteri no catz sino en aquesta sola specia la qual es fayta per efusio de materia frega.	And the cautery should not be done except in this one species, which is made by effusion of moist matter.

De cauterizacio al comensament de gilbositat.	Chapter 43: On Cauterization at the Beginning of Gout.

Many times this disease attacks small children; and the sign of its beginning in children is that it occurs suddenly on their joints, causing swelling and elevation.

que prengua le cauteri sobre tota partida del spondilh engualment.	that takes the cautery on all parts of the spine equally.

Capitol .xlv.	Chapter 45.
De cauterizacio de rompeduras.	Chapter 45: On Cauterization of Wounds.
Quan endeve rompedura en les angonars e diysendo les budels denant l’atela al genetiu, e aquo es comensan de aprop, lahoras cove que tu mandas al malaute layssar la sua comestio en le sieu dia e que use de causas leniens per so que la fenda deyssenda del sieu ventre.	When a wound occurs in the groin and says that the abscesses are bursting before the saddle at the genitals, and this is beginning to happen, then it is good for you to tell the patient to stop their diet for the day and to use gentle remedies so that the wound may close up from its own vent.
E aprop segua le malaute entre las tuas mas sobre le sieu dos, e comanda a lu que tengua le sieu ale entro que sia foro getat o aparesca l’atela o·l budels.	And then follow the patient with your hands on their back above their knees, and command him to keep his leg straight until the wound is completely healed or the abscess appears.
E aprop retorna aquel am les tieus ditz e senha am tenta la ruptura sobre le os del pentenilh am senhal la extremitat del qual sia semblant a la maytat de cercle a las subiranas partidas del cors.	And then return to that place with your fingers and signal by touch the rupture over the bone of the pubic bone, signaling the extremity of which is similar to half a circle at the divided parts of the chest.
E aprop igneys le cauteri del qual aquesta es la forma de lu:	And then ignite the cautery whose form is as follows:
entro que sia mot rog e gete cintilhas.	until it is hot and sparks fly.
E aprop reduzeys le budel o l’atela a la sua conquavitat, e aprop pause la sua ma sobre le loc per so que le budel no yesqua.	And then reduce the abscess or abscess to its natural conformation, and then place your hand on the location to prevent the abscess from bursting.
E tu ja has ubert entre las coyssas del malaute e dejos lu as pausat un coyssi, et autre servent sia sus las cambas de lu, e autre sus le pietz de lu, le qual tengua las suas mas.	And you have already located between the joints of the patient and left one joint, and another serves on his thighs, and another on his feet, which has its own masses.
E aprop pausa le cauteri sobre aquel senhal am la tua ma am cauteri stan dreyt, e te aquel entro que am lu consieguas le os del pentenilh entro al mieg del duiduni; e itera am aquel autra veguada si a tu aquel no has conseguit en la primieyra veguada entro al os.	And then place the cautery on that spot indicated by your hand with the cautery standing upright, and apply it to that area until you reach the bone of the pubic bone in the middle of the duodenum; and repeat on another occasion if you do not achieve success on the first attempt, until you reach the bone.
E observa saviament del ysiment del budel en la hora de la tua cauterizacio, que no comburas aquel budel per so que sobre le malaute no vengua in mort o autre gran malicia.	And observe wisely the signs of the abscess at the time of your cautery, lest you burst that abscess and cause harm to the patient, leading to death or great harm.
E sapias que quan tu am le cauteri no atenhas le os, no confereys la tua operacio.	And know that when you apply the cautery, do not touch the bone, nor compromise your operation.
E cove que·l cauteri dels enfants sia subtil segon le gran e la mesura de lor.	And it is good that the cautery for children be subtle according to their size and measure.
E aprop cura le loc del cauteri per tres dias am boder entro que sia remauguda la scara del foc.	And then cure the location of the cautery for three days with ointment until the scar of the fire is restored.
E aprop cura aquel am les autres enguentz entro que sia sanat.	And then cure that with other remedies until it is healed.
E le malaute sia jasent sobre le sieu dos per xl dias entro que sia sigillat le loc e la plagua.	And the patient should lie on their back for 40 days until the location and wound are sealed.
E cove que pauses le nutriment de lu segon la longitut del temps de la curacio de lu le qual le linesca le ventre de lu, e que le budel no yesca fora deves le esforsament de guerir.	And it is good that you pause the patient's nutrition according to the length of time of their cure, and that the abscess does not burst forth from the effort of healing.
E aprop quan se vol levar aprop xl dias, lahoras aministra liament decentment fayt, e tengua aquel per autres xl jorns.	And then, when it is almost 40 days, apply gentle remedies and keep that for another 40 days.
E sia mermat de trebalh e de replecio de vianda e de beure, e de votz vehementz, quar quan usa de aquest regiment de sanacio entiera sira sanat.	And let it be diminished in work and repletion of food and drink, and in violent voices, for when one uses this regimen of entire healing, they will be healed.
E yeu diyre la curacio de las rupturas en las autras partidas del ventre, e so al comensament, e vols que no treguan, lahoras cauterisa la ruptura d’aquel am cauteri redon segon la quantitat de lu, e sia aquo que es exhurit de la codena ayssi cum la tersa partida de lu; e aprop cura aquel am aquo que havem dit, e no es ajustat.	And you will say the cure of ruptures in other parts of the belly, and so at the beginning, and you want them not to stop, then cauterize the rupture with that red-hot cautery according to the quantity of it, and let it be as if it were taken out of the cord just like the third part of it; and then cure that with what we have said, and do not adjust.
E ja diyssero alcus primiers que ruptura sia cauterizada am cauteri triangular segon aquesta forma, pus que es senhada am tenta:	And already some first ones have said that the rupture should be cauterized with a triangular cautery according to this form, since it is signaled by touch:
e es pausada linha que eys per la latitut en le latz pus sobira de la ruptura, e autra linha al desus; e depausa la tua ma am un cauteri clavilh, mays le primier cauteri es pus leugier e milhor.	and it is a paused line that goes through the latitude in the lat and above the rupture, and another line above it; and then place your hand on one cautery, but the first cautery is lighter and better.

De cauterizacio de torcio.	Chapter 46: On Cauterization of Twist.
Quan endeve en alscus membres per cazement o per percussio dolor e persevera aquela dolor per lonc temps e no comfereys al u curacio am medicinas, lahoras cove que cauterizes am cauteri de punt. Donc si·s sanat per le primier cauteri, bo es; e sino, lahoras itera sobre lu le cauteri; quar de costuma de aquelas dolors es que sian punctatz de membre ad aquel membre le qual apropinque al u, per que cove que consieguas aquels am cauteri entro que·l malaute sia sanat.	Therefore, if it is healed by the first cautery, good; and if not, then reapply the cautery to him; for it is a custom of those pains that they are punctured in one member to another which approaches them, so that you must achieve those with cautery until the patient is healed.

De cauterizacio de lepra.	Chapter 47: On Cauterization of Leprosy.
Les lebros alcunas veguadas am cauteri per mot gran juvament, e magerment si la specia de lepra que es fayta per putrefaccio de flacma e de melencolia.	Some lepers have been cured with cautery for great benefit, and more so if the species of leprosy is caused by the corruption of phlegm and melancholy.
E donc cum tu vols cauterizar aquel, considera si la lepra es comussan e as aquela curada am aquo que havem dit en la divisio e no deysen, ni esta, e temes sobre le malaute que la corrupcio comprehenda tot le cors de lu e tota la compleccio de lu, lahoras cauteriza aquel sobre le cap am v cauteris: am un en le mieg loc del cap, e am le segon pus dejos de lu, eves le front a la fi dels cabels; e amdos sobre dos corns; e am un detras, sobre la nuca o servitz. And know that the more you adjust the cauteries, the more beneficial and congruent it is; and know that the patient does not have pain in the cautery, just like they do in their skin, because of which the body of him has already been stupified.

E aprop cura le cauteri am farina de errs coyta am mel e am l’autra curacio entro que sia sanat.	And then cure the cautery with flour from errors cooked with honey and with another remedy until it is healed.

De cauterizacio de corrodent.	Chapter 52: On Cauterization of Consumption.
Corrodent es corrupcio ambulant en le membre, la qual corrodeys aquel ayssi cum a foc comedent lenha secca.	Consumption is a corrupting wandering in the member, which corrupts it like fire consuming dry wood.
Donc si vezes aquel corrodent en loc le qual sufferte cauteri am foc, lahoras tu igneys cauteris clavils motz paucs, e grans segon que es convenent en aquel loc en le qual es corrodent. De cauterizacio de claus e dels autres semblants.	Chapter 53: On Cauterization of Warts and other similar things.
Motas veguadas endeve a las partidas dejos del pe malautia que s’apela clau, e es causa grossa, fentrada, la qual ladeys le pe; e cauteri en aquels es segon dos manieyras, so es cauteri am foc e cauteri am aygua cauda.	Many times it happens that there is a lingering part of the foot disease which is called a wart, and it is a big, festering cause that spoils the foot; and cauterization in those places is done in two ways, namely by fire cautery and water-boiling cautery.
Mays cauteri am foc es que igniscas le cauteri concau semblant a pena de voltor, le qual sia feyt de ferr segon la quantitat la qual contengua le clau de tota partida, e sia de subtils marguas.	But fire cautery is when you ignite the concave cautery similar to a vulture's claw, which is made of iron according to the quantity that contains the wart on all sides, and has subtle edges.

And then apply that with wild marjoram leaves mixed with salt, and loosen the plaster over it for one night, so that it is eradicated from its roots.

And if it does not convert, and many times it happens on the surface of the body, mostly in the arms and legs, then you must administer cauterization with water, and it is that you take a quill or iron or vulture's claw, and place it over the wart; and then pour into the quill a small amount of boiling water, and hold your hand, and you revolve it with compression from all sides, and press the edge of the quill into the root of the wart, and let the hot water flow slowly to the depth of the cavity; and wait for the patient a little while after the injection of the hot water for one hour, and then remove that, so that the wart with its roots is eradicated.
E ayssi fe am aquels la i aprop l’autre entro que venguas sobre totz les quals de lor so en le cors.	And thus do it to those, and then apply the other remedy until you reach all of them that are in their place on the body.
E aprop cura aquels pus que las razitz dels claus so erradicadas am aquo dels enguentz les quals la carn ve engenran.	And then cure those with pus, which is eradicated from the roots of the warts, with remedies that promote flesh growth.

When in the body are accidentally struck blows, and pustules are formed which are made of gross corrupted matter; then it is necessary at first to appear as if prepared, that a subtle cautery be applied over the entire head of the fistula with a myrtle stick whose extremity has been extended with fire; or with roots of long-estiolated herbs; or with a lentecular cautery.

De cauterizacio de fluex de sanc accident per incisio de arceria.	Chapter 56: On Cauterization of Blood Flowing from an Accidental Cut by a Sword.
Tropas veguadas endeve fluex de arceria que es inciza deves la plagua la qual endeve deforo, o deves la incizio de apostemas o cauteri del membre, e alor semblantz, e es dificil remaura aquel.	Many times it happens that blood flows from a wound caused by an accidental cut by a sword, or from the incision of apostemes or cauteries on a member, and then similar things happen, and it is difficult to stop that bleeding.
Donc cum accideys ad alcu aquo, lahoras tu·t coyta am la tua ma a l’orrifici de la arceria, e pausa sobre aquel le tieu dit endic estrenh aquel motas veguadas entro que sia ostat le fluex del sanc dejos le tieu dit, e que non yesqua.	Therefore, when it happens that blood flows excessively, then you must quickly apply your hand to the wound of the sword, and place on top of it what I have said earlier, and strengthen that many times until the bleeding is stopped, and there will be no further flow.
E aprop pausa en le foc les cauteris olivars paucs e grantz, per nombre motz, e exsuffla sobre aquels entro que sian mot ignitz.	And then place the olive-like cauteries in the fire, small and great, in many numbers, and blow on them until they are thoroughly ignited.

And then take from those one small or large according to the location and wound in which the artery is broken, on that vein more quickly than you have removed what I have said earlier, and apply the cautery until it is completely absorbed and restrained that blood.

And if the blood is expelled from the orifice of the artery when you remove what I have said and extinguish the cautery, then take another cautery carefully from the ones that are prepared in the fire, and thus do not cease to do this repeatedly until the bleeding is restrained.
E guarda te que no comburas le nervi que aqui es, e que vengua sobre le malaute autra malicia.	And be careful not to burn the nerves that are here, and that you bring another misfortune upon the patient.
E sapias que quan de l’arteria flueys sanc, lahoras no es possible en aquels restrenge la sanc, e majorment quan l’arteria es gran, si no am una de quatre manieyras: o am cauteri ayssi quo dit havem, o am extraccio quan no es extrayta, quar quan es extrayta las extremitatz de lu miels son comburidas e es restreyt le sanc, o que sia liat am fiel o am liament per fort strectura, o que sian pausadas sobre lu medicinas de las quals la vertut es restringir la sanc; e sian strengudas am pulvinar am costriccio decent.	And know that when blood flows from an artery, it is not possible to restrain the bleeding in those circumstances, and especially when the artery is large, unless by one of four methods: or by the cautery as we have said earlier, or by extraction which is not extracted, because when it is extracted, the ends of it are burned and the bleeding is restrained, or that it be tied with a thread or with a ligament through strong constriction, or that medicines be applied to it, whose virtue is to restrain the bleeding; and they should be strengthened by a pillow or by a decent constraint.
Mays aquel que aministra restriccio decent de lu am liament e am strictura am draps o per posicio de causas comburentz e de semblantz, no comfereys sino tart.	But the one who administers a decent restraint on him with a ligament and strong constriction by drapes or through position of concurring causes and similar things does not respond quickly.
Mays si aquo endeve ad alcu e no sia le metge present ni medicina, lahoras obre am pausament del dit indic sobre le orrifici de aquela vena ayssi cum havem dit, e entenda a la gran costreccio de lu entro que le sanc sia ostat de la sobirana partida de la plagua, e sobre la arceria le dit no sia remaugut; e de sobre la arceria sia aspergit am aygua frega de mot gran fregiditat entro que·l sanc sia congilat e engrossat; e mays cossire en que ha de cauteri o de medicina necessitat.	But if it happens to someone and there is no doctor present or medicine, then do the following: work slowly with the above-mentioned cautery on the orifice of that vein as we have said earlier; and understand that the great constriction of him is necessary until the bleeding is stopped from the superior part of the wound, and on the sword-cut it has not been removed; and above the sword-cut be sprinkled with boiling water of great coldness until the blood is congealed and thickened; and also consider in what kind of cauterization or medicine is needed.
Comensa la segonda partida.	Starts the second part.
De incisio e perforacio e ventozas e de fleubotomia e de plaguas e de lor semblants.	On Incision, Perforation, and Wounds, and their likenesses, including Phlebotomy and Wounds.
Aquestas son paraulas de Albucazis.	These are the words of Albucasis.
Ja havem dit en le primier capitol tota malautia en la qual cauteri am foc es convenient e am medicina comburent, e las occasios e las causas de lu, e les instrumentz en aquels necessaris am las formas dels cauteris; e he ordenatz les capitols de la subiranetat del cap entro als pes.	We have already said in the first chapter all diseases in which a cautery with fire is suitable and with medicine that concurs, and their occasions and causes, and the instruments necessary for those things, and we have arranged the chapters of this book from head to foot.
E yeu procesire en aquest capitol per aquela meteysa guisa, per que sia alliujat lo querent aquo, lahoras sobre aquo que aura demandat.	And you will proceed in this chapter by that method, so that what is sought after may be illuminated to him who asks about it, and thus over what has been asked.
E denant que yeu comense aquo, cove, fils, que aprenguatz que en aquest capitol es per terror aquo que es en le capitol primier de cauterizacio.	And before you begin this, it is necessary, dear son, that you learn that in this chapter, it is about the terrors of which we spoke in the first chapter on cauterization.
E per aquo que cove que sia en lu gran cautela, quar en la operacio la qual es en aquest capitol motas veguadas catz evacuacio la qual es am sanc am le qual esta la vida deves la aspersio de la vena o incisio sobre l’apostema o apercio de exsitura o puracio de la plagua o extraccio de sageta o incizio de peyra e a lor semblantz.	And therefore it is necessary that there be great caution in him, for in the operation which is in this chapter, many times evacuation occurs which is with blood and on which life depends; and so one must be cautious with the sprinkling of the vein or incision over the apostema or warning of exit or purgation of the wound or extraction of a sagitta or incision of a pyre, and their likenesses.
E de totz aquels so acompanhatz temor e tremor e en le mas de lor catz la mort.	And all those are accompanied by fear and trembling, and in most cases death.
E yeu amonesti vos que sobre vos no caia aquo en le qual es esitacio, quar alcunas veguadas cazo deves vos manieyras de homes am manieyras motas de malautias.	And I warn you that on you should not fall this thing in which there is occasion, for sometimes the case demands of men many manners of diseases.
E de lor es alcu que s’irays am la sua malautia e es leugiera deves lu la mort, e aysso per la vehemensia de aquo que troba de sa malautia, e per longuesa de la malautia de lu, e am la malautia es paor la qual significa mort.	And from them some go away with their disease and it is soon for him to die, and so through the intensity of what he finds in his disease, and through the length of his disease, and in the disease there is fear which means death.
E de aquels es le qual dona a tu son aver e ditta, tu esperant am aquel sanetat, e la sieua malautia es perniciosa.	And from those some receive from their son's heritage and gift, you waiting for him to be healed, and his disease is pernicious.
E donc no cove que tu consentas en aquel que ve a vos del qual es aquesta manieyra; e la vostra cautela sia major que covesitat e la vostra rapacitat; e no presumatz alcuna causa sobre aquo sino aprop sciencia certa la qual virifica aquo deves vos, e al qual perve successio lausabla.	And therefore it is not necessary that you consent to what comes to you from which this manner; and your caution should be greater than cove-ity and rapacity; and do not presume any cause over what comes to you, but rather aprop science certain which verifies what comes to you, and by which success succeeds.
E usatz en la curacio de totz vostres malautes de pronosticacio e indicacio de lu al qual es salut convertida, quar en aquel es a vos ajutori sobre adquisicio de fama e de memoria, de lausor e de gloria.	And use in the cure of all your diseases prophesying and indicating to you that which is salvation converted, for in that is aid to you over the acquisition of fame and memory, of praise and glory.
O, filhs, Dieus en vos spire le sieu entendement e no oste a vos direccio e proteccio, quar aquo es en la sua ma.	Oh, sons, God inspires His understanding in you, and does not withhold direction and protection from you, for this is in His hand.
E yeu e ordenat aquest capitol distingent per capitols segon que precedit en le capitol de cauteris, de la cura del cap entro als pes, per que sia a vos alleujat aquo que demandatz de aquo e del qual havetz necessitat.	And I have ordered this chapter to be distinguished by chapters according to what preceded in the chapter on cauteries, from head to foot, so that it may be illuminated to you what you ask about and of which you have need.
Capitol primier.	Chapter 1.
De la curacio de aygua la qual es contenguda en le cap dels enfantz.	On the Cure of Water that is contained in the Head of Children.
Sapias que aquesta malautia motas veguadas endeve als enfantz deves le enfantament e quan la noyrissa estrenh le cap del enfant ses livitat.	Know that this disease often occurs in children during childbirth and when the midwife tightens the child's head.
E alcunas veguadas endeve per causa amaguada la qual no es saubuda.	And sometimes it occurs due to a hidden cause which is unknown.
Mays yeu no vi aquesta malautia sino en les enfantz; e a totz aquels les quals yeu vi se coytec la mort, e per ayssi es a mi vist layssada obra en aquels.	But I have never seen this disease except in children; and to all those whom I have seen it has been accompanied by death, and so it is my work left undone in them.
E yeu e vist que un enfant le cap del qual era d’aygua omplit, e·l cap de lu era totjorn ayssi magnificat entro que ceser no podia sobre si meteys per la grandesa del sieu cap, e mays que la humiditat fe aucmentada entro que foc mort.	And I have seen that a child whose head was filled with water overflowed, and his head was always magnificently expanded so that it could not cease to pour forth, and more than the humidity was increased until a mortal fire.
E aquesta humiditat o es agreguada entre la codena e l’os, o es agreguada dejos le os sobre le ciphac.	And this moisture either accumulates between the skull and bone, or accumulates beneath the bone on the cranium.
Quar la operacio en aquel si la humiditat es entre la codena e l’os e le apostema es pauc, lahoras cove que tu fendas en le mieg loc del cap am una fissura en la latitut, e sia la longitut de la fissura cays dos notz entro que corra la humiditat, e aquesta es la forma del spatum:	So the operation in that case if the moisture is between the skull and bone and the apostema is small, then it is necessary to cut in the middle of the head with an incision in the latitude, and the length of the incision should be two nights so that the moisture flows out, and this is the form of the spatula:
E donc si la humiditat es mays augmentada e l’apostema es major, lahoras son aqui dos fissuras segon aquesta manieyra:	And therefore if the moisture is more increased and the apostema is greater, then there are two incisions according to this method:
E si la humiditat es dejos le os, senhal de lu es que tu vezes la comissuras del cap ubertas de tota partida e l’aygua es spremuda quan tu compremes aquela am la tieua ma a las partidas dedintz e no es aquo a tu amaguat.	And if the moisture is beneath the bone, the sign of it is that you must cut the commissures of the head on all sides and the water is squeezed out when you compress that with your hand into the partitions inside and not to be hidden from you.
Cove que tu fendas en le mieg loc del cap am tres fissuras segon aquesta manieyra:	It is necessary for you to cut in the middle of the head with three incisions according to this method:
e aprop la inscizio extratz ne tota la humiditat; e aprop strenh las fissuras am draps e plumassols; e aprop enbroca aquo de sobre am vi e oli entro al quint dia, e aprop deslia le liament e cura la plagua am tentas e enguentz, e strenh le cap am equalitat; e mange le malaute am vianda secca de pauca humiditat entro que·l membre sia confortat e sanat.	And carefully extract all the moisture from the incision; and carefully strengthen the incisions with cloths and poultices; and carefully bandage it on the fifth day, and carefully remove the ligature and care for the wound with tents and poultices, and strengthen the head with equality; and feed the patient with dry food of little moisture until the member is comforted and healed.
E es autra manieyra de incisio, que consideras hon apar la magnitut del apostema e la colleccio de l’aygua, quar alcunas veguadas es mays en le occipicii, o en la partida denant, o en la destra, o en la sinistra; e donc aten am la incizio on appar le apostema e la replecio de l’aygua, e fen aquo segon que a tu es miels possible.	And there is another method of incision, which considers how the magnitude of the apostema and the collection of water appear, for sometimes it is more in the occiput, or in the anterior part, or in the right, or in the left; and therefore attend to the incision where the apostema appears and the accumulation of water, and do so as best you can.
Et observa que no inscindas la arteria e endevengua flueys de sanc e mora le malaute per aquel flux de sanc am evacuacio de humiditat.	And observe that you do not cut the artery and thus the blood flows and the patient dies from that flow of blood with evacuation of moisture.
Capitol .ii.	Chapter II.
De inscisio de las arterias las quals so aprop las aurelhas, apeladas hilasseysse.	On the Incision of the Arteries which are near the Ears, called Hilasseyes.
Capitol segon.	Chapter 2nd.
Quan endeveno ad alcu catars o raumas als huelhs o al pietz, e es antiquat aquo, e no confereys en aquo la curacio de las medicinas, lahoras la deriera curacio en aquest es incizio de aquelas dos arterias.	When the case arises with some catarrh or rheums in the eyes or feet, and it is ancient, and does not respond to the cure of medicines, then the final cure in this case is the incision of those two arteries.
E donc cove quan tu vols inscidir aquelas que le malaute raza lo sieu cap, e aprop fregua le loc am drap aspre per so que aparan las arcerias, e aprop sia strengut le col del malaute am alcu drap; e aprop considera on polsa la vena; e les locs de quascuna sobre les locs les quals so aprop las aurelhas depremutz, e tant se occultan sino en alcus homes.	And therefore it is necessary when you wish to incise those which the patient's head becomes inflamed, and carefully palpate the location with a rough cloth so that the arteries appear, and carefully strengthen the neck of the patient with some cloth; and carefully consider where the vein pulsates; and the places of each above the places which are near the ears depressed, and they will be hidden from almost no one.
E aprop senha sobre la arceria am tenta, e aprop inscideys quascuna am le spatum de quascuna partida agut am inscizio pervenient entro al os, e sia aquo per la latitut del cap.
