And carefully cut on the artery with a tent, and carefully incise each one with a spatula from each side, sharp as if to penetrate into the bone, and so that it is in the latitude of the head.
E si vols, entromet le spatum dejos la arteria e trenqua aquala a las inciden a las partidas desus.	And if you want, insert the spatula below the artery and cut it at the same spot where the incisions are made on the sides.
E sia la longitut de la inscizio cays dos ditz ajustatz, quar quan alcuna vena es inscizida le sanc es eyssit am egressio pulsatil, le qual saut deforo per saut frequent.	And the length of the incision should be about two fingers' breadth, because when any vein is cut it begins to bleed with a pulsating egression, which jumps out frequently.
Mays si la arceria no apareys al cintiment, lahoras cove que tu mesures de la aurelha la quantitat del spazi de tres ditz, e aprop senha am tenta, e fen entro al os.	But if the artery does not appear at the incision, then it is necessary that you measure from the ear the quantity of space equal to three fingers' breadth, and carefully insert with a tent, and cut into the bone.
E aquo que cove getar del sanc es quantitat de vi unc., e fort leu ne geta de lu mays o mens, e tot aquo es segon la quantitat la qual appareys de la vertut del malaute e de la replecio de la arceria de lu.	And this amount of blood that is necessary to be taken is about one ounce of wine. and not too little or too much, and all this is according to the quantity which appears of the virtue of the disease and the accumulation of the artery in him.
E aprop considera la plagua, e donc si reman sobre le os alcuna causa del ciphac, lahoras inscindys aquo per so que no endevengua apostema caut.	And carefully consider the wound, and therefore if there remains on the bone any cause of the skull, then incise this so that no apostema appears.
E aprop strenh la plagua am plumassols e am liamentz de drap de li, e aprop cura aquela am enguentz entro que sia sanat.	And carefully strengthen the wound with poultices and bandages of linen cloth, and carefully cure that with compresses until it is healed.
Capitol .iii.	Chapter III.
De extraccio de las arcerias las quals so en las templas.	On the Extraction of the Arteries which are in the Temples.
Quan ad alcu accideys emigranea antiqua o catertz agutz, per humiditatz agrimonials e per qualiditat en les lacertz des templas, o sodo antiqua vehement e semblantz ad aquels, e es medicat am las manieyras de curacio de medicina e aquo no comfereys, lahoras nos hem sproatz en aquestas malautias extraccio de las arcerias en les templas, o cauterizacio de aquelas ayssi cum havem mostrat.	When an old emigration or catarrh occurs in the temples, due to humidities and qualities of the lacertae, or an old violent and similar condition to those, and it is medicated by the methods of cure with medicine, but does not respond, then we have resolved on these diseases to extract the arteries in the temples, or cauterize them as we have shown.
E la manieyra de la operacio e extracio de aquelas es que·l malaute raza les pels les quals son en les templas; e entenda a la arceria apparent en le templar quar ela es a tu mostrada per le sieu pols, e·s occultada sino en paucs homes per vehemencia de freg.	And the method of the operation and extraction is that the patient scratches the skin where they are in the temples; and understand that the artery appears in the temple because it is shown to you by its pulsation, and is hidden from almost no one except for a few individuals due to the intensity of the pulse.
E si a tu es occultada, lahoras le col del malaute sia strengut am alcun drap; e aprop fregua le loc am un drap aspre o evapora le loc am aygua cauda entro que aparesca a tu la arceria manifestament.	And if it is hidden from you, then the neck of the patient should be strengthened with some cloth; and carefully palpate the location with a rough cloth or evaporate the location with warm water until the artery appears to you in its full manifestation.
E lahoras tu pren le spatum del qual aquesta es la forma:	And then take the spatula of which this is the form:
E aprop tu scorja la codena am aquel am facilitat entro que pervenguas a la arceria; e aprop geta en lu onti e extratz aquela a las partidas sobiranas entro que extraguas aquela de la codena e descobras aquela de las tunicas las quals so dejos aquela, de tota partida.	And then carefully score the skull with that spatula, making it easy for you to reach the artery; and carefully cut into it on one side and extract that from the upper parts until you extract that from the skull and discover those tunics which are below it, from all sides.
Mays si la arteria es subtil, lahoras envolveys aquela am la extremitat del oncii, e aprop inscindeys de aquela una partida segon la quantitat per la qual sian alonguadas las extremitatz de lu e sian contraytas, e no endevindra flux de sanc, quar si no so inscididas no pujara le sanc de tot.	But if the artery is slender, then carefully envelop it with the extremity of the oncus, and cut into that one side according to the quantity by which the extremities of it are lengthened and contracted, and do not let there be a flow of blood, for if they are not incised, the blood will not rise at all.
E aprop evacua del sanc de vi unc. entro a tres.	And carefully evacuate about one ounce of blood. within three.
E si la arceria es gran, lahoras cove que tu lies aquela en dos locs am fiel dopble fort de ceda o am cordas a lonc, e no coyte a lu putrefaccio denant la consolidacio de la plagua e endevengua flux de sanc.	And if the artery is large, then carefully divide it into two parts with a double fold of caede or with strings to a length, and do not allow the putrefaction to occur before the consolidation of the wound and the flow of blood.
E aprop incideys la superfluitat la qual es entre dos liamentz; e fay aquo en aquela hora o aprop autra ora.	And carefully cut away the excess which is between two bandages; and do this at that hour or approximately another hour.
E si vols, cauteriza aquela am cauteri entro al os am cauteri cutellar entro que sian incididas las extramitatz de lu, e stara en loc de aquela meteyssa obra.	And if you wish, cauterize that with a cauterizer into the bone with a cutlery-like cauterizer until the extremities of it are incised and remain in the location of that middle work.
E es milhor obra sino que·l malaute aia febre o es de escalfada compleccio; quar cauteri es de aquelas causas que ajudan a las humiditatz finidoras, e donc es milhor en juvament.	And it is better work if the patient has fever or is of scorched complexion; for cauterization is one of those causes that help to dry up the humidity, and therefore it is better in this case.
E cove aprop la extraccio de las arcerias que huomplas le loc de coto antic, e sian pausatz sobre lu polvils decentement fayt, e aprop sia curat am medicinas seccas fazen naysser la carn e am calguas entro que sia sanat.	And it is necessary to carefully extract the arteries that fill the old wound, and be paused over the powder decently made, and be cured with dry medicines that make the flesh appear and with some other remedies until it is healed.
E si mentre obres autra veguada endeventa flux de sanc de la arceria, lahora tu te coyta a restrenger aquel sanc, o am cauteri, o que omplas le loc de coto, e strenh la tua ma entro que sia restreyt le sanc.	And if while you are working on another occasion the blood flow from the artery occurs again, then you should stop that blood flow, or with a cauterizer, or by filling the old wound, and strengthen your hand until the blood is stopped.
E si deguna causa de aquelas no es a tu present, lahoras pausa le tieu dit sobre le loc entro que·l sanc sia congilat, e enbroca le loc am aygua de vehement fregiditat entro que la acuitat repausa, e sia strengut segon que cove.	And if any of these causes are not present to you, then pause your hand over the location until the blood is congealed, and envelop the location with warm water of vehement coldness until the sharpness subsides, and be strengthened according to what is necessary.
E aquo que es pus leugier en extraccio de arceria es que tu cauterizes la vena am aquest cauteri haventz dos cotels, pus que tu has senhat les dos locs am tenta, e depausa quascus, mot ignitz, entro que pervenguan al os e inscindan la vena en dos locs, per so que sia elonguat aquo que es entre las extremitatz de lu, quar no son consolidadas de tot am aquest cauteri.	And what is easier in the extraction of the artery is that you cauterize the vein with this cauterizer having two coats, since you have marked the two locations with a tent, and deposit each one, hot and burning, until they reach the bone and cut the vein in two places, so that what is between the extremities of it may be lengthened, because they are not completely consolidated by this cauterization.
E aquesta es la forma del cauteri:	And this is the form of the cauterizer:
E sia la acuitat dels dos cotels esemps.	And the sharpness of the two coats is an example.
Mays empero si so mendres acuitat que dos cotels es milhor, quar si so agudas cum dos cotels propera a quascuna freg, e no enscideysso la carn am velocitat.	But however if there is less sharpness than two coats are better, for if they are as sharp as two coats, near each other, and do not cut the flesh with velocity.
Donc cum en aquels es alcuna grossitut, es tenguda la calor del foc en aquels e la carn es abscindida leugierament.	Therefore, when in those there is some thickness, the heat of the fire is held in them and the flesh is cut off gradually.
E aquesta obra es milhor en tota obra e pus leugiera.	And this work is better than all other works and easier.
E sia le spazi le qual es entre dos cotels la quantitat de la grossesa del dit.	And the space which is between two coats is the quantity of the thickness of the said.
Capitol quart.	Chapter IV.
De la cura de cors de lagremas agudas e aciduas dels huels.	On the Cure of Eyes with Sharp and Acid Tears.
Quan so lagremas aciduas, e es le cors de aquelas venas las quals so sobre le test del cap deforo, e no comfereys en aquo alcuna causa de la curacio de medicina, e vezes la cara del malaute ja enrogesir e sent en le sieu front deambulacio ayssi cum si era deambulacio de formiguas, e·ls huels de aquel so extenuatz, humitz enayssi que ja les pels de lor son conodutz, e las parpelas so scalfadas per la acuitat de las lacrimas, les antics agro mesties en la curacio de aquelas de aquesta operacio, e nompnero aquela curacio am spassa.	When the tears are acid and it is the body of those veins which are above the forehead of the head, and do not respond to any cause of medicine, and the face of the patient becomes reddened and feels a wandering movement as if ants were marching, and the eyes of that person are exhausted, damp, and so dry that their eyelids are condensed, and the eyelids are scalded by the acidity of the tears, the old mixture of herbs in the cure of those from this operation, and name that cure with a spatula.
E es que tu comandas al malaute rayre les pels les quals son en le sieu front, e aprop inscideys en le front tres fissuras engualment distans segon la longitut del front.	And it is that you command the patient to scratch the skin which is on his forehead, and carefully incise in the forehead three cuts equally distant according to the length of the forehead.
E si’ la longitut de la fissura cays dos ditz: la una fissura sia engualment distant a la longitut del nas en le mieg loc del front, e la segonda segon la longitut un petit del movement dels lacertz les quals so en le lacrimal, e la tersa del autre part.	And if the length of the cut is two fingers' breadth: one cut should be equally distant from the length of the nose in the middle of the forehead, and the second according to the length of a little movement of the lacertae which are in the lacrimal, and the third on the other side.
E guarda te de la incizio de las arcerias las quals so en dos latz, e elongua la tua ma de la continuacio de amdos las mandibulas.	And beware of the incision of the arteries which are in both sides, and stretch your hand from the continuation of both jawbones.
E si’ l’espazi de quascuna inscizio la quantitat de tres ditz ajustatz.	And if the space of each incision is equal to three fingers' breadth.
E si’ a tu una pessa d’espongua apparelhada o draps seccatz motz am les quals exsiccas le sanc.	And if you have a sponge or cloths which are dry and rough, with which to absorb the blood.
E aprop entremet le spatum de dos agudas extremitatz, del qual aquesta es la forma de la inscisio de lu:	And carefully insert the spatula of two sharp extremities, the form of which is the incision of it:
que es de la partida des templas entro a la segonda inscizio.	which is from the part of the temples to the second incision.
Exxcorja am aquel tota la codena la qual es entre dos incizios am le ciphac le qual es sobre le os, e aprop fay aquo de la inscizio migera entro a la segonda inscisio.	Excise all the flesh which is between two incisions on the skull which is above the bone, and carefully do this from the first incision to the second.
E aprop stratz ne aquest spatum e entromet en la primieyra inscizio autra vetz un autre instrument le qual es apelat cutellar, agut de una part e del autre no agut.	And carefully place this spatula and enter into the first incision once again with another instrument which is called a cutlary, sharp on one side and not sharp on the other.
E pausa le latz de aquel agut deves la carn annexa deves la codena, e le latz de lu leon dintz le os, e empelley aquel entro que pervengua a la fissura migera, e abscindeys am aquel totz les vaysels que descendo del cap als huels.	And pause the lateral part of that sharp instrument on the flesh attached to the bone, and the lateral part of it will enter into the bone, and bring that forward until it reaches the middle fissure, and cut away all the vessels that descend from the head to the eyes.
Mays que sia continuada la inscizio ad aquo appar de la codena, e aprop fay aquo en la fissura migana entro al autra fissura.	But it is necessary to continue the incision up to that point of the bone, and carefully do this in the middle fissure until the other fissure.
E pus que corr del sanc quantitat engual, exprem les locs de las pessas del sanc congilat.	And when there is a quantity of blood equal to that, express the places of the cloths which have been saturated with congealed blood.
E aprop pausa en quascuna fissura calgua de coto vielh, e pausa sobre aquels polvils enbegutz en vi e oli e vi agre, e vegas que no endevengua apostema caut.	And carefully pause in each fissure the old wound, and pause over those powder-like substances soaked in wine, oil, and vinegar, so that there will be no putrid apostema.
E en le tertz dia deslia le liament e aministra gran enfusio de aygua cauda o tebeza, e aprop cura aquo am enguent bazilicon am oli rozat e autres entro que las plaguas sian sanadas.	And on the third day, remove the bandage and administer great abundance of warm water or tea, and carefully cure with compresses made from basil, rose oil, and other remedies until the wounds are healed.
Capitol .v.	Chapter V.
De la cura de lagramas per catartz e als huels descendentz de las partidas dedintz del cap.	On the Cure of Tears by Cataracts and those that descend from the parts behind the head.
Quan ad alcu veno catartz agutz e continuantz, e vezes les huels del malaute extenuatz petitz, e ja le reguardament de lor es debelitat, e las palpebras ulceradas e de lor cazo les pels, e en le preon del cap es dolor aguda ledent e extrenutacio consequent, lahoras sapias per aquestz accidentz que las materias e catartz no veno sino de motas venas de las partidas dedintz procedent.	When some sharp and continued cataracts occur, and the patient's eyes are exhausted, small, and their regard is weakened, and the palpebral conjunctivae are ulcerated and the eyelids are dry, and in the forehead of the head there is a sharp pain and subsequent exhaustion, then you should know by these accidents that the matters and cataracts come from many veins of the parts behind proceeding.
E la milhor curacio en aquels es aquesta: que comandes al malaute que raza lo sieu front, e aprop inscideys en aquel una fissura al mieg loc del front, un petit per la latitut (e comensa am la fissura del templar senestre entro al dextre templar; e sia inscisio entro al os; e eslongua la tua ma dels lacertz del templas lesquals son maugutz deves la mastigacio), entro que sia le os descubert.	And the best cure in these cases is this: you command the patient to scratch his forehead, and carefully incise a cut at the middle of the forehead, a little distance from the lateral (beginning with the left temple and going to the right temple; and the incision goes into the bone; and stretch your hand over the lacertae of the temples which are above the mastigatio), until the bone is exposed.
Exsicca tot le sanc am espongua o am drap secc e aprop repleys entre las doas labias de la fissura am coto vielh o am draps de li.	Excise all the blood with a sponge or dry cloth, and carefully fill between the two lips of the wound with old wound dressings or cloths.
E aprop estrenh desus am polvils enbegutz en vi e oli per so que no endevengua apostema caut.	And carefully place above on those powder-like substances soaked in wine and oil, so that there will be no putrid apostema.
E quan deslias aquo e veses que l’apostema ja es diminuit, lahoras cove que fregua le os entro que comensa en lu nayser carn, e aprop cura aquel am regiment exsiccatiu le qual fassa neysser la carn, ayssi cum si tu prenes de farina de froment dos partidas e de colofania quatre partidas e mescla o, e de lor sia fayt emplastre e sia aministrat en aquestas plaguas a de la carn nativitat.	And when you have removed that and see that the apostema is already diminished, then carefully make the bone warm by applying heat to it until the flesh begins to appear, and carefully cure with an emplasting regiment which will make the flesh appear, just as if you were to take two parts of wheat flour and four parts of colophony and mix them together, and from that make a poultice and administer it to these wounds at the natural birthplace of the flesh.
Capitol .vi.	Chapter VI.
De la cura de aquo que catz en las aurelhas.	On the Cure of what occurs in the Ears.
Tota causa que catz en las aurelhas es una de quatre specias, quar o es peyra mineral o causa semblant a peyra, ayssi cum ferr e veyre, o es de planta ayssi cum ceze o fava, o es causa fluxtibla ayssi cum aygua e vi agre e a lor semblantz, o alcuna bestia.	All the causes that occur in the ears are of four species, for one is mineral or similar to mineral, such as iron and vermilion, or it is of plant origin, such as cypress or fava, or it is fluxible cause, such as water and vinegar, or its likeness, or some animal.
E donc quan peyra catz en l’aurelha o autra causa semblant de aquelas causas que no ajustan ne creysso en l’aurelha, e pausa la aurelha al solelh, e si vezes la peyra, lahoras distilla en aquela alcuna causa de oli violat o sizami, e aprop aministra la extraccio de lu, e fay le stornudar am condizi, e oppila las nars deve le aveniment de stornutacio.	And therefore, when mineral or similar cause occurs in the ear, or another cause that does not adjust or believe in the ear, and pause the ear at the sun, and if the mineral is sometimes present, then you should distill into it some cause of violet oil or sambucus, and carefully administer the extraction of it, and make the stornutation occur with conditions, and oppose the nose to the event of stornutation.
E aprop pausa en le circuit de la aurelha alscunas pessas de drap o lana, e dextendas la aurelha a las partidas desus, quar motas veguadas es foro-getada am aquestas causas.	And carefully place some cloths or woolen strips around the ear canal, and stretch the ear upwards to the upper parts, because many times it is forgotten about these causes.
E si no n’es getada, lahoras aministra extraccio de lu am le instrument apelat gesti epicicarios subtil del qual aquesta es la forma:	And if it is not gotten, then you should administer the extraction of it with the instrument called "epicicario" which is subtle and has this form:
E si es foro-getada am gesti, bo es; e sino, lahoras aministra la extraccio de lu am onci subtil de pauca duplicacio.	And if it is forgotten about the instrument, then it is good; and otherwise, you should administer the extraction of it with a subtle oncus of gentle doubling.
E donc si no es foro-getada per aquo, lahoras fay una canula de aram e entromet la extremitat de la canula en le trauc de la aurelha e claus a l’enviro de la canula am cera e am oli mollificada per so que no sia ubert sino la canula.	And therefore, if it is not forgotten about this, then you should make a tube of iron and insert the tip of the tube into the ear canal and close around the tube with wax and softened oil, so that only the tube remains.
E aprop extratz am le tieu vent am fort atraccio, quar tropas veguadas cum aquo que havem recontat.	And carefully extract the air from the tube with strong attraction, because many times, as we have recounted, such cases occur.
Mays si no es foro-getada en aquesta manieyra, lahoras pren de halka alumbat o de vecz aparelhat am le qual son preses les ausels una patita quantitat, e pausa aquel en la extremitat de ray, e aprop envolopa sobre aquel coto decentment pausat.	But if it is not forgotten in this manner, then you should take of hawthorn illuminated or of vine with its leaves which have been prepared so that birds eat a small quantity, and place that on the tip of the ray, and carefully envelop around that wound decently placed.
E aprop entromet aquel en le trauc de la aurelha am facilitat, e aprop excicca la aurelha de la humiditat.	And carefully insert that into the ear canal with ease, and carefully dry out the ear from the moisture.
E donc si no es foro-getada am totas las causas las quals havem recontadas, lahoras tu coyta a talhar aquela denant que endevengua apostema caut o espasme.	And therefore, if it is not forgotten about all the causes which we have recounted, then you should carefully cut away that before it becomes a putrid apostema or convulsion.
E la manieyra de talhar aquela es que tu al comensament sancnes le malaute de la vena sephasica e extratz del sanc segon la mannieyra de la vertut de lu, e aprop fay aquel cezer entre las tuas mas e converteys l’aurelha a las partidas desus, e fen am petita fissura en la razit de la aurelha deves lo greys de lu en le loc be premegut de lu.	And the method of cutting away that is to first bleed the patient from the saphenous vein and extract the blood according to the virtue of it, and carefully make that cease between your hands and convert the ear to the upper parts, and then make a small incision in the root of the ear above the grey hair.
E sia la fissura de figura lunar entro que pervengua a la peyra, e, la peyra atrobada, osta aquela si podes am instrumentz apropriatz; e aprop cos la fissura en aquela hora am velocitat, e cura aquela entro que sia sanat.	And the incision should be of a lunar shape until it reaches the bone, and when the bone is blackened, you can stop that if possible with suitable instruments; and carefully close the incision at that hour with speed, and cure that until it is healed.
E si la causa cazent en la aurelha es un dels gras que creysso e so inflatz, lahoras aministra la curacio e la extraccio de lu; mays si no obezeys a tu ad eyssiment, lahoras tu pren spatum teune subtil segon aquesta forma:	And if the cause occurs in the ear is one of the fat things that are swollen and inflamed, then you should administer the cure and extraction of it; but if it does not obey your instructions, then you should take a spatula made of tin or silver, shaped like this:
e aministra am aquel la abscizio de aquel gra lo qual es cazut en l’aurelha.	and administer with that the excision of that fat thing which has fallen into the ear.
E no fassas aquo quan cogitas que aquel ja es humectat per la vapor del aurelha, e pausa aquel en motas pessas, e prop extratz ne aquelas am les oncis o am gesti subtil, o ab inscizio ayssi co dit havem, quar es alleujada la extraccio de lu.	And do not make that incision when you think that the fat thing has already been moistened by the vapor of the ear, and pause that in many pieces, and carefully extract from those with onces or with subtle gestures, or with incisions as we have said, because it is alleviated the extraction of it.
Mays en l’aygua la qual es intrada en l’aurelha cove que·l malaute use de sternutacio am condizi al comensament, e omple la sieua aurelha am alcu coto vielh, e jagua sobre aquela aurelha en la qual es l’aygua, e si per aquo es foro-getada, bo es; e sino, lahoras pren tropas peyras teunas e leons segon la longitut del dit, e calfa aquelas en le foc un pauc, e le pacient entrometa una de aquelas en le trauc de la sua aurelha e saute sobre la un pe sieu de aquela partida e percussia am una autra peyra sobre la peyra la qual es dintz la aurelha.	But in the water which has entered the ear, it is necessary for the patient to use stornutation with conditions at the beginning, and fill his own ear with a little old wax, and place a small amount of that on top of the ear where the water is, and if it is forgotten, good; otherwise, you should take many iron pyrites and lemons according to the length of the finger, and heat those in the fire for a while, and the patient should insert one of those into the canal of his own ear and strike upon one piece of that part and pound with another pyrite on the pyrite which is inside the ear.
Donc no cesse aquo am peyra entro que tota l’aygua sia foro-getada.	Therefore, do not cease this treatment with iron until all the water is forgotten.
E ja l’aygua sira foro-getada enayssi que tu prenguas de papier o de gonc .i., e met la una extremetat de lu en l’aurelha e estendas l’autre extremitat am foc entro que sia comburit le may de lu.	And already the water will be forgotten in such a way that you take a piece of paper or of cloth, I, I, I. and place one end of it into the ear and extend the other end in the fire until the wick of it is consumed.
E prop met i autre gonc e fay aquo tantas veguadas entro que tota l’aygua sia foro-getada, e stratz aquel am canula ayssi co desus es dit de la peyra extrasadora.	and carefully place another cloth and make this many times until all the water is forgotten, and insert that with a tube as we have said before regarding the extracting iron.
Mays en la extraccio de bestia intrant en aquela aurelha, si es a petit cos, ayssi piussa e a lu semblant, cura aquel ayssi cum havem dit en la divisio; mays si es de gran cos la qual causa apar al sen del vezement, lahoras aministra la extraccio de lu am gesti e oncis, e la causa de lu es pus leugiera de totas las autras causas que cazo en l’aurelha.	But in the extraction of the beast that enters into that ear, if it is small and similar to a worm, then cure it as we have said in the division; but if it is of great size, which causes appear to the sense of feeling, then you should administer the extraction of it with gestures and onces, and the cause of it is more easily removed than all the other causes that occur in the ear.
Mays en la extraccio de verm engendrat en la aurelha, quan tu curas aquel am aquo que havem dit en la divisio e en le tractat de distillacios e no comfereys la tua curacio, lahoras cove que tu reguardes la aurelha al solelh.	But in the extraction of the worm generated in the ear, when you cure it with what we have said in the division and in the treatise on distillations, and your cure does not take effect, then it is necessary that you look at the ear to the sun.
E donc si apar aqui alcuna causa dels verms, lahoras extratz aquel am gesti o am onci subtils, mays si no apar deguna causa, lahoras pren una canula dejos streyta e desus ampla de la qual aquesta es la forma de lu:	And therefore, if any cause of worms appears here, then you should extract it with gestures or subtle onces; but if no cause appears, then you should take a tube made of reed and above amplified, which has this form:
E entromet la extremitat subtil en la aurelha segon la quantitat la qual suffertar puesca le malaute; e aprop sucgeys am aquela per succio fort, e fay aquo motas veguadas, entro que totz les verms sian foro-gitatz.	And insert the subtle end into the ear according to the quantity which the patient can tolerate; and carefully suck out with it a strong suction, and do this many times, until all the worms are forgotten.
Mays si no obezeysso a tu al ayssiment, lahoras tu opila e claus en le circuit de la canula am cera ayssi cum havem dit; lahoras aministre distillacios las quals han ja esproadas les antics en la curacio dels verms, e atrobaras aquo en le tractat de distillacios.	But if it does not obey your instructions, then you should apply and close the circuit of the tube with wax as we have said; and administer distillations which the ancients have already proven in the cure of worms, and find this in the treatise on distillations.
E sia la tua efusio am la qual efundas les olis medicinas en la aurelha am aquest strument del qual aquesta es la forma de lu:	And your effusion with which you pour the medicinal oils into the ear with this instrument, which has this form:
E fay aquela de argent o de eram, dejos streyt, en le qual sia un petit trauc, e am pla desus.	And make it of silver or of lead, reed-like, with a small channel and a plate on top.
E donc sia cum empellent a que es en la conquavitat de la canula de continent aqui on sira necessari.	And therefore, as you enter what is in the conquest of the tube, here where it will be necessary.
E si vols, pren le ray e envolveys en la extremitat de lu decentment coto, e aprop gieta oli en la concavitat del auziment, o suc de alcuna herba, o aquo que vols de aquestas medicinas en la canula — e aquela es en la aurelha —, e aprop entromet le ray am coto desus e exprem am la tua ma aquel am compressio temprada de lu entro que l’oli sia expellit en la concavitat del auziment e le malaute senta le oli dedintz.	And if you wish, take the thread and wrap it around the end of it decently, and carefully pour oil into the concavity of the ascending part, or juice from some herb, or whatever you like of these medicines in the tube - and that is in the ear -, and carefully insert the thread with a cut above and express with your hand that on compressing temperately until the oil is expelled into the concavity of the ascending part and the patient feels the oil going out.
E aquo que sia enfundut en la aurelha sia ja scalfat am foc un petit.	And what has been inserted into the ear is already burned with a small fire.
E guarda te que la causa la qual distillaras en l’aurelha no sia trop frega, quar las medicinas de aurelha no suffertan aquo.	And beware that the cause which you will distill in the ear is not too strong, for the ear medicines do not tolerate this.
Capitol .vii.	Chapter VII.
De curacio de opilacio de aurelhas.	On the Cure of Ear Blockage.
Alcunas veguadas alcus enfantz yeysso dels ventres de lors mayres no-perforatz, e aquo ja accideys en alcus homes, opilacio en le meat de la aurelha per plagua o per carn nada en aquela; e aquesta opilacio alcunas veguadas es fayta en le preon del trau de la aurelha la qual no consiec le vezement, e alcunas veguadas es en las partidas defora.	Sometimes children are born with unperforated ear vents from their mothers' wombs, and this already happens to some men, blockage in the meat of the ear due to wound or flesh not being there; and sometimes this blockage occurs in the front of the ear canal which does not allow for feeling, and sometimes it is in the outer parts.
E aquela que accideys en le preon de lu, la qual no comprehen le vezement, es en las majors disposicios de dificil sanacio.	And that which occurs in the front of it, which does not comprehend the feeling, is in the greatest difficulties for difficult healing.
E en aquela en qual consegueys le vezement, cove que tu pauses la aurelha del malaute al solelh e reguarda en aquela.	And in that which comprehends the feeling, it is necessary that you expose the patient's ear to the sun and look at it.
E donc si vezes oppulacio apparent, obre aquela am espatum subtil del qual aquesta es la forma de lu:	And therefore, if there is apparent swelling, open that with a subtle spatula which has this form:
Si’ la extremitat de lu en la qual sia petita la latitut, del qual la una partida sia aguda e l’autra no; e le spatum sia de dos latz leon per so que no fassa lizio al aurelha.	If the end of it has a small width, in which one part is acute and the other is not; and the spatula is two fingers wide to avoid causing injury to the ear.
E donc si la opilacio es per carn nascuda en la aurelha o en le meat de lu, lahoras te aquela am oncis subtils e incidiys aquela vehement facilitat entro que sia ostada tota la carn.	And therefore, if the blockage is due to flesh born in the ear or in the canal of it, then you should cut away that with subtle onces and incise it with a violent facility until all the flesh is removed.
E si opilacio es en le preon de la aurelha, lahoras pren ray subtil leon e escalfa aquel am foc un pauc, e aprop met aquel en le meat de l’aurelha.	And if the blockage is in the front of the ear, then you should take a subtle thread made of lemon and heat it with fire for a while, and carefully insert that into the canal of the ear.
E donc si as scentit oppulacio am aquo que le malaute atroba am facilitat, per gravetat de ausir, esforsa la oppressio de lu am facilitat; e guarda te que no plagues les nervis del aurelha.	And therefore, if you have sensed swelling with the patient's discomfort and ease, due to gravity of sound, force the oppression of it with ease; and beware that you do not harm the nerves of the ear.
E aprop pausa en l’aurelha drap de li segon la quantitat del ample del trauc lo qual tu as envolvutz en l’enguent egipciac; e fay aquo per alcus jorns entro que sias segur de la consolidacio de la plagua; o que prenguas qualgua e enfon aquela en ayguaros e pulveriza sobre lu segi trissat e usa de lu; e si vezes la aurelha ja esser apostemada, lahoras cove que tu estraguas la qualgua e permutes aquela am autra qualgua la qual tu envoloparas en cerot que sia fayt am oli rozat, entro que sia le apostema caut cedat; e aprop cura aquel entro que sia sanat.	And carefully place in the ear a cloth soaked with linen according to the quantity of the width of the canal which you have wrapped in Egyptian ointment; and do this for some days until you are sure of the consolidation of the wound; or take vinegar and dip that into water and powder it on top and use it; and if the ear has already become apostematous, then you should extract the vinegar and replace it with another vinegar which you have wrapped in cerote made with rose oil, until the apostema is cooled; and carefully cure that until it is healed.
Mays si accideys flux de sanc, lahoras submergeys esponga o drap en aygua frega e pausa sobre la aurelha, e usa del autra curacio la qual restrengeys le flux del sanc, la qual es dita en le tractat de distillacio.	But if bleeding occurs, then you should submerge a sponge or cloth in hot water and place it on the ear, and use another cure which restricts the flow of blood, which is described in the treatise on distillations.
Capitol .viii.	Chapter VIII.
De cura de athezil le qual endeveno a las palpebras.	On the Cure of Athazil, which infects the eyelids.
Athezil les quals endeveno a las paupebras dels huels alcuna veguada so humitz, alscunas veguadas son secs.	Athazils which infect the eyelids of some people are sometimes humid, and at other times dry.
Donc cove que tu tenguas aquels am tenhalhas o am onci, e inscindas aquels am espatum de las suas razitz, e aprop pausa sobre les locs segi trissat.	Therefore, it is necessary that you take those with tendrils or onces, and cut them with an instrument of the same kind as their roots, and carefully place them on the spots as if pressed.
Mays si dolor am flux de sanc veno, lahoras tu cauteriza aquels am cauteri lanticular subtil.	But if pain with bleeding occurs, then you should cauterize those with a lunar cautery, subtle and precise.
E la milhor cauterizacio es aprop las inscizios e tropas veguadas retornam quan reman alcuna causa de sas razitz; e quan so cauterizadas am foc, aquelas razitz son comburidas e no retornan.	And the best cauterization is to make incisions and multiple times return when there remains some cause of their roots; and when they are cauterized with fire, those roots are consumed and do not return.
Capitol .ix.	Chapter IX.
Cura de grandeyssa que veno a las palpebras dels huels.	Cure of Grandessia which occurs in the eyelids of people.
Motas veguadas endeve en las palpebras dels huels alcuna causa la qual es asemblada a grandissa en sa fortalicia e duricia, e per so grandissia es apelada.	Many times it occurs in the eyelids of people some cause which is similar to Grandessia in its strength and hardness, and therefore Grandessia is called.
E es agreguacio de humiditat grossa en la palpebra dejos e desus.	And it is an aggregation of great moisture in the eyelid above and below.
Donc la opperacio en lor es que consideras lahoras si la grandissia es procedent en lu en aquo que apar de la palpebra e es mauguda a tota partida; e la causa de lu es leugiera.	Therefore, the operation in them is that you should consider whether the Grandessia is coming from above in what appears to be from the eyelid and spreading to all parts; and the cause of it is light.
Donc fen sobre aquela am fissura per la latitut, e aprop escorga aquela de tota partida am facilitat entro que evasesca, e aprop suspen aquela am onci e abscindeys aquela.	Therefore, make an incision in that with a fissure by the width, and carefully cut away all parts with ease, and then suspend it with onces and dissect it.
Mays si a tu no es apparelhada la incizio de lu si no pus que penetras la palpebra am inscizio pauc a pauc, lahoras aquo no notz en deguna causa.	But if you are not prepared with the incision of it, and only push to penetrate the eyelid with a slight incision little by little, then this will not help in any cause.
E si la figura es gran, lahoras tu l’ajusta am sutura; e cura aquela entro que sia sanada.	And if the figure is large, then you should adjust it with a suture; and cure that until it is healed.
E si es pauca, a tu no sobrevindra mal per aquela quar l’anguent de lu restaura aquela e encarna.	And if it is small, then you will not suffer harm from it because the medicine of it restores that and makes it flesh.
E si la grandissia es declinant a las partidas dedintz de la palpebra deves la superficia dedintz, lahoras evesa la palpebra e suspen la grandissia am onci, otra que tu indigescas de incizio, e prem aquela de tota part, e si la palpebra per inscizio es alonguada, aquo no notz en deguna causa.	And if the Grandessia is declining to the outer parts of the eyelid, then you should remove the surface outwardly, and carefully lift the eyelid and suspend the Grandessia with onces, unless you are forced to make an incision; and press that part thoroughly, and if the eyelid becomes elongated through incision, this will not help in any cause.
E aprop la incizio, lava le huel am aygua salada; e cura le loc am aquo que encarna entro que sia sanat.	And carefully wash the eyes with salted water; and cure the spot with that which becomes flesh until it is healed.
Capitol .x.	Chapter X.
De la cura axcirnah en la palpebra desus del huel.	On the Cure of Axirnach in the upper eyelid of the eye.
Axcirnath es grays le qual es engendrat en las tunicas de la palpebra desus, e majorment endeve als enfantz, agrava les huels de aquels et accideyso a lor catartz le mayti; e no podon reguardar la claror del solelh per aquo quar lagremas se coytan ad aquels.	Axirnach is a greyish substance which is generated in the tunic of the upper eyelid, and more often affects children, aggravates their eyes, and causes their pupils to become constricted; and they are unable to gaze at the brightness of the sun because tears are shed upon them.
E per so tu vezes aquels jaser sobre les lors caras tot temps, e sobre les lors caras dormen; e so a las palpebras de lor dejos les sobrecils humidas, las quals ja ha cuberta imflacio, e iminencia de accernac apparent es en l’uelh; e que quant tu premes le loc am les tieus ditz, tu centes accernac entro aquels.	And therefore you should wet their faces with tears all the time, and upon their faces they sleep; and so on the eyelids of theirs above, there are moistened cilia, which have already been covered by inflammation, and apparent danger is in the eye; and when you press the spot with those same drops, you will cause the swelling to go away.
E alcuna manieyra de opperacio es en aquel que le malaute pausa le sieu cap en le tieu se, e aprop pausa drap de li e de lu fay calgua, e fay de lu cercle segon la quantitat la qual contena arthernach de tota partida, e aprop pausa aquel sobre aquela e prem am les tieus ditz de tota per que sia agreguat arcernac en le mieg del cercle, e aprop fen en le mieg de aquela humiditat am spatum inscident am fissura per la latitut, e la fissura no sia major que la fissura que es fayta en flaubotomia.	And some manner of operation is in that which the patient places his own head on a certain spot, and carefully places a cloth made from linen and water, and makes a circle according to the quantity which contains Axirnach from all parts; and carefully places that upon it and presses with the same drops throughout so that swelling occurs in the middle of the circle; and carefully ends in the middle of that humidity with a spatula incised by a fissure for width, and the fissure is not greater than the one made in flaubotomia.
Mays en le preon cove que tu fendas la codena tota entro que pervenguas ad arcernach, quar en las mays desposicios proceseys arcernach per fissura segon la forma de grayseza blanca.	But in the front it is necessary that you cut through the cord entirely until you reach Axirnach, because in the most difficult processes Axirnach proceeds by fissure according to the form of white gravel.
Donc extratz aquela am draps los quals tu as envolopatz entre les tieus ditz a las partidas deforo e revolv entre la ma dextra e sinistre entro que sia dispargut.	Therefore, extract that with cloths which you have wrapped between the same drops to the outer parts and turn it between your right and left hand until it is dispersed.
E guarda te que no ajustes en la fissura per so que am le spatum no pervenguas al huel e ladescas aquel.	And beware that you do not adjust in the fissure because with the spatula you will not reach the eye and you will cause it to be lost.
Mays si no apar a tu arternach en le comensament de la fissura, mays que tu ajustes en la fissura un petit am fecilitat entro que procesisca arternach; e aprop extratz aquela ayssi quo havem dit; e aprop submargeys draps de li en aygua e vi agre e pausa les sobre le loc e estrenh aquels am polvils.	But if there is no Axirnach at the beginning of the fissure, then adjust in the fissure a little with facility until Axirnach processes; and carefully extract that as we have said; and carefully submerge cloths made from linen in water and vinegar and place them on the spot and strengthen those with powders.
E so alcus que trissan sal e pausan aquel en la conquavitat de la fissura per so que aquo que es remas de aquela humiditat.	And so, some that are salted place it in the concavity of the fissure because this which remains from that humidity.
E aprop cura aquel entro que sia sanat.	And carefully cure that until it is healed.
Mays si accideys en le loc apostema caut, lahoras cura aquel am emplastres cedatils entro que sia sanat.	But if an apostema occurs in the spot, then carefully cure that with compresses which cool down until it is healed.
Capitol .xi.	Chapter XI.
De manieyras de tactimi del huel.	On Manner of Touching the Eye.
Quan en las palpebras dels huels so natz pels ajustatz dejos les pels naturals e so antiquatz, lahoras aquels noso al huel e fan endevenir manieras de malautias ayssi cum lacrimas assiduas e mollificacio de palpebras e tela entro que aquo sia causa de destruccio del huel que s’apela tactinir del huel, e cura se en quatre manieyras: o per cauteri am foc; o am medicina acuta segon que denant es dit en le capitol de cauteri; o es fayt atactini per inscizio e sutura; o per cannas segon que yeu diyre.	When in the eyelids of people there are found by adjustment, the natural hairs and so become old, then those eyes are not suitable for the eye and cause a method of maladies such as continuous tears and softening of eyelids and skin, until that is the cause of destruction of the eye which is called touching the eye, and cure it in four ways: or by cauterization with fire; or with acute medicine according to what is said before in the chapter on cauterization; or it is made to touch by incision and suture; or by canals as I will say.
E donc cove que tu pauses le cap del malaute en le tieu se; aprop converteys la palpebra del uelh am la tua ma sinistra, e si es convertida, bo es; e sino, entromet agulha en aquela en la qual sia fiel de la partida pus dejos de la palpebra, e fay penetrar la agulha am fiel desus, e aquo sia — prop del marge de la palpebra en le qual naysso les pels — prop dels pels, e tira le fiel a las partidas desus am la palpebra, e converteys aquela am le ray.	And therefore it is necessary that you place the patient's head in the correct position; carefully convert the eyelid of the eye with your left hand, and if it is converted, be careful; and if not, insert an awl into that which has a thread from the more distant part of the eyelid, and make the awl penetrate through the thread above, and so - next to the edge of the eyelid where there are hairs - next to the hairs, and pull the thread up to the parts above with the eyelid, and convert it with the ray.
E aprop fen en la partida dedintz de la palpebra dejos les pels ajustatz am spatum inscidentz del lacrimal major entro al lacrimal mendre; e aprop extratz le fiel e pausa dejos la palpebra polvilhs petitz de coto o de drap, e aprop senha sobre la palpebra am tenta, e sia ayssi cum figura de fuelha de mirt.	And carefully end in the outer part of the eyelid behind the hairs with a spatula incised for the lacrimal major into the lacrimal gland; and carefully extract the thread and place it behind the eyelid with small powder or cloth, and carefully sew on the eyelid with a needle, and be like that as a figure of myrtle's leaf.
Mays empero cove que sia la figura segon la quantitat de helevacio de la palpebra, quar aquo ja es diversificat en les homes, quar de aquels es le quals indigeys que sia inscidit de la palpebra gran quantitat segon la quantitat per la qual la palpebra es mollificada.	But however it is necessary that the figure be according to the quantity of elevation of the eyelid, because this already varies among men, because some of them require a great amount to be incised from the eyelid according to the quantity by which the eyelid is softened.
E aprop fen am le spatum sobre las doas linhas las quals has senhadas, e comensa del lacrimal major entro al lacrimal menor.	And carefully end with the spatula on the two lines which you have sewn, and begin from the lacrimal major into the lacrimal minor.
E si’ la tua fissura prop dels pels naturals ayssi cum es la grossetut del rey.	And if your fissure is next to the natural hairs like it is the greatest thickness of the king.
E aprop met le onci en un dels dos angles de la codena, e aprop excoria aquela tota, e aprop ajusta am la scitura las doas labias am gula o fiel de lana subtil, e abstergeys le sanc, e fay adherir aquo que superflueys dels fiels sobre dos sobrecils am alcunas causas enviscans, si voles far aquo, e sino, non cures.	And carefully place the onyx in one of the two angles of the cord, and carefully remove it all, and carefully adjust with the sutura the two lips with a subtle thread or wool, and wash away the blood, and make what is superfluous from the threads to stick to the eyelids with some causes that are visible, if you wish to do so, and if not, do not cure.
E aprop leyssa la sutura dels fiels entro a tres dias o quatre, e aprop cura aquo.	And carefully loosen the sutura of the threads within three or four days, and carefully cure that.
E si vols, layssa la plagua ses sutura, e cura aquela am aquo que exsicca e constrenh, quar la palpebra es alevada deves la sigillacio de la plagua e la agreguacio de lu; mays sutura es milor E donc aysso diysso les antics de taxanir.	And if you wish, leave the wound without suturing and cure it with what dries up and constrains, because the eyelid is elevated due to the sealing of the wound and the aggregation of pus; but suturing is better. And so thus say our ancient ones who practiced touching.
Mays empero en lu sia sollicitut sobre le malaute, e es de bona operacio, e no es en lu temor.	But meanwhile in him there was solicitude about the patient, and it was of good operation, and not in him fear.
E es autra manieyra en taxmir, e es que senhes sobre la palpebra figura ayssi cum fuelha de mirt, e aprop eleva la palpebra am tres uncis segreguatz e congreguatz segon aquesta forma:	And there is another manner of touching, and it is that you sew on the eyelid a figure like a myrtle leaf, and carefully elevate the eyelid with three threads separated and gathered according to this form:
Mays si no es possible aquo, tener les uncis, e aquo no es engualhat, lahoras pren una agula en la qual haia fil e met aquela en le mieg de la figura, e entromet le autre fiel prop le lacrimal major, e·l fiel segon prop le lacrimal mendre, e ajusta entre les tieus ditz les fiels am equalitat, e aprop am aquels eleva la tua ma am elevacio engual, eleva tota la codena sobre la qual es senhat ayssi cum havem recomtat.	But if it is not possible to take the threads, and this is not equated, then carefully take an awl with thread and place that in the middle of the figure, and insert the other thread next to the lacrimal major, and the second thread next to the lacrimal minor, and adjust between the same drops the threads with equality, and carefully elevate all the cord on which is sewn as we have recounted.
E aprop ajusta las doas labias de la plagua am sutura, e cura aquel entro que sia sanat.	And carefully adjust the two lips of the wound with a suture, and cure that until it is healed.
Mays si accideys apostema deves la tua inscizio o la tua fissura, seda aquel apostema am cerot e a lu semblantz, e am enguentz.	But if an apostema occurs due to your incision or your fissure, then carefully dress that apostema with cerote and lint, and cover it with powders.
E alcunas veguadas endeve a la palpebra que·ls sieus pels sian convertitz, adonc cove que tu uses en aquela de aquo que havem dit de inscizio; mays sutura en quascus es mays artificial.	And sometimes it happens that the eyelid is converted into its own hairs, then it is necessary to use on it what we have said about incision; but suture in each case is more artificial.
Ataxinir am cannas es segon aquesta forma:	Taxinating with canals is according to this form:
e es que tu convertas la palpebra e scindas la figura qu’es dedintz segon que he recontat; e aprop per art fay doas cannas o doas astelas subtils de las quals longitut sia segon la longitut de la palpebra e la latitut de lor sia mendra de la latitut del spatum.	and it is that you convert the eyelid and divide the figure which is outside according to what I have recounted; and carefully, by art, make two canals or two subtle astels of which the length is according to the length of the eyelid and the width of theirs is smaller than the width of the spatula.
E tu ja has inscidit en las extremitatz de quascunas partidas, la on tenes les fils.	And you have already incised at the extremities of each partition, where you have the threads.
Aprop agregua quascuna am subtilitat subre aquo que superflueys de la palpebra del huel, e constres las cannas de quascunas partidas am fort strictura, e layssa aquela per alcus jorns, quar la codena per la strictura morira e sira denegada e se poyrira entro que per si meteyssa cayra.	And carefully add each one with subtlety over what superfluously remains of the eyelid of the eye, and tighten the canals of each partition with a strong stricture, and leave it for some days, because the cord will die and become denuded and will settle in as it will naturally fall.
Mays si es tardat, lahoras trenca la am las toroyras, e aprop cura la plagua entro que sia sanat.	But if it is delayed, then carefully cut the thread with scissors, and carefully cure the wound until it is healed.
Donc cum es solidada, la palpebra es elevada e les pels no pungo.	Therefore, when it has hardened, the eyelid is elevated and the hairs do not sting.
E aquesta es la forma de doas cannas las quals faras segon aquesta forma:	And this is the form of two canals which you will make according to this form:
e haia la quantitat de la longitut e de la latitut ni mays ni mens.	and has the quantity of length and width neither more nor less.
Capitol .xii.	Chapter XII.
De elevacio de pels pungentz en le huel am agula quan le pel es dur.	On the Elevation of Stinging Hairs in the Eye with an Awl when the Hair is Hard.
Quan son pels no-naturals, durs e aspres e pungentz les huels, lahoras la operacio en lu es que tu prenguas agula subtil e pauses en aquela fiel de ceda subtil e leon, e aprop que tu ajustes las extremitatz de lu e nozes quascu en manieyra mot subtil.	When the hairs are unnatural, hard, rough, and stinging the eyes, then the operation in that is that you take a subtle awl and place it in that subtle thread of cedarn or lemon, and carefully adjust the extremities of it and notice each one in a manner very subtle.
E sia la longitut dels fiels de quantitat de una palma.	And the length of the threads should be of the quantity of a palm.
E aprop tu compon2 autre fiel subtil dejos lu en breu, e nuza las extremitatz de aquel si tu·t vols.	And carefully compose another subtle thread below it in brief, and bind the extremities of that if you wish.
E aprop pause le malaute le sieu cap en le tieu se, e sia prop del solelh per que la tua obra sia declarada, quar es operacio subtil e menuda.	And carefully place the patient's head in the correct position, and be next to the sun so that your work is declared, for it is a subtle and minute operation.
E aprop intromet la agulha en la razit del pel ajustat la qual ha necessitat de engen, e fay aquela penetrar en la palpebra festinantment entro que extraguas aquela desus le pel natural.	And carefully insert the awl into the root of the adjusted hair which has required engineering, and make it penetrate the eyelid quickly until you extract that above the natural hair.
E aprop tire le pel entro desus e intromet aquel en alixati, e sian les pels un o dos o tres e no mays.	And carefully pull out the hair above and insert it into the socket, and let the hairs be one or two or three and no more.
E aprop tira la tua ma am aquel entro que·l pel sia fora-gitat am alixolati en la palpebra am le pel natural.	And carefully pull your hand with it until the hair is outside the socket in the eyelid with the natural hair.
Mays si es atirat alixalati e non es gitat le pel, atiraras alixati a las partidas dejos am le fiel le qual tu has compost am aquela, entro qu’en sia gitat alixalati del trau sobira.	But if it is attracted to the socket and not pulled out the hair, you will pull the socket towards the parts below with the thread which you have composed in that, until it becomes extracted from above the brow.
E vegas aquela am la visio del huel, quar lahoras tu gitaras alixati e lo fiel, e grotan quascu e clautz le huel, e laysse le claus per dos dias o tres, entro que·l pel adheresca al sieu loc e nasque sobre aquel bona carn.	And leave it with the vision of the eye, because you will extract the socket and the thread, and each one will be closed and tightened the eye, and leave the closure for two or three days, until the hair sticks to its place and grows over that good flesh.
E si es mays breu le pel, lahoras tu ajusta un pel lonc dels pels naturals, e es elevat am aquel, o que·l leysses entro que sia alonguat aprop alcu spazi, e lehoras tu eleva aquel.	And if the hair is too short, then you will adjust a long hair from the natural hairs, and it will be elevated with that, or let it settle until it becomes stretched to some space, and then you will elevate that.
Capitol .xiii.	Chapter XIII.
De la cura de ehacratir la qual ve en la palpebra desus.	On the Cure for the Condition which appears on the Eyelid above.
Quan ve en le huel ehacratir, e es contraccio de la palpebra quan es contrayta en sus, o a dextra o a sinistra partida, per mala consolidacio de plagua o de seccio o de cauteri, e es apelada leporina, e aquesta ahercrati o es natural o accidental, e es fayta per consolidacio de plagua o de seccios o de cauteri, o per semblantz a lor malcuratz.	When it appears on the eye as ehacratir, and it is contraction of the eyelid when it is contracted in its own direction, or to the right or left side, due to bad consolidation of wound or section or cauterization, and it is called leporina, and this ehacratir either is natural or accidental, and is caused by consolidation of wound or sections or cauterizations, or by resemblance to their maladies.
May la manieyra de la operacio en lu es que tu fendas aquela consolidacio e que separes las labias de lu, e pauses en lu en aquo que es entre aquelas una meca de drap de li, e ligues aquelas entro que sian sanadas.	The manner of the operation in that is that you cut open that consolidation and separate the lips of it, and place it in what is between them a piece of linen cloth, and tie those together until they are healed.
E no cove que tu uses de curacio de lu de las causas las quals exsiccan, constrenho; quar si tu fas aquo retorna alixacratir pus mal que nulh temps no foc habantz.	And it is not necessary that you use a cure for that from the causes which dry out and constrict; because if you do so, it will return to ehacratir even worse than before there was no time at all.
Usa en aquela de causas que mollifico ayssi cum es fenugrec, e embroca am la aygua en la qual son coytz altea e semensa de li, o enguent dyaquilon, le qual sia liquefayt am alcu dels olis, e submergeys en aquel la meca, e cura am aquel.	Use in that a remedy which softens, such as fenugreek, and soak it in the water in which are cooked high and full of seeds, or emblument oil, which is liquefied with some of the oils, and submerge the cloth in that, and cure with that.
E lo tesaur de la tua curacio es que tu perforsses am tot engen que no sia consolidat segon la forma que foc al comensament.	And the treasure of your remedy is that you pierce all that which is not consolidated according to the form that was at the beginning.
E aquesta operacio la qual havem dita, no es sino alcuna rectificacio de ehalixacrati que no retorna la forma del loc segon que foc denant.	And this operation which we have said, is nothing but some correction of ehacratir that does not return to its original form as it was before.
Capitol .xiiii.	Chapter XIV.
De la cura de ehacrati le qual es fayt en la palpebra dejos.	On the Cure for Ehacratir which is made in the Eyelid below.
Aquesta alxacrati la qual es fayta en la palpebra dejos, la qual es nompnada vertadierament alxacrati; e es de lu alcuna natural, autra accidental.	This ehacratir which is made in the Eyelid below, which is truly called vertadierament ehacratir; and it is of him some natural, other accidental.
Mays accidental es fayta per plagua o per scissura o per cauteri o per autres semblantz.	But accidental is made by wound or section or cauterization or by other likenesses.
E la via de la operacio de lu es que tu prenguas una agula en la qual haga fil doble, e fiques aquela en la carn, e que la fassas passar del lacrimal de senestre entro al lacrimal dextre, entro que·l fil pervengua en las doas extremitatz de la carn.	And the way of the operation in that is that you take an awl with a double thread, and place it in the flesh, and make it pass from the lacrimal gland on the left side to the lacrimal gland on the right side, until the thread reaches both extremities of the flesh.
E aprop exten la carn a las partidas desus am la agula e cus aquela am la agula, e inscideys am spatum ample.	And carefully extend the flesh to the upper parts with the awl and cut it with the awl, and incise with a spatula wide.
E donc si retorne la figura de la palpebre segon que cove, bo es; e sino, pren le ray e pausa aquel en la figura fenduda, e am aquel converteys la palpebra, e fen las doas fissuras en le latz de la palpebra dejos.	And therefore if the figure of the eyelid returns to its proper shape, it is good; and otherwise, take the thread and place it in the cleft figure, and with that convert the eyelid, and make the two fissures on the side of the lower eyelid.
E sian las extremitatz de las doas fissuras de dos angles de la inscizio, la qual has fayta entro que concurren, e sia de lor fayt angle entro que quan se congreguan sia fayta figura de lor.	And the extremities of the two fissures are at two angles of the incision, which you have made so that they converge, and it is to be done with their own natural angle, so that when they come together, a figure is formed from them.
E aquesta figura es letra greca: la landa.	And this figure is the Greek letter: lambda.
E aprop osta la carn aquela per la quantitat que es le latz de lu agut dejos de lu, aquo que siec la palpebra.	And carefully cut off the flesh to the quantity that is the width of the lacrimal gland below, which marks the eyelid.
E aprop ajusta las partz seperadas e cos aquelas am le fil de lana; e aprop cura aquelas am aquo que havem dit de las medicinas mollificativas e de las calguas entro que sia sanat.	And carefully adjust the separated parts and sew them with a thread of wool; and carefully cure those with what we have said about softening medicines and poultices until they are healed.
E si alxacrati endeve per fissura o sutura o cauteri, lahoras cove que tu fendas am fissura plana sobre les pels de la palpebra segon que es precedit.	And if ehacratir occurs due to a fissure or suture or cauterization, then it is necessary that you cut with a flat incision on the hairs of the eyelid according to what has been previously mentioned.
E aprop separa am la calgua entre doas labias segon que havem dit.	And carefully separate with a poultice between two lips according to what we have said.
En la suma del sermo de la cura de alxacrati quan es desus o dejos, que corra en lu operacio, segon que es preparat de la forma de alxacrati, e aquela es en forma de motas diversitatz.	In the summary of the sermon on the cure for ehacratir when it is above or below, that which occurs in that operation, according to what has been prepared in the form of ehacratir, and that is in the form of diverse varieties.
E le artifexs savi totz temps prepara engen en quascuna manieyra la qual es possibla a lu entro que fassa retornar la figura a la forma natural, o prop de aquela, e aquel malaute segon que a lu conveneys de la operacio e dels strumentz en las majors disposicios.	And the skilled artisans prepare skillfully in every possible way that is possible to them, so that they may return the figure to its natural form, or almost to that, and that patient according to what is convenient for him, regarding the operation and the instruments in the best dispositions.
Capitol .xv.	Chapter XV.
De la adherencia de la palpebra am la conjunctiva o am la cornea.	On the Adhesion of the Eyelid to the Conjunctiva or to the Cornea.
Quan accideys aquesta consolidacio a motz homes enayssi que sia solidada la palpebra pus desus am le album del huel, e sia prohibida de la facilitat del movement e de las suas obras naturals, donc cove que tu entrometas la extramitat del ray dejos la palpebra, e eleva en sus aquela, o exten aquela am le unci.	When this consolidation occurs in many men, it is solidified on top of the eyelid as if it were a film, and prohibited from the ease of movement and its natural works, therefore it is necessary that you intervene at the extremity of the ray below the eyelid, and lift it up or extend it with an instrument.
E aprop tu inscideys la adherencia am spatum subtil, le qual no sia am acuitat de las inscisios, habantz obtus un petit per so que·l malaute no sia inquietat deves la operacio, e remau le spatum que no ledesca le huel am la sua acuitat.	And carefully incise the adhesion with a subtle spatula, which is not sharp like the incisions, having obtuse edges a little bit so that the patient is not disturbed during the operation, and remove the spatula so as not to injure the eye with its sharpness.
E sia la tua inscizio quays excorjan aquela adherencia am facilitat entro que sia retornada la palpebra segon la sua forma natural e que sia sanada tota la adherencia.	And be the incision which carefully separates that adhesion with facility, so that the eyelid is returned to its natural form and all the adhesion is healed.
E aprop tu met en le huel aygua salada am la qual tu laves; o distilla en lu de zunia dissolvut en l’aygua.	And carefully put in the eye salted water with which you wash; or distill on it dissolved zinc in water.
E aprop separa entre la palpebra e l’huel am calgua de li, e pausa sobre le huel lana infuza en album de huou, e aprop le tertz jorn usa de causas consolidativas entro que sia sanat.	And carefully separate between the eyelid and the eye with a poultice of lint, and place it over the eye wool infused in the albumen of egg, and carefully use for three days causes that consolidate until it is healed.
Capitol .xvi.	Chapter XVI.
De inscizio de ungla e de eminencia de carn dels lacrimals.	On the Incision of the Nail and Eminence of Flesh of the Lacrimals.
Sapias que ungla es segon dos manieyras, quar o es nervosa, e es semblant a ciphac dur subtil; o es no-nervosa, semblant a humiditat blanca congilada, la qual quan ferr la toca, o es forsat aquela prendre am onci, es abscindida e le onci no es ficat en lu.	Know that the nail is according to two manners, for either it is nervous, and resembles a hard and subtle cypress; or it is non-nervous, resembling white congealed moisture, which when iron touches it, or takes hold of the onychium, is abscinded and the onychium is not fixed in place.
E amdos las specias no comensan sino del lacrimal major entro que va petit a petit que cobre la vista e prohibeys le lum e·l movement de huel.	And both species do not begin until the lacrimal major, and gradually become smaller as they cover the eye and prohibit light and movement of the eye.
Mays la manieyra del obrar en la inscizio de lu es que·l malaute pause le sieu cap en le tieu se, e aprop obre les huels de lu, e eleva la palpebra am la tua ma, e aprop colligeys la ungla am onci de pauca duplicacio e exten aquela a las partidas desus.	But the manner of working in this incision is that the patient places his head in the correct position, and carefully opens the eyes, elevates the eyelid with his hand, and carefully collects the nail with an onychium of slight duplication and extends it to the upper parts.
E aprop pren una agula e entromet en aquela un pel de cavalh o de buou o de vaqua, o de semblantz, o de fiel fort, o duplica la extremitat de la agulha petit a petit e fica aquela en le mieg de la ungla, e penetra aquela am la agulha, e lia am fiel la ungla; e exten aquela a las partidas desus, e excorja am le pel le latz de la ungla lo qual siec la pupilla.	And carefully take an awl and insert into it a horse, ox, or cow hair, or something similar, or a strong thread, and duplicate the extremity of the awl little by little and place it in the middle of the nail, and penetrate it with the awl, and tie with thread the nail; and extend it to the upper parts, and excise on one side of the nail what is seen as the pupil.
E ayssi tu sieguas aquela am le pel entro al derier de lu.	And thus you follow that with the hair until the end of it.
E aprop tu inscideys le romanent en la razitz del lacrimal am spatum subtil o am petitas forfexs, e leysa la carn del lacrimal natural per so que per inscizio de aquela no endevengua fluxs de lagremas continuabla.	And carefully incise the remnant in the root of the lacrimal with a subtle spatula or small forceps, and loosen the natural flesh of the lacrimal so that through the incision there is not a continuous flow of tears.
E alscunas vetz la ungla am le sol onci estenduda o am fiel, ayssi co havem dit, e aprop sia excurjat am spatum leon del qual aquesta es la forma de lu:	And in some cases the nail with the sole onychium extended or with thread, just as we have said, and carefully excised with a lion's spatula of which this is its form:
E guarda te que am le spatum no toques la tunica cornea e que avengua en lu ruptura, e que la pupilla sia perforada.	And be careful not to touch the corneal tunic with the spatula, lest you cause a rupture and perforate the pupil.
Aprop la inscizio geta en le huel un pauc de sal trissa o di cief fayt de siniar, e leyssa aquel entro al autre dia; e aprop cura aquel am aquo que cove entro que sia sanat.	And carefully place the incision in the eye a little salt powder or made from sinew, and let it sit for another day; and carefully cure that with water as needed until it is healed.
E si la ungla no es nervoza e no podes metre la agulha, ni es ficada en aquela le onci, lahoras motas veguadas aquesta specia de ungla es curada am medicinas, e es sanada ayssi cum yeu e recomtat en la divisio.	And if the nail is not nervous and you cannot insert the awl, nor is it fixed in that place the onychium, then many times this species of nail is cured with medicines, and is healed just as I have said and recounted in the division.
E si tu vols inscindir aquela, lahoras tu obre le huel del malaute e pren spatum subtil leon de freul acuitat segon aquesta forma:	And if you want to incise that, then you will work on the patient's eye and take a subtle spatula of lion's fur with keen edges according to this form:
am subtilitat.	with subtlety.
E si vezes que aquela es rarificada e es confugida e empren en aquela razit, lahoras distilla de la tua ora en le huel de cief fayt de siniar o am cief rog o am sal trissat, e opila le huel entro a l’autre dia.	And if at times it is rarefied and is confused and enters into that root, then you will distill from your own eye with sinew or with rosy cheeks or with salt powder, and apply the eye to another day.
E aprop itera sobre aquela la operacio entro que sia remaugut tot aquo que es de lu, sino que·l contrari apostema caut sia en le huel, quar lahoras tu leyssa aquela, e cura al comensament la apostema entro que sia sanat.	And carefully iterate over that the operation until all that is of it is removed, except for the opposite apostema which is in the eye, because then you will leave it and cure the apostema from the beginning until it is healed.
E aprop itera la tua operacio sobre aquela am razo entro que sia sanat.	And carefully iterate your operation over that with reason until it is healed.
La emenencia de la carn lacrimal, si notz en le huel per gran nocument, sia suspendut am onci; e inscideys aquela de aquela una partida, e no ultimes la inscizio per so que no inscidesqua fluxs de lagremas.	The eminence of the lacrimal flesh, if noticed in the eye with great harm, should be suspended with onychium; and incise that from one part, and do not finish the incision so as not to cause a flow of tears.
E aprop distilla en le lacrimal cief rog e fayt de siniar entro que sia sanat.	And carefully distill into the lacrimal rose-colored and made from sinew, until it is healed.
Capitol .xvii.	Chapter XVII.
De inscizio de alguazardenic e de aquo que es nascut de carn ajustada en le huel.	On the Incision of Algae and Water that is born from flesh adjusted in the Eye.
Alcunas veguadas en les huels de alcus es nascuda carn roga, e es sobre-pausada entro que cobre la pupilla, o apropinqua o estrenh sobre las palpebras e fort leu comprem las palpebras a las partidas deforo e es assemblada a roza de balaustra.	Some times in the eyes of some people is born red flesh, and it is superimposed to cover the pupil, or approaches or stretches over the eyelids and strongly compresses the eyelids at the outer parts and is assembled like a rose bush.
Mays la operacio en lu es que·l malaute pausa le sieu cap en le tieu se; e aprop obre les huels de aquel e colligeys tota aquela carn am oncis convenientz ad aquo, e te aquo am una forcep o am cesti; e aprop inscindiys la carn el comensament entro que tot sia finit am le encisori, e guarda te del huel que no ledescas aquel deves la tua operacio.	But the operation in this case is that the patient places his head in the correct position; and carefully opens the eyes of that and collects all that flesh with onychium convenient for water, and takes water with a forceps or a basket; and carefully incises the flesh from the beginning until everything is finished with the instrument, and be careful not to injure the eye which might lead to your operation.
E sia la tua inscizio am la qual inscides aquelas o am espatum le qual nos havem recomtat en la inscizio de la ungla, o am petitas forfexs am las quals es colligit ascebel segon que vindra la forma de lu aprop aquest capitol.	And be the incision with which you cut those or with the spatula which we have recounted in the incision of the nail, or with small forceps with which it is gathered according to the form that will come forth at this chapter.
Donc cum es complida la tua inscizio e es remauguda tota aquela carn, lahoras omple le huel de sal trissa, o destilla en lu polvera roga e semblantz a lu de las medicinas corrossivas, e pausa sobre le huel deforo coto am album de huou entro que sia asegurat de apostema caut.	And so when your incision is completed and all that flesh is removed, then fill the eye with salt powder, or distill into it red powder similar to those medicines corrosive, and place over the eye a cloth made from albumen of egg, until you are assured of apostema cautious.
E si roman alcuna causa de alguardenici e es senhoragat sanc caut, e temes apostema caut, lahoras leyssa le huel e cura aquela apostema am aquo que ceda aquela apostema, e aprop itera sobre aquel am operacio entro que sia sanat, e semblantment fay en la carn ajustada la qual accideys en le huel de aquesta especia.	And if there remains some cause of algae and is carefully removed cautious, and you fear apostema cautious, then leave the eye and cure that apostema with water which will cause that apostema to heal, and carefully iterate over it with operation until it is healed, and similarly do in the adjusted flesh which occurs in the eye of this species.
Mays empero tu cove que alienes tota curacio del huel freul per via natural o per via accidental, obran am ferr, e no metas la tua ma en alcuna de aquestas operacios entro que veges que aquel membre sia suffertant aquela operacio.	But always keep in mind that you must alienate all cure of the eye from natural or accidental means, working with iron, and do not put your hand in any of these operations until you see that that member is sufficient for that operation.
Capitol .xviii.	Chapter XVIII.
De colleccio de sabel en le huel.	On the Collection of Scales in the Eye.
Sabel so venas rogas las quals son testudas sobre le huel e prohibeysso al vesement la sua operacio, e develican le huel am longitut de dias.	Scales which come red and are rough on the eye and prevent the veament from performing its operation, and unfold the eye along with days.
Donc necessari es al comensament que tu consideres si le huel en le qual es sabel es fort e en lu no es autra malautia que sabel, lahoras tu colligeys aquel sabel.	Therefore it is necessary at the beginning that you consider whether the eye in which scales are present is strong and there is no other disease besides scales, then you will collect those scales.
E es que tu comandes al malaute que pause le sieu cap en le tieu se, e aprop suspen aquelas venas am un onci o am dos segon la tua prudencia; e sia aquel onci de subtil duplicacio segon aquesta forma:	And it is that you command the patient to place his head in the correct position, and carefully suspend those veins with one or two according to your prudence; and be that one thread of subtle duplication according to this form:
o so dos oncis gradantment en un cos segon aquesta forma:	or two threads gradually in one case according to this form:
E aprop sian colligidas aquelas venas am forses subtils, am subtilitat, e abstergeys le sanc hora aprop hora, entro que vegas aquelas venas esser remaugudas del huel e sian revolgudas.	And carefully collect those veins with subtle forces, with subtlety, and wipe away the blood hour by hour, until you see those veins being removed from the eye and turned back.
E guarda te que tu no ledes le huel am las extremitatz del spatum; e si’ la tua operacio en le miegjorn denant le solelh, e sias mot ferm en la tua operacio que no inscidas sino aquelas venas.	And be careful that you do not injure the eye with the extremities of the spatula; and if your operation is in the middle of the day before the sun, and be very firm in your operation so as to cut only those veins.
E quan tu auras complitz, lahoras tu distilla en le huel cief vert o rog per que am sa acuitat corrodesca aquo que es remaugut del sabel.	And when you have completed, then you will distill into the eye green or red liquid so that with its keenness it may dissolve the water that is removed from the scales.
Mays si aquo no es a tu possible colligeys tot en aquela hora, e lahoras tu emplastra tot am aquo que cede la dolor de lu, e leyssa lu per alcus dias entro que sia sedada la dolor de lu e que sia asegurat de apostema caut.	But if this water is not possible for you to collect at that hour, then gather everything in that hour and carefully apply all the water that relieves the pain of it, and leave it for some days until the pain of it is soothed and you are assured of cautious apostema.
E aprop itera sobre lu segon que la mateyssa manieyra entro que sia sanat.	And carefully iterate over it according to the same manner, until it is healed.
E aquesta es la forma de las forfexs:	And this is the form of the forceps:
Capitol .xix.	Chapter XIX.
De reduccio de arizati al nas.	On the Reduction of Rhinorrhea to the Nose.
Quan tu curas arisati am cauteri o am medicina aguda comburent segon que es precedida la narracio de lu e no es sanat, lahoras no es engen en lu sino que fendas sobre le apostema deves la maturitat de lu, e que extraguas tota la humiditat la qual es en lu e·l poyre entro que sia descubert le os.	When you cure a rhinorrhea with cauterization or acute medicine, and it is not healed as previously described, then do not intervene in it, but rather cut over the apostema of that maturity, and extract all the moisture which is in it and pour it into until the bone is revealed.
