E donc cum es descubert le os e vezes en lu corrupcio o negror, lahoras tu ratz lu am un sturment del qual aquesta es la forma:	And therefore when the bone is revealed and corruption or blackness appears in it, then you will scrape it with an instrument whose form is:
E es nompnat de aspre cap, e sia feyt de fer indi, e sia le cap redon ayssi cum asir le qual sia fayt punctat per punctacio de lima o aliskalfati per punctacio subtil (ayssi cum es en la forma seguent).	And it is called "Aspercap", and is made of iron, and has a red head like an ash, which is pointed with a fine point by lime or alkali for a subtle point (like in the following form).
E pausa aquel sobre le loc corrumput del os, e aprop revolveys aquel entre les tieus ditz, e prem la tua ma petit a petit entro que sapias que aquela corropcio es rasa.	And place that on the corrupted spot of the bone, and carefully rotate it between the said digits, and press your hand little by little until you know that that corruption is removed.
E aquo sia fayt alcunas veguadas, e aprop restaura le loc am causas exsiccativas e stipticas.	And this should be done several times, and carefully restore the spot with drying and astringent causes.
Donc si·l loc es consolidat e es en lu nascuda bona carn e es abscindit le cors de la sania e roman per xl dias, e no es renovat e no es apostemat e no accideys en lu accident, lahoras tu sapias que es sanat.	Therefore if the spot is consolidated and good flesh has grown in it, and the purulent abscess has been removed and remains for 40 days without being renewed or becoming apostematous, nor does any accident occur in it, then you know that it is healed.
E sino, lahoras no es en lu engen sino reduzir la fissura a la forma del nas, e segon aquesta manieyra: e es que tu descuebras de segon os am ferr o am medicina acuta, e cum sira descubert le os, lahoras tu pren tribo segon aquesta forma:	And if not, then do not intervene in it, but rather reduce the fissure to the form of the nose, and according to this manner: and it is that you uncover from below with iron or acute medicine, and when the bone is uncovered, then you take a thread according to this form:
Sia la extramitat de lu ferr triangulada, e·l fust de lu sia prim extenuat entro a la extremitat ayssi cum vezes assi.	Be the extremity of the iron triangular, and the handle of it first reduced to the extremity in that way as if times were thus.
E aprop pausa aquel sobre le os, e sia aquel prop del lacrimal; e alongua la tua ma un pauc del huel, e aprop revol la tua ma am le tribo entro que penetre tot le os, e aquel sente le malaute per asso que atroba vent yssir per so quan te la sua ma.	And carefully place that over the bone, and it should be that prop of the lacrimal; and stretch your hand a little from the eye, and carefully turn your hand with the thread until it penetrates all the bone, and that feels the patient by finding air to come out so when you put your hand.
Donc lahoras restaura le loc am medicinas stipticas exsiccantz ayssi cum t’e eyssenhat.	Therefore carefully restore the spot with drying and astringent medicines as if it were well taken care of.
Donc cum nays la carn e·l loc es endurazit, lahoras la materia la qual effundia a las partidas deforo retorna al nas, donc aquo es pus leugier sobre le malaute.	Therefore when the flesh and the spot are hardened, then the material which flows to the outer parts returns to the nose, therefore this is less troublesome for the patient.
Capitol .xx.	Chapter XX.
De reduccio de la eminencia del huel.	On the Reduction of the Eminence of the Eye.
Quan le huel emineys am la sua totalitat e no accideys en le vezement nocument ni diminuacio, lahoras cove que laxas le malaute, e aprop que·l segues, e aprop que pausas ventozas en le cervitz ses scarificacio e succa per bona succaccio; e aprop pausa sobre le huel liniment le qual sia fayt de acatra e aloe e enses e sarcocolla, e aprop strenh le emplaustre sobre le huel am motz polvils.	When the eye protrudes in its entirety and there is no accident or diminution in the veament, then you must loosen the patient, and carefully follow, and carefully pause for breathing exercises without scarification and sucking for good suction; and carefully place a poultice on the eye made of acacia and aloe and onions and sarcocolla, and carefully strengthen the emplaustre on the eye with many powders.
E la manieyra dels polvils es que prenguas draps de li leons motz, e quascun drap sia duplicat en quatre plecs; e fay de aquels motz.	And the manner of the powders is that you take cloths of lion's mane many times, and each cloth be doubled into four folds; and make from those many.
E aprop pausa aquels la un sobre le autre segon la quantitat de la qual ha le huel necessitat.	And carefully place one on top of the other according to the quantity that the eye requires.
E aprop strenh sobre aquels am drap dur am fort strictura; e itera las ventosas am succio ses scarificacio; e aprop osta las ventosas e leyssa le huel streyt le dia e la nueyt.	And carefully strengthen on top of those with a strong cloth, and iterate the suction without scarification; and carefully stop the suction and leave the eye tightly wrapped day and night.
Mays si entretant le liguament es mollificat, lahoras cove que sia mot streyt.	But if the ligament is softened in the meantime, then you must make it very tight.
E aprop osta le liament aprop le dia e la nueyt ayssi cum havem dit.	And carefully stop the ligament tightly day and night just as we have said.
E si vezes le huel ja esser redusit, bo es, e sino, lahoras itera le emplastre am les polvils e la strictura e las ventosas entro que sia sanat.	And if the eye is already reduced, good; and if not, then carefully repeat the poultice with the powders and stricture and suction until it is healed.
Capitol .xxi.	Chapter XXI.
De la inscizio de la eminencia de la tunica uvea.	On the Incision of the Eminence of the Uveal Tunic.
Quan endeve disrupcio en la tunica uvea, e aprop es eminent e procezeys fora las palpebras ayssi cum un gra de rasim, e es orrazada la forma de home per aquo, e vols aquo inscidir, lahoras la operacio en lu es ayssi cum havem recomtat, que tu entrometas la agula en la razitz de la uvea de la partida dejos en la partida desus, e aprop met la agula autra en la qual sia fil doble de la part del lacrimal, e fay aquela penetrar e leyssa la primieyra agula segon la sua disposicio; e aprop inscideys le loc del fiel doble e leva am aquel la partida de la uvea en le circuit de la agula, e strenh aquela mot.	When there is a disruption in the uveal tunic, and it is elevated and proceeds forth from the eyelids like a grain of rice, and its form resembles that of a human being by this, and you want to incise it, then the operation on it is as we have recounted, which you will insert the awl into the root of the uvea at the lower part and leave the upper part above, and carefully place another awl in the double thread part from the lacrimal side, and make that penetrate and leave the first awl according to its disposition; and carefully incise the location of the double thread and lift with it the part of the uvea into the circuit of the awl, and strengthen that motion.
E aprop extratz la agula e pausa sobre le huel lana infusa en album de huou e leyssa entro que cayha le fil am la uva.	And carefully extract the awl and place it on the eye lanolin infused in egg white, and leave it until the thread falls onto the grape.
E aprop cura le huel am aquo que conforte aquel entro que la plagua sia sanada.	And carefully cure the eye with water that comforts it until the wound is healed.
E alcunas veguadas aduna de tota partida am cercle de drap entro le huel ajuste eminencia gran, e aprop sia perforat am le spatum subtil que vengua al preon del huel, e corra la humiditat albuginea, e descen le huel e intra tantost.	And some times gather all parts together with a circle of cloth into the eye adjusted to great prominence, and carefully be perforated by the subtle spatula that comes to the edge of the eye, and flow the humoral fluid albuginea, and descend the eye and enter soon.
E aprop strenh entro que sia sanat.	And carefully strengthen until it is healed.
Capitol .xxii.	Chapter XXII.
De curacio de alconati.	On the Cure of Alcunati.
Aquesta malautia que es apelada alconati no es sino sania la qual es ajustada en le huel semblant a aygua dessendent e no es aquela.	This disease which is called alcunati is nothing but pus which is adjusted in the eye similar to water descending and it is not that.
Mays la manieyra del obrar en ela es que fasses le malaute sezer sobre la sela aparelada e dreyta, e aprop pren le cap sieu en las tuas mas de doas partz e mau aquel entro que veias la sania pervenir a las partidas dejos, e aprop sia siccada e no descenda, e sia ostat le lum, e·l malaute veia las causas ayssi cum vezia.	But the manner of working on it is that you make the patient sit over a prepared and straight seat, and carefully take their head in your hands from two parts and make them look until you see the pus coming to the outer parts, and carefully be dried and not descend, and stop the light, and the patient sees the causes just as they saw.
E si no descendra en jos, sapias que es aygua.	And if it does not descend below, you will know that it is water.
Mays si no es preparat le descendement a la sania am aquo que havem dit, lahoras fay le malaute sezer entre las tuas mas e aprop pren spatum subtil e fen am aquel sobre le pannicol cernent un petit deves la continuacio de la conjunctiva am la tunica cornea en la corona (entro al loc vuet), entro que sia fora-getada la sania.	But if the descent of the pus is not prepared with water as we have said, then you will make the patient sit between your hands and carefully take a subtle spatula and find that spot on the panniculus cerning a small part of the continuation of the conjunctiva with the corneal tunic in the crown (into the location that is seen), until the pus is forgotten.
Donc cum es fora-getada, lahoras tu distilla en le huel aygua cauda en la qual has mesclat mel o aygua en la qual ja has bulit fenugrec e mel.	Therefore when it is forgotten, then you will distill into the eye cold water in which you have mixed honey and water in which fenugreek and honey have been boiled.
E aprop sia curat am las autras causas entro que sia sanat.	And carefully be cured with other causes until it is healed.
Capitol .xxii.	Chapter XXIII.
De la curacio de la aygua descendent del huel.	On the Cure of the Water Descending from the Eye.
Ja havem dit las specias de la aygua en la divisio e qual conveneys a perforar am sermo declarant, lahoras aquel segon la sanetat.	We have already said the types of water in the division and which are suitable to be poured into a sermon declaring it, therefore you will do that according to health.
Lahoras cove que tu fassas sezer le malaute entre las tuas mas sobre un cayrat e lia le sieu huel sa, lu mot stringent.	Therefore you must make the patient sit between your hands on a carpet and bind their own eye tightly.
E aprop pausa prop de la palpebra del sieu huel la tua ma senestra, si le huel en le qual es l’aygua es le huel senestra; o am la tua ma dreyta, si le huel es le dextre.	And carefully place your left hand near the eyelid of their own eye, if the eye in which the water is located is the left one; or with your right hand, if it is the right one.
E aprop am la tua ma dextra pren almagda, si le huel es senestre; o am la tua ma senestra, si le huel es de dreyt.	And carefully take almond with your right hand if the eye is left; or with your left hand if it is right.
E aprop pausa la extremitat de almagda prop de la corona per la grossesa del ray en le album del huel de part del mendre lacrimal, e aprop enpelleys almagda am vertut e revol la tua ma am aquel.	And carefully place the tip of the almond close to the crown by the thickness of the ray in the album of the eye from the smaller lacrimal part, and carefully anoint the almond with virtue and rotate your hand with it.
E aprop penetre en le album del huel e sentas que almagda ja es pervenguda a causa vueda.	And carefully penetrate into the album of the eye and feel that the almond has already reached the visible cause.
E cove que sia la masura del cami de almagda al preon la mesura del spazi le qual es de la pupilla entro a la fi de la negror, e es la corona del huel; quar tu veyras am aquel pupilla am la visio de l’huel per la clartat de la tunica cornea.	And carefully measure the path of the almond to the point where it measures the space which is from the pupil to the end of the darkness, and it is the crown of the eye; because you will see with that pupil through the vision of the eye by the clarity of the corneal tunic.
E aprop pausa almagda entro al loc en le qual es l’aygua, e aprop tu la atira en jos una veguada aprop autra, e donc si la aygua descen tantost, lahoras vetz le malaute aquo sobre le qual huebre la sua vista tantost, e almagda en le sieu huel.	And carefully place the almond into the location where the water is, and carefully bring it down once or twice, and therefore if the water descends soon, then you will see the patient's eyesight improved over that which they previously had, and the almond in their own eye.
E aprop repausa se un pauc; donc si la aygua es descenduda, lahoras tu depausa aquela autre veguada abantz que almagda ne sia getada.	And carefully pause for a moment; therefore if the water has descended, then you will pause that other time before the almond is released.
E donc quan es sicada e no descen, lahoras tu extrat almagda am facilitat, e revol am aquel la tua ma pauc a pauc, e aprop dissolveys en l’aygua un petit de sal clara de gemma e am aquela lava le huel dedintz; e aprop pausa fora le huel coto o stopa o lana infusa en oli rozat e album de huou e ligua am aquo le huel sa.	And therefore when it is dried and does not descend, then you will carefully extract the almond with ease, and slowly rotate your hand with it, and carefully dissolve a small amount of clear gemstone salt in that water, and wash the eye outward; and carefully pause outside the eye cut or stoppered or lanolin infused in rose oil and egg white, and bind with water the patient's own eye.
Mays nos e aquels que so de nostre temps pause sobre aquel comi trissat am album de huou.	But we are those of our time who pause over that which is triflingly mixed with egg white.
E si no obezeys a tu almagda al intrament de l’huel per la sua duricia — quar es alcu dels homes del qual le huel es dur mot —, lahoras cove que prenguas le spatum le qual es nompnat alberid del qual aquesta es la forma:	And if it does not obey your almond at the entrance of the eye due to its hardness - for it is one of the men whose eye is very hard -, then you must take the spatula which is called "alberid" and has this form:
E donc perfora am aquel aquela conjunctura, e no ultimes la tua ma en le trauc, e no es si no que fassas via ad almagda loc subtil.	And therefore pierce through with that spatula the conjuncture, and do not leave your hand in the hole, and it is only if you make a way for the almond to reach its subtle location.
E aprop entromet almagda segon que havem dit.	And carefully introduce the almond according to what we have said.
E deves le compliment de la tua obra, sia preparat al malaute dormitori descentment fayt en le qual dorma sobre le sieu dos en mayson tenebrosa, e sia prohibit de totz movementz .	And you must complete your work, and be prepared for the patient's sleep, a gentle descent made in the location where they will lie on their back in a dark room, and it is prohibited from all movements.
E pausa en la natura de lu aquo per que sia linida la sua natura, e no maugua le sieu cap a la partida dreyta ni senestra de tot.	And pause in the nature of that water so that its nature may be aligned, and not move their head to either side at all.
E sia le liament segon la sua disposicio entro al tertz dia.	And let the ligature remain according to its disposition for three days.
E aprop deslia aquel en aquela maysso tenebrosa e exproha la freol vista, e fay li vezer alcunas causas, e aprop retorna le liament entro al dia .vii.	And carefully remove that in a more dark and obscure manner, and expose the hidden vision, and make them see some causes, and then return to the ligature on the seventh day.
E no cove que fassas aquo en la hora de las curacios o tantost aprop la infusio.	And it is not necessary to do this at the time of the remedies or soon after the infusion.
Habantz cove que tu alienes aquo per so quar la aygua puega leugierament per gran e vehement de reguardament.	They had need that you would allay this by reason that the water flows more slowly through great and vehement observation.
Mays si accideys apostema caut, lahoras cove que deslias le huel denant le vii dia, e rectifica aquel am aquo que ceda apostema.	But if an apostema occurs, then you must remove the eye before the seventh day, and correct that with water which brings forth the apostema.
Lahoras tu absol la vista de lu e pausa sobre la cara de lu oral per le qual sia regit le vezement de lu dejos lu per alcus dias, lu existent en la mayszo tenebrosa.	Therefore you must absolve the vision of him and pause over his face, as if he were being governed by something dark for some days, existing in the most obscure.
E aprop sia gitat de aquela mayzo gradantment e conversa8 en las suas causas.	And carefully be taken away from that great darkness gradually and converted into its causes.
E sapias que in alchatea no es excusat le discipol de visio alcunas veguadas, e lahoras tu sias ardit sobre la operacio.	And know that in some cases, the disciple is not exempt from vision a few times, and therefore you should be bold in your operation.
E ja es pervengut a nos de alcu de aquels les quals so al Artach , e alcu disse que fayt foc en al Ayrac magdaam perforat am le qual es succada la aygua.	And it has already been achieved by some of those who are in Atach, and someone said that made a fire in the Ayrac, a great perforation at which the water was sucked.
Mays empero yeu non e vist degu en la nostra terra le qual haia perfeyt aquo, ni e aquo legit en alcu dels libres dels antics; e es possible que aquo sia novel.	But however, you do not see this done in our land, which has perfected this water, nor do you read about it in some of the ancient books; and it is possible that this is new.
E aquestas so las formas de las specias de magdaan per que sia sobre aquelas aquel le qual ignora aquelas:	And these are the forms of the species of magdans by which one can be above those who ignore these:
E sian faytas de eram o de ferr propriament, e sian las extramitatz de lor am aquesta subtilitat triangulada, la extremitat aguda ayssi cum aquela es la forma.	And they were made of iron or bronze properly, and they had the extreme points of their own shape and this subtlety triangularly, the sharp point just as it is the form.
Capitol .xxiv.	Chapter XXIV.
De la curacio de carn nada en le nas.	On the Cure of Carnage in the Nose.
Quan en le nas so nascudas carns diversas ajustadas de las quals es alcuna causa la qual es assemblada a scorpio de motz pes, o a polip peys; e aquesta malautia es apelada polipus quar es a semblansa de aquel peys representat.	When in the nose there are born various skins which are adjusted to some cause which is assembled to the tail of a scorpion or a polygamous pes; and this disease is called polypus because it resembles that represented by the shape of those pes.
E de lu es carn cancrosa, lapadea, de fusca color; e de lu es que es carn leon no de color fusca.	And from it comes a cancerous flesh, blackened and of dark color; and from it also comes the flesh of a lion, not of dark color.
Donc en aquela que es en aquestas carns leon no fraudulenta ni cancroza, cove que fassas le malaute sezer entre las tuas mas e posat al solelh, e huebre las nars de lu, e picoys le tieu onci en aquelas carns.	Therefore in that which is in these lion-like skins that are not fraudulent or cancerous, you must make the patient sit between your hands and place them in the sun, and anoint their nose with it, and pierce once into those skins.
E aprop extrat aquela a las partidas deforo, e aprop inscindeys aquo que has comprehendut de aquelas am spatum agut subtil de la una partida entro que sapias que tota la carn ja es ostada; que si roman de lu deguna causa de la qual la abscisio es possibla, lahoras tu ratz aquo am la un dels estrumentz subtils am facilitat entro que de lu romangua denguna causa.	And carefully extract that from the outer parts, and carefully incise into it with a sharp and subtle spatula from one side until you know that all the flesh has been removed; if there remains any cause by which ablation is possible, then you must ratify this with one of the subtle instruments with ease so that no cause remains in him.
Mays si senhoreja am sanc o accida apostema caut, lahoras tu pausa a lu aquo que cove; o es dels apostemas malignes, lahoras tu coyta e cauteriza aquel entro que sia abscindit sanc e sian ostadas las cavas totas.	But if it bleeds or an apostema occurs cautiously, then you must pause in that which is necessary; or if it is one of the malignant apostemas, then you must cut and cauterize that until the blood is stopped and all the cavities are removed.
E aprop sia getatz en le nas aprop la inscizio vi agre e aygua o vi.	And carefully be taken away from the nose, carefully by the incision, with water or vinegar.
Mays si le nas es ubert e de lu procezeys humiditat entro al palat, lahoras sapias que ja es sanat.	But if the nose is dry and from it proceeds humidity into the palate, then you must know that it is already healed.
Mays si la humiditat no penetra segon que cove, lahoras tu sapias que dedintz lu es carn nada en los pus sobiras osses de las nars als quals non es pervengut abscizio.	But if the humidity does not penetrate according to what is necessary, then you must know that behind it there is flesh growing in the pustules of the nose, which are above the bones and have not been removed by ablation.
Donc lahoras cove que entromitas fiel de li al qual sia alcuna grosseza, e nuza en lu motz nuzes, e pausa entre quascun nutz la quantitat del dit o mens, e engene le malaute e entromet una extremitat del fiel en le nars am lo ray o am autra causa la qual es a lu possibla.	Therefore it is necessary that you enter faithfully into the one who has some grossness, and annoy him in his own words, and pause between each phrase the quantity of the said or less, and generate the patient and enter one extremity of the thread into the nose with the ray or other cause which is possible to him.
E pus que aquo aura fayt, que atire le sieu odorament entro que pervengua a las canals de las nars, e sia eyssit sobre le sieu golayro, quar tropas veguadas le semblant ad aquesta accio fan les enfantz a las scolas, e es leugiera causa ad aquel que ho vol far.	And since this will have been done, that he will draw his own odor into being so that it will reach the canals of the nose and be seated on his golayro, for many times children are taught at school to do this, and it is a light cause for one who wishes to do so.
E aprop pausa las dos extramitatz del fiel, una extremitat que iesca sobre le nas et l’autra que romangua en le nas, e aprop aministra serratura de carn am les nuzes que so en le fiel, e fay aquo entro que sapias que las carn ja so am les nuzes del fiel.	And carefully pause the two extremities of the thread, one extremity that will come out over the nose and the other that will remain in the nose, and carefully administer a serration of flesh with the threads that are in the thread, and do this until you know that the flesh is already threaded.
E aprop extratz le fiel, e pausa en le nas aprop la abstraccio del sanc una calgua , e fay aquo per tres dias o mays entro que l’enguent corrodo tot aquo que es romas de las carns.	And carefully extract the thread, and pause in the nose about an inch from the abstraction of the blood a quarter of an inch, and do this for three days or more until the engendered flesh is completely consumed all that remains of the flesh.
E aprop en la fi de la causa, pausa en le nas una canula de plom per alscus jorns entro que sia sanat.	And carefully pause in the nose at the end of the cause, with a leaden cannula for several days until it is healed.
Mays si endigeys de curacio que exsique, usa de aquela.	But if you need further cure that exists, use this one.
E aquesta es la forma del instrument a capipurge fazedor am le qual son distillatz olis e medicinas en le nars:	And this is the form of the instrument, the capipurge maker, with which oils and medicines are distilled in the nose:
E fay aquo de argent o de eram, la qual sia semblant a una petita lampesa uberta, ayssi cum petita conqua, e le meat semblantment.	And make this of silver or bronze, which is similar to a small opened lamp, just like a small shell, and the mouth similarly.
E si vols, fay una canula clausa ayssi cum cana, e la cancula del estrument a capipurge fazedor e sia plana, descuberta; a la qual sia manubre en lo derier de lu, am le qual tenguas aquela quan escaufas en lu oli o aquo que tu vols dels sucs e de las causas suctiblas.	And if you wish, make a closed cannula like a reed, and the cannula of the instrument, the capipurge maker, be flat and uncovered; to which is attached at the end, with which you will hold it when you squeeze out in oil or water whatever juice or causes are suitable.
E aquestz capipurgi es precios: recipe de enforbi de castor, de balayra blanc, de giengiebre, e piletre de safra, de pebre lonc, de escafragia, de epetum de spic ana unc. vi cumfizeys am suc de bleda e de caul, e sian faytas pillulas, e sia destemprada una pillula am aygua tebeza, e sia gitat en las nars del malaute jasent envers.	And these capipurges are precious: a recipe of castoreum from the beaver, of white bayberry, of ginger, and saffron of piling pepper, of long pepper, of escarole, of epetimium, of spice anise one. And you will combine with the juice of bleda and of caul, and make pills, and one pill be tempered with water of Thebes, and be given to the patient's nose as they sit facing.
Capitol .xxv.	Chapter XXV.
De theyls natz en las extramitatz del nas.	On the Natures of Warts in the Extremities of the Nose.
Motas veguadas es nat theyl en las extramitatz del nas, e es magnificat e omentat en alscus dias entro en que mot es leg le reguardament de lu.	Many times is born a warty growth on the extremities of the nose, and it is magnified and increased in some days until one can see the regard of it.
E per aquo cove que tu inscidas aquel en le comensament de la apparissio de lu, e erediques tot aquel.	And therefore you must incise that in the beginning of its appearance, and root out all of it.
E aprop pausa sobre le loc o cauteri o medicina comburent la qual estia en loc de lu.	And carefully pause over the spot or cauterize or medicine which is present in that place.
Mays si es tardada la sua inscizio entro que sia magnificat, lahoras considera si es lapificat, dur, de fusca color e de pauc sentiment, lahoras no toques aquel am ferr quar es apostema crancos; quar motas veguadas ad aquel que inscideys aquesta apostema endeve per lu granda malicia sobre aquel le qual aquel havia.	But if it is delayed in its incision, so that it becomes magnified, then you must consider whether it is hardened, dark-colored and lacking sensation; then do not touch it with iron because it is a cancerous apostema; for many times the one who incises this apostema will develop great malice towards him whom it had affected.
E si le apostema es de leon tocament e no es de fosca color, e vezes que inscizio es possibla en tot aquel, lahoras evacua le malaute e inscideys aquel senes temor, e cura le loc am aquo que exsique e costrenh entro que sia sanat.	And if the apostema is of a lion-like touch and not dark-colored, and sometimes incision is possible in all that, then you must evacuate the patient and incise that without fear, and cure the spot with what exists and constrains until it is healed.
Capitol .xxvi.	Chapter XXVI.
De sutura del nas e de las labias e de la aurelha quan la continuitat es dissolvuda per plagua o per semblantz.	On the Suturing of the Nose and Lips and Ears when Continuity is Dissolved by Plague or Similarities.
Sapias que quan accideys solucio de continuitat en una de aquestas cartillages, pauc confereys en aquela operacio sino en alcus homes.	Know that when dissolution of continuity occurs in one of these cartilages, few confer in that operation except with some men.
Donc cove, quan endeve ad alcu alcuna causa de aquelas, que consideres si es plagua fresca am le sieu sanc, e lahoras tu ajusta las doas labias de la plagua am sutura, e aprop cura aquel entro que sia sanat.	Therefore, when you need to deal with some cause of those, consider whether it is fresh plague with the patient's blood, and then you must adjust the two lips of the wound with sutures, and carefully cure that until it is healed.
E si las labias de solucio de continuitat so ja separadas, e quascuna es fayta sana, lahoras cove que tu excorjes quascuna partida de la sua codena apparent entro que n’iesca sanc.	And if the lips of dissolution of continuity are already separated, and each is made whole, then you must carefully excise each part of its visible cord until blood comes out.
E aprop ajusta las doas labias am sutura e strenh aquelas, e sobre aquelas pulveriza sanc de drago e enses trissat, e pausa sobre la polvera una pessa de emplaustra diafinicon, o de alcu autre dels emplastres consolidatius, e leyssa aquel liat per dos jorns o per tres, e aprop deslia aquel e permuta aquel emplaustre e leyssa aquel entro que·ls fiels per si sian abscinditz, e aprop cura am enguent entro que sia sanat.	And carefully adjust the two lips with sutures and strengthen those, and over those sprinkle blood of dragon and thrice-trissed, and pause over the powder one day, or some other consolidative plaster, and bind that wrapped for two days or three, and carefully remove that and replace it with another plaster and bind that until the faithful ones are ablated, and carefully cure with engenderment until it is healed.
Mays la manieyra de la sutura es que tu agregues la solucio de continuitat o am agulhas ayssi cum havem recomtat en la sutura del ventre, o agregua la solucio de continuitat am fiel ayssi cum a tu e fayt saber.	But the manner of suturing is that you add the solution of continuity or with needles just as we have recounted in the suturing of the belly, or add the solution of continuity with thread just as to your own and make it known.
Capitol .xxvii.	Chapter XXVII.
De extraccio de aquela causas que veno en las doas labias en las partidas dedintz.	On the Extraction of those Causes that come in the two lips in the parts behind.
Motas veguadas endeve a motz homes en las partidas dedintz de las suas labias alcus apostemas durs semblantz a gras de errs, e alscunas de lors son mendres e alcunas son majors.	Many times it happens that some men in the parts behind their lips have certain hard and similar-looking apostemas resembling errors, and some of theirs are smaller and some are greater.
Donc cove que tu convertas las labias e fendas quascuna de aquelas duricias de tota part, e aprop la abscizio umpliscas le loc de sagi trissat entro que·l sanc sia restrengut, e aprop sia lavat am vi agre e sia curat le loc am aquo que es stipticitat, entro que sia sanat.	Therefore, you must convert the lips and fissures each of those hardness from all part, and carefully fill the wound with sagacious triple thread until the blood is restrained, and carefully wash it with vinegar and cure the wound with water that is stipticized, until it is healed.
Capitol .xxviii.	Chapter XXVIII.
De inscizio de la carn ajustada en las gengivas.	On the Incision of the Flesh Adjusted in the Gums.
Granre de veguadas nays sobre la gengiva carn ajustada la qual les antics apelero albulus, adonc cove que tu suspendas aquela am onci o que tenguas aquela am las forfecs e inscidas aquela deves la sua razit, e leyssas la sania correr o le sanc.	Great many times, nay, over the gummed flesh which the ancients called albulus, then it is necessary that you suspend that with once or that you hold that with the forceps and incise that as the reason requires, and let the wound bleed or run with blood.
E aprop pausa sobre le loc sagi trissat o autra polveras stipticas o excicativas.	And carefully pause over the spot with sagacious triple thread or other powders stipticized or excitatory.
E si aquela carn retorna, lahoras inscideys aquela segundariament, e cauterisa aquela, quar aprop le cauteri no retornara.	And if that flesh returns, then you must incise it secondarily and cauterize it, for the cautery will not return.
Capitol .xxix.	Chapter XXIX.
De razo de dentz am ferr.	On the Reason of Teeth with Iron.
Quan en la superficia de las dentz de las partidas dedintz e de las de foro e entre las gingivas so ajustadas escorsas aspras, legas, e alcunas veguadas son de nigradas e son faytas citrinas o vertz entro que a la gingiva ve per aquo corrupcio e son faytas las dentz legas.	When in the surface of the teeth on the sides and fore and between the gums are adjusted rough, sharp, and some blackened, and are made citrines or greenish until they can be seen through the gum because of corruption, and are made the teeth rough.
E donc cove que tu fassas sezer le malaute entre las tuas mas e pausar le cap de lu en le tieu se, e ratz las dents en las quals apareysso aquelas escorsas e causas semblantz arena entro que de lor no romangua deguna causa, e aquo fay de la negror e de la citrinitat e de las autras entro que sian mondificadas.	And therefore it is necessary that you make the patient sit between your hands and pause the top of him in your seat, and remove the teeth in which those roughnesses and causes like sand appear until there remains no cause in them, and this will be done with the blackness and citrinity and the others until they are purified.
Donc si es ostat aquo que es en aquelas del comensament de la razio, bo es; e sino, lahoras tu itera la razio sobre aquelas al autra dia e al segon e al tertz entro que vengua al derier stament en aquo que tu vols.	Therefore, if this is the case that is in those of the beginning of the reason, good it is; and otherwise, then you must iterate the reason over those for another day, and second, and third until it comes to the last statement as you wish.
E sapias que las dentz han necessitat de motz rezoris de diversas formas e de motas figuras segon que es preparat a la tua operacio.	And know that teeth have need of many resins of diverse forms and figures according to the preparation for your operation.
E per so quar le razori am le qual la dent es raza de la partida dedintz es autre del razori am le qual es ras entre las dentz segon autras formas, e aquestas formas de razoris sian deves tu preparadas las quals veyras tantost:	And for this reason, the resins with which the tooth is prepared in the part behind are another of the resins with which it is rasped between teeth according to other forms, and these forms of resins must be prepared by you which you will see shortly:
Capitol .xxx.	Chapter XXX.
D’eradicacio de dentz.	On the Extraction of Teeth.
Cove que tu cures la dent de la sua dolor am tot engen e tardes en tota eradicacio de lu, quar no es denguna causa que suplisqua la veguada de lu quan es eradicada, quar es sustancia sublima entro que es excusacio en la eradicacio de lu.	Carefully that you cure the tooth of its pain with all diligence and patience in total extraction from it, for there is no cause that supplies its vigor when it is extracted, for it is subtle substance entering into excuse in the extraction of it.
Mays cove quan le malaute es forsat aquela dent eradicar, que fermament deves tu sia certificat quala es la dent dolent, quar motas veguadas la dolor descep le malaute e cuga que sia en dent sana, e tu eradicas aquela e aprop la dolor no cessa entro que la dent malauta e dolent sia eradicada, quar nos ja havem vist aquo per operacio dels barbies.	But it is necessary when the patient is forced to extract that tooth, that you firmly certify which is the aching tooth, for many times the pain deceives the patient and takes it to be in a healthy tooth, and you remove that one and carefully pause the pain until the diseased and aching tooth is extracted, for we have already seen this by the operation of barbers.
Donc cum deves tu es sertificat qual es la dent dolent, e que o sabes be, lahoras cove que tu scarifiques en le circuit de la dent am spatum en le qual sia alcuna vertut, entro que sia dissolvut de la dent de la gingiva de tota partida, e aprop mau aquel am les tieus ditz, o am forfexs subtils al comensament petit a petit entro que aquela concucesquas.	Therefore, since you must certify which is the aching tooth, and you know well, then it is necessary that you scarify in the circuit of the tooth with a spatula in which there is some virtue, until it is dissolved from the tooth and the gum from all part, and carefully remove that with your own words, or with fine forceps little by little until it is concluded.
E aprop alogua en lu fortz tenalhas grans per bona loquacio o estuptura fort, e pausa le cap del malaute entre les tieus denolhs que be le tengues que no·s maugua, e aprop tratz la dent segon rectitut en manieyra que no trenques aquela, ni al malaute major dolor no dones.	And carefully hold in it the strong forceps for good speaking or sudden fort, and pause the head of the patient between your fingers which you will hold so that they do not become annoyed, and carefully grasp the tooth according to rectitude in a manner that does not break it, nor gives greater pain to the patient.
E donc si no es foro-getat, lahoras pren un de aquels instrumentz, e met aquel dejos lu de tota part am facilitat e esforsa la remocio de lu ayssi que es feyt al comensament.	And therefore, if it is not forgotten, then take one of those instruments and place that below the tooth from all parts with facility and effort to remove it as it was done at the beginning.
Mays si la dent es trauquada o corrosa, lahoras cove que tu comples de drap aquel trauc e estrenguas aquel am la extremitat de ray subtil per so que no sia trinquada en la hora de la tua constriccio sobre aquela am tenalas.	But if the tooth is torn or corroded, then it is necessary that you wrap that tear with cloth and strengthen it at the subtle edge of a ray so that it will not be torn in the hour of your constriction over it while holding.
E cove que tu obres exquesitament am scarificacio en le circuit de tota part de la gingiva e guarda mot la tua fortaleza que no trenques aquela e romangua partida de lu, e retorne sobre le malaute per la malicia que sia majo que la primieyra dolor de lu.	And it is necessary that you work with great skill with scarification in the circuit of all part of the gum and guard your strength so as not to break it and leave a part of it, and return upon the patient for the malice that may be greater than the first pain of it.
E guarda te que no fassas aquo que fan alscus ignorantz barbiers en lor fistinacio e audacia sobre la eradicacio de lor, ses que no aministran aquo que nos havem recomtat; quar motas veguadas fan venir sobre les homes malautias grans las quals son pus dificils que sian trinquadas, e las razitz de lor remaugudas totas, o alcunas de aquelas, o que extrayguas aquela am alcus osses de la mandigula ayssi cum motas veguadas havem testificat.	And beware that you do not act as some ignorant barbers do in their haste and audacity towards the extraction of theirs, without administering what we have recommended; for many times they bring upon men great illnesses which are more difficult to be torn out, and their roots become all inflamed, or some of those, or that you extract it with some bones of the jawbone just as many times we have testified.
E aprop la eradicacio de lu sia lavada la boca am vi caut o vi agre am sal.	And carefully wash the mouth with vinegar or sour apple with salt after the extraction is done.
E si endeve fluxs de sanc per aysso, ayssi cum motas veguadas endeve, lahoras trissa alcuna quantitat de zegi e aspergeys sobre la plagua, e si no confereys aquel zegi, cauteriza.	And if it is necessary to stop the bleeding with this, just as many times it has been, then carefully squeeze out some quantity of egg white and sprinkle it over the wound, and if that egg white does not suffice, cauterize.
La forma de las forceps e tenalas subtils am las quals es mauguda la dent al comensament sia de longua extramitat, de breu manubre e gros, per so que no sian doblatz quan am aquels deves obrar.	The form of the forceps and fine tweezers with which the tooth is grasped at the beginning should be of long extra tip, short handle and thick, in order that they are not bent when you must work with them.
E sian ayssi cum vezes de gros manubre entro que quan estrenhas am aquelas no sian dobladas, sian breus extramitatz.	And should be like times of thick handle so that when you grasp with those they are not bent, with short extra tips.
E sian faytas de ferr de India descentment faytas de dreytas extramitatz, e en las extramitatz de aquelas sian dentz de las quals las unas intron en las autras e estrenhan per constriccio descent fort, e alscunas veguadas las extramitatz de aquelas sian la forma del bec d’un auzel le qual ha nom ciconia, so es guanta, e son de fort constriccio.	And should be made of Indian steel with descending tips and right-angled extra tips, and on the extra tips of those should be teeth which some intrude into others and strain by strong constriction, and sometimes the extra tips of those are in the shape of a bird's beak which has no name, it is called ciconia, so that they are guarded and have strong constriction.
Capitol .xxxi.	Chapter XXXI.
De erradicacio de dentz e d‘estraccio dels osses de las mandibulas trincadas.	On the Extraction of Teeth and Removal of the Bones of the Mandibles Broken.
Quan deves la eradicacio de dent le qual es trinquat roman alcuna causa, lahoras cove que tu pauses sobre le loc coto am boder per un jorn o per dos entro que·l loc sia mollificat; e aprop entromet algesti o tenalhas las extramitatz de las quals so asembladas al bec de un auzel apelat ciconia o guanta, la forma de las forceps:	When you must extract a tooth which is broken with some cause, then it is necessary that you pause over the spot cut off with a border for one day or two until the spot is softened; and carefully introduce or grasp the extra tips of those which are assembled to the beak of a bird called ciconia or guanta, the form of the forceps:
Las extramitatz de lor sian faytas dedintz ayssi cum lima o alfagi.	Their extra tips are made behind like lime or almond.
E si no obediys a tu a eyssiment am aquestas forceps o tenalas, lahoras cove que tu caves sobre la razit e descrobas tota la carn e entrometas le instrument le qual ha nom atali, so es palanca petita del qual la forma es aquesta:	And if you do not obey your own eye with these forceps or tweezers, then it is necessary that you cut away the root and uncover all the flesh and introduce the instrument which has no name, but is a small lever whose form is this:
E sia de breu extremitat grossa un petit, e no sia enbegut per so que no sia trinquat.	And it should be of short extra tip thick and small, and not be encumbered so that it will not break.
Donc si per aquo la razit es foro-getada, bo es; e sino, ajuda te am aquestz autres instrument dels quals aquestas son las formas: la forma del primier instrument es de triangulada extramitat en la qual sia alcuna grossesa:	Therefore, if by this the root is forgotten, good it is; and otherwise, help yourself with these other instruments of which these are the forms: the form of the first instrument is a triangular extra tip in which there should be some thickness:
La forma del segon instrument es que sia de triangulada e de pus subtil extremitat.	The form of the second instrument is that it should be triangular and with a more subtle extra tip.
E ja so ajudatz am aquest instrument havent dos ramps del qual aquesta es la forma aprop la seguent:	And now help yourself with this instrument having two rams of which this is the form, approximately as follows:
e am autres instrumentz les quals precidero en rasura de dentz; quar juvament es fayt am aquest instrument le qual es asemblat a onci gran, e aquesta es la forma:	and with other instruments which precede in the removal of teeth; for shortly after it is made with this instrument which is assembled to great force, and this is the form:
de la triangulada extremitat torta o curta, la qual sia alcuna grossesa, e no sia enbegut per so que no sia trinquat.	of a triangular extra tip bent or short, which should have some thickness, and not be encumbered so that it will not break.
E otra sapias que·ls instrumentz de las dentz motz so e semblantment les autres instruments.	And know that the instruments of teeth many are so and similarly to other instruments.
Mays le artifexs savi e subtil en l’art, atroba per si mateys segon aquo que a lu significa la operacio e las malautias diversas; quar son de las malautias a las quals les antics no diysero ni pausero propri instrument, per las formas de diversas specias.	But the skilled craftsmen and subtle in their art, find for themselves according to this what the operation means and various diseases; for there are diseases which the ancients did not know nor pause over with proper instruments, due to the forms of diverse species.
Mays si es trinquat l’os de la mandibula o dels autres osses de la boca, o si poyreys, lahoras sia pes curat sobre aquel en son loc am aquo que es a lu convenient dels instrumentz e de las forceps las quals havem dit en la extraccio de las razitz de las dentz, e ajuda te am gesti del qual aquesta es la forma:	But if the bone of the mandible or of other bones in the mouth is broken or splintered, then it is necessary to carefully place a plaster cast on that spot in its location where it is convenient for the instruments and forceps which we have mentioned in the extraction of tooth roots, and help yourself with gestures of which this is the form:
E sia en lu alcuna grosseza petit a petit, e sia instringida o tenguda am la boca per que no evasesca o fuga entro que l’os de tot sia foro-getat; e aprop restaura le loc am medicinas convenientz ad aquo.	And it should be in some thickness small by small, and wrapped or held in the mouth so that it does not escape or flee until the bone of all is forgotten; and carefully restore the place with medicines suitable for this.
Mays si en l’os es petita poyredura, lahoras ratz aquel de aquela poyredura e de la sua negror, e cura aquel entro que sia sanat.	But if there is a small splinter in the bone, then carefully remove that from that splinter and its blackness, and cure it until it is healed.
Capitol .xxxii.	Chapter XXXII.
De la cura de las dentz eminentz sobre las autras.	On the Cure of Teeth Elevated above Others.
Quan las dentz so eminentz no segon lor cors natural per aquelas la forma es laga, e majorment quan endeve a las femnas, e majorment a las piuselas venerablas; donc cove que tu consideras: si dent es nada aprop autra dent, e no es possibla sarradura ni linament de lu, lahoras radica aquela; mays que no sia annexa am autra dent, lahoras tu inscideys aquela am aquest instrument del qual aquesta es la forma; e es semblant a morr de porc, e sia feyt de ferr de India de extramitat mot aguda.	When teeth are elevated above their natural form and shape is lost, and especially when they need to be removed from women and even more so from venerable old ladies; therefore it is necessary that you consider: if a tooth is not properly attached to another tooth, and it is not possible to secure or bind it with anything, then carefully remove it; but if it is attached to another tooth, then you must incise it with this instrument which has the following form; it resembles a pig's jawbone, and is made of Indian steel with an extremely sharp extra tip.
E sia la tua inscizio am la qual inscideyses aquela en trops dias per la duricia de la dent, e que no sia comauguda autra de las dentz.	And your incision should be made with the instrument in which you will incise that tooth over many days due to the hardness of the tooth, and so that it is not confounded with another tooth.
E si es dent eminent expausat a limadura, lahoras lima aquel am lima de ferr de India del qual aquesta es la forma:	And if the elevated tooth is exposed to decay, then carefully remove that with a file of Indian steel which has this form:
E sia tot de ferr de India e·l margua eysament; e sia de motz menutz puntz ayssi cum lima am la qual son faytas agulhas, am la qual la dent sia limada pauc a pauc en motz dias am fecilitat, per so que no sia autra dent comauguda e caga.	And it should be entirely of Indian steel and the margin very sharp; and it should have many small points just like a file with which needles are made, with which the tooth is filed little by little over many days with ease, so that no other tooth becomes confounded and decayed.
E aprop lineys aquela en la fi, e ratz aquela am alscus razoris.	And carefully file that in the end, and remove it with some rasors.
E si es dent del qual una partida es trinquada e lideys la lengua, lahoras cove que tu limescas aquel entro que l’aspretat de aquela fraccio sia ostada e engualhada, e sia aplenada per so que la lengua no ledesca ni la paraula no corrumpa.	And if it is a tooth whose part is broken and irritates the tongue, then it is necessary that you file away that portion until the sharpness of that fracture is removed and smoothed out, and be filled so that the tongue does not become irritated nor the word corrupted.
Capitol .xxxiii.	Chapter XXXIII.
De restauracio de dentz maugudas am fiel de aur o de argent.	On the Restoration of Damaged Teeth with Gold or Silver Filling.
Quan accideys a las dentz devant concussio e remossio per percussio o per cazament, e le malaute no pot strenher sobre aquo que manga, e tu has curat aquel am medicinas stipticas, e no ha valgut la tua curacio, lahoras per so que no cagan es engen en aquelas que sian strengudas am fiel de aur e no de argent, quar argent se fa vert e aprop se poyreys aprop alscus dias, mays aur nul temps no es mudat.	When accidents occur to teeth before concussion and removal by percussion or collapse, and the patient cannot sustain on what they have, and you have treated that with stiptic medicines, and your treatment has not been effective, then for this reason it is necessary to fill those which are strong with gold and not silver, because silver becomes green and soon turns black, but gold never changes.
E sia le fiel en tal subtilitat e grocesa segon la quantitat que puesca entrar entre las dentz; e la forma de la reccio es que prenguas le fiel e pren lo doble de lu entre doas dentz sanas, e aprop que cresques am doas tortuositatz del fiel entre doas maugudas, o si’ una o motas, entro que pervengua la tela a la dent sana del autra partida.	And the filling should be in such subtlety and thickness according to the quantity that can enter between the teeth; and the form of the recipe is that you take the filling and take twice as much of it between two healthy teeth, and carefully increase with two twists of the filling between two damaged ones, or if one or many, until the filling reaches the healthy tooth on the other side.
E aprop itera le teyssiment entro a la partida de la qual comenciest, e strenh la tua ma am facilitat e savieza entro que no sia mauguda.	And carefully repeat the process into the part from which you began, and strengthen your hand with facility and wisdom until it is not damaged.
E sia la tua striccio am la qual strenhas le fiel deves las razitz de las dentz que no evasesca.	And carefully bind with the filling that you should strengthen the roots of the teeth so that they do not escape.
E aprop inscindeys las extramitatz del fiel superfluens am las forceps o tosoyras, e agregua aquelas en quascun loc am gesti, e converteys aquelas e las occulta entre la dent sana e la dent mauguda, per so que no fassa lesio a la lengua.	And carefully insert the extra tips of the filling with forceps or tweezers, and add those to each location by gesture, and convert them and hide them between the healthy tooth and the damaged one, so that they do not cause injury to the tongue.
E aprop leyssa aquela ayssi streyta cum roman.	And carefully leave it as straight as Roman.
Mays si es desliada o rumpuda, strenh aquela o aquelas am autra fiel en tal manieyra en tot son temps.	But if it is loosened or broken, then strengthen that or those with another filling in such a manner throughout its entire time.
E aquesta es la forma de las dentz e la figura de la rectacio de doas dentz sanas e de doas maugudas, ayssi cum vezes aquestas liadas:	And this is the form of teeth and the figure of the restoration of two healthy teeth and two damaged ones, just as these are linked:
E quan se fa que retorno una dent o doas aprop le cazement de quascuna en lors locs, e sian recrescutz ayssi cum havem recomtat, e que remauguan.	And when one returns or two return to their places, and are recreated just as we have described, and remain.
E no fa aquo sino bo artifexs e savi.	And only a skilled and knowledgeable craftsman can do this.
E alcunas veguadas es aptat alcuna causa dels osses de vaca, e es fayt de lor ayssi cum forma de dent, e es pausada en loc en le qual defayl la dent, e es strengit ayssi cum havem dit, e reman e serveys am aquel per lonc temps.	And sometimes it is suitable for some cause of cow bones, and it is made from them just like the form of a tooth, and it is placed in a location where the tooth falls out, and it is strengthened just as we have said, and remains and serves that one for a long time.
Capitol .xxxiv.	Chapter XXXIV.
De inscizio del liament le qual ve en la lengua e prohibeys loquela.	On the Incision of the Ligament Which Goes to the Tongue and Prohibits Speech.
Aquest liguament le qual ve dejos la lengua alcunas veguadas o es natural am le qual hom nays, o accidental e accideys per plagua la qual ja es consolidada.	This ligament which goes to the tongue sometimes or is natural in those who are born with it, or accidental and happens by chance due to a wound that has already consolidated.
E la operacio en lu es que huobres la boca del malaute, le sieu cap existent en le tieu se; e eleva la sieua lengua, e aprop inscideys aquel liament nervos segon la latitut entro que sia solvuda la lengua de la sua recencio.	And the operation on it is that you open the mouth of the patient, his existing head in your sight; and lift up his tongue, and carefully incise that ligament nerve according to its latitude until the tongue is freed from its recent stiffness.
Mays si en aquela es alcuna duricia o denodacio, e aquo es stat per consolidacio de plagua, lahoras tu gieta unci e scindeys aquel per la latitut entro que aias inscindit le liament e sia dissolvuda la nodacio.	But if in that area there is some hardness or nodulation, and this is due to the consolidation of the wound, then you should take a knife and carefully cut it along its latitude until you have divided the ligament and dissolved the nodulation.
E guarda te que no sia fayta fissura en le preon de la carn e que scindas aqui arceria e vengua flux de sanc.	And be careful that there is not a fissure made in the skin of the flesh, and that you do not cut too deeply and come out with blood.
E aprop sia lavat le vestigi de la inscisio am ayguaros o am vi agre o am aygua frega; e aprop pausa dejos la lengua licini; so es meca la qual tengua le malaute dejos la lengua en quascuna nuoyt per so que no sia consolidat autra veguada.	And carefully wash the vestige of the incision with warm water or vinegar or cold water, and carefully pause after leaving the tongue to relax; this is the way that the patient should leave the tongue relaxed each night so that it will not be consolidated again.
Mays si accideys flux de sanc, pausa sobre le loc vetriol trissat; mays si le sanc ventz, lahoras cauteriza le loc am cauteri lantiginos le qual conveneys ad aquo.	But if bleeding occurs, pause over the spot with a piece of lint; but if the blood flows, then carefully cauterize the spot with a caustic lotion that is suitable for this.
E aprop aquel cura am las autras causas entro que sia sanat.	And carefully cure it with other causes until it is healed.
Capitol .xxxv.	Chapter XXXV.
De extraccio de ranula dejos la lengua.	On the Extraction of Ranula below the Tongue.
Alcunas veguadas accideys dejos la lengua apostema asemblant a nomla petita prohibent la lengua de la sua operacio natural; e fort leu es magnificada entro que huempla la boca.	Sometimes, below the tongue, an abscess forms like a small swelling that prohibits the tongue from its natural operation; and very little it is magnified until it fills up the mouth.
E la operacio en lu es que huebras la boca del malaute sesent devant le solel e considera le apostema.	And the operation on it is that you open the patient's mouth and examine the abscess in front of the sun.
E si tu le vezes de fusca color o de negra, dur, al qual le malaute no atroba sentiment, lahoras no toques aquel quar es cranc.	And if it appears to be a dark or black, hard swelling that the patient does not feel, then do not touch it because it is cancerous.
E si es declinat a blancor, en le qual es humiditat, lahoras tu met le onci en lu, e inscideys aquel am spatum subtil, e inscindeys le de tota partida; e si sanc te ventz en la hora de la tua operacio, lahoras tu pausa desus zegi trissat, so es vetriol, entro que sia restreyt le sanc.	And if it appears to be declining towards whiteness, with moisture, then you should put a sponge into it, and carefully incise that part with a subtle spatula, and remove the entire swelling; and if blood flows during your operation, then pause above a piece of lint, so it is vetriol, until the bleeding stops.
E aprop retorna a la obra tua entro que lo haias trayt am compliment de lu, entro que sia lavat am vi agre e sal; e cura aquel am l’autra curacio ad aquo entro que sia sanat.	And carefully return to your work until you have completely treated it with the remedy, until it is washed with vinegar and salt; and cure that part with another treatment suitable for this, until it is healed.
Capitol .xxxvi.	Chapter XXXVI.
De extraccio de apostema de doas aurelhas e de aquel que es nada en le golayro e de las autras apostemas.	On the Extraction of Abscesses from both Ears and that which is nothing in the Gullet and other Abscesses.
Quan endeveno en le golayro godat, so son glandulas las quals son asembladas algodat, las quals accideysso deforas e son nompnadas doas aurelhas, las quals quan tu las curas am aquo que havem dit en la divisio e no es sanat, lahoras tu considera si le apostema es dur, de fusca color, de pauc sentiment, lahoras no toques aquel am ferr.	When it occurs in the Gullet, so are the glands which are assembled together, those which protrude outside and are called two Ears, those which when you treat them with what we have said in the division and they do not heal, then you should consider if the abscess is hard, dark-colored, without sensation, then do not touch it with iron.
E si es de roga color e la razic es grossa, lahoras no toques aquela am ferr per le flux del sanc; abantz layssa aquel entro sia madurat, e lahoras o tu trauqueras aquel, o sira romput per si.	And if it is of a red color and the root is thick, then do not touch it with iron for the flow of blood; before leaving it to ripen, and either you will remove it or break it off by yourself.
E si es de blanqua color, radon, e la razit de lu es subtil, lahoras aquel es que cove esser inscidit.	And if it is of a white color, smooth, and the root of it is subtle, then that which must be cut.
E la operacio en lu es que consideras, denant la tua operacio, si ja ha repausat le apostema de lu caut am repaus complit o si es deminuit am alcuna deminucio; e lahoras fay sezer le malaute denant le soleyl, e·l cap de lu sia en le tieu se, e huebre la boca de lu, e le servidor prenent entre las suas mas prema la lengua de lu dejos am instrument mot noble del qual aquesta es la forma:	And the operation on it is that you consider, before your operation, if the abscess has already settled down and has reached complete rest or if it has diminished with some diminution; and then have the patient sit in front of the sun, and his head in your sight, and open his mouth, and the servant takes between his hands the tongue of the patient below with an instrument very noble which has this form:
E sia fayt de argent o de aram, e sia subtil cum cotel.	And it is made of silver or iron, and is subtle like a knife.
Donc cum tu premes am aquel la lengua e es mostrat a tu la apostema, e catz sobre aquel le tieu vezement, lahoras pren onci e fica aquel en l’amenla, e tira aquel a las partidas defora tant quant podes.	Then as you grasp with that tongue and it is shown to you the abscess, and you gaze upon it with your own eyes, then take hold of it and place it in the amnion, and pull it out to the outside parts as much as you can.
Otra aquo que tiras alcuna causa de las tunicas, e aprop incideys aquela am instrument del qual aquesta es la forma:	Or another thing that pulls some cause of the tunics, and carefully cut with an instrument which has this form:
e es asemblat a forceps, empero las extramitatz de lu son corvadas, ayssi que l’orrifici de quascuna de aquelas es en le endreyt del autra, mot agudas, le qual sia de ferr indi enbegut.	and it is assembled like forceps, however the extra tips of it are curved, so that the orifice of each of those is in the end of the other, very sharp, which is made of Indian steel well embedded.
Mays si aquest instrument no es a tu present, lahoras inscideys aquel am spatum del qual aquesta es la forma de lu: E sia agut de la una part, no agut del autra part.	But if this instrument is not at your present, then carefully cut with a spatula which has this form of it: And it should be sharp on one side, not sharp on the other side.
E pus que has inscidit una mella, inscideys l’autra segon aquesta meteyssa manieyra de inscizio, e aprop la inscizio le malaute guarguarise de aygua frega	And after you have cut one notch, carefully cut the other in the same manner of cutting, and then have the patient gargle with cold water.
Mays si endeve flux de sanc, guarguarise aygua de decoccio de scorsa de milgrana o de fuelha de mirtra e semblantz ad aquel de las causas stiptiquas entro que·l flux del sanc sia restreyt, e aprop cura aquel entro que sia sanat.	But if bleeding occurs, gargle with decoction of scorsa of milgrana or of myrtle leaves and similar to those of the causes stiptic until the flow of blood is stopped, and then carefully cure that part until it is healed.
E alcunas veguadas naysso en le guolayro autras apostemas otra aquelas doas aurelhas, e inscideys aquelas segon que yeu e dit en la inscizio de doas mellas engualment.	And sometimes there are other abscesses in the gullet besides those two ears, and cut them according to what I have said in the incision of two notches evenly.
E yeu ja fu medicat una femna de apostema le qual era nat en le golayro de lu, le qual apostema tendia a color fusca, de pauc sentiment, le qual ja havia claus le golayro de lu, e la femna respirava am meat streyt, e ja havia prohibit a lu comestio e beure de aygua, e ja era pervenguda a la mort si mays agues stat per un dia o per dos.	And I had already treated a woman with an abscess which was situated in her gullet, which abscess was tending towards a dark color, without sensation, and which had already closed the gullet of hers, and the woman was breathing very tightly, and she had been prohibited from eating and drinking water, and if I had not acted for one day or two, she would have surely died.
E l’apostema ja tant havia pugat que havia mezes dos ramps entro que eyssiro per dos traucs.	And the abscess had already penetrated so deeply that it had eaten through two ridges in order to come out through two holes.
Donc yeu me cuytegui fisturalment e fiquegui en un de lor onci, e tiregui aquel, e atirada es de lu gran porcio, e aprop yeu incidigui aquela de on comprendegui del autre trau, e aprop yeu obrigui la boca de lu, e compremegui la sua lengua, e aprop yeu fiquegui le onci en aquela apostema.	Therefore I carefully cut the fistula and remained in one of them, and pulled it out, and pulling out was a great portion, and then I carefully cut that part of which the other hole understood, and then I had to force her mouth open, and comprehended her tongue, and then I placed the instrument in that abscess.
E aprop yeu abscizi gran partida de lu, e no corria de lu sino un pauc de sanc.	And then I carefully cut out a great part of it, and there was only a little blood flowing from it.
Donc absolut es le guolayro de aquela femna, e comensec tantost beure aygua, e aprop presec vianda, donc yeu no cessegui inscidir de aquela apostema motas vetz per lonc temps, e succesia apostema en loc de aquel, le qual inscizia entro que es prolonguat aquel.	Therefore the gullet of that woman was absolutely cured, and she began to drink water soon after, and then I prescribed food for her, so I did not cease cutting out from that abscess many times for a long time, and successive abscesses occurred in place of it, which I cut into until it was prolonged.
Donc yeu engen agui e cauterizegui le guolayro de lu, donc astec de addicio; e aprop yeu perambulegui e no saubi que fec Dieus de aquela aprop mi.	Therefore I mixed and cauterized the gullet of hers, thus adding nothing more; and then I walked away and didn't know what God had done for her through me.
Capitol .xxxvii.	Chapter XXXVII.
De inscizio de huvela quan es apostemada.	On the Incision of a Hovel when it is Abscessed.
Quan catarr deysen a la huvula, e es apostemada e es longa, lahoras ela es nompnada perpendicular; e si es en la partida dejos grossa e redonda, e lahoras ela es apelada buba.	When the catarrh descends to the hovel, and it is abscessed and is long, then it is called perpendicular; and if it is in the posterior part thick and rounded, then it is called a bubo.
Mays quan es curada am aquo que havem dit en la divisio, e no comfereys la tua curacio, e eyssament ja vezes que apostema caut ja es ostat de lu e es subtil, lahoras cove que tu inscidas aquela que es agreguadas redonda; e si es ad aquela longitut, e es sanguina, de fusca color o de negre, e no es a lu centiment, lahoras cove que tu temtes la inscizio de lu, quar en aquela es temor sobre le malaute.	But when it is cured with the remedy that we have said in the division, and your cure does not take hold, and indeed sometimes the abscess becomes stagnant and is subtle, then you should cut out that which is thickened and rounded; and if it is of such length, and is bloody, dark-colored or black, and there is no sensation to it, then you should tremble at the incision of it, because in that case there is fear for the patient.
E quan tu vezes aquela segon la manieyra que yeu he dita de la sua blancor e longuesa, que tu fassas sezer le malaute e premas la lengua de lu am instrument del qual procesic la sua forma e aprop fica le onci en la nuva, e tira aquela en jos e inscideys aquela am un de dos instrumentz les quals e ditz en la inscizio de dos mellas.	And when you cut out that part according to the manner which I have said of its whiteness and length, then you should make the patient swallow and press her tongue with an instrument whose form is described in the incision of two notches; and place the instrument on the notch and pull it down, cutting it with one of the instruments which are described in the incision of two notches.
E cove que no inscidas aquela sino aquo que es ajustat sobre le terme natural ses addicio, quar si tu inscides de lu mays, lediyras le sieu parlar.	And you should not cut out that part unless it is adjusted to the natural term without addition, for if you cut too much, you will destroy their own speech.
E aprop la inscizio, usa de aquo le qual havem recomtat en la inscizio de dos mellas, e cura aquela entro que sia sanat.	And then use the same remedy which we have recommended in the incision of two notches, and cure that part until it is healed.
Mays si era le malaute espaventat per la inscizio de lu, cove que use de engen en la cauterizacio de lu ses temor, e la manieyra del cauteri en lu no es sino am aygua aguda, e es que tu pauses le cap del malaute en le tieu se, e aprop prem la lengua de lu am le instrument le qual havem dit, e aprop pren de l’aygua la qual havem dita en le capitol de cauterizacio, e comfeys am aquela caus viva, e pausa aquela no spessa ni subtil, e de aquela omple la concavitat de l’estrument del qual aquesta es la forma:	But if the patient is frightened by the incision of it, then you should use your skill in the cauterization of it without fear, and the manner of the cauterizer in that place is nothing but with sharp water, and it is that you pause the head of the patient in its own sight, and carefully press the tongue of it with the instrument which we have said, and take from the water which we have said in the chapter on cauterization, and fill it with living cause, and pause it not thick or subtle, and fill the concavity of the instrument whose form is this:
Sia la extramitat de lu conquavitat en la qual sia pausada la medicina ayssi cum la conquavitat de culher de ray, e pausa le strument am la medicina sobre la vula, e·l malaute jagua sobre le sieu latz per so que corro saliva o musellage de la boca de aquel per la intrinscequa medicina, per so que no deyssenda de aquela deguna causa sobre le golayro de lu e que ledesca aquel.	The extra tip of it should be in the concavity where the medicine is placed, just like the concavity of a spoon, and pause the instrument with the medicine on the vulva, and the patient will lie down on his own side so that saliva or mucus from the mouth of that part may flow through the intrinsic medicine, in order to prevent any cause from descending onto the gullet of it and to cleanse it.
E aprop te la tua ma am la medicina, e exprem aquela sobre la uvula per l’espazi de miega hora entro que vegas aquela esser denegrada e sedada per la mordicacio de la medicina.	And then carefully take your hand and the medicine, and express it on the uvula for about an hour's space until you see that part being darkened and calmed down by the biting of the medicine.
E si vols, prengues coto e envolopes aquel sobre la extremitat del ray, e submergeys le coto en la medicina, e entrometas le ray am le coto en una canula de sobre entro que·l coto adheresca en aquela canula, e fay aquo tantas vetz entro que consiegues aquo que vols de la cauterizacio de la uva, e aprop leyssa aquela quar ela se seccara e cayra aprop tres dias o quatre.	And if you want, take a cloth and wrap it around the extremity of the ray, and immerse the cloth in the medicine, and insert the ray with the cloth into a hollow reed until the cloth sticks to that reed, and do this many times until you achieve what you want from the cauterization of the uvula, and then leave it be for three or four days.
E si indigeysses que iteras la medicina, itera aquela, e aprop la cauterizacio abstergeys en le circuit de la uva am coto enbegut en boder, e mondifica am aquel aquo que es en le circuit de lu de la medicina, e sia lavat am aygua frega, e sia curat deforo am embrocacio, e dedintz am guarguarismes entro que sia sanat.	And if you need to repeat the medicine, repeat it, and then cauterize the abscess with a cloth wrapped around the uvula, and cleanse it with that cloth soaked in the medicine, and wash it with cold water, and treat it externally with embrocation, and gargle inwardly until it is healed.
E aquesta especia de curacio es pus salva que inscizio e pus long de temor.	And this kind of treatment is more saved than incision and more free from fear.
Alcunas veguadas es curada la uvuola am aquo que es pus subtil que cauteri e inscizio, quar es curat am subfumigacio en aquesta manieyra: recipe calament, ysop, origua, ruda, scicados arabic, camamilla, broyda e semblant ad aquels de las erbas, e ajusta totas aquelas causas, o alcunas de lor, en una ola, e sian submergidas am vi agre, e bulhan; e la ola sia be lutada am lut decentment, e sia en le mieg loc de la ola un trauc, sobre le qual sia pausat un instrument conquau de aram segon aquesta manieyra; sia fayt de argent o de aram.	And sometimes the uvula is cured with this remedy which is more subtle than cauterization and incision, for it is treated with subfumigation in this manner: take calament, hyssop, origan, rue, Arabic gum, chamomile, and similar herbs to those of the plants, and mix all these causes or some of them together in a pot, and immerse them in vinegar water, and boil; and let the pot be well stirred with decent stirring, and let there be a hole in the middle of the pot, above which is placed an instrument made of iron or silver according to this manner.
E sia entromesa la extremitat en la boca del malaute entro que la vapor poge a la uvula sobre la quanula, entro que la uvula sia mot ofuscada.	And the extremity should be inserted into the mouth of the patient until the vapor reaches the uvula on the concha, until the uvula is very obscured.
E aprop itera sobre aquela motas veguadas entro qu’es secca, e guarda te que no fassas aquesta curacio al comesament de l’aveniment de apostemas, quar trop ajustaria en le apostema, e no cove que tu fassas aquo, sino deves la declaracio de apostema de lu caut.	And then repeat this remedy many times until it is dry, and be careful not to do this cure at the beginning of the appearance of abscesses, for it would too much fit into the abscess, and you should not do so, but rather declare the abscess of him first.
Mays si no es a tu present aquest instrument, lahoras pren una cana e compon en la extramitat de lu un clos de huou, per so que la boca del malaute sia comborida, quar le closc del huou prohibeys la vapor comburir la boca.	But if you don't have this instrument present, then take a reed and shape it into the extremity of it a hood of cotton, in order that the mouth of the patient may be covered, for the closeness of the cotton prevents the vapor from burning the mouth.
E aquesta curacio es bona am salut.	And this cure is good for health.
Capitol .xxxviii.	Chapter XXXVIII.
De extraccio d’espinas e de aquo que adhereys en le golayro e de las autras causas.	On the Extraction of Thorns and that which adheres in the Gullet and other Causes.
Motas veguadas adhereys en le guolayro o spina de peys o alcuna autra causa.	Many times things adhere in the gullet or thorn of the pharynx or some other cause.
Adonc cove que tu extraguas aquo que de aquels es apparent, sobre le qual catz la vista, pus que tu premes la lengua am instrument denant solelh, per so que a tu sia declarat aquo que es en la guola.	Then you must extract what is apparent from those things, above which the sight falls, because you press the tongue with an instrument before the sun, in order that it may be declared to you what is in the gullet.
E aquo que no apar e es a tu occultat en le guolayro, cove que tu fassas vomir le malaute denant que la vianda sia degerida en l’estomac, quar fort leu la causa annexsa le golayro sira foro-getada per vomit; o que deglusia le malaute una pessa de nap o de razit de laytuga o un boci de pa sec; o prengua una pessa de sponga marina sequa leon, e lia aquela fortment am fiel, e aprop le malaute transglussia aquela, quar cum perve al loc en le qual so spinas e es extrahuda, lahoras so foro-getatz.	And that which does not appear and is hidden from you in the gullet, then you must make the patient vomit before the food is digested in the stomach, because very strongly the attached cause of the gullet will be forgotten through vomiting; or that the patient would take a piece of nap or of razit of lettuce or one bunch of bread, or take a piece of dried sponge and tie it tightly with thread, and then have the patient swallow it, because when it reaches the place where the thorns are and is extracted, then they will be forgotten.
E mays pren una anguila e be am fiel liada, e sia dedintz mesa e soptament sia extrayta; o pren un porr e soptament le metas e soptament l’en tratz.	And take a snake and tie it tightly with thread, and then place it inside and later extract it; or take a pipe and insert it and later pull it out.
Mays si no so foro-getatz am aquelas causas las quals havem ditas, lahoras husa de un instrument de plom segon aquesta forma:	But if they are not forgotten with those causes which we have said, then use an instrument of lead according to this form:
E sia pus gros que ray un petit, e en la extramitat de lu sia conquavitat la qual tu entrometas en la sua guola am facilitat.	And it should be thicker than a ray, a little one, and in the extremity of it there should be a concavity which you insert into the patient's gullet with ease.
E el aga le sieu cap elevat en sus, e guarda te que·l tocament del sieu os de la gola, per so que endevengua a lu cos e am aquela que enpellesca le os o la spina, o que aquel le metge am la sua ma.	And it will make the patient's head rise up and look towards you, and be careful that the touch of your hand on the patient's neck, for so that the bone or the spine will end up in the way or that the patient will put their hand on it.
Mays empero que·l malaute aquel entrometa es miels, per la sua sciencia del loc de la causa annexa e enpellisca en jos, e tira la sua ma am le instrument en sus, tot aquo segon la quantitat la qual es a lu preparada entro que sia foro-getada.	But meanwhile the patient will insert it [the instrument] into me, through their knowledge of the location of the attached cause and end up in the lower part, and pull out their hand with the instrument above, all according to the quantity prepared there until it is forgotten.
Capitol .xxxix.	Chapter XXXIX.
De extraccio de sancguisugua annexsa al golayro.	On the Extraction of Blood-sucking Worms attached to the Gullet.
Quan es medicada sanguisugua am aquo que havem dit en la divisio de la curacio am medicinas e no comfereys, considera lahoras en le guolayro del malaute al solelh, pus que tu aias compremuda la lengua de lu am instrument le qual a tu havem recomtat.	When the blood-sucking worm is medicated with the remedy we have said in the division of cures with medicines and it does not take hold, then consider the patient's gullet to be in the sun, because you have comprehended the tongue of him with an instrument which we have recommended.
Donc si tu vezes la sancguisugua, extratz aquela am onci petit o am gesti subtils decentment.	Therefore, if you find the blood-sucking worm, extract it with a small forceps or subtle gestures decently.
E si no es a tu possible estrayre am aquel, lahoras pren una canula concava e entromet aquela en lo guolayro del malaute, e aprop pausa en la concavitat de la canula un ferr ignit, e fay aquo tantas vetz (entro que la sancguisugua sia morta e se osta del guolayro) e abstengua se le malaute tot lo jorn de aygua.
