And if it is not possible to extract it [the blood-sucking worm] by that means, then take a concave reed and insert it into the patient's gullet, and carefully pause in the concavity of the reed an ignited iron, and do this many times (until the blood-sucking worm is dead and has come out of the gullet) and abstain from giving the patient water for the whole day.
E aprop prengua una veyria plena de aygua frega, e obra la boca de lu en aquela, e lava la boca am aquela; e no trasglucia de aquela alcuna causa e maugua l’aygua una hora aprop autra am la sua ma, quar la sancguisugua tantost cum sent l’aygua catz.	And then take a full vial of cold water, and open the patient's mouth with it, and wash the mouth with it; and do not make any cause or trouble in it, and waste no time drinking from that water for an hour more with your own hand, because the blood-sucking worm will soon sense the water flowing.
Mays si no es foro-getada am aquo que havem recomtat, lahoras subfumigua le malaute am cimetz o am assafetida per le instrument le qual havem recomtat en la sufumiguacio de uvula.	But if it is not forgotten with what we have recommended, then subfumigate the patient with cymets or asafoetida by the instrument which we have recommended in the subfumigation of the uvula.
Fay aquo, so en quar cayra.	Do this, and it will come to be so.
E es un’autra manieyra de operacio en sufumiguacio de aquela, es que tu prenguas una ola en la qual sian carbos ignitz e la ola sia cuberta am una cobertora en le mieg de la qual sia un trauc, e sia compausat en aquel trauc la extremitat del instrument; e aprop dega desus la subfumigacio; e pause le malaute la sua boca en la extremitat de la canula, e claugua la sua boca per que la subfumiguacio no sia foro-getada entro que sapias que la subfumigacio es pervenguda a la sancguisugua, quar la sancguisugua tantost cayra.	And it is another way of performing the operation in suffumigation of that, namely: take a pot in which there are ignited coals and cover the pot with a cloth in the middle of which is a hole; and compose the extremity of the instrument in that hole; and then place above the suffumigation; and have the patient open their mouth to the extremity of the canula, and close their mouth so that the suffumigation is not forgotten until you know that the suffumigation has reached the blood-sucking worm, because the blood-sucking worm will soon fall.
E si no catz, lahoras tu itera la subfumiguacio motas vetz, e abstengua le malaute de beure, e mange causas saladas e alhs, e no begua aygua, e ayssi necessari es que am aquest regiment sia fora-getada.	And if it doesn't work, then you must repeat the suffumigation many times, and abstain from giving the patient water, and make them eat salty and bitter causes, and not drink any water, and so it is necessary that with this regimen everything should be forgotten.
E aquesta es la forma del instrument am le qual es trayta sancguisugua del guolayro quan es vista; e es semblant a forceps ayssi cum vezes, sino quar es en lu alcuna curvitat:	And this is the form of the instrument with which blood-sucking worms are extracted from the gullet when seen; and it is similar to forceps like those, except that there is some curvature in it.
le qual sia mesa al guolayro, e la extremitat de lu es semblant a bec de ciconia, que es guanta, en la qual es aspretat de lima, per so quar, quan comprem alcuna causa, aquela no leyssa.	The one which is placed in the gullet, and the extremity of it is similar to a stork's beak, which is grasping, in which there is sharpened lime, so that when you grasp any cause, it will not let go.
Capitol .xl.	Chapter XL.
En le qual es la suma del sermo en apercio de apostemas e en seccio de lor.	In which is the summary of the sermon in warning about abscesses and their section.
Les apostemas so motas specias, de motas manieyras, segon que ve rememoracio de lor, de quascuna en aquest libre.	The abscesses are many species, of many manners, according to the remembrance of them, each one in this book.
E so diversas en perforacio e seccio de lor per doas manieyras, de las quals la una es per la specia de apostemas en si meteys; e per aquo que comprem de las humiditatz.	And thus diverse in perforation and section of them by two manners, of which one is according to the species of abscesses themselves; and because we comprehend of the moistures.
E la segonda manieyra es prop les locs en les quals accideys del cos, quar le apostema accident en le cap es autra de la apostema accident en le cul; e le apostema en le loc carnos accident es autra del apostema accident en junctura; e a quascun de lor es son juguament per operacio.	And the second manner is according to the locations in which they occur in the body, because an abscess that occurs on the head is different from one that occurs at the anus; and an abscess that occurs in the fleshy part of the body is different from one that occurs at a joint; and each of them has its own judgment by operation.
E mays de apostemas so alcunas las quals cove que no sian perforadas sino aprop maturacio de la sania en aquels o compliment de lor.	And besides, some abscesses are such that they do not need to be perforated, but rather should be left to mature and heal on their own or complete their natural course.
So autras apostemas les quals cove que sian traucatz quan son cruzes, e no son maturatz segon lor compliment, ayssi cum apostemas que son propdas a las juncturas, quar apostema quan ve prop junctura, lo esser de lu es prolonguat entro que·s poyreys aquo que es en le circuit de lu, e fort leu son corromputz les liamentz o les nervis de aquela junctura, per que es fayta causa de contraccio de aquel membre; o es apostema prop de membre principal, e si tu tardas la perforacio de lu entro sia madurat nosira al membre principal; o es prop le cul, donc perfora aque no-madurat; e no cove que·l perforas cru, de no-complida degestio, sino aquel que es prop del cul, per so que no poyresca le preon de lu e sia elonguat a las partidas dedintz del cul, e sia fayta fistula, o que sia fayt en le terme de lu que no sia sanat.	And other abscesses that need to be drained when they are crossed, and not mature according to their natural course, such as those that occur near joints, for an abscess that occurs near a joint is prolonged in its own way until it reaches the circuit of the joint, and very soon corrupts the ligaments or nerves of that joint, causing a contraction of that member; or it is an abscess near a main limb, and if you delay the drainage of it until it becomes inflamed to the main limb; or it is one near the anus, then drain it without waiting for it to mature; and do not perforate it with a rough instrument, but rather with a smooth one that is appropriate for the anus, so that the wound does not spread to the surrounding tissues and become elongated outside the anus, causing a fistula to form, or else be left in its final stage without being healed.
Mays cove que tu sapias la hora de la perforacio de la apostema, e aysso es quan es maturat.	But it is necessary that you know the time of the drainage of the abscess, and that is when it has matured.
E sapias que es madurat quan es la cedacio de la dolor e la cessacio de la febre, e aprop la diminucio de la rogor e de la pulsacio, e la acuitat del cap del apostema, e les autres senhals.	And you know that it has matured when there is the subsiding of pain and cessation of fever, and proper decrease in swelling and pulse, and sharpness at the tip of the abscess, and other signs.
E quar cove que sapias la perforacio cazer en le loc pus dejos del apostema e de pus venient de curacio de la eminencia.	And then know that the drainage should be done in the most dependent part of the abscess and from the direction of the cure of the prominence.
E perforacio tostemps sia per le lonc de la carn o del cors, si las apostemas son en las partidas de las mas o dels pes, e en loc dels lacertz, de las cordas dels nervis, de las arcerias; e, al derier, en totz locs enguals en les quals no es reflecio; quar en aquels que so reflectitz, usa de perforacio segon aquel membre.	And the drainage should be done through the length of the flesh or body part if the abscesses are in the fat folds or at the joints, and in places where there is no reflection; for in those that are reflected, use drainage according to that member.
Mays quan le apostema es en loc carnos, lahoras miels es que leysses la perforacio de lu entro que sia confermada la digestio de lu segon compliment, ayssi quo havem dit; quar si tu perforas aquel denant aquo, es prolonguat le cors del poyre de lu e de mota sordicia, e fort leu las labias de lu so enduradas e la profunditat de lu.	But when the abscess is in a fleshy location, then it is better to wait until the perforation of it is confirmed through natural digestion according to its natural course, just as we have said; for if you perforate it prematurely, the body will be prolonged in its suffering and much harm will result, and very soon the lips of the wound will become hardened and the depth of it.
Mays alcus apostemas so perforatz segon la latitut de la carn o del cos deves la necessitat, o segon aquo del qual lo membre indigeys.	But some abscesses are perforated according to the necessity of the flesh or body part, or according to what the member demands.
E cove que administres petita perforacio , e·n les apostemas grans gran perforacio e ampla o motas seccios segon la diversitat de la grandesa dels apostemas.	And it is necessary to administer small perforations in small abscesses, and large perforations and many sections in large abscesses according to the diversity of the size of the abscesses.
E autras so dels apostemas en les quals cove que la codena sia conquavada e sia encidida, quan es fayta ayssi quo pan e fayta es en terme que ja stigua, ayssi cum aquel que accideys en trops de dubelec e de bubos.	And others are abscesses in which the code is concave and should be cut when it is made like a bread and butter plate, in term that has already stopped, just as those that occur in clusters of boils and buboes.
E de aquels so que so insciditz am seccio havent tres angles; e de aquels es en le qual es inscidit ayssi cum figura de fuelha de mirtra, ayssi cum las apostemas dels angonars.	And of those that are cut with a section having three angles; and of those is one in which it is cut like the figure of a myrtle leaf, just as the abscesses of the gangreners.
E de lor so en les quals es administrada seccio redonda e seccio lunar, e semblantz ad aquels.	And of those that are like them, some have a round section and a lunated section, and resemble those that are similar.
Mays aquel al qual no es cap ayssi cum son apostemas leons superficials, cove que tu perforas aquel am perforacio superficial, o plana tant solament.	But as for the one which is not like those abscesses of lions that are superficially visible, you must perforate it with a superficial or flat perforation only.
E cove quant le apostema es gros e ya ha colligit mota sania, que perfores aquel e no te coytes que extraguas tot le poyre en aquela hora; habantz extratz de aquel una partida, e aprop opila le apostema entro al autre dia, e aprop extratz una partida major, e aprop fa aquo motas veguadas segon graduacio entro que sia foro-getat.	And it is necessary when the abscess is large and has already collected much pus, that you perforate it and do not stop until you have extracted all the pus in that hour; having extracted one part, and then covering the abscess with a dressing until the next day, and then extracting another larger part, and doing this many times according to graduation until it is forgotten.
E majorment si·l malaute es de freol vertut, o femna prens, o enfant petit, o viel en decrepitut, quar l’esperit animal motas vetz es resolvut am la egressio de la sania, e fort leu mor le malaute, e tu operte les.	And especially if the patient is a young person, or a woman in childbed, or a small child, or an old person in decrepitude, for the animal spirit many times is resolved with the emission of pus, and very soon the patient will die, and you should open them.
Don guarda aquest capitol am gran cautela, e aprop la tua perforacio en la qual perforas aquestz apostemas, cove que abstergescas las plagues e consideras donc si la plagua del apostema es pauca, o es una seccio plana, lahoras tu aministra las qualguas de li o de coto antic; e si le apostema es gran, e las fissuras de la perforacio son motas, lahoras cove que tu pauses meca en quascun trauc entro que pervenguan ensemps.	So guard this chapter with great caution, and carefully consider your perforation of these abscesses, for it is necessary that you abstain from plagues. Consider then whether the plague of the abscess is slight, or a flat section, then you should administer some oil or old cloth remedies; but if the abscess is large, and the fissures of the perforation are many, then you must pause in each wound until they all come together.
E si en le apostema es abscindit una partida de la codena o has concavada aquela en le circuit, lahoras cove que tu la complescas de coto viel o de fil fayt de drap de li, ayssi cum quan has traytz pans o razizos, ses humiditat; e strenh aquel entro al tertz dia; e aprop proceseys aquel e cura le am aquo que cove dels enguentz entro que sia sanat.	And if in the abscess a part of the code or has concaved it in the circuit, then you must complete it with old cloth or a thread of linen fabric, just as when you have extracted pus or roots, their moisture; and strengthen that within three days; and then process it and cure it with what is needed from the bandages until it is healed.
Mays si accideys flux de sanc en la hora de la operacio tua, lahoras tu aministra aygua frega e vi agre en les quals mules un drap de li, e pausa aquel sobre le loc del fluxs del sanc motas veguadas.	But if there is bleeding during the hour of your operation, then you must administer cold water and vinegar in those vessels where a linen cloth has been placed, and pause that over the location of the bleeding many times.
Mays si persevera le fluxs del sanc, lahoras cove que tu aministres regiment e curacio e polveras las quals he recomtadas en motz locs de aquest nostre libre e de divisio.	But if the bleeding persists, then you must administer remedies and treatments as recommended in many places of this our book and division.
Mays si es en temps de hivern, e·l loc de la apostema es loc de motz nervis, lahoras cove que tu enfundas pulvils en vi e oli caut, e pauses aquels sobre les locs.	But if it is in the time of winter, and the location of the abscess is a location of many nerves, then you must wrap powders in vinegar and oil that are warm, and pause them on those locations.
E si es en estiu, e les locs son carnoses, lahoras cove que tu pauses pulvils enbeguts am aygua e oli o am vi e oli, e tot aquo sia freg entro que sia le ters dia, ayssi cum havem dit, e lahoras cove que tu deslies le apostema e abstergescas aquel e aministres en la curacio de lu aquo que a lu conveneys entro que sia sanat.	And if it is in summer, and the locations are fleshy, then you must pause powders wrapped with water and oil or with vinegar and oil, and all that should be cool within three days, just as we have said; and then you must loosen the abscess and abstain from plagues and administer to it what is needed in its cure until it is healed.
E aysso es aquo que es necessari de la cognicio de la curacio de apostemas universalment, mays segon la via de distinccio ja he dit de tot apostema en qual manieyra es via de la cura de lu per capitols singularment.	And thus is what is necessary for the knowledge of the universal cure of abscesses, but according to the method of distinction which I have already said for each abscess in its own way, by chapters.
Capitol .xli.	Chapter XLI.
De seccio de apostemas les quals veno en la codena del cap.	Of the Section of Abscesses which occur on the Scalp.
En la codena del cap petitz apostemas, e so de specias de nodes les quals conteno tunicas que so a lor factz ; e las specias de lor so motas.	On the scalp, small abscesses and species of nodes which contain tunics that are for their uses; and the species of them are many.
E de lor son pingas, e de aquelas so que conteno humiditat semblant a lima.	And among them are pimples, and those that contain humidity similar to lime.
E de aquelas so las quals conteno humiditat semblant a pols, et asemblantz a lor; e de aquelas so que son lapideas, durs.	And among them are those that contain humidity similar to powder, and resembling their own kind; and those that are lapidescent, hard.
E en la seccio de totz, e en la extraccio de aquels no es temor, cum deves la exteccio de aquels no fa contrariat arceria.	And in the section of all, and in the extraction of those, there is no fear, since the extraction of them does not cause irritation to the surrounding tissues.
E la operacio en seccio de aquels es que tu esproes aquels am instrument la forma del qual ve aprop aysso, le qual es apelat entromes, entro que sapias que contengua.	And the operation in section of those is that you express them with an instrument whose form is similar to this one, which is called "entromes", until you know what they contain.
Quar si aquo que conte es humiditat, lahoras scindeys aquel am seccio segon la longitut per seccio superficial segon aquesta forma:	So if what is contained is humidity, then you should divide it with a section according to length, by making a superficial incision in this form:
E comensa en la seccio de la linha de .B. entro a la linha de .G. Donc cum la humiditat es evacuada, lahoras tu excoria aquela pel que conte aquela humiditat, e no leysses de aquela alcuna causa de tot, quar tropas veguadas retorna, si roman de aquela alcuna causa.	And begin in the section of the line .B. up to the line .G. Then, when the humidity is evacuated, you should excoriate that part which contains that humidity, and not leave any cause of it, for many times it returns if some cause remains.
E aprop submergeys coto en enguent egipciach, si es present, e sino, en aygua e sal; e umpleys am aquel la plagua e layssa aquel entro ad autra dia, quar am aquo corrodeys tot so que es romas de aquela pellicula.	And then submerge the cloth in Egyptian ointment, if present, and if not, in water and salt; and fill it with that the wound and leave it for another day, since at that time everything will be corroded from what remains of that skin layer.
E aprop itera sobre aquel coto am enguent egipciach segondament e tersament si indigeyses de lu, entro que·t comfides que no y haia romas alcuna causa de aquela pellicula; lahoras cura la plagua am enguent entro que sia sanada.	And then repeat the process on that cloth with Egyptian ointment, second and third times if necessary, until you are confident that there is no remaining cause of that skin layer; then cure the wound with ointment until it is healed.
E si apostema conte nodi gras, lahoras tu inscideys aquel segon aquesta forma:	And if the abscess contains fatty nodes, then you should incise it in this form:
am seccio havent forma de crotz, e geta oncis entre doas labias de la seccio e scorsa aquel de tota partida, e esforsa la tua vertut en extraccio de la tunica la qual conte aquel.	with a section having the form of a cross, and cutting one incision between two lips of the section and scraping off that part entirely, and exert your best effort in extracting the tunic which contains it.
Mays si a tu arceria fa contrarieta, lahoras fay aquo que yeu t’e recontat primieyrament.	But if your surgery causes irritation to the surrounding tissues, then do what I have previously recounted first.
E semblantment fay en le apostema lapificat de seccio e de curacio segon que a tu havem dit; e seccio sobre apostema lapificat es pus leugiera, quar es de pauc sanc e de pauca humiditat.	And similarly do with the abscess that has hardened in section and cure according to what we have said; and section on a hardened abscess is less difficult, since there is little blood and little moisture.
E alcunas vetz so alcus de aquestz apostemas les quals so en le cap en alcus homes am los quals de tot no es humiditat; la qual causa es quar yeu inscindigui sobre un apostema en le cap de una femna vielha e atrobegui le apostema ayssi cum peyra sorda, aspra, blanqua, la qual no podia esser trinquada, e si a alcu fos am aquela percussit, plaguera aquel.	And some times there are cases of these abscesses that are on the head of certain men who do not have moisture; and this cause is because you incised over an abscess on the head of an old woman and then proceeded to extract the abscess in a way that was as if it were a deaf, harsh, white pustule that could not be squeezed out, and if anyone pressed against it, it would hurt.
Mays en les autres apostemas accidentz en le cap otra aquest no es aquest capitol, ayssi cum les apostemas que veno als caps dels enfantz e deves las razitz de las aurelhas, mays la seccio de aquestz totz sia seccio superficial.	But in other abscesses that occur on the head, this is not applicable to this chapter, such as those that appear on the heads of children and ears, but the section of these all is superficial.
E pausa la perforacio de aquels de la partida pus bassa de lor per so que sia alleujat le cos de la sania a las partidas pus bassas.	And pause the perforation of those from the lower part of them, so that it is relieved to the body of the pus in the lower parts.
E aprop cura aquelas am aquo que conveneys ad aquel de curacio.	And then cure those with what is needed for its cure.
Capitol .xlii.	Chapter XLII.
De seccio de scrophulas las quals accideyso en le col.	Of the Section of Scrofulas which occur in the Neck.
Motas veguadas endeveno aquestas apostemas en le colh e en las aysselhas e en les angonars; e alcunas veguadas accideyso en las autras partidas del cos.	Many times these abscesses occur in the neck and armpits and groin; and sometimes they occur in other parts of the body.
E so aquelas que accideysso en le colh, e so motas que so engendradas entre lor, e tota scrofula de aquelas es dintz la sua tunica propria, e ayssi cum en les nodis e apostema del cap, ayssi cum havem recomtat.	And those that occur in the neck, and many that are generated between them, and all scrofula of these is surrounded by its own tunic, just as in the nodes and abscesses of the head, as we have recounted.
E las specias de aquestas scrophulas son motas, quar de aquelas so alcunas lapideas, e de aquelas so que conteno humiditatz, e de aquelas so malignas las quals no obeseysso a curacio.	And the species of these scrofulas are many, for some are lapidescent, and some contain humidity, and some are malignant which do not respond to treatment.
Donc en aquela la qual tu vezes de bona disposicio en le Tocament, de la qual la color de aquo que es manifest es propda a la color de la codena, e es mauguda a tota partida, e no es annexsa am le nervi del colh, ni am las venas, ni am la arceria, e no es preonda, cove que tu inscidiscas aquela am siccio superficial de la partida desus a la partida dejos del cos de la linha de .G. entro la linha de .B., e scorja aquela de tota partida, e exten dos labias de la codena am onci, o am motz oncis si has necessitat de aquels, ayssi cum havem dit en las apostemas del cap, e extratz aquela petit a petit.	So, when you encounter one that is well-disposed in the Touchment, whose color manifestly appears to be like the color of the code, and which is spread evenly throughout the entire part, and not annexed to the nerve of the neck, nor to the veins, nor to the surrounding tissues, and is not swollen, then you should incise that with a superficial section from above to below, along the line .G. up to the line .B., and scrape off that entire part, and extend both lips of the code by one incision, or by many incisions if necessary, just as we have said in the abscesses of the head, and extract it little by little.
E es mays cautela que no sia inscidida la vena o nervi.	And be more cautious so that you do not cut into the vein or nerve.
E sia le spatum no mot agut, que no ajuste a tu la tua ma am inscizio, o que enquiete le malaute, e que inscidas aquo que no es necessari inscidir; quar si inscideysses vena o arceria e prohibeys tu de la tua operacio, lahoras pausa en la plagua vetriol trissat o autras polveras las quals ostan fluxs de sanc, e estrenh la plagua, e layssa aquel entro que·s repausa la acuitat de la apostema e sia mollificada la plagua e comense esser poyrida.	And be careful not to cut too deeply, so that you do not adjust your hand with a false motion or wound the patient, and do not cut where it is not necessary to cut; for if you cut into the vein or nerve and forbid yourself from continuing the operation, then pause in the wound and apply vinegar or other powders which stop bleeding, strengthen the wound, and leave it until the abscess becomes calm and the wound begins to heal.
Quan le sanc es abscindit.	When the blood is drained.
Donc retorna a la tua operacio entro que l’aias complida.	Then return to your operation until you have completed it.
E aprop inquireys am le tieu dit indic si es romas alcuna causa de las autras petitas scrophulas, donc inscideys aquelas e munda aquelas.	And then inquire about the signs your teacher has taught you if there is any remaining cause of the other small scrofulas, and then incise those and cleanse them.
E si es en la razit de la scrophula gran vena, cove lahoras que no inscidas aquela scrophula de la sua razitz.	And if it is in the root of the great vein, then you should not incise that scrofula from its roots.
Abantz cove que lies aquela am fiel doblat fort e que leysses aquela entro que caia per si ses nocument.	Instead, it is better to leave that alone and not touch it at all, nor incise it, until it falls out by itself without causing any harm.
E aprop omple la plagua de coto vielh le qual tu has ja submirgit en enguent egipciac, e aprop cura aquel.	And then fill the wound with old cloth that you have already submerged in Egyptian ointment, and then cure it.
E si inscides aquela scrophula tota, lahoras cove que tu ajustes las doas labias de la plagua e cuzas2 tantost pus que no y ha romasa deguna superfluitat.	And if you incise that scrofula entirely, then it is necessary to adjust the two lips of the wound and sew them together as soon as possible, so that there is no remaining superfluity.
Mays si tu vezes que haia romasa superfluitat per la grandeza de la scrofula, cove que tu entendas a inscidir la razit de aquela, e astrayra aquela e aministra sutura e aquo que es dit.	But if you find that there is remaining superfluity due to the greatness of the scrofula, then it is necessary for you to understand how to incise the root of that, and extract it and administer suturing and what is said.
E aquela de las scrophulas que conteno humiditatz, perfora aquela am perforacio superficial aqui la on appar a tu le loc de maturacio de lu, e pausa perforacio de aquo que siec le pus bas del cos, ayssi cum havem dit.	And that of the scrofulas which contain humidity, pierce it with a superficial incision at the location where you see the abscess maturing, and pause the incision below the pus, just as we have said.
E aprop aministra perforacio, calguas am enguent e semblantz ad aquels, per so que corroda aquo que es romas de la corropcio.	And then administer the incision with ointment and resembling those, so that it corrodes what remains of the corruption.
E aprop quan tu vezes la plagua ja esser mundada, lahoras tu cura aquela am enguent de carn generatiu entro que sia sanada.	And then, when you see the wound already cleansed, cure it with ointment of generative flesh until it is healed.
Capitol .xliii.	Chapter XLIII.
De seccio del pilhot del apostema accident dintz le guolayro.	Of the Section of the Pilhot (drainage) of the Abscess that occurs in the Groin.
Diyssero les antics aquesta seccio en le epilhot, e no vist alcu hom en nostra terra que aquela aia fayta.	They called this section "Epilhot" and there is not seen in our land any man who has practiced it.
E aquesta es la inscriptura del sermo de aquels.	And this is the inscription of the sermon of those.
Mays en les homes haventz esquinencia, cove que sia esquivada la extraccio del epilhot, cum per aquo no sia fayt juvament per so quar totas las venas e las majors del malaute so aqui.	But in men with varicose veins, it is necessary to avoid the extraction of the epilhot, because through this it would not be beneficial for the patient since all the veins and major vessels are here.
Mays en aquels que han apostemas cautz en la boca o guolayro o dos aurelhas, quan la malautia no es en la cana, cove husar de la seccio de epilhot a fugir la perdicio la qual es fayta per perfocacio.	But in those who have abscesses in the mouth, groin or both ears, when the disease is not in the canal, it is necessary to use the section of epilhot to avoid the destruction which is caused by perforation.
Donc cove quan volem aquo, que inscidam le epilhot dejos tres cercles dels cercles del epilhot, o quatre am petita seccio per la latitut en aquel que es entre dos cercles per quantitat, que la seccio sia en ciphac, no en la cartillage, e aquest loc es convenent a seccio, quar es privat de carn e les vayselhs de sanc de lu son luhen.	So when we want this, it is necessary to incise the epilhot below three circles of the epilhot, or four with a small section along the latitudinal in between two circles for quantity, so that the section is in ciphac, not in cartilage, and this location is suitable for section because it is devoid of flesh and the vessels of blood are nearby.
E si le metge es pauruc, cove lahoras que extenda la codena del golayro am onci, e aprop fenda la codena entro que pervengua a la canal, mays evite les vaysels de sanc si vetz de aquelas alcuna causa.	And if the doctor is hesitant, then it is necessary to extend the code of the groin by one incision, and then cut through the code into the canal, but avoid the blood vessels if you see any cause.
E aprop inscida li ciplach segon que havem recomtat; e es significat sobre la seccio de la canal per le flacma le qual es de aquela eyssit am aquo que es de lu disromput e per la abscizio de la votz.	And then incise the ciphac according to what we have recounted; and it is signified on the section of the canal by the flame which is of that essence mixed with water that is broken down and by the abscess of the voice.
E layssa la plagua uberta per alcun temps.	And leave the wound open for some time.
Donc cum la hora es remauguda en la qual perforacio es temuda, agregua doas labias de la codena de la plagua, e cus aquela sola ses la cartillage.	So when the hour is arrived in which the perforation is feared, add two lips of the code to the wound, and sew it alone except for the cartilage.
E aprop administra medicinas que fan naysser la carn entro que sia sanat.	And then administer medicines that make the flesh healthy until it is healed.
E diyssec Albucasis que la summa del sermo le qual havem recomtat, exposicio no es sino que veias que alcus de aquetz apostemas ja han opilat lo guolayro del malaute, e le malaute es vengut entro a mort, e le ale de lu es entresecat, e alcus van a inscidir le epiglos per so que respire le malaute sobre le loc de la plagua per alcuna respiracio, e sia salvat de mort.	And I, Albucasis, say that the sum of this sermon which we have recounted is nothing but to see that some of these abscesses have already obstructed the groin of the patient, and the patient has come to death, and the artery of life has been cut off, and some go to incise the epigloss to make the patient breathe over the location of the wound by some respiration, and thus be saved from death.
E per aquo comandero layssar la plagua uberta entro que sia consumida la malicia de la malautia; e es la malicia de lu per tres dias; e donc lahoras comandero cosi la plagua, e cura aquela entro que sia sanat.	And therefore I command to leave the wound open until the malice of the disease is consumed; and it is the malice of life for three days; and thus I command to dress the wound, and cure it until it is healed.
E aquo que yeu he vist per mi meteys, es que una sirventa pres un cotel e mesec le en le sieu golayro e inscidic am aquel una partida de la cana del pulmo, e yeu fu apelat a la curacio de lu, e atrobegui la mugen ayssi cum es mugit del moridos, e descubrigui la plagua e atrobegui le sanc le qual era yssit de la plagua petit.	And what I have seen through my own eyes is that a servant took a hot iron and placed it on their groin and incised into the wound with it, cutting off a part of the lung's tube, and you were called to treat him, and he began to cough as if it was the dying breath, and uncovered the wound and bled out the blood which had collected from the wound small.
Donc yeu fo confessat que aquela no havia inscidit vena ni guidegi, e le vent yssia de la plagua, e curegui aquela entro que foc sanada.	Therefore you confessed that he had not incised a vein nor guided it, and the air was coming from the wound, and cured it until it was fully healed.
E no accidic a la sirventa si no rauquiera en la votz, e aprop alcus dias retornec ad miloracio de las suas dispozicios.	And there was not a single accident to the servant except for a slight change in his voice, and then after some days he returned to his better dispositions.
E ara dic yeu que en la seccio del epilhot no ha temor.	And now I say that in the section of the epilhot there is no fear.
Capitol .xliv.	Chapter XLIV.
De seccio sobre apostema le qual accideys en le golayro defora, e es apelat hernia del golayro.	Of the Section on Abscess which occurs in the groin outside and is called Hernia of the Groin.
Aquest apostema nompnat hernia del golayro es apostema gran segon la color del cors, e es mot en las femnas.	This abscess known as hernia of the groin is a great abscess according to the color of the body, and it occurs more frequently in women.
E es segon dos manieyras, quar o es natural o accidental.	And it is according to two manners, either natural or accidental.
E en le natural no es engen de curar.	And in the natural case there is no need to cure.
E l’accidental es segon dos manieyras del qual la un es semblant a nodes grasses, e l’autra manieyra es semblant apostema le qual es fayt per nodacio de arteria, e en aquel es temor.	And the accidental case is according to two manners of which one resembles green nodes and the other resembles an abscess made by occlusion of an artery, and in that there is fear.
E no cove que·s fassa presumpcio a lu cum ferr sino en aquel que es petit.	And it is not necessary to make a presumption about it as if with iron, except in the case where it is small.
E tu proha aquel e investigua aquel am le dit, e si atrobas lu semblant a nodi gras, e no es suspendut am alcuna de las venas, lahoras tu inscideys aquel ayssi cum les nodes, e extratz aquel am aquo que conte lu de la pel e bursiclam; e sino, lahoras es perscrutat tot le sieu esser, e aprop cura le loc am aquo que cove de curacio entro que sia sanat.	And then proceed to investigate it with the said method, and if you find that it resembles green nodes, and is not suspended from any of the veins, then you should incise it just as one would cut into the nodes, and extract it with the water that contains the skin and bursa; and otherwise, then thoroughly search all his being, and then cure the location where it needs to be cured until it is healed.
Capitol .xlv.	Chapter XLV.
De seccio de las specias de nodes.	Of the Section on the Species of Nodes.
Dels nodes so motas specias e yeu ja he dit totas las specias de lor en la divisio.	Of the nodes, many species and I have already said all their species in the division.
E cove que yeu recomte assi la diferencia entre node e exitura cum fassa dubitacio.	And it is necessary for you to recount thus the difference between node and exitura, as it causes doubt.
Donc yeu dic que am exitura es caliditat e febre e dolors vehementz entro que es sedada la ebullicio de la superfluitat; e es complida putrefaccio que lahora cessa la febre, la dolor e la calor.	So you say that in exitura there is heat, fever, and violent pains until the ebullition of the superfluity is calmed; and it is completed putrefaction which then ceases the fever, pain, and heat.
Mays am node no es caliditat ni febre ni dolor, e conte aquel ciphac leon le qual es al u sac propri.	But in a node there is no heat, nor fever, nor pain, and it contains that ciphac lion which is on its own sac.
E es segon la color del cors, e le comensament de lu es cum un ceze e es fayt ayssi cum vace, sia major o minor, e son segon dos specias, quar o so grassas e conteno humiditat, e las colors de la humiditat son motas, segon que yeu diyssi en la divisio.	And it is according to the color of the body, and its beginning is like a cheese and it is made thus with a vessel, whether greater or lesser, and they are according to two species, either greenish and contain moisture, and the colors of the moisture are many, as you said in the division.
Donc cove, quan pervenas a la curacio de node, que exprohes aquel e inquiras aquel al comensament am sturment le qual es apelat intromes, segon que vindra la sua forma en le capitol le qual es aprop aquest.	So then, when you come to the cure of a node, it is necessary for you to expose it and inquire into its beginning with an instrument which is called introitus, according to what will be said in the chapter which is approaching this.
E es manieyra de inquisicio de apostemas e de totz nodes, e es que tu prenguas aquest sturment e entromet aquel en le loc pus humit le qual atrobas en le apostema, e tu revolveras les tieus ditz am aquel petit a petit entro que sapias que·l sturment ja ha penetrat la codena.	And it is the manner of inquiry for abscesses and all nodes, and it is that you take this instrument and introduce it into the most humid location which you find in the abscess, and then rotate the tips of the instrument little by little until you know that the instrument has penetrated to the code.
E aprop ultima la tua ma segon la mesura de la grandeza del apostema, e aprop extratz le entromes e considera aquo que es yssit en le vestigi de lu.	And then, with your hand according to the measure of the greatness of the abscess, and then extract the introitus and consider what is situated in the vestige of life.
E si es fora-getada la humiditat corrent, de qualque color sia, lahoras tu le inscideys am seccio superficial segon que he dit en les autres apostemas.	And if the humidity that flows is forgotten, of whatever color it may be, then you should incise it with a superficial section according to what I have said in other abscesses.
E si del vestigi de l’intromes no hieys humiditat, lahoras sapias que es gras.	And if from the vestige of the introitus there is no humidity, then you will know that it is green.
E secca sobre lu am seccio havent forma de crotz segon aquesta forma:	And dry it with a section having the form of a cross according to this shape:
ayssi cum t’e ensenhat, e suspen aquel am oncis, e excorja la codena de tota part am facilitat, e guarda la pel o sac, si podes, sobre aquel e extraguas aquela sania am le node.	just as I have shown you, and suspend it with one incision, and excise the code of all parts with facility, and preserve the skin or sac, if possible, over that and extract that pus from the node.
Mays si es romput en la operacio, no es possible extrayre aquela sana, e motas veguadas endeve aquo, e lahoras tu la extratz a pessas entro que de lu no romangua denguna causa.	But if it is broken in the operation, then it is not possible to extract that pus, and often times it happens thus, and then you should extract it piece by piece until there remains no further cause.
Quar si de lu roman denguna causa, pauc o trop, le node retorne segon le mays.	For if from that point there remains no further cause, be it little or much, the node will return to its former state.
E si tu vezes que de lu roman alcuna part petita, lahoras comple la plagua de alcunas polveras corrosivas agudas e strenh la plagua, e pausa sobre aquela que sede apostema caut, e cura aquel del autra curacio entro que sia sanat.	And if you find that from that point there remains a small part, then complete the wound with some corrosive powders sharp and strengthen the wound, and pause over it where the abscess is quiet, and cure that other way until it is healed.
E si es node gran, lahoras tu cus las doas labias de lu e cura aquel am aquo que encarna.	And if it is a great node, then you should sew the two lips together and cure that with what embodies.
Mays si vena pulsatil es a lu contraria, o no-pulsatil, lahoras tu coyta e huemple le loc de zegi trissat que es vetriol e leyssa aquel streyt per dos dias o per tres entro que·s poyresca la plagua e que repause la ebullicio del sanc; e aprop retorna a inscindir aquo que es romas del node.	But if the pulsating vein is opposite to it, or not pulsating at all, then you should stop and cover the location of the gauze which is like vitriol, and let that stretch for two days or three until the wound becomes quiet and the ebullition of blood subsides; and then return to incising what remains of the node.
Capitol .xlvi.	Chapter XLVI.
De las formas del sturmentz necessaris en seccio e perforacio.	Of the Forms of Instruments Necessary in Section and Perforation.
De aquels so las formas dels intromesas, e so de tres specias, que de aquels es alcu gran, e de lor es migier, e de lor es petit.	Of those, the forms of introitus are three species, that is to say, some are great, and some are medium-sized, and some are small.
La forma de intromes gran es aquesta:	The form of great introitus is this:
La forma de intromes migier es aquesta:	The form of medium-sized introitus is this:
La forma de intromes petit es aquesta:	The form of small introitus is this:
Sian faytz de ferr, de alfulud, de extremitatz cayradas decentment, per so que festino le intrament en les apostemas.	Are made of iron, with a rounded end, and a curved extremity, so that the instrument may be inserted into abscesses.
E aquestas so las formas dels experientz, e son nompnatz albered, e un de aquels es apelat berid.	And these are the forms of instruments, and they are called "albered", and one of them is called "berid".
E so de tres especias, quar de lor es gran, migier e pauc.	And these are three species, that is to say, some are great, some are medium-sized, and some are small.
La forma de experient gran, forma de lu:	The form of the large instrument, form of this:
La forma de experient migier, forma de lu:	The form of the medium-sized instrument, form of this:
La forma de experient pauc, forma de lu:	The form of the small instrument, form of this:
Conveneysso que sian per aquels apostemas e exituras e fistulas e bubos per so que entre aquelas so dels osses e de autras causas.	So that they may be used for those abscesses, exitures, and fistulas, and for buboes caused by bone problems and other causes.
E so faytz redontz, grosses, leons, ayssi cum grans agulhas am las quals son cosidas las selhas, e son faytas de eram citri, o de eram o de ferr, o de argent, E las milhors so quan so faytas de eram citri.	And thus, they are made red-hot, large, and sharp-pointed, like great needles with which the sinews are sewn, and they are made of copper, or iron, or silver. And the best ones are when they are made of citrine-iron.
E son faytz les experient de plum negre, les quals se acordan que per aquels sian ubertas las fistulas en la conquavitat de las quals so reflexios, que sian reflectidas am la sua levitat am aquelas refleccios.	And they are made the instruments of black lead, which are adapted to those who wish to open up the fistulas in the convolution of which there are reflections, that are reflected into their lightness with those reflections.
E so de tres specias, quar alcus de lor so loncs, e dels autres migiers, e dels autres breus, segon la quantitat del ample de la fistula e de la strictura de lu.	And these are three species, that is to say, some of them are long, and some medium-sized, and some short, according to the quantity of the width of the fistula and its constriction.
Forma del experient gran de plom:	Form of the great instrument made of lead:
Forma del experient migier de plom:	Form of the medium-sized instrument made of lead:
Forma del experient petit de plom:	Form of the small instrument made of lead:
Las formas dels oncis so de motas specias, quar de aquels so alcus simples, als quals es una curvitat solament, e so de tres specias: grans, paucs e migiers.	The forms of the needles are many species, that is to say, some are simple, with only one curvature, and there are three species: great, small, and medium-sized.
E de lor so uncis orps, e so de tres specias.	And among them there are needle-shaped instruments, and there are three species.
E de aquels so uncis haventz doas curvaturas, e so de tres specias.	And among those there are needles that have two curvatures, and there are three species.
E de lor so haventz tres curvaturas, e so de tres specias.	And among those there are needles that have three curvatures, and there are three species.
E totz aquetz so necessaris en lor loc.	And all these are necessary in their place.
Forma de unci simple gran, forma de lu:	Form of a great simple needle, form of this:
Forma de unci simple migier:	Form of a medium-sized simple needle:
Forma de unci simple pauc, forma de lu:	Form of a small simple needle, form of this:
Forma de unci orp gran:	Form of a great needle-shaped instrument:
Forma de unci orp migier, forma de lu:	Form of a medium-sized needle-shaped instrument, form of this:
Forma de unci orp pauc, forma de lu:	Form of a small needle-shaped instrument, form of this:
Forma de unci gran havent dos curvaturas:	Form of a great needle that has two curvatures:
Forma de unci migier havent dos curvatas:	Form of a medium-sized needle that has two curvatures:
Forma de unci pauc havent dos curvaturas:	Form of a small needle that has two curvatures:
Forma de unci gran havent tres curvaturas:	Form of a great needle that has three curvatures:
Forma de unci migier havent tres curvaturas:	Form of a medium-sized needle that has three curvatures:
Forma de unci pauc havent tres curvaturas:	Form of a small needle that has three curvatures:
E aquestas so las formas dels scalpels am les quals son seccatz e scorjatz les nodes e le apostemas, e so de tres specias, quar de aquels es gran, migier, e pauc.	And these are the forms of scalpels with which nodes and abscesses are cut and scraped, and there are three species, that is to say, some are great, some medium-sized, and some small.
Forma de scapel gran:	Form of a great scalpel:
Forma del scapel migier:	Form of a medium-sized scalpel:
Forma de scapel pauc:	Form of a small scalpel:
Las extramitatz de aquels am les quals es fayta seccio so agudas e las autres extramitatz so no-agudas, e no so pausadas en tal manieyra, sino per que sia fayt juvament en la excorjacio dels nodes la temor de inscizio de vena o de nervi, e per aquels sia sanat le malaute e atrobe tranquilitat un petit per la adustio la qual atroba deves la excoriacio del apostema.	The extremities of these instruments with which the section is made are sharp and the other extremities are not sharp, and they are not paused in such a way that it is done gently in the excoriation of nodes to avoid cutting into a vein or nerve, and for this reason the patient should be healed and then have tranquility a little due to the adaptation which is found to be necessary for the excoriation of the abscess.
E aquestas son las formas de almagidas, e so de tres specias: gran, migier e pauc, ayssi cum veyras.	And these are the forms of ligatures, and there are three species: great, medium-sized, and small, as well as those of very fine threads.
La forma de magda gran:	The form of a great ligature:
Forma de magda migier:	Form of a medium-sized ligature:
Forma de magda pauc:	Form of a small ligature:
Sian faytas de eram e so semblantz de ray am le qual e fayt alcofol.	Are made of copper and resemble a thread which is also made of gold.
E es en la extramitat lada punctada am spatum occultada e en aquela corr a las partidas dedintz e defora, quan tu vols, ayssi cum veses.	And it is at the extremity that there is a small puncture made with a spatula hidden and in which runs the threads outside and inside, when you want, just as you see.
Las formas de spatimis, les quals so amaguatz entre los ditz deves la perforacio dels apostemas e no les percebo les malautes, e so de tres specias: gran, migier e pauc.	The forms of spatulas, which are hidden between the threads that make up the perforation of abscesses and do not touch the patients, and there are three species: great, medium-sized, and small.
E aquestas so las formas de aquels:	And these are the forms of those:
Las formas de ventozas am las quals es abscindit le flux del sanc, e so de tres specias; gran, migiera e pauca; las formas de lu:	The forms of drains with which the flow of blood is absorbed, and there are three species: great, medium-sized, and small; the forms of them:
Sian faytas de eram citri, redondas am alcuna longitut , e sian subtils.	Are made of citrine-iron, rounded with some length, and are subtle.
E cove que sian aquestas specias de ventosas deves tu grans, migieras e paucas, per so que per aquelas abscindas flux de sanc am velocitat en necessitat, e lahoras quan a tu primieyrament no es medicina.	And it is necessary that these species of drains, great, medium-sized, and small, be used by you in order to absorb the flow of blood with speed when needed, and then when your primary intention is not medicine.
Enpero no uses de aquelas ad abscidir sanc en tot loc del cors, e non uses sino en locs carnoses, ayssi cum en les lacertis de las cambas e de las coyssas, e en les lacertz dels brasses, e de las mamillas e del ventre e dels engonars, e semblantz a lor dels lacertz carnoses humitz.	However, you should not use these drains to absorb blood in all parts of the body, and you should only use them in fleshy locations, such as in the groins of the thighs and shoulders, and in the armpits and breasts, and similar to theirs, the fleshy humors.
E alcunas veguadas son faytz de aquels strumentz autres petitz semblantz scorsas de fisacs segon aquesta forma; per les quals lo sanc es abscindit quan es fayt per fleubotomia, o deves inscizio de vena o de arceria.	And sometimes they are made from those instruments small and similar to little scissors according to this form; by which the blood is absorbed when it is done through phlebotomy, or incision of a vein or artery.
E alcunas veguadas son faytas redondas segon aquesta forma:	And sometimes they are made rounded according to this form:
Capitol .xlvii.	Chapter XLVII.
De la cura de las mamillas dels homes las quals so asembladas de femnas.	Of the cure of men's breasts which are similar to those of women.
Alcunas veguadas so infladas las mamillas de alcus homes deves le compliment del dormir cum comensan esser pellutz, e aprop so infladas las mamillas, e so asembladas las mamillas de las femnas, e romano apostemosas, lejas.	Sometimes the breasts of some men become inflamed as they begin to sleep when they are tired, and then the breasts become inflamed, and similar to those of women, and full of abscesses, distant.
E ad aquel que avoreys aquo, cove que inscidisca aquelas am seccio lunar segon aquesta forma, de la linha de .B. entro a la linha de .G., e aprop excorja la groceza tota, e aprop uempla la plagua de medicament encarnatiu, e aprop ajusta las doas labias de la plagua am cosidura, e cura aquel entro que sia sanat.	And for the one who suffers from this, it is necessary to incise these with a lunar section according to this form, between the lines of .B. and .G., and then excise the entire tumor, and then fill the wound with an encarnative medication, and then adjust the two lips of the wound with suturing, and cure that one until it is healed.
Mays si la mamilla declina a las partidas dejos e es mollificada per la sua magnitut ayssi cum endeve a las femnas, lahoras sia fendut en dos latz sieus pus sobiras, am dos seccios semblantz a figura lunar, de las quals quascuna sia contenguda en l’autra deves la fi de quascuna, entro que sia que la linha major contengua la menor segon aquesta forma de la linha de .B. e la linha de .G. E aprop excorja la codena la qual es entre dos labias de la plagua, e osta la pingueza, e aministra aquo que havem dit de la sutura e de las polveras aquo que es necessari en la curacio entro que sia sanat.	But if the breast descends to the partitions and is softened by its magnitude just like in women, then it should be cut into two halves, each with a scar similar to a lunar section, where each one contains the end of the other, until the major line contains the minor according to this form of the line from .B. to .G. And then excise the code which is between the two lips of the wound, and stop the swelling, and administer that which we have said about suturing and those powders which are necessary for healing until it is healed.
E si tu non conpleysses la inscizio de aquo que cove inscidir per la inquietut del malaute, e per flux de sanc, lahoras cove que huemplas la plagua de coto submergit en enguent corrosiu e layssa aquel entro que aquo corroda que es romas de la grayssa, e aprop cura aquel entro que sia sanat.	And if you do not complete the incision of that which needs to be cut because of the unrest of the patient and the flow of blood, then it is necessary to fill the wound with a submergible poultice in corrosive agent and leave that one until the corroding substance that remains from the grease has disappeared, and then cure that one until it is healed.
Capitol .xlviii.	Chapter XLVIII.
De perforacio de apostemas que veno dejos le titillic.	Of the perforation of abscesses that come from behind the titillium.
Aquetz apostemas que veno dejos le titillic so de las specias de scrophulas, durs, las quals conte una pel que es sac.	Those abscesses that come from behind the titillium are of the species of scrophulae, hard ones, which contain a sac.
E de aquelas so alcunas que conteno humiditatz; e aquelas que conteno humiditatz cove que sian inscididas am seccio lunar segon aquesta figura: de la linha de .G. a la linha de .B. E cum es tot evacuat aquo que es en le apostema de la sania, lahoras tu le comple de coto viel e leysa le entro al autra dia.	And some of these abscesses contain moisture; and those that contain moisture must be incised with a lunar section according to this figure: from the line .G. to the line .B. And when all the blood that is in the abscess has been evacuated, then you should fill it with a poultice and let it rest until the next day.
E aprop le coto sia ostat e sia curat am enguent convenient ad aquo, entro que sia sanat.	And then the poultice should be stopped and cured with a suitable application of a poultice to the wound, until it is healed.
E si le apostema de las specias dels nodes es, e de las scrophulas, lahoras tu scindeys sobre aquel ayssi cum havem dit en la seccio sobre las scrophulas engualment.	And if the abscess is of the species of nodes and scrophulae, then you should cut on it as we have said in the section on scrophulae in like manner.
May si la plagua es extenduda en aysso que yesca poyredura, lahoras administra en lu cauteri segon que en aquo havem denant dit.	And if the wound is extended to such an extent that it seems to be putrid, then administer in it a cauterization according to what we have said previously.
Capitol .xlix.	Chapter XLIX.
De seccio de apostemas que accideysso per arceria o per vena.	Of the section of abscesses that occur through artery or vein.
Quan arceria es rompuda, e la codena es consolidada la qual es sobre aquela, lahoras motas veguadas accideys apostema E les senhals per les quals es conoguda que imflamacio e apostema sian per la arteria o per vena: quar quan apostema es per arceria es lonc agreguat en le preon del cors; e que quan inpelleysses le apostema am les tieus ditz, sentes en lu quays sia stridor.	When an artery is ruptured and the code is consolidated which is above it, then many times an abscess occurs. And the signs by which it can be known that inflammation and abscess are due to the artery or vein: for when an abscess is caused by an artery, it is long and aggregated in the anterior part of the body; and if you press the abscess with your fingers, you will feel a stridor there.
E aquel que es per vena es redon al manifest del cors.	And that which is caused by a vein is round about the manifestation of the body.
E seccio sobre aquest apostema es error, e majorment en aquel que es dejos las aysselhas, e en les angonars, e en le col, e en motz locs del cors; e es mot gran, donc cove que la sua curacio am ferr sia esquivada, e aquel que es en las extramitatz, o al cap, cove que sia evitat.	And the section on this abscess is an error, and more so in those that are left behind in the armpits, and in the neck, and in many places of the body; and it is very great, therefore it is necessary to avoid its cure with iron, and that which is in the extremities or at the head should be avoided.
Mays sobre aquel que es de lor per imflacio de l’orrifici de la arceria, scindeys en la codena seccio en le lonc; e aprop huebre la seccio am uncis e aprop la arceria, e deliura de las tunicas entro que sia descuberta.	But in that which is caused by the inflamation of the orifice of the artery, cut in the code section along its length; and then insert the section with needles and tie it to the artery, and deliver it from the tunics until it is uncovered.
E aprop met sobre aquel agulha e fay aquela penetrar entro al autre latz, e estrenh la arceria am fiel doble en dos locs, — la qual causa yeu a tu eyssenhegui en extraccio de doas arcerias les quals so en les templars.	And then make an incision on that and have the needle go through to the other side, and strengthen the artery with double ligature in two places, — which cause will be a guide for your extraction of two arteries which are in the temples.
E aprop punh le loc le qual es entre dos liamentz am spatum entro que yesca le sanc tot que es en lu, e sia dissolvut le apostema.	And then push the location between two ligatures with a spatula until all the blood that is in it is let out and the abscess is dissolved.
E aprop administra curacio en la qual es engendrat poyre entro que caian les liamentz; e aprop cura aquel am enguentz convenientz ad aquo entro que sia sanat.	And then administer a cure in which the pus is generated until the ligatures fall away; and then cure that with suitable applications to the wound until it is healed.
E si es apostema per seccio de vena, lahoras cove que tu tenguas am la tua ma aquo que es a tu possible del apostema am la codena, e aprop intromet la agulha dejos le loc le qual tu has tengut dejos la tua ma, e fay aquela penetrar; e sia en aquela fil doble entro que tu extraguas aquel del autre latz, e aprop ligua le apostema am bo liament segon que yeu he dit a tu en le liament de uva4 de doas partz am doas extremitatz del fil.	And if the abscess is caused by an incision of a vein, then you must take with your hand as much of the abscess and its code as is possible to you, and then introduce the needle behind the location which you have kept with your hand, and make it penetrate; and be in that thread double so that you can extract that from the other side, and then ligate the abscess with two ligatures according to what we have said to you about the ligature of two parts on both extremities of the thread.
Mays si temes que extraguam le fil, lahoras entromet le fiel am aquela agula dejos tot le apostema deves la inscizio de la agulha primieyra, e strenh les tieus fiels en quatre locs.	But if you fear that the thread will be extracted, then introduce the ligature with that needle behind all the abscess, and strengthen those ligatures in four places.
Aprop secca le apostema en le mieg loc de lu entro que quan es yssit aquo que es en lu, lahoras tu inscideys la superfluitat de la codena, e layssa aquo que de lu es liat.	And then cut the abscess in the middle of it until when it is settled there, you will incise the excess of the code, and let that which remains be tied.
E aprop pausa sobre lu pulvil le qual has submergit en vi e oli, e aprop administra la curacio la qual es fayta am calguas e enguentz entro que sia sanat.	And then pause over the poultice which you have submerged in vinegar and oil, and administer the cure which is made with some and applications until it is healed.
Capitol l del apostema le qual accideys per torcio de nervis.	Chapter 1 of the abscess which occurs due to twisting of nerves.
Ayssi cum accideys apostema en arceria e en vena, e semblantment accideys apostema en les nervis quan accideys en lor percussio o accideys per trebal superfluable, e per semblantz.	In the same way as an abscess occurs in an artery and a vein, and similarly an abscess occurs in nerves when it occurs in their percussion or occurs due to excessive labor, and by similar causes.
E es fayt le mays de lu en les locs dels adjutoris o del talo, o en tot loc en le qual so maugudas las juncturas.	And it is made in the most part of the places of the assistants or of the ankle, or in any place where the joints are inflamed.
E es apostema greu, e es asemblat a la color del autre cors, e es en las majors de lu disposicios ses de lor e quan es streyt am vehementia, sent en lu le malaute semblant stupor.	And it is a great abscess, and it resembles the color of another flesh, and it is in the greatest parts of the body, disposed of its own kind, and when it is stretched to its utmost vehemence, one feels in it as if the patient were in a state of stupor.
E no es apostema agreguat en le preon del cors, e per so es dejos la codena, e el es maugut a tota partida e no va a las partidas denant ni detras.	And it is not an abscess aggregated in the anterior part of the body, and therefore it is left behind the code, and it is swollen to all parties and does not go to the parts before or behind.
Donc aquo de aquels que es en las juncturas no cove que sia envasit am ferr, quar fort leu endevenguera contracio.	Therefore, those that are in the joints should not be incised with iron, for it would very easily lead to contraction.
Mays aquel que es en le cap o en le front fen la codena am spatum.	But that which is in the head or forehead should have the code sectioned with a spatula.
Mays si es apostema pauc, lahoras te aquel am les forfecs e abscindeys aquel de razitz.	But if it is a small abscess, then take it with forceps and excise it from the roots.
E si es gran, lahoras tu le suspen am unci, e excorja aquel, e aprop osta aquel; e ajusta la plagua am sutura, e cura aquel entro que sia sanat.	And if it is large, then suspend it with needles, and excise it, and then stop the bleeding; and adjust the wound with suturing, and cure that until it is healed.
Capitol .li.	Chapter LI.
De seccio de apostema le qual accideys de cheil que accideys al ventre.	Of the section of abscess which occurs in the cheek that occurs in the abdomen.
Endeveno ad alcus homes motas veguadas en les ventres de aquels e en las autras partidas del cors de aquels theils les quals son apelatz funguals per similitut de aquels am funges, dels quals la razitz es subtil e·l cap de aquel es gros; e ja las labias de aquels so conversas, e es de aquels que es petit, e es de aquels que es mot magnificat.	I have observed in some men many times in their bellies and in other parts of their bodies, which are called fungals by similarity to those with fungi, from whose roots is subtle and the head of that is large; and already the lips of those are converted, and it is of those who is small, and it is of those who is very magnificent.
E yeu ja e vist un, e en le ventre de lu eran dos theils les quals eran mays a funges semblantz, e no era diferencia entre aquels blancs, de menuda razitz.	And I have already seen one, and in the belly of it there were two fungi-like things, which were more like fungi, and there was no difference between them white, with thin roots.
E ja las labias de aquels eran enversadas e se fendian, e humiditat corria de aquel tot temps.	And already the lips of those had turned inward and were splitting open, and moisture was flowing from it all the time.
Donc yeu inscidegui aquels e atrobegui en la un en pes quays xviii unc. e l’autre quays vi unc.	Therefore, I incised them and carried away one in a weight of 18 ounces. and the other weighed 1 ounce.
E la operacio en la inscizio de lor es que consideres lahoras si·l malaute es humit, e la color de atheil es blanca, humit, de subtil razitz; lahoras tu le inscideys am spatum lat, e sian en la presencia tua cauteris en le foc, quar motas veguadas deves la seccio de lu es expellit mot sanc; e si te ventz le sanc, cauteriza aquel.	And the operation in the incision of them is that you consider then if the patient is humid, and the color of their fungus is white, humid, with subtle roots; then you will incise them with a spatula late, and they should be in your presence over fire, because many times the section of it is expelled much blood; and if you see the blood flowing, cauterize that.
E si vezes le malaute pauruc e temeros, guarda te de inscizio am ferr; mays lahoras pren fiel de plom recent fayt, e strenh am aquel atheil, la manieyra del qual es aquela que havem dita; e leyssa aquel per dos dias.	And if the patient is pale and tremulous, beware of incising with iron; but rather take a leaden thread, freshly made, and strengthen it in that fungus, according to the manner which we have said; and let it be left for two days.
E aprop ajusta en la strictura del fil de plom; donc, no cesses strenher le plom granre devetz en theil, entro que sia abscindit e cayha per se ses trebalh.	And then adjust it in the constriction of the lead thread; therefore, do not cease to strengthen the lead thread greatly in that fungus, until it is excised and falls away by its own natural labor.
Mays si theil es de grossa razitz, lahoras en la inscizio de lu es alcuna causa de temor e de paor, e majorment en aquel que es en le ventre.	But if the fungus is of large roots, then in the incision of it there may be some cause for fear and dread, and especially in that which is in the belly.
Mays possibla es que tu inscindas la maytat de lu , e aprop cauteriza aquel per que no retorne.	But possible is that you excise most of it, and then cauterize it so that it does not return.
E aprop cura aquel entro que sia sanada la plagua.	And then cure that until the wound is healed.
E guarda te que tu no presumas inscidir theil le qual es de fusca color, de pauc sentiment, de leg reguardament, quar aquel es absi cancros.	And beware that you do not presume to excise a fungus which is of dark color, with little sensation, and little regard, for it is an abscessed cancer.
E yeu vindre am rememoracio de cranc aprop aysso.	And I will remember this as a warning to others.
Capitol .lii.	Chapter LII.
De curacio de eminencia del umbilic.	Of the cure of an eminence of the navel.
Eminencia del umbilic es fayta per motas causas; o per fissuras del ciphac le qual es sobre le ventre, e yeys de lu la tela o budel segon que endeve en las autras rupturas; o per sanc le qual flueys de vena o de arceria segon que es denant dit, o per ventositat coarctada en lu.	An eminence of the navel is caused by many reasons; or by fissures of the skin which is on the belly, and you see it as a film or blister according to how it develops in other ruptures; or by blood which flows from a vein or artery according to what has been said before, or by constricted wind in that place.
Mays si es per fissura del ciphac e per yssiment de la tela, lahoras la color del apostema es semblant a la color del cors; e es leon ses dolor, e aprop appar de divers situament.	But if it is due to a fissure of the skin and swelling of the film, then the color of the abscess is similar to the color of the body; and there is no pain, and you will see various situations.
E si es per egressio del budel, lahoras le situament de aquel am lu de aquo que havem recontat, de mays vehement diversitat, e cum tu premes aquel am les tieus ditz es occultat, e aprop retorna; e fort leu es am lu so, e es magnificat mot deves le introt de banh e vehement trebalh.	And if it is due to the eruption of the blister, then the situation of that with the liquid that we have recounted, but with more violent diversity, and when you press it with those fingers it is hidden, and then returns; and very quickly it is in its place, and it is magnificently swollen many times with great pain and violent labor.
Mays si per humiditat, lahoras es leon e no es occultat quan premes am la tua ma, ni es constrengut, ni es cregut.	But if it is due to moisture, then there is no pain and it is not hidden when you press it with your hand, nor is it constricted or creased.
E si es per sanc, lahoras am aquestz senhals apareys le apostema a negror declinant.	And if it is due to blood, then with these signs the abscess appears declining into blackness.
Mays si es per carn nada, lahoras es apostema greu, gros e dur, e es ficat segon una quantitat.	But if it is due to raw flesh, then it is a great and large abscess, hard and thick, and is filled according to a quantity.
Mays si es per ventositat, lahoras le tocament de lu es leon.	But if it is due to wind, then the touching of it is painless.
E la operacio en lu es que consideras lahoras si la eminencia de l’umbilic es per sanc de arceria, o de vena, o per ventositat; lahoras cove que sias prohibit de la curacio de lu, quar en aquela es temor e paor ayssi cum t’e ensenhat en le capitol en le qual he dit les apostemas per arceria e per vena.	And the operation in this case is that you consider then if the eminence of the navel is due to blood from an artery, or a vein, or wind; and then it is necessary that you be prohibited from the cure of it, because there is fear and dread in that as I have taught you in the chapter where I mentioned the abscesses caused by arteries and veins.
E si la eminencia del umbilic es per le budel o per la tela, lahoras cove que comandes al malaute que tengua le ale sieu, e sia stant extendut; e aprop senha am tenta en le circuit de tot le umbilic, e aprop comanda a lu que stia envers entre las tuas mas sobre le sieu dos, e aprop circunda am spatum lat en le circuit del umbilic sobre le loc le qual has senhat am la tenta; e aprop exten la maytat del apostema a las partidas desus am unci gran; e aprop lia en le circuit am fiel fort o am ceda e la manieyra del liar decent.	And if the eminence of the navel is due to the blister or film, then you must command the patient to hold their breath and be still extended; and then sense with your tentacle in the circuit of all the navel, and then command it to be turned towards between your hands on its back, and then circle with a spatula late around the navel on the location which you have signified with your tentacle; and then extend most of the abscess into the upper parts with large needles; and then tie in the circuit with strong thread or with waxed cord and the manner of tying decent.
E aprop huebre le mieg del apostema extendut sobre le liament e intromet le dit tieu en aquel indic e quereys le budel; e si tu l’as atrobat ni guardat per le liament, lahoras tu extratz alxorati e impelleys le budel a las partidas dedintz del ventre.	And then make the middle of the abscess extended over the ligature and introduce the said finger into that indicated spot and seek out the blister; and if you have found it or guarded it by the ligature, then you must extract the remaining part and impel the blister towards the outer parts of the belly.
E si has atrobada la tela, lahoras pren aquel am unci; e inscideys las superfluitatz de lu.	And if you have found the film, then take it with needles; and excise the excesses of it.
Mays si es contraria a tu arceria o vena, lahoras circunda aquel mot, e aprop retorna a la tua operacio; e pren dos agulhas e met en aquelas dos fiels fortz e entromet dos agulhas en le circuit le qual has feyt entorn le apostema en manieyra de crotz, las quals fassas penetrar; e aprop strenh le apostema en quatre partidas sobre las agulhas.	But if it is contrary to your artery or vein, then circle around that much, and then return to your operation; and take two needles and put them in those two strong threads and introduce the two needles into the circuit which you have made around the abscess in a cross-like manner, so that they will penetrate; and then strengthen the abscess in four parts over the needles.
E si tu vols, osta las agulhas e leyssa le loc entro que poyresca la carn extenduda e caia per si; o inscideys aquel quan es subtiliat e se poyreys, e aprop cura aquel am aquo que cove dels enguentz entro que sia sanat.	And if you wish, stop the needles and leave the location until the flesh extends and falls away by itself; or excise it when it is subtle and can be pried loose, and then cure that with water as needed, until it is healed.
E si la eminencia del ombilic es de carn nada en lu o per humiditat, lahoras cove que tu conquaves le apostema ayssi cum havem dit e estraguas le sanc o la humiditat, la qual atrobas en lu, e aprop cura aquel am aquo que cove e que consolide le loc.	And if the eminence of the navel is due to raw flesh or moisture in it, then you must conquer the abscess as we have said and extract the blood or moisture which you find there, and then cure that with water as needed and consolidate the location.
Capitol .liii.	Chapter LIII.
De curacio de cranc.	Of the cure of a cancer.
Ja havem dit, en la divisio, de specia de cranc e en qual manieyra es via a la curacio de lu am medicinas, e que es squivador en lu la curacio am ferr per so que no sia ulcerat; e havem dit cranc engendrat en la mayra e cautela de la curacio de lu.	We have already said in the division, about the species of cancer and how it is to be treated with medicines, and what should be avoided in treating it with iron so that it does not ulcerate; and we have also said that cancer is generated through excessive and careless treatment of it.
E diyssero les antics que alcunas veguadas cranc es en loc on es possibla la eradicacio de lu, ayssi cum de cran le qual es en las mamillas o en la coyssa e a lor semblantz dels membres allocat a estrayre tot aquel, e majorment quan es comensant petit.	And the ancients said that some times cancer is in a place where it is possible to eradicate it, such as breast cancer or scirrhous cancer and its like, which are located on the limbs and can be completely removed, especially when it is first starting out small.
Mays quan es antiquat e es gra, no cove que te propries a lu, quar yeu non pogui sanar de aquel alcu ni no he vist autre, ni que sia pervengut ad aquo.	But when it is old and large, it is not worth attempting to treat it, for you cannot heal it nor have I seen anyone else do so, nor can it be cured.
E la operacio en lu es quan es allocat ayssi cum havem dit, es que tu precedescas e laysses le malaute e purgues de colera negra alcunas veguadas, e aprop sagna aquel, si es atrobada replecio manifesta.	And the operation in this case is when it is located as we have said, that you precede and leave the patient and purge with black cholera some times, and then sign him, if it is found to be a manifest replenishment.
E aprop prepara le malaute am preparacio en le qual sia locat am operacio, e aprop prohiceys en le trauc uncis les quals cove ad aquel; e aprop concava de tota part am la codena sego bona perexcrutacio entro que no romangua alcuna causa de las razitz de lu.	And then prepare the patient with preparation for the operation, and prohibit in the track of needles those which are necessary for it; and then concave from all parts with a good code of examination so that there is no remaining cause of the roots of it.
E layssa correr le sanc, e no abscidas aquel leugierament, e exprem les locs, e abstergeys le sanc gros tot am la tua ma o am instrument am le qual es a tu possible dels instruments.	And then let the blood flow, and do not stop it slightly, and press out the places, and wipe away the thick blood with your hand or with an instrument that is at your disposal among the instruments.
Mays si a tu fa contrarietat de sanc gros inscizio de vena o de arceria, lahoras cauterisa aquela entro que·l flux del sanc sia cessat, e aprop cura aquel am l’autra curacio entro que sia sanat.	But if you encounter resistance from thick blood in an incision of a vein or artery, then cauterize that until the flow of blood is stopped, and then cure it with other cures until it is healed.
Capitol .liv.	Chapter LIV.
De curacio de ydropici.	Of the Cure of Hydrocele.
Nos ja havem recomtat, en la divisio, de las specias de ydropici de l’aygua, e les senhals de quascuna especia, de la curacio de lu am medicinas.	We have already recounted in the division, about the species of hydrocele of water, and their signs, as well as the cure for it with medicines.
E aquela la qual es curada am ferr no es sino la specia de althitas sola, e no es aproximat am ferr a la specia de timpanistres ni a la especia de yposarcha, quar aquo es mortal.	And that which is cured with iron is only the species of althitas alone, and it is not approached with iron to the species of timpanists or to the species of hypoarchaeus, because this is mortal.
E quan tu ja has medicat aquesta especia de ydropici timpanistre am medicinas e no comfereys la tua medicacio, lahoras considera, quar si al malaute ja es conseguida debelitat, o es am aquel autra malautia otra ydropici, ayssi cum si es en lu tos o cos de ventre e semblant ad aquels, lahoras guarda te que no le mediques am ferr, quar temor es sobre aquo.	And when you have already medicated this species of hydrocele timpanistre with medicines and do not confirm your medicine, then consider, because if the patient is already debilitated, or has another malady, such as in his lungs or bowels and similar to those, then beware that you do not medicate him with iron, for fear is over it.
Mays si tu vezes le malaute de vertut exuberant, e am lu no es autra malautia sino ydropici tant solament, e no enfant ni vielh, lahoras la manieyra de la operacio de lu es que tu eleves le malaute entre las tuas mas, e le ministre aprop lu exprema le ventre de lu am la sua ma, enpellen la aygua a la partida dejos del pentenilh, e aprop pren spatum spinos segon aquesta forma:	But if you find the patient to be of excessive virtue, and in him there is no other malady except for hydrocele alone, and he is neither young nor old, then the manner of operation for it is that you lift the patient between your hands, and minister to him appropriately, by draining his belly with his own hand, filling the water at the exit from the penthyl, and then take a spatula with spines according to this form:
sia de dos partz agudas lonc, de aguda extremitat ayssi cum spatum; mays empero sia en lu alcuna brevitat petit a petit, per so que en la operacio am aquel no passes entro al budel, e que ledas aquel.	be two sharp edges long, with a sharp extremity like a spatula; but however it should be in there some smallness little by little, so that in the operation on him it does not go into the blister and lead to trouble.
