E aprop considera si la generacio de ydropici es de part dels budels, quar lahoras cove que tu am la seccio te alonhes del ombelic per la quantitat de tres ditz a las partidas dejos, en le dreyt de lu sobre le pentenilh.	And then consider if the generation of hydrocele is from one of the blisters, because then it is necessary that you with the section go away from the navel by the quantity of three said to the left parts, in the right of him above the pentyl.
Mays si la generacio de hydropici es per malautia del fietge, lahoras la tua seccio sia sinistra del ombilic per tres ditz.	But if the generation of hydrocele is due to illness of the liver, then your section should be left-handed from the navel by three said.
E si la generacio de lu es per la melsa, lahoras la tua seccio sia en le las dreyt.	And if the generation of it is due to bad luck, then your section should be in the right hand.
E no cove que la tua seccio sia sobre le costat sobre le qual vol jaser le malaute per que no corron las superfluitatz ad aquel loc freul.	And it is not necessary that your section be on the side which the patient wishes to lean towards, so that the superfluities do not flow towards that place freely.
E aprop perfora am le instrument tota la codena, e aprop entromet en aquela seccio, e eleva la tua ma am le spatum entre la codena e·l siphac, e tu excorja aquel; e si’ la quantitat de una ungla o enviro.	And then pierce the entire code with the instrument, and then enter into that section, and raise your hand with the spatula between the code and the siphon, and you excise that; and if it is the quantity of one fingernail or thereabout.
E aprop perforo le ciphac entro que pervengua le spatum al loc vuoyt, e es loc de l’aygua.	And then pierce the skin until the spatula reaches the location where you want it to be, and that is the place of water.
E aprop extratz aquel e entromet un instrument del qual aquesta es la forma:	And then extract that and enter with an instrument whose shape is this:
e es semblant a canula de argent subtil; es fayt de argent o de eram o de lato leon, al qual en la partida pus bassa de lu es un petit trauc, e en les costatz de lu so tres traucs: dos de una partida e un del autra partida; e fayta es la extremitat de lu insciza segon la manieyra de pluma, ayssi cum vezes:	and it is similar to a silver cannula; it is made of silver or of iron or of lead, with a small hole at the lowest part of it, and on its sides there are three holes: two from one side and one from the other side; and the extremity of it is incised according to the manner of a feather, just as we use to say:
E en la extramitat de lu pus sobirana es armilla, quar quan le instrument perve al aygua, lahoras aquela tantost deysen sobre le instrument, donc evacua de l’aygua en la ora miega quantitat, quar si tu evacuas de aquela mes que no cove en la hora, fort leu mor le malaute per resolucio del sieu spirit animal, o accideys a lu cincopi que es appropinquada la mort.	And in the extremity of it is an annulus, because when the instrument reaches the water, then that annulus will soon rest upon the instrument, therefore evacuating from the water in the middle quantity, for if you evacuate more than what is necessary at that time, very quickly the patient will die by resolution of their animal spirit, or you will be led to it, which is approaching death.
Mays evacua de aquela segon la quantitat de la vertut de lu e segon que significan a tu las disposicios del malaute de la vertut del pols de lu e de la bontat de lu.	But evacuate from it according to the quantity of the virtue of it and according to what signifies to you the dispositions of the patient's virtue, the pulse of it and the goodness of it.
E aprop extrats le instrument, e rete l’aygua la qual causa es quar tantost es retenguda per la codena la qual rete le trauc que es sobre le ciphac del qual e recomtat a tu que perfores aquel segon aquela manieyra.	And then extract the instrument, and retain the water which is caused because it is retained by the code which retains the hole that is on the skin of which I have recounted to you that you should pierce it according to this manner.
E aprop itera le instrument al autra dia si vezes le malaute tollerant aquo, e extratz de la aygua petita quantitat, e fay aquo per alcus jorns sobre temor, e guarda te de error entro que no romangua de l’aygua sino pauc.	And then iterate the instrument on another day if you find the patient tolerating this, and extract a small quantity of water, and make it so for some days with caution, and beware of error until there is only a little water remaining.
Mays si tu temes sobre le malaute, e leyssas de l’aygua gran quantitat, lahoras cura aquel am sepultura en arena cauda, e mota suzor en banh, e al solelh espere per lonc temps; e cura aquel am medicinas dessicativas entro que sia sanat.	But if you fear for the patient, and leave a large quantity of water, then cure that with burial in hot sand, and much sweat in bath, and wait for it under the sun for a long time; and cure that with drying medicines until it is healed.
E cauteriza sobre le stomac, e la melsa e·l fitge aprop la extraccio de l’aygua, segon que yeu he recontat en aquo que es precedit.	And cauterize on the stomach, and the gallbladder and liver nearby the extraction of water, according to what I have recounted in this, which is preceded.
Capitol .lv.	Chapter LV.
De la curacio dels enfants les quals so natz les locs de la urina no-perforatz.	Of the Cure of Children Whose Bladders Do Not Perforate Naturally.
Alcunas veguadas alcun dels enfantz es eyssi del ventre de la sua mayre e·l cap de la sua mixtio no es perforat (o es trauc streyt o no es en son loc).	Sometimes some children are thus from the womb of their mother and the head of their mixture is not perforated (or it is a narrow hole or not in its place).
Donc cove coytar am perforacio de lu tantost que es nascut am spatum mot subtil segon aquesta forma:	Therefore, it is necessary to pierce it with perforation as soon as it is born with a subtle spatula according to this form:
E aprop pausa en le trauc un clavil subtil de plom e ligua aquel, e te per tres jorns o per .iiii.tre.	And then pause in the hole a small key of lead and tie it, and let it be for three days or for four.
E quant vol urinar sia remaugut e hurine; e aprop retorne aquel.	And when he wants to urinate, be removed and washed; and then return that.
E si tu no pauses le plom, ja es possible que la urina la qual va sobre le loc, no leysa aquest claure.	And if you do not pause the lead, it is possible that the urine which flows over the place will not let it close.
Mays aquel del qual le trauc es streyt sia medicat am clavil de Plom, ayssi cum havem dit, per trops dias entro que sia amplificat.	But that of which the hole is narrow should be treated with a lead key, as we have said, for many days until it is expanded.
Mays aquels en les quals es le trauc no en son loc, so leditz, la qual causa es quar de aquels, aquel que es nat e·l trau es deves la fi del cap de la vergua per que no pot urinar a las partidas dedintz, entro que eleva la vergua am la sua ma a las partidas desus; e no es a lu generacio, per so quar le sperma no pot pervenir a la mayre segon rectitut, e es malautia mot laga.	But those in whom the hole is not in its place, are led astray, which cause is because of them, that which is born and grows is at the end of the head of the urethra, so that it cannot urinate into the outer parts, until the urethra raises itself with its own hand to the upper parts; and it is not a generation, therefore the sperm cannot reach the mother according to rectitude, and it is a miserable disease.
E la manieyra de la operacio en lu es que·l malaute sia envessat sobre le sieu dos, e aprop exten le cap de la vergua de lu am la tua ma sinistra am vehement extraccio, e inscideys le cap del cap de la vergua del loc del perpucii am spatum agut, ayssi cum es inscizio de pluma, o que tu ne razas alcuna partida, per so que·l mieg de lu vengua semblant al cap de la vergua e que le trauc caia en le mieg loc segon que cove.	And the manner of the operation in this is that the patient should be placed on his back, and then extend the head of the urethra with your left hand with a vehement extraction, and incise the head of the head of the urethra at the location of the perineum with a sharp spatula, just as it is incised with a feather or if you remove some part, so that the middle of it becomes similar to the head of the urethra, and the hole falls in the middle place according to what is necessary.
E guarda te que en la tua operacio de flux de sanc, quar motas vetz accideys aquo; e pausa te a lu am aquo que abscindeys le sanc, e cura la plagua entro que si’ sanada.	And beware that in your operation of bleeding, because many times it happens like this; and pause for him as much as is necessary to stop the bleeding, and cure the wound until it is healed.
Capitol .lvi.	Chapter LVI.
De albater le qual accideys en le prepucii en le cap de la vergua e de corropcio e negror e adherencia del prepucii del cap de la vergua.	Of the Ablation which occurs in the Prepuce at the head of the Urethra and of Corruption, Blackness, and Adherence of the Prepuce to the head of the Urethra.
Motas veguadas accideys aquest albater en la vergua e es eminencia de carn laga.	Many times this ablation occurs in the urethra and is an eminence of flaccid flesh.
E de aquela una es maligna e autra es no-maligna.	And one of them is malignant, and the other is not malignant.
No-maligna, cove que suspendas am unci subtil e abscindas aquela entro que aquela mondes tota; e aprop pausa sobre aquela coto submirgit en enguent egipciac; e aprop aquel, cura le am enguent diafinicon entro que sia sanat.	Not malignant, requires that you suspend with a subtle needle and remove it until it is completely gone; and then pause above it, submerged in Egyptian ointment; and then, cure it with divine ointment until it is healed.
E si albater es maligna, de lega color, lahoras cove que tu aministres cauteri aprop la inscizio de lu e la razio de lu.	And if the ablation is malignant, of dark color, then you must administer cauterization near the incision and the ratio of it.
Mays si albater es en le prepuci del cap de la vergua no-circumcis, e la una partida de albater es dedintz le prepucii e l’autra partida es defora, lahoras cove que tu ostes albater le qual es dedintz al comensament entro que es consolidat; e lahora tu cura aquel deforo, quar quan tu curas aquel ensemps le prepuci, no es asegurat que no sia trinquat.	But if the ablation is in the prepuce of the head of the urethra, uncircumcised, and one part of the ablation is inside the prepuce and the other part is outside, then you must remove the ablation that is inside first, so that it is consolidated; and then you cure that outside, because when you cure that together with the prepuce, it is not certain that it will not be torn.
E ja eysamen accideys en les genetius e en le prepuci negror e corruccio, adonc cove que tu conquavas tot aquo que ja es denigrat e que ja se vol corrompre o que ja es corrumput; e aprop lineys sobre aquel aprop aquo am mel, le qual es contusit am farina de scorsa de milgrana e de errs trissatz e crivellatz.	And also it often happens in the genitals and prepuce, blackness and corruption; therefore you must conquer all that which is already denigrated and which already wants to corrupt or has already corrupted; and then apply a poultice over it, using honey mixed with meal of corn cobs and errors crushed and sifted.
E aprop cura aquel am l’autra curacio entro que sia sana.	And then cure that with the other remedy until it is healed.
Mays si endeve flux de sanc, lahoras aministra cauteri lunar segon aquesta forma:	But if there is excessive bleeding, then administer lunar cauterization according to this form:
quar cauteri juvatiu es a dos disposicios ensemps, so es a flux de sanc e a la plagua quan es corrumpuda.	because cauterizing juice is in two dispositions together, that is, in bleeding and in the wound when it is corrupted.
E si le cap de la vergua es corrodut e es destruit tot en la hora, lahoras cove que tu intrometas en lo meat del prepucii una canula de plom per so que le malaute urina per aquela.	And if the head of the urethra is corroded and destroyed entirely in an hour, then it is necessary that you insert a lead cannula into the flesh of the prepuce, so that the patient may urinate through it.
En la adherencia del prepucii am le cap de la vergua (et aquesta adherencia no accideys sino en aquel del qual le prepucii es sa, e sobre lu no es exhigida circumcizio; e quan accideys adherencia per plagua o per apostema) cove que excorjas am spatum obtus entro que sia dissolvut le liament e sia deliurat le cap de la vergua de tota partida.	In the adhesion of the prepuce with the head of the urethra (and this adhesion does not occur except in those whose prepuce is sound and has not been circumcised; and when adhesion occurs due to wound or abscess) it is necessary that you excise with a blunt spatula until the bond is dissolved and the head of the urethra is completely freed from all parts.
E si es dificil desirnir aquelas exquisidament, lahoras cove que tu excorjes am spatum alcuna causa del cap de la vergua e del prepucii, e aysso es quar le prepucii, quan es subtil, fort leu es perforat per la sua subtilitat leugierament.	And if it is difficult to dissect those things delicately, then it is necessary that you excise with a spatula some cause from the head of the urethra and the prepuce, and thus it is because the prepuce, when it is subtle, is easily perforated by its own subtlety slightly.
E aprop separa entre·l prepucii e·l cap de la vergua am dra7 de li subtil, le qual ja es mulhat en l’aygua frega per que no adherescan autra veguada.	And then separate between the prepuce and the head of the urethra with a thin thread, which is already moistened in water so that they do not adhere again.
E aprop sia curat am vi stiptic entro que sia consolidat.	And then it should be cured with a warm styptic until it is consolidated.
Capitol .lvii.	Chapter LVII.
De mundificacio dels enfants e de la curacio de aquo que accideys ad aquels de circumcisio.	Of the Purification of Children and the Cure of that which occurs to those who have been Circumcised.
Circumcisio no es solucio de continuitat ayssi cum las autras plaguas: mays empero cum sia de la nostra operacio e de nostra voluntat, e lus de aquela sia propriament en les enfants, es necessari que asignem en aquela milhor operacio e via pus leugiera perdusent a salut.	Circumcision is not a solution of continuity as are other wounds: but rather it is from our operation and our will, and the purpose of that is properly in children; therefore it is necessary to assign in that the best operation and way most easily lost without harm.
Donc dic que les antics no diyssero circumcisio en alcu dels lors libres, quar no n’usan en las suas leys, e no es sino quar havem aquisit per speriment, la qual causa es que yeu he atrobat la major partida dels artifexs e dels barbies usar circumcisir e mundificacio am novacula e am torores; e usan de liament am fiel e de inscizio am la ungla.	Therefore, I say that the ancients did not teach circumcision in their sacred books, because they did not use it in their laws, and it is only because we have acquired through experience, which is why you have found that most of the surgeons and barbers use to circumcise and purify with a new knife and torches; and they bind with a thread and incise with the finger.
E yeu ja he prohadas totas aquestas manieras e no atrobegui milhor mondificacio am forfexs, am liament am fiel que en mondificacio cum la ungla, quar motas vetz efugeys la codena pus desus, quar la codena del prepucii a dos tunicas, e roman la tonica pus dejos, e fort leu es forsat ad autra inscizio e dolor sicura.	And I have already condemned all these methods and did not find better purification with forceps, with thread and needle that is used in purification like the fingernail, because many times the code above has fled, because the code of the prepuce has two tunics, and remains the tonic below, and very easily it is forced to another incision and certain pain.
E am mundificacio le qual es fayta per alphecati, e es digital, del qual usan les sabatiers, no es segurada la inscizio de la extremitat del membre viril, quar fort leu intra en le trau de lu.	And with purification made by alphecats, which is digital and used by surgeons, it is not certain that the incision of the extremity of the male member is secure, because very easily it enters into the wound.
Mays en la operacio am ungla, fort leu obazeys ferr e corromp la tua operacio.	But in the operation with fingernail, iron very easily obstructs and corrupts your operation.
E la codena del enfant es breu per natura, e motas veguadas nays en tal manieyra que no ha necessitat de mondificacio, e yeu he vist aquel.	And the code of the child is short by nature, and many times it happens in such a way that there is no need for purification, and I have seen this.
Mays de la mondificacio que·s fa am forfexs e liamentz am fiel, la bontat, experiment descrobic a mi, quar las forfexs so de proporcional inscizio, per aquo quar la acuitat que es desus es ayssi cum la acuitat que es dejos; e donc cum tu premes la tua ma so proporcionadas dos acuitatz, e inscideysso segon una comperacio en un temps; e es fayta compressio del fiel am figura contenent la codena de la vergua de tota partida, am le qual no catz error de tot.	But the purification made with forceps and threads with needle, goodness, experience has revealed to me, because the forceps are of proportional incision, therefore the sharpness that is above is just like the sharpness that is below; and thus, when you press your hand so proportionally two sharpnesses, and inscribe it according to a comparison at one time; and it is made compression of the needle with a figure containing the code of the urethra from all parts, without any error.
E la manieyra de la operacio primeyra es que tu fassas estar le enfant majorment si es de aquels que entendo un petit, que no fassas sino que tu lies le fiel en la sua vergua tant solament, e que leysses aquel entro al autra dia.	And the manner of the first operation is that you should make the child remain mostly still if it is one of those who understands a little, and not do anything except to insert the needle into his urethra only so much, and leave it there until the next day.
E aprop fay aquel alegrar en tota aquela manieyra que es a tu possibla de aquo que recep la sua intelligencia.	And then make him happy in all that manner which is possible to you, from what he receives of his intelligence.
E aprop fa aquel estar entre las tuas mas estatuir preparadament, e no sia ges cezent; e occulta las forfexs en la tua ma o dejos le tieu pe, que l’enfant no veia aquelas ni degun autre dels instruments.	And then make him stay between your two most established preparations, and not at all astonished; and hide the forceps in your hand or leave them on your lap, so that the child does not see those nor anyone else of the instruments.
E aprop entremet la tua ma a la vergua de lu e suffla en la codena, e tira aquela entro que sia eyssit le cap de la vergua, e aprop mondifica aquel de aquo que es agregat en ela de sordicia.	And then insert your hand into the urethra of him and blow into the code, and pull that in so that it is out of sight from the head of the urethra, and then purify that which is aggregated in it of sordes.
E aprop lia le loc signat am fiel dobla, e aprop ligua pus bas de aquel un petit le segon liament, e aprop te am le dit pous e endic tieu le loc del liament dejos am bona retencio, e inscideys entre dos liaments.	And then bind the marked place with doubled needle, and then bind a small piece below that with another thread, and then keep it with good retention, and inscribe between two threads.
E aprop eleva la codena sus leugierament e estratz le cap de la vergua; e aprop leyssa le sanc corre petit e petit, quar es milhor ; e pausa polvera desus e sobre la polvera pausa drap en le qual es spandut mugol de huou coyt en ayguaros concosit am oli rozat recent bo; e layssa aquel sobre aquel entro al autra dia; e cura aquel am curacio entro que sia sanat.	And then lift the code slightly and extract the head of the urethra; and then allow the blood to flow slowly and slowly, because it is better; and pause powder above and over the powder, pause a cloth on which a mule has been spread with warm water mixed with red oil freshly boiled; and leave that on him until the next day; and cure him with remedy until he is healed.
La forma de las forfexs a mondificacio, aquesta es la forma:	The shape of the forceps for purification, this is the form:
Sian las unas extramitatz no-talhantz e las autras sian talhant, que non sia yssit le ram del clau, e sia la longitut de las doas acuitatz ayssi cum la longitut de dos manubres engualment.	Be the outer tips not cutting and the others cutting, so that there is no exit of the claw, and be the length of both sharpnesses just like the length of two handles equally.
Mays la error en mundificacio es quar fort leu efugeys la codena intrinseca tota, o partida de lu deves la inscizio.	But the error in purification is that very easily the inner code is lost entirely or part of it escapes from the incision.
Donc cove que tu extendas aquela de la tua hora am la tua ungla denant la apostemacio del loc e que inscidas aquela segon equalitat.	Therefore, it is necessary that you extend that of your hour with your fingernail in front of the abscess of the place and incise according to equality.
E si no la podes tenir am la tua ungla, lahoras extratz aquela am unci e inscideys aquela.	And if you cannot hold it with your fingernail, then take it out with a needle and incise it.
Mays si son passatz tres dias, e roman aquo que es imflat dejos la vergua apostemat, lahoras tu leyssa aquo entro que sia cedat le apostema caut, e excorja aquel am fecilitat, e inscidex aquel segon que a tu es preparat.	But if three days have passed and the abscess remains below the urethra, then you should leave it until the abscess is calm, and then remove that with ease, and incise according to what is prepared for you.
E guarda te del cap de la vergua, quar no nosera a lu aquo.	And beware of the head of the urethra, because it will not be affected by this.
E donc cura aquel am aquo que la plagua consolida de las polveras las quals havem recomtadas en le tractat de las polveras.	And therefore cure that with the remedy that the wound consolidates with the powders which we have recounted in the treatise on powders.
E si es inscidit de la codena sobre mesura, e obezeys a las partidas desus, aquo no notz a lu.	And if it is incised with the code according to measure, and obeys the parts above, then this will not harm him.
E mays cura aquel am aquo que havem dit entro que sia sanat.	And therefore cure that with what we have said until he is healed.
Capitol .lviii.	Chapter LVIII.
De curacio de urina retenguda en la vesiqua.	Of the Cure of Retained Urine in the Bladder.
Retencio de urina en la vesica es fayta per oppulacio fayta per peyra o per sanc congilat, o per poyre o per carnada, e semblantz ad aquels de aquo que havem dit de las manieyras de curacio en la divisio.	Retention of urine in the bladder is caused by oppression made by pressure or by blood congealed, or by pus or flesh, and resembles those of what we have said about the manners of cure in the division.
E si no es dissolvuda la urina, e veses retencio de lu esser per peyra le qual ja es en le col de la vesica, lahoras cove que le malaute sia encorbat sobre les sieus denolhs.	And if the urine is not dissolved and retention of it is seen to be due to pressure which is already in the neck of the bladder, then it is necessary that the patient be bent over his own knees.
E aprop conponeys les pes de aquel sobre le sieu dos e extendas le sieu ventre de la partida pus desus del sieu dos, e le malaute estrengua le sieu ale tant quant es a lu possible.	And then you should place the patient's weight on his own back and stretch out his belly from the upper part of his back, and the patient should strain his abdomen as much as is possible for him.
Donc lahoras le col de la vesica es costreyt ha espulsio de la peyra a las partidas detras, per que la urina es absolta.	Therefore, then the neck of the bladder is constricted and the expulsion of the pressure behind causes the urine to be absorbed.
E si no es dissolvuda am aquo que havem dit he vehement es fayta la causa sobre le malaute, lahoras cove que aministres extraccio de lu am instrument le qual es apelat siringua, del qual aquesta es la forma: Sia de argent e sia subtil leon conquau, ayssi cum canula de pena de ausel am subtilitat de ray lonc en similitut d’un palm e mig, al qual sia cana subtil en le cap de lu.	And if it is not dissolved with what we have said, then the cause is made to be violent on the patient, then it is necessary that you administer an extraction of him with an instrument which is called syringe, of which this is the form: It should be of silver and subtle like a lion's claw, just like a quill from an ostrich with subtlety of ray long in similarity to a palm and a half, at which there is a thin thread on its head.
E la manieyra del eyssiment de la urina per aquel es que prenguas le fiel doblat e lies en la extramitat de lu lana o coto per bona liadura; e entrometas las extramitatz del fiel en la partida dejos de la ciringua, e inscideys am las forfexs si superflueys alcuna causa de la lana, mays intromet la en la canula am vehemencia E aprop enongeys la ciringua am boder e am album de huou.	And the manner of extracting urine with that is that you take the doubled needle and insert it into the extremity of the lana or coto for good binding; and then insert the extremities of the needle into the left part of the syringe, and incise with forceps if there is any superfluous cause of the lana, but introduce it into the canula with vehemence.
E fay cezer le malaute sobre la selha, e embroca la vesiqua de lu e la vergua am olis umitz, e oli de oliva e ayguaros.	And make the patient sit on a stool, and wrap his bladder and urethra with olive oil and water.
E aprop entromet la ciringua am facilitat entro que pervengua a la razit de la vergua; e aprop dobla la vergua desus a la partida del embelic; e aprop empelleys la ciringua dintz aquela; e aprop empelleys aquela entro que pervengua a la vesica, e aquela centa le malaute esser pervenguda a la causa vuoda, e no es fayt asso segon aquest orde, sino le meat en le qual va a tortuositat.	And then insert the syringe with ease into the root of the urethra; and then double the urethra above at the part of the belly; and then push the syringe inwards until it reaches the bladder; and then push that until it reaches the patient, and it is said to have reached the cause of the disease, and not done so according to this order, but rather takes a tortuous route.
E aprop exten le fiel am la lana petit a petit, quar la urina siec la lana.	And then extend the needle with the thread little by little, because the urine is drying up the thread.
Aprop extratz aquela e fay per curacio urina, e usa ciringua, no cesses fer aquo e usa ciringua entro que sia evacuada la vesica e le malaute atrobe alleviacio.	And then remove that and make it for urinary cure, and use syringe, do not stop doing this and use syringe until the bladder is emptied and the patient receives relief.
Capitol .lix.	Chapter LIX.
De qualitat de clisterizacio de la vezica am clampcedra e am semblantz instrumentz les quals sian acordants ad aquo.	Of the Quality of Cathartics for the Bladder with Clamp-cedra and similar instruments which are in accordance with this.
Quan accideys en la vesica ulceracio o apostema, o sanc congilat en aquela, o es coartat poyredura, e vols en aquela destillar ayguas e medicinas, lahoras sia fayt am instrument le qual es apelat clampcedra, e aquesta es la forma de lu:	When ulceration or abscess occurs in the bladder, or blood congealed in it, or is compressed by pus, and you want to distill waters and medicines into that, then make it with an instrument called Clamp-cedra, and this is its form:
sino que en la extramitat de lu es sorda, so es clausa.	but in the extremity of it, it is deaf, i.e. it is closed.
Et en aquela so tres traucs: dos de la una partida , ayssi quo vezes.	And in that there are three holes: two from one side, just like sometimes.
En le comensament es loc concau, en le qual es aquo que es enpellit, e sia segon quantitat que oppile aquel, ses addicio, entro que quan alcuna causa es ab aquel tirada de las humiditatz, sia atirada, e quan es expellida, am aquo sia atirada, e quan es expellit lonc, segon que fa clampcedra am la qual es phicat naphta en las batalhas de mar.	In the beginning it is a concave location, in which there is water that is poured in, and it should be according to the quantity that fills it, without addition, until when some cause is pulled out by it with the moistures, it is drawn towards it, and when it is expelled, it is drawn towards it, and when it is long, as clamp-cedra does, which is filled with naptha in naval battles.
Donc cum tu vols prohicir humiditatz en la vesica, entromet la extremitat de clapcedra en la humiditat, e atira am aquel aquo que es empellit a las partidas desus, quar la humiditat es atirada en la conquavitat de clapcedra.	Therefore, when you want to draw out moistures from the bladder, insert the extremity of clamp-cedra into the moisture, and pull towards it the water that is poured in above, because the moisture is drawn into the concavity of clamp-cedra.
E aprop entromet la extramitat de clapcedra en la vergua segon que havem recomtat en la ciringua; e aprop empelleys la humiditat am aquo que empelleys, quar aquela humiditat perve a la vesica tantost, e le malaute cent aquela.	And then insert the extremity of clamp-cedra into the urethra according to what we have recounted in the syringe; and then pull out the moisture with water that you pour in, because that moisture flows into the bladder at once, and the patient is cured by it.
Forma del cristeri subtil am le qual la vesica es cristerizada, e es aquela la forma:	The Form of the Subtle Catheter by which the Bladder is Catheterized, and this is its form:
E sia fayta de argent o de lato, de la qual le cap pus aut sia semblant a petita pluma, e dejos lu cana dedintz liament.	And it should be made of silver or lead, with the head being similar to a small feather, and having a thin thread at its end.
E aprop pren vesica de moto, e pausa en aquela la humiditat que vols cristirizar en la vesica, e aprop lia aquela entre dos am fort liguatura am fiel doble, e escalfa aquela humiditat sobre le foc.	And then take a vessel of motion, and pour into it the moisture that you want to catheterize in the bladder, and then tie it between two with a strong ligature made of double thread, and heat that moisture over the fire.
E aprop entromet la extremitat del cristeri en la vergua.	And then insert the extremity of the catheter into the urethra.
E aprop estrenh la tua ma sobre la vesica am la humiditat am strectura descent entro que·l malaute centa que aquela humiditat ja es pervenguda a la vesica.	And then stretch your hand over the bladder with the moisture and stretching downward until the patient's disease is cured because that moisture has reached the bladder.
Mays si a tu no es present vesica, lahoras tu pren una pessa de parguames e fay de aquel cercle; e perfora aquel de tota la sua retonditat; e aprop entromet fiel fort en aquels traucs, ayssi quo so revolgut; e aprop agregua le cercle ayssi quo es agreguat alsofatur, pus que tu pausas en aquel aquo que tu vols de las humiditatz, e olis e ayguas.	But if you do not have a bladder present, then take a bag made of papyrus and make it into a circle; and perforate it all over its roundness; and then insert a strong thread into those holes, just like they are revolved; and then add the circle in such a way that it is added also to the future, so that you put into it what you want from the moistures, and oils and waters.
E aprop tu lia aquel en le instrument e fay am aquel ayssi cum has fayt am la vesica, e exprescio am la tua ma entro que la humiditat pervengua a la vesica.	And then tie that onto the instrument and do with it just as you did with the bladder, and express it onto your hand until the moisture reaches the bladder.
Capitol .lx.	Chapter LX.
De extraccio de peyra.	Of the Extraction of Pus.
Nos ja havem dit en la divisio las specias de peyra e curacio de lu am medicinas, e la diferencia entre peyra engendrada en los ronhos e peyra engendrada en la vesica, e les senhals de aquela.	We have already said in the division the kinds of pus and its cure with medicines, and the difference between pus generated in the lungs and pus generated in the bladder, and the signs of it.
E havem dit la peyra en la qual catz operacio am ma, e seccio.	And we have said the pus in which operation with hand and section occurs.
E la peyra engendrada en la vesica propriament es aquela que es ficada en la vesica.	And the pus generated in the bladder properly is that which is formed in the bladder.
E yeu so narrant aquel am exposicio manifesta e abreviacio.	And you should narrate it with manifest exposition and abbreviation.
Donc dic que peyra engendrada en la vesica majorment ve als enfantz; e dels senhals de lu es que la urina que es eyssida de la vesica es semblant a aygua en la sua subtilitat, e apar en aquela arena; e le malaute fregua la sua vergua, e motas veguadas pen, e aprop es dressada; e am aquo yeys foro le cul en motz de aquels.	So I say that pus generated in the bladder mostly occurs in children; and one of its signs is that the urine which comes out of the bladder is similar to water in its subtlety, and appears in it like sand; and the patient frequently wipes his urethra, and many times pulls back his penis, and then stands up straight; and with this you will know that there is a discharge from those parts.
E es laugiera la sanacio dels enfants de aquela entro que han conseguitz xiiii ans; e es dificil curacio en les viels.	And it is easier to heal the children of this disease until they have reached 14 years old; and it is difficult to cure in the elderly.
Mays en les joves es migiera per aquo quar es entre aquels.	But in the young, it is mid-term because it is between them.
E de aquel del qual la peyra es major e la curacio es pus leugiera; E si es pauca, es contraria ad aquela.	And of that from which pus is more abundant and the cure is easier; And if it is little, it is contrary to that.
Donc cum pervenem a la curacio de aquela, cove al comensament de aquela que mondifiquem le malaute am cristeri le qual extragua tota la fenda la qual es en les sieus budels; quar aquela fenda alcunas veguadas prohibeys la envencio de la peyra deves la inquisicio de lu.	Therefore, when we come to the cure of this disease, it is necessary at first that we purify the patient with a catheter which extracts all the abscesses that are in his bowels; for that abscess sometimes prevents the evacuation of the pus from the bladder.
E aprop sia pres le malaute am les sieus pes e sia contosit e maugut enjos per so que la peyra descenda al preon de la vesica, o que saute de loc aut alcunas veguadas.	And then the patient should be pressed with his own weight and continued in a comfortable position for so that the pus descends to the bottom of the bladder, or else it may jump from one place to another.
E aprop fay aquel cezer entre las tuas mas preparat, e las mas de lu sian dejos las coysas de lu, per so que la vesica tota sia fayta declinant a las partidas dejos.	And then make that person sit between your most prepared things and those of him be left the things of his, so that the bladder is made to decline towards the parts below.
E aprop perquier aquela e tota aquela deforo.	And then pour it out all at once.
Donc si sentes la peyra en l’espazi, lahoras tu te coyta tantost am seccio sobre lu.	Therefore, if you feel the pus in space, then you should cut into it immediately with section above it.
E si no catz de tot dejos le tieu tocament, lahoras cove que tu untes am oli le tieu dit indic de la ma sinistra, si malaute es enfant, o le dit miga si es jove complit, e entrometas aquel en le sieu cul.	And if you do not find the entire discharge of your touch, then it is necessary that you anoint with oil the indicated digit of your left hand, whether the patient is a child or a young adult, and insert that into his anus.
E perquier de la peyra entro que stia dejos le tieu dit.	And pour out the pus until it remains below your said finger.
E converteys aquela petit a petit entro al col de la vesica.	And convert that little by little into the neck of the bladder.
E aprop prem sobre aquel am lo tieu dit, e expelleys aquel a las partidas defora ves le loc del qual vos la seccio.	And then press upon it with your said finger and expel that out to the external parts below the location where you made the section.
E comanda al ministra que prema la vesica am la sua ma; e comanda a un autra ministra que am la sua ma dextra extenda les genetius a las partidas desus, e am la sua autra ma remaugua la codena la qual es dejos les genetius, en partida del loc en le qual se fa la seccio.	And command the assistant to press the bladder with her right hand; and command another assistant to extend the patient's legs upwards with her left hand, and with her other hand to relax the code which is below the legs, in the part of the location where the section is being made.
E aprop entromet espatum be inscident del qual aquesta es la forma de lu:	And then insert the spatula which is incident from which this is its form:
e scindeys en lu aquo que es entre·l cul e·ls genetius, no en le mieg loc, abantz al latz de la coyssa sinistra; e sia la seccio sobre aquela peyra e·l tieu dit sia en le cul, e sia fayta seccio transversa, per que la seccio defora sia ampla e dedintz streyta segon la quantitat que egrecio de la peyra sia a lu possibla, e no major, quar fort leu comprem le tieu dit le qual es en le cul la peyra deves la seccio, e es foro-getada ses defacultat.	and cut into it where there is between the anus and the legs, not in the middle location, but before the left side of the cleft; and let the section be on that pus and your finger be in the anus, and let it be a transverse section, so that the external section may be wide and narrow inside according to the quantity that you extracted from the pus, and no greater, for fear that too soon compresses your finger which is in the anus, and forgets the difficulty.
E sapias que de la peyra es alcuna a la qual so angle e margers, per que le eyssiment de lu es fayt deficil per aquo.	And know that from the pus there is some which has an angle and margins, for which the extraction of it is made difficult by this.
E de aquela aquo es leon semblant a glan, e es redonda, e es fayt de lu leugier eyssiment.	And from that pus, it is like a glans, and is round, and is made for easier extraction.
Donc si es aquela al qual so angles e marger, ajusta en la fissura.	Therefore, if it is this kind with angles and margins, adjust in the fissure.
E si no es ayssi foro-getada, lahoras cove que tu engenes sobre aquel, o que strenguas sobre aquel am gesti decentment, la extremitat del qual sia ayssi cum lima am le qual strenguas sobre la peyra, e no evasesca de lu; o que entrometas dejos lu instrument subtil de curvada extremitat.	And if not, then it is necessary that you gently push on it, or that you strengthen on it with decent gestures, the extremity of which should be like a file with which you strengthen on the pus, and do not dislodge from there; or that you insert below it the subtle instrument of curved extremity.
Mays si tu no podes sobre aquel, lahoras tu amplifica le trauc un petit, e si tu veus flux de sanc, abscindeys en strenh aquel am vitriol trissat.	But if you cannot push on it, then you should enlarge the hole a little bit; and if you see a flow of blood, cut in strength with vitriol thread.
Mays si la peyra es mays de una, lahoras al comensament tu impelleys la ma a la boca de la vesica, e aprop inscideys sobre lu; e aprop impelleys un petit aprop aquo; e semblantment fay si son motas mays de doas.	But if the pus is more than one, then at first you should push your hand into the mouth of the bladder, and then insert it onto that; and then push a little bit further; and similarly do so if there are many more than two.
E si es peyra mot gran, lahoras ignorancia es que tu inscidas aquel am gran seccio, quar accideys al malaute una de doas causas: o que mora o que endevengua a lu destillacio de urina continuabla, per aquo quar le loc no es de tot consolidat.	And if the pus is very great, then ignorance is that you insert it with a great incision, for it will happen to the patient one of two causes: either death or obstruction of the urinary distillation continuous, therefore the location is not fully consolidated.
Mays aministra expulcio de lu entro que sia fora-getada, o engenia en la fractura de lu am las forfexs entro que extragua aquela en pessas.	But administer expulsion of it until it is forgotten, or shape in the fracture of it with forceps until it extracts that in pieces.
Donc cum tu auras cumplit la tua opperacio, lahoras omple la plagua de enses de aloe e de sanc de drago, e strenh aquel.	Therefore, when you have completed your operation, then fill the wound with the juice of aloe and dragon's blood, and strengthen it.
E pausa sobre aquel drap enfus en oli e vi, o en oli rozat e aygua frega, per so que apostema caut sia cedat.	And pause over that cloth soaked in oil and vinegar, or in rosinated oil and cold water, so that the abscess may be calmed.
E aprop resupina le malaute sobre le sieu col, e no deslias le liament entro al tertz dia.	And then resupply the patient with his own bed, and do not loosen the bond until the third day.
E cum aquel auras desliat, embroca le loc am aygua e mot oli, e aprop cura aquel am enguent diafinicon e am enguent diabazilicon entro que sia sanat.	And when you have loosened it, wrap the wound with water and much oil, and then cure that with divine balm and devil's balsam until it is healed.
Mays si en la plagua accideys apostema caut, adhust e corrosiu, e de aquel semblantz ayssi cum si le sanc es en la vesica congelat, e per lu es la hurina prohibida (e aquo es conogut per la egressio del sanc am urina), a donc entromet lo tieu dit en la plagua e extratz aquel sanc, quar si roman provoca la vesica a corropcio de la vesica e de lu putrefaccio.	But if in the wound there occurs an abscess that is calm, adjusted and corrosive, and it resembles as if the blood is frozen in the bladder with congelation, and because of this the urine is prohibited (and this is known through the egress of blood with urine), then therefore insert your finger into the wound and extract that blood, for if left it will provoke the bladder to corruption of the bladder and putrefaction.
E aprop lava la plagua am vi agre, aygua e sal, e am opposicio a tota specia, am aquo que conveneys a lu de la curacio entro que sia sanat.	And then wash the wound with vinegar, water and salt, and with opposition to all species, according to what is necessary for its cure until it is healed.
E cove en las horas de tota la curacio que tu lies amdos las coyssas e ajustes las medicinas las quals so pausadas sobre le loc.	And it is necessary during the entire course of the cure that you keep both things in order and adjust the medicines which are placed on the wound.
E si la peyra es petita e es en le meat de la vergua, e es ficat en lu, e eyssement de urina es prohibit, lahoras cura aquel am aquo que yeu recomti denant que pervenguas a seccio, quar tropas veguadas per aquesta curacio yest acusat de seccio; e ja yeu e esproat aquo, e es que tu prenguas un perforador de ferr alfelut, del qual aquesta es la forma de lu:	And if the pus is small and is in the urethra, and is stuck there, and the discharge of urine is prohibited, then cure that with what I recommended before you reach section, for many times by this cure you are accused of section; and now it has been tried, and it is that you take a perforator made of iron with an alfelut, from which this is its form:
de triangulada extramitat, agut, ficat en fust.	of triangular extremity, sharp, fixed in a handle.
E aprop pren fiel, e lia am aquel la vergua dejos la peyra per so que no retorne a la vesica.	And then take a thread, and tie it onto that urethra below the pus so that it does not return to the bladder.
E aprop entromet le ferr en la vergua, perforant am fecilitat entro que·l perforador vengua ad aquela peyra.	And then insert the iron into the urethra, piercing with ease until the perforator comes to that pus.
E revolveys le perforador am la tua ma en aquela peyra petit a petit, e tu perforsa la perforacio de lu entro que fassas aquel del autra part penetrar; quar la urina tantost es absolta.	And then turn the perforator with your hand in that pus little by little, and you pierce through the hole until it comes out on the other side; for the urine is soon absolved.
E aprop prem la tua ma sobre aquo que es romas de la peyra de la partida deforo de la vergua, quar aquela es trinquada, e es foro-getada am la urina, e le malaute es sanat.	And then press your hand on that which is left of the pus from the outside part of the urethra, because it is torn, and forgotten with the urine, and the patient is healed.
Mays si aquesta curacio no es a tu aparelhada per alcuna causa la qual prohibeys de aquela, lahoras lia un fiel dejos la peyra, e autra fiel desus la peyra.	But if this cure is not prepared by you for some reason which prohibits it, then tie one thread below the pus, and another thread above the pus.
E aprop encideys sobre la peyra en aquela vergua entre doas liaduras.	And then insert on top of the pus in that urethra between two threads.
E aprop extratz aquela.	And then extract it.
E aprop deslia le liament e mondifica le sanc congilat, le qual es fayt en la plagua.	And then loosen the bond and purify the congealed blood which is in the wound.
E no es necessari liament de fiel dejos la peyra, sino per que no retorne a la vesica, e l’autre liament desus sino, quar quan es desliat le fiel aprop la egrecio de la peyra, la codena retorna a son loc e cobra la plagua.	And it is not necessary to tie the thread below the pus, except that it does not return to the bladder, and the other thread above, only because when the thread is loosened next to the extraction of the pus, the code returns to its place and closes the wound.
E per aquo es a tu necessari quan lias le fiel desus, que tu eleves la codena a las partidas desus, o que retorne deves le tieu compliment, e cobra la plagua ayssi co havem dit.	And therefore it is necessary to you when you tie the thread above that you raise the code to the upper parts, or that you return to your previous statement, and close the wound as we have said.
Capitol .lxi.	Chapter LXI.
De extraccio de peyra de las femnas.	Of the Extraction of Pus from Women.
Peyra en las femnas pauc es engendrada.	Pus in women is rarely generated.
Mays si ve peyra ad alcuna de aquelas, lahoras dificil es la curacio de lu, e es prohibida per tropas manieyras.	But if you see pus in some of those women, then it is difficult to cure it, and is prohibited by many methods.
La una de lor es quar la femna fort leu es verges.	One of them is because the woman is very proud.
E la segonda es quar tu no trobas femna be scient que descroba si meteyssa al metge quan es casta, o es de las femnas haventz maritz.	And the second is because you do not find a woman well knowing that she does not understand if she confides in a doctor when she is chaste, or one of those women who are married.
La tersa es quar tu no hatrobas femna be sabent aquesta art, majorment la operacio am ma.	The third is because you do not have a woman well knowing this art, mainly the operation with hand.
E la quarta es que·l loc de la seccio sobre peyra en las femnas es longinc del loc de la peyra, per que indigeys de seccio preonda, e en aquela es temor.	And the fourth is that the location of the section on pus in women is too far from the location of the pus, so you need to make a previous incision, and in that there is fear.
Mays si necessitat provoca a tu ad aquo, lahoras cove que tu prenguas una femna metga be scient, e pauc es atrobada.	But if necessity prompts you to this, then it is necessary that you take a married woman who is well knowing, and little is troubled.
Mays si tu es privat de aquela, lahoras cerca metga quast e subtil, o presenta una femna matrona be esenhada en le feyt de las femnas, o femna que en aquesta art ennueys partida del art.	But if you are deprived of that, then seek out a midwife who is quick and subtle, or present an elderly woman well experienced in the affairs of women, or a woman who has parted from this art.
Donc fay aquela present, e comanda a lu que fassa tot aquo que tu li mandaras, de la enquisicio sobre la peyra al comensament; la qual causa es que reguarde si la femna es verges, lahoras cove que meta lo sieu dit en le cul de lu e quiera la peyra.	Then present that one and command them to do all this which you will instruct them to do, from the inquiry about the pus to the beginning; which cause is that they should regard whether the woman is a virgin, then it is necessary that she put her finger into the urethra and seek out the pus.
Donc si atroba aquela, coarte aquela dejos le sieu dit, e lahoras comanda a lu que inscida sobre aquela.	Then if she finds it, cut it below her finger, and then command her to insert something onto that.
Mays si no es verge, lahoras comanda a la matrona que entrometa lo sieu dit en le conh de la malauta e enquiera sobre la peyra, pus que pausa la sua ma sinistra sobre la vesica, e comprem aquela am bona comprecio.	But if she is not a virgin, then command the matron to insert her finger into the woman's private parts and inquire about the pus, since she places her left hand on the bladder, and compress it with good compression.
Donc si atroba aquela, lahoras cove que gradantment maugua aquela de l’orrifici de la vesica a las partidas dejos am somman de la sua vertut entro que pervengua am aquel a la razit de la coyssa.	Then if she finds it, then it is necessary that gradually she relaxes that from the bottom of the bladder to the parts below with the summit of her virtue until it comes out at the root of the urethra.
E aprop inscida sobre aquela apposicio de la maytat del conh deves la razit de la coyssa de qualque part sia a lu parada e cent la peyra en aquela partida, e·l dit de lu no sia remaugut de la peyra coartan dejos lu.	And then insert onto that an apposition of the middle of the private parts, at the root of the urethra, from which some part may be paraded and centered the pus in that part, and the said finger should not be removed from the pus cut below.
E la seccio sia pauca al comensament; e aprop entrometa lo ray sobre aquela seccio, e si sent la peyra, lahoras ajuste en seccio segon la quantitat la qual sap que la peyra sira getada de aquela.	And the section should be small at first; and then insert a ruler onto that section, and if you feel the pus, then adjust in section according to the quantity which you know will be extracted from that.
E sapias que las specias de peyra son motas: quar de aquelas es pauca e gran, e leon e aspra, e longua e redonda, e havent ramps.	And know that the kinds of pus are many: for some is small and great, and hard and sharp, and long and round, and having ridges.
Donc tu sapias quantas specias so de lu per aquo que tu signifiques sobre aquo que vols.	Then you know how many kinds there are of it by this which I signify about that which you want.
E si tu veus flux de sanc, ajusta en le loc vetriol trissat e te aquela per una hora entro que sia abscindit le sanc, e aprop retorna a la tua operacio entro que la peyra sia fora-getada.	And if you see a flow of blood, adjust with vitriol thread and keep it for one hour until the blood is stopped, and then return to your operation until the pus is forgotten.
E fay que prepares am tu dels instrumentz les quals e ditz en la extraccio de peyra en les homes, per so que sias ajudat per aquels en la tua operacio.	And prepare with you the instruments which I say in the extraction of pus in men, so that you may be helped by them in your operation.
E si tu veus flux de sanc, e sabes que la expulcio del sanc es de la arceria que es insciza, lahoras tu pausa polvera sobre le loc e estrenh aquel am pulvils e strictura descent, e no iteras aquo; e layssa la peyra e no extraguas aquela, quar fort leu morira la malauta.	And if you see a flow of blood, and know that the expulsion of the blood is from the artery which is inserted, then you pause powder on the place and strengthen it with powders and strictura descent, and do not repeat this; and leave the pus and do not extract it, for very soon the patient will die.
E aprop cura la plagua.	And then cure the wound.

Capitol lxii.	Chapter LXII.

And then take hold of the code of the testicles with your hand, and stretch out the white pouch on the left side, and lift up the humor with the pouch to the part of the section; and command the minister to extend the humor upwards and you dissolve the adherence that is behind with complete solution.
E cerqua am les tieus ditz que lay no sia alcuna causa del budel envelopat en le ciphac blanc dur.	And search with those fingers mentioned above, so that there be no cause for the bowel to be enveloped in the white pouch.
Mays si tu atrobas de lu alcuna causa, lahoras tu enpelleys aquel al ventre dejos.	But if you find some cause from him, then you compress it to the belly below.
E aprop tu pren una agulha en la qual sia fiel gros fayt de x fiels, e entromet aquel deves le derier del ciphac, le qual es jos la codena dels testicols, la qual siec seccio; e aprop inscideys las extremitatz las quals emineysso del fiel entro que sian quatre fiels, e aprop compausa alcus de lor sobre alcuna figura en manieyra de crotz; e lia am aquel le ciphac del qual havem dit que es dejos la codena dels testicols am fort liament de dos partz.	And then take a needle with a thick thread of 10 threads, and insert it into the last part of the pouch, which is below the code of the testicles, which is the section; and then insert the extremities which emanate from the thread until they are four threads, and then tie them together on some figure in the manner of a cross; and tie with that pouch which we have said that is below the code of the testicles with strong binding of two parts.
E aprop envolveys las extremitatz dels fiels e lia aquelas am liament vehement entro que alcu dels vayssels que noyrrisso aquels no puscan trametre alcuna causa per so que de aqui no accida apostema caut.	And then wrap the extremities of the threads and tie them with strong binding, so that some of the vessels which nourish those cannot transmit any cause by which a abscess may occur here.
E pausa autra veguada liament segon foro le primier liament, lonh de lu mens tres ditz; e aprop aquestz dos liaments layssa del ciphac le qual es dejos la codena dels testicols la quantitat de la grandeza del dit, e inscideys tot le romanent segon redondeza, e osta de lu le huou.	And then pause another binding, similar to the first one, about three times; and then leave that pouch which is below the code of the testicles with the amount of greatness of the said, and insert all the remaining part in a rounded manner, and stop from him the humor.
E aprop inscideys en la partida dejos de la codena dels testicols per seccio de la qual corra sanc e sania ayssi cum havem recomtat en aquo que havem dit.	And then insert into the part below the code of the testicles by section of which blood and pus may flow in such a way as we have recommended above.
E aprop aministra lana submersa en oli, e pausa en la plagua; e aministra le liament le qual havem recomtat (e alcunas veguadas le ciphac blanc es cauterizat, le qual havem dit aprop la inscizio de lu temen de flux de sanc, quar motas veguadas accideys aquels) e leyssa le liament entro que per si caia.	And then administer the linen soaked in oil to the wound; and pause there; and administer the binding which we have recommended (and sometimes the white pouch is cauterized, as we have said above, in order to prevent flux of blood, for many times those things occur) and leave the binding until it falls by itself.
Mays si le cazement de lu es tardat, lahoras de aygua cauda sia embrocat, e pausa sobre aquel entro que caia segon que havem dit.	But if the bleeding is delayed, then let cold water be poured over it, and pause there until it falls as we have said.
E aprop cura la plagua am l’autra curacio de las plaguas entro que sia sanat.	And then cure the wound with the other cure of wounds until it is healed.
Capitol .lxvi.	Chapter LXVI.
De hernia ventosa.	Of Hernia Ventosa.
En aquesta hernia no e vist alcu que sia estat ardit sus la curacio de lu am ferr.	In this hernia, no one has seen anyone who was burned by the cure with iron.
E les primiers diyssero que es fayta ayssi cum havem recomtat en la hernia que es am vi; la qual es que tu lies les vayssels aprop la seccio sobre aquela am fecilitat de lu; e aprop secca en le mieg loc en enviro le apostema am aquo que obro aquel, entro que caian les vayssels.	And the first ones said that it is done just as we have recommended in the hernia which is with wine; which is that you tie up the vessels near the section over there with ease of him; and then cut in the middle place around the abscess with water that brings that about, until the vessels fall.
E cura la plagua segon que havem dit entro que sia sanada.	And cure the wound according to what we have said, until it is healed.
Capitol .lxvii.	Chapter LXVII.
De la disropcio que es fayta en les anguonars.	Of the Disruption that is made in the Anginors.
Alcunas veguadas endeve ruptura en les angonars ayssi cum havem dit, e emineys le loc.	Sometimes a rupture occurs in the anginors just as we have said, and it protrudes to the location.
E no deyssen als genetius alcuna causa dels budels al genetius; e si deyssen, aquo es pauc; e retorna s’en en totas horas.	And there is no need for the genitals to have any cause of the bowels at the genitals; and if there is, it is little; and it returns again in all hours.
Mays si es prolonguat le temps am aquo, es ajustada fissura en le ciphac entro que deysenda le budel en le ciphac; e accideys aquo per la extencio del ciphac le qual es en le angonars ayssi cum havem dit, la qual causa es quar le ciphac es estendut, e aprop es mollificat e·l loc es apostemat e emineys.	But if the time is prolonged with this, it is adjusted fissure in the pouch until it descends into the pouch; and it occurs because of the extension of the pouch which is in the anginors just as we have said, which cause is that the pouch is stretched, and then it becomes softened and the location is abscessed and protrudes.
E la cura de lu es am cauteri ayssi quo es precedida la narracio de lu.	And the cure for this is with a cauterizer just as we have previously described.
E alcunas veguadas es curada am ferr segon aquesta manieyra: e es que·l malaute jagua sobre le sieu dos entre las tuas mas, e aprop secca le loc de la ruptura dels apostemas emineys am seccio per la latitut segon la quantitat de tres ditz.	And sometimes it is cured with iron according to this manner: and it is that the patient lies on his back between your hands, and then cuts the location of the rupture of the abscesses protruding in a section by latitude according to the quantity of three fingers.
E aprop strenh le ciphac blanc que es jos la codena entro que sia descubert.	And then strengthen the white pouch which is below the code until it is revealed.
E aprop pren le ray e pausa aquel sobre le loc eminent del ciphac, e prem aquel al preon del ventre.	And then take a ray and pause that over the protruding part of the pouch, and press that against the belly's forepart.
E aprop cus le dos locs eminentz sobre la extremitat del ray del ciphac, e ajusta am la sutura un de aquels am l’autre.	And then close the two protruding parts over the extremity of the ray of the pouch, and adjust with a suture one to another.
E aprop extratz la extremitat del ray, e no inscidas del ciphac de tot, ni no extenda le huou, ni autra causa ayssi cum yeu te fi saber en la curacio de hernia entestinal.	And then extract the extremity of the ray, and do not insert it into the pouch entirely, nor extend the humor, nor any other cause just as you would know to be in the cure of intestinal hernia.
E aprop cura aquela am la curacio de las plaguas, e cum inscideyses les fiels, mundifica aquela e restaura la plagua entro que sia consolidada; quar le ciphac es contrayt e no es ajustada la eminencia de ruptura.	And then cure that with the cure of wounds, and as you insert the threads, cleanse it and restore the wound until it is consolidated; for the pouch has constricted and the prominence of rupture is not adjusted.
E cauteri es milhor en aquest loc, quar es pus propda a salut.	And cauterization is better in this location, since it is closer to health.
Capitol .lxviii.	Chapter LXVIII.
De mollificacio de la codena dels testiculs.	Of Softening of the Code of the Testicles.
Motas veguadas la codena dels testiculs en alcus homes es mollificada per aysso quar las carns que so entre aquela son mollificadas, e es fedat le reguardament de lu.	Many times the code of the testicles in some men is softened because those fleshy parts that are between it are softened, and it is conducive to its regulation.
Adonc necessari es ad aquel que es preguat en la curacio de lu que fassa jazer le malaute segon le sieu dos, e enscida tota la codena la qual es mollificada sobre la codena natural; e aprop que ajuste doas labias am la sutura.	Therefore it is necessary for the one who is present in the cure to make the patient lie on his back, and insert all the code which is softened over the natural code; and then adjust two lips with a suture.
E si vols, cus en le comensament la superfluitat de la codena mollificada am tres cozeduras o quatre e am ferma sutura.	And if you wish, close at the beginning the excess of the softened code with three or four cauterizations and a firm suture.
E aprop inscideys entre las suturas; e aprop cura per curacio de las autras plaguas entro que sia sanat e caian les fiels.	And then insert between the sutures; and then cure by curing other wounds until it is healed and the threads fall.
Capitol .lxix.	Chapter LXIX.
De castracio.	Of Castration.
Sapias que castratio en nostre ley es excomengada, mays per causa es legut a mi que·m remembre de lu en aquest libre; e no es necessaria la rememoracio de lu sino per doas manieyras, de las quals es la una per so que aquo sia en la sciensa del metge quan es enterroguat de aquela, que sapia la curacio de lu al qual accideys; e l’autra manieyra es que nos motas vetz havem necessitat de castracio de autras bestias per les juvamentz nostres per aquelas, ayssi cum de motos, e de bocs, e de porcs, e de semblantz a las bestias.	Know that castration in our law is excommunicated, but for a reason it has been written to me, so that I may remember it in this book; and it is not necessary to recall it except by two manners, of which one is because of the science of the doctor when he is interrogated about it, knowing the cure of him to whom it occurs; and the other manner is that many times we have needed castration of other beasts for our own purposes through those, just as with horses, oxen, pigs, and similar animals.
E donc dic que castracio es fayta en dos manieyras: o per atrissio, o per fissura a seccio.	And therefore I say that castration is done in two manners: either by incision or by section through a cut.
Mays en aquela que es fayta per atrissio, la via de la opera es que nos fassam cezer la bestia en aygua cauda entro que·ls genetius de lu sian mollificatz e sian linhitz e que pendan.	But in that which is done by incision, the way of the operation is that we make the animal be cut in cold water until its genital parts are softened and tied with linen threads.
E aprop pren aquels am la tua ma entro que sian resols e no apparescan dejos le tocament.	And then take those with your own hand, until they are resolved and do not appear to be left behind the touchment.
Mays en castracio fayta per fissura e seccio, cove que tu tenguas la bestia e premas la codena dels testicols de lu am la ma senestra.	But in castration done by section and cut, it is necessary that you hold the animal and press the code of the testicles with your left hand.
E aprop lia le suspensori, e inscideys sobre quascun huou am una seccio entro que dos huous proceseysso.	And then tie the suspenders and insert one section over each humor until two humors process.
E aprop inscideys aquels pus que auras quascu excorjat.	And then insert those more than you will have excoriated.
E no leysses sobre aquels del ciphac alcuna causa, sino le ciphac subtil le qual es sobre les vazes.	And do not leave any cause on the pouch of the testicles, but only the subtle pouch which is above the veins.
E aquesta manieyra de castracio es milhor la qual es fayta per atrissio, quar atrissio fort leu layssa alcuna causa dels testicols per que la bestia desira coyt.	And this manner of castration is better which is done by incision, because incision does not leave any cause of the testicles so that the animal desires to copulate.
E aprop cura la plagua entro que sia sanada.	And then cure the wound until it is healed.
Capitol .lxx.	Chapter LXX.
De la cura de hermafrodozia.	Of the Cure of Hermaphrodism.
Hermafrodozia en les homes es segon dos manieyras: la una es quar o appar en aquo que siec l’espazi en la codena de testiculs, en aquel que es entre dos testiculs figura quar cunh de femna en la qual so pels.	Hermaphrodism in men is according to two manners: one is when it appears in that which is the space in the code of testicles, between two testicles, a figure like that of a woman's, with breasts.
E alcunas veguadas de aquel corr urina le qual es en la codena dels testiculs.	And sometimes from it flows urine which is in the code of the testicles.
Mays en las femnas es una specia: e es que·l conh de la femna sobre le pentenilh es ayssi cum dos testiculs de home un pauc de tot yminiheys a la partida deforo ayssi cum le perpucii de home e dos testicols.	But in women, it is a species: and it is that the woman's vulva on the pubis is like two testicles of a man a little bit outside, just as the male perineum and two testicles.
E la curacio es de tres specias: de dos dels homes e de una specia de las femnas.	And the cure is of three species: of two of men and one species of women.
E es que cove que tu inscidas aquelas carns ajustadas entro que efuga la emprecio de aquela, e aprop que cures aquelas am curacio de las autras plaguas.	And it is that you must insert those adjusted fleshy parts until it escapes the pressure of that, and then cure those with the cure of other wounds.
E en la segonda specia dels homes de la qual yeys urina la qual es en la codena dels testiculs, no es curacio ni opperacio en lu.	And in the second species of men from which urine flows which is in the code of the testicles, there is no cure or operation in it.
Capitol .xxi.	Chapter XXI.
De lentinge e de carn eminent per causas de las femnas.	Of Leninge and Fleshy Eminence due to Causes of Women.
Lentige fort leu es ajustada sobre causas naturals entro que es etressat e es fayt leg le reguardament; e alcunas veguadas es magnificada en alcunas femnas en tant entro que es spandit ayssi cum en les homes e perve entro al coito.	Leninge is quickly adjusted over natural causes until it is stretched and its regulation is made firm; and sometimes it is magnified in some women to the point where it spreads like in men and penetrates into coitus.
Adonc cove que tu tenguas la superfluitat de lentinge am la tua ma o am unci e inscidas.	Therefore, it is necessary that you take the excess of Leninge with your own hand or with a forceps and insert it.
E no ultimes en inscizio, majorment en le preon de la razit, per so que no endevengua flux de sanc.	And do not leave any excess, especially in the region of the rectum, for fear that blood may flow.
E aprop cura aquela am curacio de las plaguas entro que sia sanada.	And then cure that with the cure of wounds until it is healed.
Mays carn nascuda es carn que nays en le horrifici de la mayre entro que umple aquel, e fort leu es eyssit a las partidas deforo segon semblansa de coa (e per aquo alscus primiers appelero aquo “malautia caudada”); donc cove que nos inscidam ayssi cum inscidem lentinge, e curem aquela entro que sia sanada.	But born flesh is flesh that grows in the horrific of the mare until it fills that, and quickly it is emitted to the outside parts like a cock (and therefore we will call this "malautia caudata"); therefore it is necessary that we insert it just as we insert Leninge, and cure it until it is healed.
Capitol .lxxii.	Chapter LXXII.
De curacio de alratica.	Of the Cure of Alratica.
Alratica es que le conh de la femna no sia perforat, o sia le trauc petit.	Alratica is when a woman's vulva is not perforated or if it is only slightly pierced.
E es o natural o accidental.	And it is either natural or accidental.
Accidental es per malautia la qual ha precedit, e aquela es fayta o per carn nada ajustada o per ciphac subtil o espes.	Accidental is due to disease that has preceded, and it is caused either by flesh not well adjusted or by subtle or thick pouch.
E es fayt o en le preon de la mayre, o en les costatz de lu, o en le pus sobira de lu, o en le pus bas de lu, e prohibeys de cuoyt e de enprenguacio e de enfantament, e fort leu prohibeys las mestruas.	And it is caused either in the back of the mare, or in the sides of him, or in the highest part of him, or in the lowest part of him, and forbids coitus, engagement, and childbearing, and strongly forbids menstruation.
E la cognicio de aquela es fayta per reguardament de la metrona, si la oppilacio es apparent, propdana; mays si no es apparent, lahoras tu cerqua aquela am les tieus ditz o am le ray.	And the knowledge of that is made by examination of the metro-na, if the obstruction is apparent, direct it; but if it is not apparent, then search for it with the threads or with a probe.
Mays si oppilacio es per ciphac subtil, e es propda a las doas labias, lahoras tu coyta e disromp aquela.	But if obstruction is due to subtle pouch and is directed towards the two lips, then you must cut and disrupt that.
E es que pauses sobre las doas labias pulvils, e aprop pausa les tieus ditz indicz de amdoas las mas encemps.	And it is that you pause over the two lips of the pulse, and then pause the threads indicated by both hands at the same time.
E la femna sia sobre le sieu dos, las sieuas coyssas extendudas, e aprop exten las doas labias am forsa entro que aquel ciphac subtil sia romput e la oppilacio sia uberta.	And the woman lies on her back, her arms extended, and then extends the two lips with force until that subtle pouch is broken and the obstruction is opened.
E aprop pren lana e enbeu le4 en oli e pausa aquela sobre·l loc, e jagua am home le dia per so que·l loc inscis no sia consolidat.	And then take lanolin and anoint it with oil and pause that over the location, and lie down as a man by day for so that the location is not consolidated.
Mays si le ciphac es gros e espes, lahoras cove que tu inscidas aquel am spatum lat o am fuelha de mirta.	But if the pouch is thick and dense, then it is necessary that you insert it with a spatula or with myrtle leaves.
Mays si la oppilacio es per carnada, lahoras suspen aquela am unci, e inscideys aquela.	But if the obstruction is due to fleshiness, then suspend that with forceps and insert it.
E sian am tu las medicinas que fan cessar flux de sanc ses mordicacio, ayssi cum ahacatia, e sanc de drago, e enses, ajustat am album de huou.	And are with you the medicines that stop blood flow without biting, such as ahaemia, dragon's blood, and resin, adjusted with album of humor.
E aprop aministra una canulha de plom ampla per so que la plagua no sia consolidada leugierament.	And then administer a leaden cannula wide enough to prevent the wound from being consolidated slightly.
E tengua aquela per alcus jorns e aministra calgua de li sec.	And keep that for some days and administer lukewarm water.
E aprop sia curada am l’autra curacio de consolidacio entro que sia sanada.	And then be cured with another cure of consolidation until it is healed.
E alcunas vetz accideys en la mayre nativitat de autres carns, e lahoras cove que inscidas segon aquesta manieyra.	And sometimes accidents occur in the natural birth of other flesh, and it is necessary that you insert according to this manner.
Mays si aysso es per apostema crancos, a l’apostema crancos le qual es en la mayre no sia fayta contrarietat am ferr en deguna manieyra.	But if it is due to green abscess, then do not make any contradiction with iron in any manner at the green abscess which is in the mare.
Capitol .lxxiii.	Chapter LXXIII.
De la cura de emorroydas e de tayl e de botor roja que accideysso en le conh de las femnas.	Of the Cure of Hemorrhoids and Tail and Red Botch that occurs in the Vulva of Women.
Emorroydas so apprecio dels orificis de motas venas entro que de aquelas corro mot sanc continuadament; e cum so antiquadas emorroydas e son fayts theyls.	Hemorrhoids are an affection of many veins' orifices, until those veins flow with continuous blood; and when old hemorrhoids become formed and their throats are filled.
E ja yeu he dit en la divisio las specias de aquelas e les senhals de aquelas, e diyre ayssi aquelas que recebo curacio e aquelas que no recebo curacio.	And I have already said in the division of those species and signs of those, and to say that those who receive cure and those who do not receive cure.
Donc dic que emorroydas e theyls quan so en le preon de la mayre e no apparo al sentiment, lahoras en aquelas no sia fayta curacio am ferr.	Therefore I say that hemorrhoids and throats when they are in the back of the mare and do not appear to the sense, then in those there is no cure made with iron.
Mays aquelas las quals so en le orrifici de la mayre sobre las quals catz sentiment, so aquelas que so curadas.	But those which are in the orifice of the mare above which one feels sensation, are those that can be cured.
E cove que tu metas la femna en mayso frega e aprop exten atheyl am les forfexs, o am drap aspre, e inscideys aquelas am las razitz.	And it is necessary that you put the woman in a warm bath and then extend the throat with forceps or with rough cloth, and insert those into the roots.
E aprop pulveriza sobre aquelas deves le fluxs del sanc de una de las polveras insciscivas ses mordicacio, ayssi cum acassia e semblant ad aquels.	And then powderize over those the flows of blood from one of the insertable powders without biting, such as acaasia and similar to those.
E aprop enpellesca les sieus pes per una hora, e aprop pausa aquela en aygua freja.	And then apply her feet for an hour, and then pause that in cold water.
E si persevera le fluxs del sanc, lahoras fay aquela sezer en decoccio de sumat e de scorsas de milgranas e de gualas e de semblantz.	And if the bleeding persists, then make that cease in a decoction of Sumatra and scorched millet and gallberries and similar things.
E aprop pren farina de ordi e comfiys aquela am miel e vi agre e fay emplastre am aquo sobre le dos de lu.	And then take oatmeal flour and mix it with honey and vinegar and make an embalmment with water on the back of him.
E si le sanc es abscindit, bo es; e sino, fay adherir am dos ventozas, e a las mamilhas ses escarificatio.	And if the blood is stopped, it is good; and otherwise, make adhere with two poultices, and to the nipples without scarification.
E aprop pren lana e submergeys aquela am suc de coliandre o am suc de arnagloza o am suc de guarravier am vi pentit e fay adherir al loc; e aprop cura le loc am enguentz entro que sia sanat.	And then take lanolin and submerge that in the juice of colicandre or in the juice of arnagloza or in the juice of guarravier with pentit vinegar and make adhere to the location; and then cure the location with ointment until it is healed.
Mays athyl rog le qual es de aspre reguardament, cove que tu inscidas aquo que a tu appar de aquel segon que he dit en theyl engualment.	But if the throat is rough and needs to be treated with harsh consideration, it is necessary that you insert there what appears to you according to what I have said in the previous description.
E cura aquel entro que sia sanat.	And cure that until it is healed.
Capitol .lxxiv.	Chapter LXXIV.
De perforacio de eyssedura accident en la mayre.	Of the Perforation of Accidental Discharge in the Mare.
Motas specias de apostemas accideysso en la mayre, ayssi cum cranc e apostema lapident e ulceracios e adhubelat e erpetromens e fistulas emorroyas e raguarrias e thyl e autres apostemas.	Many species of accidental abscesses occur in the mare, such as green abscess, lapidated abscess, ulcers, adhubelation, erpetromenitis, fistulas, hemorrhoids, and rough throats, and other abscesses.
E yeu ja he dit aquestas malautias e las specias de aquelas e les senhals de aquelas, e las curacios de lor en la divisio.	And I have already said these diseases and the species of those and their signs, and their cures in the division.
E cove que yeu digua en aquest tractat de apostema caut le qual ve en la mayre quan es dels apostemas que collegeysso sania, e si vols saber en qual manieyra se fa la opperacio de lu am ferr.	And it is necessary that you say in this treatise of cauterized abscess which appears in the mare when it is one of the abscesses that requires surgery, and if you want to know how the operation is done with iron.
Adonc cove que tu consideres si la dolor de la apostema en le sieu comensament es aguda am percussio e flecma e febre, e vezes aquel enrogezir e si catz sobre aquel le sentiment, lahoras no·t coytes am perforacio de lu, e cura aquel am aquo que ajuda sobre la maturacio entro que cesse la acuitat dels accidentz.	Therefore it is necessary that you consider whether the pain of the abscess in its initial stages is sharp with percussion and inflammation and fever, and at times becomes inflamed and if one feels sensation on it, then do not open it by perforation, but cure it with water that helps with maturation until the acuity of the accident subsides.
E lahoras cove que tu fassas cezer la femna sobre una cezelha que aia doas cezelhas; e recline sobre le sieu dos e ajusta les sieus pes a la partida pus dejos del ventre, e las sieus coyssas sian expandudas, e pausa les sieus brasses dejos les sieus denols, e lia quascus am liament ad aquo convenient.	And then it is necessary that you make the woman lie on a cushion that has two cushions; and recline on her back and adjust her feet at the lowest part of the belly, and her arms be expanded, and pause her hands below her nails, and tie each one with a ligament to water suitable.
