E aprop la matrona segua del latz dreyt e aministre le instrument am le qual es ubert le orrifici de la mayre, la forma del qual vindra en aquelas causas que·s faran aprop.	And then the midwife follows directly and administers the instrument with which the orifice of the mare is opened, in the shape that will come forth according to those causes that are about to be made.
E cove quan vols ministrar aquest instrument que tu fiques am lo ray le preon de la mayre de la femna, e aquo que del instrument es intrat en la mayre no sia mays que·l preon de la mayre e leda le malaute.	And then it is necessary when you want to administer this instrument that you make it in the shape of a ray on the back of the mare of the woman, and what is entered into the mare from the instrument is not more than the back of the mare and leads the patient.
Mays si l’estrument es major que·l preon de la mayre, lahoras cove que tu pauses pulvils sobre la textura del preon de la mayre per sso que sia prohibit l’intrament de tot instrument en le preon de la mayre.	But if the instrument is greater than the back of the mare, then it is necessary that you powderize over the texture of the back of the mare so that it prohibits the entrance of any instrument into the back of the mare.
E cove que tu pauses le vertitge que corr en le strument del latz pus desus e que le ministre tengua le strument e revolva le vertitge entro que sia ubert le orrifici de la mayre.	And then it is necessary that you pause the vertebrae which runs in the instrument of the left side and above, and that the minister hold the instrument and turn the vertebrae so that the orifice of the mare is opened.
E cum appar la excitura, e es tocada am la ma e es leon e molh, lahoras cove que tu secces aquela deves le cap de lu am spatum lat.	And when the excitation appears and is touched with the hand and is lion-like and moist, then it is necessary that you dry that part of the head of him with a spatula.
E cum la sania es evacuada, lahoras cove que tu pauses en la plagua una meca submersa en oli rozat o oli vert en le qual sia alcuna stiptisitat; e pausa la calca7 en la seccio en le preon de la mayre.	And when the pus is evacuated, then it is necessary that you pause in the wound a poultice submerged in rose oil or green oil with some stiptic properties; and pause the caustic in the section on the back of the mare.
E pause deforo la mayre e sobre le pentenilh lana munda submersa en aygua en la qual sian bulidas malvas.	And then pause before the mare and above the pubic area a clean lanolin submerged in water in which mulberries have been boiled.
E aprop sia curada aprop dos dias am enguent le qual conveneys ad aquo entro que sia sanat.	And then be cured within two days with ointment which is suitable for that until it is healed.
E alcunas veguadas es lavada la mayre e la plagua enayssi que es cristerisat am aygua e mel, e aprop am aygua en la qual es bulhida razit de liri o de aristologia longua, e aprop retorna al enguent.	And sometimes the mare is washed and the wound is cleaned with water and honey, and then applied with water in which is boiled root of lily or long aristology, and then returns to the ointment.
E si la plagua es dedintz en la mayre ameguada, lahoras cove que tu sias prohibit de la curacio de lu am ferr, habantz cura aquel am aquo que havem dit en la divisio.	And if the wound is deep in the mare's udder, then it is necessary that you be prohibited from curing it with iron, having cured it with water as we have said in the division.
Capitol .lxxv.	Chapter LXXV.
A ensenhar las matronas en qual manieyre les enbrios bius sian medicatz quan yeysso segon figura no-natural.	To teach midwives how to medicate children's bodies when they are sick according to an unnatural figure.
Necessaria causa es que la matrona conogua en le comensament la figura del enfantament natural per senhals de lu, e es que quan tu vezas la femna expremar a las partidas dejos e desira odorar le ayre, e sobre aquo es enleujada per aquo que sobre ela es del part, e festina le eyssiment del enbrio, lahoras sapias que aquest part es segon figura natural, e es l’eyssiment de lu sobre le sieu cap, e la segondina am aquel o suspensa o pendent del ombelic.	It is necessary that the midwife knows at the beginning the figure of natural childbirth by signs from above, and is that when you see the woman expelling at the lower partings and desires to smell the air, and above this is relieved by what is on her, and hastens the emission of the child, then you know that this part is according to a natural figure, and it is the emission of the child over its head, and the secondine with that or suspended or hanging from the umbilicus.
Donc cum tu vezes aquels senhals, lahoras cove que·l ventre de lu sia compremut per so que l’embrio deysenda leugerament quar quan deyssen sobre le sieu cap, deysen a lu la segondina, e es mondada de aquelas superfluitatz am bona mondificacio.	Therefore, when you see those signs, then it is necessary that the child's belly be compressed so that the child descends slightly because when they are born over its head, they give secondine to it, and it is cleansed of those superfluities with good cleansing.
Mays aquel que es otra aquest part es no-natural e no-lausable, quar quan le enbrio es eyssit sobre sos pes e·l cos de lu es eyssit devant le cap de lu e·ls pes de lu, e la ma de lu una, o al pe de lu .i., o es eyssit le cap de lu e la ma de lu, o al ventre de lu, e fort leu es convertit sobre le sieu col, e semblant de las figuras de lu no-lausablas.	But that which is another part is not natural and not acceptable, because when the child is born over its feet and its body is born before its head and its feet, and the hand of it one or at the foot of it, ..., or is born the head of it and its hand, or at the belly of it, and very strongly it is converted over its neck, and similar to the figures of it not acceptable.
Don necessaria causa es a la matrona que sia savia e subtil en totas aquelas causas, e que·s guarde de error e de decepcio.	Therefore, it is necessary that the midwife be wise and subtle in all those causes, and that she guards against error and deception.
E yeu so mostrant tota figura de aquelas, e qual engen es en aquelas per so que sia significat per aquo e sia stat sobre aquo.	And you are showing the whole figure of those, and what kind of sign is in them so that it may be signified by that and has been on that.
Quan le feyt es eyssit sobre le sieu cap per egrecio natural, e aquel es vehement sobre la femna e es fayt a lu part dificil, e vezes la vertut de lu ja debelitada, lahoras fay aquela sezer , o que las femnas tenguan lu, e evapora le conh de lu am fenugrec coyt e am olis humitz.	When the child is born over its head by natural extraction, and that is vehement on the woman and is made to her part difficult, and sometimes the virtue of it already weakened, then make that cease, or that women have it, and evaporate the womb with fenugreek powder and moist oil.
E aprop entrometa la metrona entre les sieus ditz espatum petit e fenda am aquel la segondina, o secce aquela am la sua ungla entro que corro aquo que es en ela de humiditat.	And then insert the metro-na between the two said spatula and gap with that, or cut it with its own nail into what is in her of humidity.
E preme le ventre de la femna entro que deyssenda le fet.	And press the woman's belly until the fetus descends.
Mays si no deyssen, lahoras cove que la femna sia cristirizada de mucellage de ptilli e mucellage de fenugrec am cizami.	But if it does not descend, then it is necessary that the woman be cleansed with ptilly mucus and fenugreek mucus with camomile.
E aprop comanda a lu, aprop le cristeri, que sia compremuda e fay aquela stornudar am condisi; e te la boca de lu e·l nas de lu per huna hora, quar le fet sira foro-getat tantost.	And then command it to him, and to the cleanser, that it be compressed and make it sneeze with condiments; and take his mouth and nose for an hour, because the fetus will soon forget.
E si las doas mas del fet so foro-getadas al comensament, lahoras cove que tu redusiscas aquelas am fecilitat petit a petit.	And if the two hands of the fetus are forgotten at the beginning, then it is necessary that you reduce them with small steps of ease.
Mays si no obezeys al intrament, lahoras pausa la femna sobre una cezelha e leva les pes de lu sus, e aprop concuceys la cezelha sobre la terra; e la femna sia tenguda que no caia deves la concussio.	But if it does not obey the instrument, then pause the woman on a cushion and lift her feet up, and then conceive the cushion on the ground; and the woman be held so that she does not fall from the conception.
E si las mas no son dedintz tornadas e morr le fet, lahoras inscideys aquelas e extratz le romament del fet o lia le cors a la ma de lu am drap e extratz aquel am equalitat, quar aquel sira foro-getat.	And if the hands are not returned and the fetus dies, then insert those and extract the remnant of the fetus or tie the body to the hand of it with cloth and extract that with equality, because it will soon be forgotten.
De eyssiment del embrio sobre les sieus pes.	The Birth of the Fetus on its Feet.
Quan le fet yeys sobre les sieus pes, lahoras cove que tu impelliscas aquels en sus, e aprop convertas le fet petit, e aprop que engualhes aquel, e aprop que prenguas un pe de lu e extendas aquels petit a petit.	When the fetus is born on its feet, then it is necessary that you impel them inwards, and then convert the small fetus into one, and then bring forth one foot of it and extend those little by little.
Mays cum son eyssit entro a las coyssas, lahoras tu comanda a lu que se exprema, e fay aquela extornudar am condizi, quar sira foro-getat si Deus lo vol.	But when they are born into the armpits, then you command it to come forth, and make it sneeze with condiments, because it will soon be forgotten if God so wills.
E si no es foro-getat am aquo que havem recomtat, lahoras tu retorna le fet petit a petit entro que pauses aquel segon figura natural, quar aquel sira lahoras foro-getat am leugier eyssiment.	And if it is not forgotten with what we have recounted, then you return the small fetus little by little until it pauses according to natural figure, because that will be forgotten at a lighter birth.
E si es prohibit am tot aquo que havem recomtat, lahoras pren de musellage de altea e de goma dissolvuda, e percuteys tot en le mortier per bona percussio, e aprop linieys am aquo le conh de la femna, el pus bas del ventre de lu.	And if it is prohibited by all that we have recounted, then take mugwort and dissolved gum, and strike everything in the mortar for good striking, and then line up with water the vulva of the woman, at the lowest part of her belly.
E aprop fay aquela cezer en aygua tebeza, entro que consegua les ypocondias.	And then make that cease in warm water until it reaches the hypochondria.
E cum vezes que las partidas dejos de lu so lenificadas, lahoras fay a lu subfumiguacio de mirta e sub-pausa aquela a lu.	And when the lower parts of it are relaxed, then make a sub-fumigation with myrtle and pause that on it.
E quan te la sub-fumiguacio per una hora, lahoras tu la fay sezer sobre una cezelha, e aprop fay aquela stornudar e extrenh la boca de lu, e levas de aquela, e prem la partida pus bassa del ventre de lu am leugiera compressio, quar le fet sira tantost foro-getat.	And when the sub-fumigation is done for an hour, then you make it cease on a cushion, and then make that sneeze and extend its mouth, and take it from there, and press the lower part of her belly with gentle compression, so that the fetus will soon be forgotten.
Eyssiment del fet sobre les sieus denols e las suas mas.	Birth of the Fetus on its own fingers and thumbs.
Quan le fet eyssira segon aquesta forma, lahoras tu engenies en entrometen las suas mas petit a petit; e aprop la femna stia evessada sobre le sieu col, e les pes de lu pengo en jos, e aquelas sia jasent sobre le lieyt, e complegua las suas mas.	When the fetus is born in this form, then you ease its fingers little by little; and then the woman lies on her back, and her feet hang down, and those are resting on the bed, and complete its fingers.
E aprop prem sobre le ventre de lu petit a petit, e aprop extratz aquo que es dejos les pes de lu de las aurelhas entro que sia preparada en la partida pus dejos.	And then press on her belly little by little, and then extract what is left from her feet to the ears, until it is prepared in the lower part.
E si le fet no es fora-getat, lahoras pren les pes de lu e mau aquels am movement vehement, e aprop prem aquo que es sobre les ypocondres petit a petit entro que le fet puege a las partidas desus.	And if the fetus is not forgotten, then take her feet and move them with a vehement motion, and then press that which is above on the hypochondria little by little until the fetus reaches the upper parts.
E aprop entrometa las suas mas e engualhe le fet petit a petit, e comanda a la femna que se exprema entro que le fet sia foro-getat.	And then insert its fingers and bring forth the fetus little by little, and command the woman to come forth until the fetus is forgotten.
Eyssiment del fet latutidinalment pendent una de las suas mas.	Birth of the Fetus sideways hanging one of its fingers.
Sia engeniat en reduccio de la ma de lu, mays si no podes aquela reduzir, lahoras eleva la femna e fe aquela anar.	It is eased into reduction with the hand of her, but if you cannot reduce that, then lift up the woman and make her go.
E si anar no pot, lahoras fay la jazer sobre le lieyt, e concuteys las coyssas de lu am concussio vehement, e aprop aministra liamentz les quals yeu e recomtatz de mucillages.	And if she cannot go, then make her lie down on the bed, and conceive the armpits of her with violent concussion, and then administer lukewarm lukewarms which we have recounted.
E si es vengut le enfantament, lahoras fay aquela sezer sobre cezelha, e aprop studia sobre la reduccio de la ma, e enguala le fet segon figura natural, e fay stornudar la femna e comanda a lu que comprema a si entro que sia foro-getat.	And if the childbirth is complete, then make that cease on a cushion, and then study on the reduction of the hand, and bring forth the child according to natural figure, and make the woman sneeze and command it to compress itself until it is forgotten.
Eyssiment del fet sobre·l col expandudas las suas mas e la fassia de lu es al dos de la sua mayre.	Birth of the Fetus with its fingers spread out and the fold of it on the back of the mother's shoulder.
Cove que la matrona tengua la ma del fet e aprop revolva aquel petit a petit, e eque aquel am facilitat.	It is necessary that the midwife take the hand of the fetus and then turn it little by little, and make it easy for it.
E cum es e quant so es engualhat, e lahoras pausa sobre le conh de lu aquo que havem recomtat de oli e de mucellages.	And when it is and when it is equalized, then pause on the vulva of her with that which we have recounted of oil and mucus.
E aprop comandas a lu que·s maugua petit a petit, e quan auras feyt aquo, lahoras fay aquela cezer sobre una cezelha e comanda li que sia inclinada sobre le latz dreyt, e aprop comanda a lu que sia compremuda; e fay aquela stornudar am condizi.	And then command it to be massaged little by little, and when you have done that, then make that cease on a cushion and command it to be inclined over the right side, and then command it to be compressed; and make it sneeze with condiments.
Exitus foetus praeparati super latus.	The exit of the prepared fetus onto the side.
Quan deyssen a horrifici de la mayre segon aquesta manieyra, considera, e lahoras tu inscideys la segondina am la tua ungla entro que sia evacuada de la humiditat.	When the horror of the mother is over according to this manner, consider, and then you insert the secondine with your nail until it is evacuated of humidity.
E si le fet es suspendut sobre la cara e·l col de lu, lahoras tu inscideys aquela del embelic, per so que no sia retengut e mora.	And if the fetus is suspended over the face and back of her, then you insert that of the umbilicus, in order that it not be retained and die.
E aprop empelleys le fet a las partidas dedintz entro que pauses aquel segon que cove, e manda a la femna que comprema a si alcunas veguadas, e el sira fora-getat am eyssiment leugier, si Dieus o vol.	And then push the fetus into the lower parts until it pauses according to what is necessary, and command the woman to compress herself several times, and if God so wills, it will be forgotten at a lighter birth.
Exitus geminorum aut foetuum multorum.	The exit of twins or multiple fetuses.
Sapias que gemels motas veguadas so natz, e alcunas vetz naysso tres o quatre , mays aquo es estranh e tart s’endeve; mays v so causas foro natura, e no vivo.	Know that twins are sometimes born multiple times, and sometimes three or four, but this is strange and does not end well; yet there are causes of nature, and they do not live.
E conte aquelas, ja sia que sian montiplicatz, una segondina, e son seperatz per ciphac, distingen aquels enter le liguament en l’ombilic de cascun de aquels E alcunas veguadas so foro-getatz ayssi cum es un fet per eyssiment natural leugier, e so eysitz alcunas veguadas per eyssiment no-lausabla ayssi cum havem recomtat.	And then, whether they are multiple or not, a secondine is formed, and they are separated by ciphac, distinguishing them between the ligament in the umbilic of each of those. And sometimes they are forgotten like one fetus at a lighter birth, and sometimes they are born non-naturally like what we have recounted.
E si son dificils alcus de lor deves le enfantament e perveno ad aquo que havem dit de las figuras no-naturals, lahoras tu cura aquels ayssi cum havem recontat.	And if some of them are difficult to deliver and come to what we have said about the non-natural figures, then you cure those just as we have recounted.
E si’ la matrona subtil e fassa aquo que fa am facilitat e subtilitat, e am tarditat, e sia ingeniat segon tota figura segon que es a lu preparat de l’engen amenant a salut.	And if the midwife is subtle and makes it so that it brings about ease and subtlety, and in tardiness, and is inclined according to all figure as it is prepared by nature leading to salvation.
Rememoratio eius quod formatur in matrice ex embrionibus et Abortiuntur.	Remembrance of what is formed in the womb from embryos and aborted fetuses.
Alcunas veguadas son formatz en la mayre un, e dos, e tres, e quatre, e v, e vi, e vii, e mays x, e ja es deves mi verificat que una femna abortem ne getet vi, e una autra x totz formatz, la qual causa fo fayta per mensuracio dels glorios savis.	Some women are formed in multiples of one, two, three, four, five, six, seven, and up to ten, and it is necessary for me to verify that one woman aborts at the seventh month, and another has all her children, which was caused by measurement according to the wise sages.
E tot aysso cove que sia en la sciencia de la matrona quar fort leu ad aquela parve semblant de aquo, e donc opause se ad aquo am so que cove.	And thus it is necessary for the midwife to have knowledge of this because very much alike is similar to that, and therefore pause at that point with so many as are needed.
Capitol .lxxvi.	Chapter LXXVI.
De extraccio del fet quan es mort.	On the extraction of the fetus when it is dead.
Quan tu curas le fet mort am aquo que havem dit en la divisio de la medicacio e no es defora eyssit, e tu yest forsat usar de opperacio am ma, lahoras cove que consideras si la femna es de sana vertut e no es am alcu dels accidentz per les quals sobre ela es temuda perdicio.	When you treat the dead fetus with what we have said in the division of medicine and it is not forthwith extracted, and you are forced to use operation by hand, then it is necessary that you consider if the woman has a healthy virtue and is not affected by any of the accidents whereby upon her is feared destruction.
Lahoras cove que la femna sia envessada sobre le lieyt sobre le sieu dos, e sia le cap de lu enclinat enjos e las coyssas de lu sian elevadas.	Then it is necessary that the woman be laid on her back on a bed, and have her head inclined downwards and her armpits elevated.
E·l ministre tengua aquela de doas partz o sia liada en le lieyt per so que·l cos de lu no se extenda deves la extraccio del fet.	And the attendant shall hold that in two parts or bind it on the bed, for the sake of the body not extending too far during the extraction of the fetus.
E aprop tu humecta la boca de la mayre de lu am olis humitz e am mucellage de altea e de fenugrec e de semensa de li.	And then you moisten the mouth of the mother with oil and mucus, and with mugwort and fenugreek and seed of flax.
E aprop unte la matrona la sua ma am aquels olis e mucellages, e aprop entrometa la sua ma am fecilitat en la mayre, e aprop cerque am la ma loc en le qual fique les uncis en le fet.	And then the midwife inserts her hand with those oils and mucus into the mother's body, and then eases it in with facility, and then searches for the spot where the fingers will rest on the fetus.
E locs convenient en aquo: adonc tu considera si le fet es preparat que deysenda sobre le sieu cap, e lahoras tu fique les uncis en les huels de lu, o en le col, o en la boca, o en le palat, o dejos la barba, o en la furcula de lu, o en les locs propdas de las costas, o dejos les ypocondres.	And finds a suitable spot: then you consider if the fetus is prepared to descend onto its head, and then place your fingers on the nose of it, or on the neck, or in the mouth, or on the palate, or below the beard, or in the furrow of it, or in the places proper for the ribs, or below the hypochondria.
Mays si le deysendiment es sobre les pes de lu, lahoras en le pentenilh, o en le mieg de las costas.	But if the descent is onto the feet of it, then in the armpit or in the middle of the ribs.
E cove que tengua le unci am la ma dreyta, e pausa la curvitat de lu en aquel loc le qual es entre les ditz de la ma senestra, e entrometa la ma am facilitat e fique le unci en alcu de aquels locs les quals havem ditz, entro que pervengua a la causa boyda.	And it is necessary to take the fingers with the right hand, and pause the curvature of it at that spot which is between the said bones of the left arm, and insert the hand with ease and place the fingers in some of those spots which we have said, until one comes to the cause of birth.
E aprop pause e fique en la apposicio de lu un autre unci, o le tertz si es necessitat, per so que sia atraccio engual, e no sia extencio segon la sua rectetut tant solament.	And then pause and place another finger or the third if necessary, for a drawing equalization, and not an extension according to its straightness only.
Ans sia maugut a tota partida, per so que l’eyssiment de lu sia alleujat ayssi cum es fayt en dent deves la eradicacio de lu.	And thus be good at all part, for that the delivery of it is alleviated as if made in debt towards the eradication of it.
E cove en lu aquo que es entre lor que la extencio sia mollificada; e si alcuna partida de lu es retenguda, lahoras cove que la matrona unte alcus sieus ditz am oli e entrometa aquels espertament e revolva am aquels aquo que es retengut.	And it is necessary in that which is between them that the extension be softened; and if any part of it is retained, then the midwife must anoint some of its bones with oil and insert those expertly and turn around with those waters which are retained.
Donc si la partida del fet es fora-getada, lahoras les uncis sian permudatz entra loc le qual sia pus aut; e fay aysso entro que tot le fet sia fora-getat.	Therefore, if the part of the fetus is forgotten, then the fingers must be made pliable to get into the place where it is higher up; and make so that the entire fetus is forgotten.
Mays si la ma es eyssida denant l’autra, e no es possible reduzir aquela per la coartacio de lu, lahoras cove que drap sia envolopat sobre aquela; e aprop extratz aquela entro que tota sia fora-getada, e inscideys aquela o en la junctura de la ma o en le coyde.	But if the hand is stuck before the other, and it is not possible to reduce that by the contraction of it, then it is necessary to wrap a cloth around that; and then extract that until all is forgotten, and insert it either at the junction of the arm or in the armpit.
E ayssi cove que fassas en l’autra ma e en les dos pes.	And thus it is necessary to do so with the other hand and both feet.
Mays si le cap del fet es gran, o accideys a lu coartacio en le eyssiment, o es en le cap de lu aygua ajustada, lahoras cove que entrometa entre les ditz espatum spinos e fenda le cap e extragua la aygua, o que discroba aquel am un instrument le qual es nompnat “alundat”, la forma del qual vindra am las formas dels autres instruments en le capitol le qual es aprop aquest.	But if the head of the fetus is large, or there occurs contraction during delivery, or water is adjusted in the head, then it is necessary to insert between the bones spines and cut the head and drain the water, or that dissects that with an instrument which is called "alundat", whose form will come with the forms of other instruments in the chapter which is next to this.
E semblantment fassa si·l fet es de gran cap per natura: e lahoras cove que inscida aquel am algematu, o que prengua aquel am alunda ayssi cum havem dit; e aprop extra les osses am les forceps.	And similarly do so if the fetus is naturally large-headed: and then it is necessary to insert that with an algemate, or take that with an alundat as we have said; and then extract the bones with forceps.
E si le cap es eyssit e es coartat deves la furcula, lahoras sia fendut entro que la humiditat la qual es en le pietz sia efunduda.	And if the head is extracted and is contracted at the furrow, then it is necessary to cut through until the moisture which is in the feet is poured out.
Mays si no es complicat, ni obezeys a eyssiment, lahoras tu inscideys le cap tantost segon que a tu sira possible.	But if it is not complicated, nor follows extraction, then you should insert the head as soon as possible according to what seems best to you.
E si le dejos del ventre es apostemat o es en lu ydropici, lahoras cove que tu perfores aquel entro que corro la humiditat que es en lu.	And if the afterbirth is apostematic or is in a state of hydroptic swelling, then it is necessary to perforate that until the moisture which is in it runs out.
Mays si le fet es sobre les sieus pes, lahoras la atraccio de lu es leugiera e la direccio de lu a la boca de la mayre es leugiera.	But if the fetus is on its feet, then the attraction of it is slight and the direction of it to the mouth of the mother is slight.
Mays si es coartat deves le ventre e·l pietz, lahoras cove que tu extraguas aquel am drap le qual auras envolopat sobre la tua ma, e que fendes le ventre e·l pietz entro que corra aquo que es en aquels.	But if it is contracted in the belly and feet, then it is necessary to extract that with cloth which you have wrapped around your hand, and cut open the belly and feet until the water that is in them flows out.
Mays si les autres membres so ostatz e torna le cap, lahoras la metrona entrometa la ma senestra; mays si la boca de la mayre es huberta, lahoras intrometa la ma en le preon de layre, e cerque am aquela le cap, e atira aquel am les ditz entro a la boca de la mayre, e aprop entrometa en lu un unci, o dos uncis, e atire lu am aquels.	But if the other members are still and turn back to the head, then put your left hand into it; but if the mouth of the mother is swollen, then insert your hand into the pelvis, and search for that head, and pull it with those fingers into the mouth of the mother, and then put one finger, or two fingers, into it, and draw it along with them.
E si la boca de la mayre es coartada per apostema caut le qual accideys a l’u, lahoras cove que no sia trebelhat sobre lu; abantz cove lahoras aministrar efusio de causas humidas grassas.	And if the mouth of the mother is contracted by an apostematic swelling which comes to one, then it is necessary that no trouble be given about it; but rather administer an effusion of humid and fatty causes.
E aministre emplastres; e segua le pacient en ayguas que mollifican e humectan.	And minister plasters; and follow the patient with waters that soften and moisten.
E si le fet es sobre le sieu costat, lahoras si possible es, sia agulat: e sia aministrat aquo que havem dit en le fet viu.	And if the fetus is on its side, then if possible, it should be punctured: and water that we have said in the living fetus should be administered.
E si aquo no es possible, lahoras sia inscidit en pessas, e sia extrayt.	And if this is not possible, then insert it into pillows, and extract it.
E cove que non layssas alcuna causa dedintz de la segondina.	And it is necessary that no cause be left behind the secondine.
E cum tu auras complida tota la tua opperacio, lahoras aministra aquo que havem dit de la curacio en les apostemas cautz les quals accideysso de la mayre.	And when you have completed all your operation, then administer the water that we have said for the cure of apostematic swellings which occur in the mother.
E si accideys flux de sanc, lahoras deyssendas en ayguas stipticas e aministra l’autra curacio.	And if bleeding occurs, then administer purgative waters and give the other treatment.
E yeu ja e vist una femna en le ventre de la qual era fet mort, e aprop sobre aquel foc autra veguada emprenhada, e aprop foc mort es le fet autre.	And I have already seen a woman in whose womb was a dead fetus, and then another pregnancy had begun, and the dead fetus was another.
Accidit al u aprop lonc temps apostema en le sieu embelic; e inflat es entro que foc ubert, e comensec a getar brac.	An accident occurred to me, about a long time ago, an apostematic swelling in my own umbilicus; and it inflated so that it became a large boil, and began to suppurate.
E yeu fu appelhat a la cura de lu, e medicat a lu per lonc temps, e la plagua no es consolidada.	And I was called to the cure of it, and medicated it for a long time, but the wound did not consolidate.
Adonc yeu pausegui sobre lu de alscunas causas emplastra de forta atraccio, e eyssic de lu un os, e aprop passero alcus jorns, e eyssic un autre os; e yeu fu trop meravilhat, cum en le ventre no sia os.	Then I applied to it some plaster of strong attraction, and extracted from it a bone, and after passing some days, extracted another bone; and I was too astonished, as in the belly there is no bone.
E adonc yeu cogitegui que eran dels osses del fet mort.	And then I thought that they were the bones of the dead fetus.
Donc yeu enguisigui la plagua, e extrayssi de lu motz osses , la femna existent en las sieuas milhos disposicios, e ja visquec en tal manieyra per lonc temps, correc de lu un petit de brac.	Then I examined the wound, and extracted from it many bones, the woman existing in her own milks and dispositions, and already living in such a way for a long time, brought forth one small piece of flesh.
E yeu no afermegui asso esser stranh, sino quar en aquo es sciensa e ajutori ad aquo que le metge artifec am la ma per curacio aministra.	And I did not find it strange, but rather because in that is science and aid to that which the physician-artificer administers with his hand for cure.
De las formas dels instrumentz que so necessaris a extrayre le fet.	Of the forms of instruments that are necessary to extract the fetus.
Forma de vertitge am la qual es uberta la mayre:	Form of vertex which is opened in the mother:
Aquesta es la forma de strenhedor en le qual so engualhatz les libres, al qual engualhament sian dos virtitges en doas extremitatz de dos futz.	This is the form of strengthener in which are equalized the freed limbs, to which equalization two vertebrae are joined at two extremities of two feet.
May empero aquesta virtitge cove que sia pus subtil de strictori, e sia fayt o de eba o de fust de boys.	And however this vertebra must be more subtle than the strictor, and made of ebony or of boxwood.
E sia la latitut de quascun fust quays dos ditz e le marge de quascu amdos quays un dit, e la longitut de quascu es un palm e mig; e en le mieg loc de dos fustz so dos ajustaments de aquel meteys fustz les quals ja son fermatz, dels quals la longitut es la maytat de un palm e un pauc mes, e la latitut de quascu es quay dos ditz, o un pauc mes.	And the length of each stick is two fingers and a half; and in the middle place of two sticks are two adjustments of those same sticks which are already fixed, the length of which is one palm and a little more, and the width of each is two fingers or a little more.
E aquestz dos additamentz sian entromeses en la boca de la mayre per que sia uberta am aquels quan tu revolves las doas prescriptas virtigges.	And these two adjustments are inserted into the mouth of the mother so that it is opened to receive them when you revolve the two prescribed vertebrae.
Forma autra semblant de aquela pus subtil e pus leugiera:	Another form similar to that one, more subtle and lighter:
Sia fayta de fustz de eba o de boys segon la semblansa de forceps.	Is made of sticks of ebony or boxwood according to the likeness of forceps.
Mays empero en la extremitat de lu so dos additament ayssi cum vezes, e la longitut de aquels additament es quays un palm, e la latitut de quascu es dos ditz.	But in the extremity of it are two additional pieces like that, and the length of those additions is one palm, and the width of each is two fingers.
E cum tu vols am aquels ubrir la mayre, lahoras tu fay cezer la femna sobre le lieyt les pes pendentz, ubert aquo que es entre las coyssas de lu.	And when you want to open the mother with those, then you must make the woman lift her feet off the bed and bend over, opening what is between her armpits.
E aprop obre la tua ma am le instrument ayssi cum fas am forfexs engualment segon la quantitat que vols de la aprecio de la boca de la mayre entro que la metrona fassa so que vols.	And then, with your hand on the instrument, as you would make forceps equalize according to the quantity that you want of the appreciation of the mouth of the mother until she makes what you want.
La forma de vertitge la qual diysero les antics:	The form of vertex which was said by the ancients:
Forma de impellent am le qual es empellit le fet:	Form of impeller, with which the fetus is impelled:
Forma de amisidat2 am le qual es conterit le cap gran	Form of misdirection, with which the large head is counteracted.
E es asemblat a forceps al qual so dentz en la extremitat, ayssi cum vezes, e alcunas veguadas es fayt lonc ayssi cum forceps segon aquesta forma, ayssi cum vezes, al qual so dentz ayssi cum dentz de ressegua am le qual es inscidit e conterit.	And it is assembled to forceps which has teeth on the extremity, like times, and some times is made long like forceps according to this form, like times, to which teeth are similar to teeth of a saw that is inserted and counteracted.
Forma de amesidat pauc:	Form of misdirection slightly:
Forma de unci havent una spina:	Form of finger having one spine:
Forma de unci havent doas spinas:	Form of fingers having two spines:
Forma de forceps a la qual so dentz de cerra am le qual le cap del fet sia conterit:	Form of forceps to which are teeth of a saw with which the head of the fetus is counteracted.
Forma de spatum havent dos extremitatz am le qual le cap es abscindit:	Form of spine having two extremities, with which the head is cut off.
Forma de dos espatums latz:	Form of two lateral spines:
Totz aquels instrumentz so excersitatz, e quan mes so multiplicadas las specias de aquel e so preparadas deves le artifexs, quant es pus leugier a la sua opperacio e pus aut deves les homes per la sua quantitat.	All those instruments are exercised, and when more species of them are multiplied and prepared, then the artisans should be more skilled in their operation and have greater quantity of them.
E no obres de aquels instrumentz ja sia qua sia deves tu aparalhat, quar la necessitat de aquels no es excusabla.	And do not neglect those instruments however small they may be, because the necessity for them is inexcusable.
De extraccio de la segondina.	Of the extraction of the secondine.
Quan la segondina es retenguda deves le enfantament, lahoras cove que tu comandes a la malautae que retengua le sieu ale, e aprop fay aquela stornudar am condizi, e strenh la tua ma sobre la boca de lu e sobre las nars de lu, e si per aysso es defora eyssit, bo es.	When the secondine is retained in childbirth, then it is necessary to command the patient to retain her breath and then make that stornudate under certain conditions, and strengthen your hand over the mouth and nostrils of it, and if by this means it has been expelled, good is.
E sino, lahoras tu pren una ola e perfora en la cuberta un trauc e pausa en aquela erbas ubrent la boca de la mayre, ayssi cum calament e ruda e anet e camamilla e scicados arabic e cassia lignea e santaurea.	And if not, then you take a cloth and pierce it in the cover of a hole and pause in that herb which opens the mouth of the mother, like calament, ruda, anet, camomilla, Arabian squill, and cassia lignea, and saffron.
Totas aquestas erbas o alcunas de lor sian submersas en aygua en la ola, e pausa aquela sobre le foc.	All these herbs or some of them are submerged in water in the cloth, and pause that on the fire.
E aprop pausa una canula de canaviera en la boca de la mayre, e tengua aquela entro que la evapor vengua a la concavitat de la mayre.	And then pause a reed of cane in the mouth of the mother, and hold it until the evaporation comes to the concavity of the mother.
E aprop fay aquela stornudar ayssi cum havem dit, e la segondina sira fora-getada am velocitat.	And then make that stornudate as we have said, and the secondine is expelled quickly.
Mays si roman aprop aquesta curacio e no es eyssida, lahoras tu comanda a la matrona que submerge la sua ma sinistra en oli sizami o en micellage de altea, e aprop entrometa aquela en le conh e queresca am aquela la segondina, e cum aquela auras trobada, lahoras pren la e exten aquela pauc a pauc Mays si es annexsa en le preon de la mayre, lahoras entrometa la sua ma segon que havem recomtat, e quan aura trobat la segondina, extragua aquela petit a petit segon rectetut per so que la mayre no caja deves la atraccio vehement.	But if this cure does not work and the secondine remains, then you command the midwife to immerse her left hand in sesame oil or in a mixture of high-quality alta, and insert it into the concavity and seek out the secondine, and when she has found it, take it and stretch it little by little. But if it is annexed in the pelvis of the mother, then insert your hand according to what we have recounted, and when you have found the secondine, extract it gradually, following its natural course, so that the mother does not suffer from the strong attraction.
Abantz cove que sia permudada als costatz dreyt e sinestre am facilitat.	Before all, it is necessary to make it pliable at the right and left sides with ease.
E aprop sia ajustat en la quantitat de atraccio, quar ela obedira e evasira de adhirencia.	And then adjust it in the quantity of attraction, for it will obey and withdraw with adherence.
E si la boca de la mayre es coartada, nos ja havem recomtat la curacio am sturnutacio e am medicacio de la ola am erbas.	And if the mouth of the mother is contracted, we have already recounted the cure with stornudation and medication of the cloth with herbs.
Mays si no es fora-getada am totas las causas las quals havem recomtadas, lahoras guarda te que no fetigues sobre aquela en iteracio de abstracio, mays empero cove que aquo que es eyssit de lu a la boca de la mayre lies a la coyssa de la femna, e aprop cristeriza aquela am enguent e tetrafarmacon; quar aquel fara poyrir aquela aprop alcus dias e sira dissolvuda e sira fora-getada.	But if it is not expelled with all the causes that we have recounted, then beware that you do not fetigues on it in iteration of abstraction, but rather make sure that what has issued from it to the mouth of the mother lies at the breast of the woman, and then christenize it with a gentle touch and tetrachloride; for that will cause it to be putrid after some days and dissolve and be expelled.
Mays quan se poyreys, es de lu elevada mala audor al cap, e al estomac, e aquo ledeys la malauta; e adonc cove que sian aministradas sub-fumiguacios e convenientz ad aquo.	But when it putrefies, it is elevated to bad authority at the head and stomach, and then leads the patient astray; and therefore it is necessary that sub-fumigations and conveniences be administered accordingly.
Mays alcus dels Antics ja so esproatz sub-fumigacio de nazitort e de figuas seccas.	But some of the Ancients have already been experimented with sub-fumigation of navel-worts and dried figs.
Forma de instrument am le qual la femna es sub-fumiguada deves la retentio de mestruas e de la segondina:	Form of instrument by which the woman is sub-fumigated for the retention of menses and secondine:
Sia fayta de veyre o de eram.	Is made of veyre or eram.
E sia pausada la extremitat subtil en le conh e la extremitat ampla sobre le foc, e la sub-fumiguacio sia pausada sobre las brazas del foc.	And it is paused with the subtle extremity in the concavity and the broad extremity over the fire, and the sub-fumigation is paused above the arms of the fire.
E tengua aquela entro que sia consumida aquela sub-fumiguacio e itera·n autra.	And hold it until that sub-fumigation is consumed and iterate another.
De curacio del cul del enfant no-perforat.	Of the cure for the child's unbroken navel.
Motz enfantz naysso e les culs de lu no so perforatz, les quals ya ciphac subtil e opilat.	Many children are thus and their navels are not pierced, which already have a subtle and opaque cicatrix.
Adonc cove a la matrona que perfore am le sieu dit aquel ciphac; e sino, perfora aquel am spatum agut, e guarda se que no toque le lacert.	Then command the midwife to pierce it with her finger that cicatrix; and if not, then pierce it with a sharp awl, and be careful not to touch the skin.
E aprop pause sobre aquel lana enfusa en vi e oli; e aprop cura aquel am enguent entro que sia senat.	And then pause on that lanolin infused in wine and oil; and then cure it with a gentle touch until it is clean.
Mays si temes que sia opilat, lahoras pausa en le trauc una canula per motz dias, e osta la quan le enfant voldra degerir.	But if you fear that it may be obstructed, then pause in the hole a reed for many days, and stop when the child will desire to pass.
E ja accideys oppilacio del cul per consolidacio de plagua o de apostema; adonc cove que aquela consolidacio sia inscidida, e aprop sia curada am aquo que avem dit de la curacio e del plom.	And if an obstruction of the navel occurs due to consolidation of a wound or apostema; then command that this consolidation be inserted, and then cure it with the water we have said for the cure and with lead.
De curacio de las fistulas que endeveno dejos.	Of the cure for fistulas that remain after childbirth.
Las fistulas que endeveno en la partida dejos pus bassa so nodacio e grossetut las quals endeveno prop del cul defora o en l’espazi de la una partida.	The fistulas that remain in the aftermath of childbirth, which are lower and more swollen due to edema and grossness, and those that remain close to the navel or in the space of one part.
E es una fistula o motas.	And it is a single fistula or multiple ones.
E cum aquela nodacio es antiquada e corr de la humiditat aygosa blanca o poyridura subtil, e alcunas veguadas so de aquestas fistulas alcunas penetrantz.	And when that swelling is ancient and flows with white watery humor or subtle putrefaction, and some times are penetrated by these fistulas.
E aquelas penetrantz so conogudas per aquo que es eyssit de aquelas per la egressio e per ventosetat; e alcunas vetz use le malaute de egressio, e fort leu es eyssit de aquelas verm.	And those that are penetrated are known by what has issued from them through egression and flatulence; and some times the patient uses laxatives, and then a great deal is issued from these fistulas.
E so de aquelas fistulas alcunas veguadas en l’espazi penetrantz entro a la vesica, e entro al meat de la vergua; e so de aquelas penetrantz entro la junctura de la coyssa e entro al notz de la coeta.	And some times those fistulas penetrate into the space between the bladder and the urethra, and even into the flesh of the vulva; and some of these penetrate into the junction of the scrotum and into the notch of the clitoris.
E aquo en que es conoguda fistula penetrant entro al cul e no-penetrant, es que tu metas le tieu dit endic en le cul, e entrometas tenta subtil de eram o de ferr en la fistula quan no y es turtuositat.	And this is how a penetrating fistula that does not penetrate is known, namely by inserting the tip of your finger into the navel and then introducing a subtle probe made of eram or iron into the fistula when there is no tumorosity.
Mays si en aquela es turtuositat, lahoras entromet en aquela tenta subtil de plom o de pels de caval entro que tu sentas la tenta o le pel en le tieu dit.	But if there is a tumor in that fistula, then insert into it a subtle probe made of lead or horsehair until you feel the probe or hair in your finger.
E si no sentas aquela de tot ni no procezeys del trauc alcuna causa de egestio ni verm ni ventositat, ayssi cum havem dit, lahoras sapias que es no-penetrant, e lahoras coyta te a la curacio.	And if you don't feel it at all or if there is no discharge of anything from the hole, neither pus nor wind, as we have said, then know that it is not penetrating, and be careful to proceed with the cure.
E quan la fistula es penetrant entro a la vesica o entro al meat de la vergua, lahoras la significacio de lu es eyssiment de urina de aquela e prohibicio de lu ad aysso que·l loc am medicina sia consolidat.	And when the fistula is penetrating into the bladder or into the flesh of the vulva, then the significance of it is issuing urine from that place and prohibiting it to that extent, so that the location where medicine is applied is consolidated.
Mays si es penetrant entro la junctura de la coyssa o entro al os e envencio de dolor en le circuit, lahoras senhal de lu es que la tenta perve entro aqui si en lu no es turtuositat entro al os, e envencio de dolor en le circuit de la partida; e que de lu yeys poyredura tostemps; e que no val en aquela medicacio, ni es consolidada am enguent.	But if it is penetrating into the junction of the scrotum or into the bone and causing pain in the circuit, then the sign of it is that the probe passes through here if there is no tumor in the bone, and pain in the circuit of the part; and that from it there will be a putrid discharge at all times; and that it will not be cured with medicine, nor consolidated with gentle touch.
E en totas aquelas fistulas penetrant no es curacio de tot, e la curacio de aquelas es trebalh e vanetat dels folyls metges sobre·l qual so fermatz.	And in all those penetrating fistulas there is no complete cure, and the cure of these is a great deal of labor and expertise of skilled physicians upon which we have fixed.
Mays en aquela que no es penetrant e no antiqua, sanacio am ferr es sperada segon que yeu a tu recomtare, e aquo que ja yeu e proat.	But in that which is not penetrating and not ancient, healing with iron is hoped for according to what I have recounted to you, and what has already been tried.
E es que le malaute jagua entre las tuas mas sobre le sieu dos e eleva las cambas de lu entro sus, las coyssas sian enclinadas al ventre de lu, e aprop entromet tenta de plom, o de eram si es en la fistula turtuositat, entro que sapias le loc on perve la tenta.	And it is that the patient lies between your knees over their back and lifts their legs up to yours, with the thighs inclined towards the belly of theirs, and then insert a probe made of lead or eram into the fistula if there is tumorosity in it, until you know the place where the probe goes in.
E si aquela sent le malaute entorn le cuol, lahora cove que tu entrometas le tieu dit endic en le cuol.	And if the patient feels pain around the navel, then command that you insert your finger into the navel.
E si sentas en le tieu dit la tenta ja per si meteyssa descuberta penetrar, otra aquo que sentas entre le tieu dit e aquela siphac o carn, lahoras sapias certanament que aquela es penetrant; e adonc no trebalhes en aquela, quar no es en aquela sanacio, ayssi cum havem dit.	And if you feel the probe already having passed through and penetrating, or if you feel between your finger and that siphac or flesh, then you will certainly know that it is penetrating; and then do not trouble with it, as there is no healing in it, just as we have said.
Mays empero diyssero alcus que es sana en alcus homes tart.	But however, some may say that it heals in certain people.
E de la medicacio per la qual es sperat juvament en lu es que tu ignes cauteri subtil segon le ample de la fistula, ayssi cum es precedit, e intrometas aquel ignit en la fistula entro que pervengua entorn le cuol; e aprop itera aquel doas o tres vetz entro que sapias que ja son adhustas totas aquelas carns ajustadas fistuladas que so semblantz a cana de pluma de ausel.	And the medication by which healing is expected in this case is that you ignite a subtle cauteri according to the size of the fistula, just as we have said, and then insert that ignited cauteri into the fistula until it reaches around the navel; and then repeat that process two or three times until you know that all those adjusted flesh folds that are like feathers on an owl's tail are now adjusted.
E aprop cura aquela am calguas envolopadas en boder entro que en yescan totas aquelas carns que so adhustas, e aprop cura aquela am medicinas la carn engendrantz e consolidantz, e si es sanada, bo es; e sino, lahoras no es sana en degun temps per autra curacio.	And then cure that with cloths wrapped in boiled linen until all those adjusted flesh folds are fully healed and consolidated; and then cure it with medicines generating and consolidating the flesh, and if it is healed, good is; and otherwise, never will be cured by any other treatment.
E si la tenta intra, e no penetra entro·l tieu dit le qual es en le cul, e entre aquel e la tenta que es velament spes de carn o de ciphac, e vezes la fistula en aquo que siec la superficia de la codena, lahoras secca la codena del comensament de la fistula, e tu ve seccan am la tenta, e sia en la fistula entro que la seccio pervengua al loc en le qual perve la extremitat de la tenta, e per la tenta es liberat e catz.	And if the probe enters and does not penetrate into the navel which is in the navel, but rather passes through that soft flesh or cicatrix, and sometimes the fistula opens up on the surface of the skin, then dry the skin from the beginning of the fistula, and you will see it drying with the probe, and be in the fistula until the drying reaches the location where the extremity of the probe is inserted, and through the probe is liberated and cleansed.
E aprop mundifiqua aquelas carns fistuladas las quals so asembladas a canula de pena de ausel e no romangua de aquelas alcuna causa.	And then clean those flesh folds which are like the feathers of an owl and do not remain with any remaining cause.
Mays si flux de sanc vezes que vengua entre tu e la tua opperacio quan ensideysses aquelas carns, lahoras le milh que sia e del pus leugier instrument es cauterizar am foc o am medicina acuta, quar cauteri am foc ajusta bonas doas habitutz: so es adhustio de aquelas carns ajustadas, e abscizio del sanc exseccacio de las humiditatz.	But if there is a flow of pus that comes between you and your operation when you are cleaning those flesh folds, then use the mill that is and take the least painful instrument, which is cauterization with fire or acute medicine, for cauterization with fire adjusts two good habits: it is adjustment of those adjusted flesh folds, and ablation of pus from excessive humidity.
E aprop cura aquela am calguas envolopadas en boder o en caus trissat entro que·l loc geta brac, e aprop lahoras cura la plagua am enguentz carn dura engendran e consolidan.	And then cure that with cloths wrapped in boiled linen or in threefold cloth until the location gets firm, and then command to cure the wound with gentle touch, generating and consolidating hard flesh.
E so medicinas en las quals so stipticitat e exseccio; quan lahoras es restaurada ja es sanada e no temes iteracio.	And thus medicines in which there is astringency and excess; when the patient is restored, it is already healed and you do not fear relapse.
Mays si la fistula ja perve entro al preon del cul e es elonguada de lu superficia del cos, lahoras entromet le tieu dit en le cul e inquireys am aquel.	But if the fistula has already penetrated into the pelvis of the navel and is elongated from its surface to the body, then insert your finger into the navel and investigate with it.
E donc si centes la tenta e entre tu e ela es velament de ciphac o de carn, e es propda a la penetracio, lahora no es operacio en lu sino segon via di fiducia e de speransa.	And therefore if you feel the probe and it is gently on cicatrix or flesh, and is prepared for penetration, then there is no operation in this case except according to the way of faith and hope.
La qual causa es aministrar en lu una de tres manieyras: o que cauterize aquela ayssi cum havem dit; o que secces aquela entro que consieguas la conquavitat de lu per que sia a tu possible entrometre las qualcas e la curacio propdana; e no procesiscas mot am seccio per so que no inscidas le lacert contenent le cuol, e que accidisque sobre le malaute eyssiment de la egistio ses voluntat; e aprop cura aquel am aquo que havem dit quar fort leu sira sanat; o que elongues aquel velament e mondes aquel pus que seccas aquel entro prop le cul, ayssi cum havem dit, o am tenta o am autre instrument de aguda extremitat, e aprop mondifique aquelas carns fistuladas las quals so en la seccio entro la on podes am percrustacio; e aprop esforsa te a far la restauracio de tota la plagua am seccio, e si le orrifici pus desus no es consolidat, e romangua la fistula uberta en la partida del cul, e sira pus leugier per le malaute.	The cause is to administer in this case one of three ways: either to cauterize it as we have said; or to dry it until you achieve the desired condition of the navel so that you can insert your fingers and carry out the cure provided; and do not proceed with any drying method so that you do not incise the skin containing the navel, and what happens is in accordance with the patient's own will; and then cure it as we have said, for it will soon be healed; or to lengthen it slightly and remove the pus that has accumulated by drying it out as much as possible over the navel, either with a probe or another sharp instrument of acute extremity, and then thoroughly cleanse those flesh folds which are in the section where you can see perforation; and then make every effort to restore the entire wound through drying, and if the opening above is not consolidated, and the fistula remains open on the part of the navel, it will be even easier for the patient.
E alscunas veguadas la fistula es finida segon aquesta manieyra: es quan tu entrometas la tenta en la fistula, e es en le latz del cul entorn la superficia del cos am la codena e en le marge del cul, lahoras pren tenta de perforada extremitat, que es ayssi cum agulha de preparantz les coers segon aquesta forma:	And sometimes the fistula is finished in this manner: when you insert the probe into the fistula, and it is in the lateral part of the navel around the surface of the body with the skin and on the margin of the navel, then take a probe of perforated extremity, which is like an awl that prepares the holes according to this form:
e entromet en aquela fiel envolopat de v fiels o entorn aquels; e aprop entromet tenta am fiel en la fistula entro que consiegua la conquavitat de lu.	and insert it into that faithful envelope of 5 or those around them; and then insert the probe gently into the fistula until you achieve the desired condition.
Mays si es penetrant en le marge del cul prop dedintz, lahoras tu extratz le fiel de aquel trauc ayssi que tu intrometas le tieu dit en le cul; e extraguas la extremitat del fiel e ajustes las duas extremitatz essemps, e estrenh cascuna, e leyssa aquo per un dia o per dos, e quan mays inscideys le fiel en la carn, estrenh be aquel entro que aquelas carns sian inscididas las quals so entre doas extremitatz del fiel e que cajan.	But if it is penetrating in the margin of the navel, then you extract the probe from that hole just as you insert your finger into the navel; and extract the extremity of the probe and adjust the two extremities together, and strengthen each one, and let it remain like that for a day or two, and when more you insert the probe into the flesh, strengthen it well so that those flesh folds are inserted which are between the two extremities of the probe and fall.
E aprop cura la plagua entro que sia consolidada e sanada.	And then cure the wound until it is consolidated and healed.
Mays si le orrifici de la fistula no es penetrant, lahoras fay aquel penetrar, en qualque manieyre sia a tu preparat, sino que sia mot en le preon, quar no es a tu que fassas aquo per que no inscidas le lacert; e aprop fay am aquela entro que sia sanada.	But if the opening of the fistula is not penetrating, then make it penetrate, in whatever way you are prepared, but not so that it is in the prepuce, because it is not for you to do this so as not to incise the skin; and then make it so until it is healed.
La forma de spatum spinos am lo qual es fenduda la fistula: la curvitat del qual es mot aguda e l’autra partida es no-aguda, per so que no inscidas aquo que no es necessari, ayssi cum vezes.	The form of the awl with which the fistula is pierced: its curvature is very acute and the other part is not acute, so that you do not incise what is not necessary, just as sometimes.
De sutura de emorroydas en las quals corra sanc en la inscizio de aquelas.	Of the suturing of hemorrhoids in which blood flows during the incision of those.
Emorroydas so segon dos manieyras, quar o so entre le cul semblantz aysi que es de carbos, o quays aquelas sian cum a gras de rasim.	Hemorrhoids are according to two ways, for either they are between the anus resembling charcoal or those which are like ripe grapes.
E de aquelas so petitas e grans, e que le sanc corr de aquelas tostemps e es una, e so motas, e so fora·l cul, e en las extremitatz de lu.	And of those that are small and large, and the blood flows from them at all times and is one, and many, and outside the anus, and in the extremities of it.
Mays empero aquelas que so foro le cul so segon las mes de pauca humiditat, de las quals corr aygua citrina o un petit de sanc am cos continuabla, e so segon la color del cos.	But however, those that are outside the anus are according to the months of little humidity, from which a yellowish water or a small amount of blood flows with the body continuingly, and according to the color of the body.
E la curacio de aquela que es dedintz le cuol es que comandes al malaute que se assela e que se exprema entro que le cuol yesca e las emoroydas apparescan a tu.	And the cure for that which is outside the anus is that you command the patient to settle down and express himself until the anus opens up and the hemorrhoids appear to you.
Adonc tu te coyte e suspen am uncis o que tenguas aquelas am la tua ungla, e aprop incideys aquelas deves las suas razitz.	Then you take hold of them and suspend with the fingers or what you have as your fingernail, and then cut off those roots.
Mays si les uncis no so tengutz en aquelas per la humiditat de lor e mollificacio de aquelas, lahoras pren aquelas am drap aspre o am coto o am flassada de lana, e extratz aquelas am les tieus ditz, e aprop inscideys aquelas e polveriza sobre lor alcunas polveras caudas aprop la inscizio, per que sian ad aquelas en loc de cauteri; o cauteriza aquelas segon que es precedit en le capitol de cauterizar.	But if the fingers are not suitable for grasping those due to their moisture and softness, then take them with a rough cloth or a piece of leather or a woolen rag, and extract them with your fingers, and then cut off those roots and powder some powders nearby the incision, so that they stick to those places like cauterization; or cauterize those as is preceded in the chapter on cauterization.
E aprop cura aquelas am l’autra curacio entro que sian sanadas.	And then cure those with the other cure until they are healed.
E si le cul no obezeys a egressio, lahoras cristerisa le malaute am cristeri en le qual sia mordicacio petita, e sia lavat am aquel aquo que es en le cuol e que obezesca a egressio leugierament quan le malaute s’esprem.	And if the anus does not obey evacuation, then anoint the patient with an ointment in which there is a small amount of bitter substance, and wash it with that water that is in the navel and that will cause evacuation slightly when the patient presses.
Mays si las emorroydas so defora le cul, lahoras la causa de lor es leugiera, e es que tu prenguas aquelas am la tua ungla, o que prenguas aquelas am unci, e inscidas aquelas, e aprop cura aquelas am aquo que havem dit entro que sian sanadas.	But if the hemorrhoids are outside the anus, then the cause of their being is slight, and it is that you take them with your fingernail or with an awl, and cut off those roots, and then cure those with water as we have said until they are healed.
E aquel que avoreys inscizio, cove que aministres sutura de lor segon aquesta manieyra: pren fiel envolopat e entromet aquel en agulha e aprop extratz las emorroydas a las partidas dessus, e fay aquel penetrar am la agulha en la razit del autra part, e envolveys las doas extramitatz del fiel en la partida pus dejos de la agulha, e so latitudinalment; e estrenh la emorroyda am strectura fort, e aprop noza le fiel e extratz la agulha.	And that which you have incised, you must administer suturing of theirs according to this manner: take a needle wrapped and insert it into the awl and then extract the hemorrhoids from the upper parts, and make it penetrate into the root of the other part, and wrap the two extremities of the needle in the outermost part of the awl, and so latitudinally; and strengthen the hemorrhoid with strong stitches, and then remove the needle and awl.
E fay aquo a totas, e layssa de aquelas una e no la cozes, per so que la superfluitat del sanc corra de aquela.	And do this to all of them, and leave one and not close it, for so that the superfluity of blood flows from it.
E aprop pausa sobre le cul drap enfus en oli rozat o en cerot; e pausa aquel sobre·l cuol e comanda al malaute que·s repause.	And then pause over the anus with a cloth dipped in rose oil or cerote; and pause that over the anus and command the patient to rest.
E aprop layssa aquela entro que caja; e quan es casuda, cura aquelas am enguentz o am autra curacio entro que sia sanat.	And then let it rest until it is closed; and when it is closed, cure those with gentle touch or another cure until it is healed.
De curacio de fistulas.	The cure of fistulas.
Motas veguadas accideys per exseccacio de fenda o per costriccio de natura.	Many times accidents occur due to excessive division or constriction of nature.
E cum so antiquadas e no val en aquela medicina, lahoras cove que tu razas aquelas am la puncta de spatum o am la tua ungla entro que sian faytas humidas e sia hostada de aquelas la escorsa pus desus, la qual prohibeys aquelas de consolidacio; e aprop cura aquelas entro que sian consolidadas.	And since they are so old and do not respond to that medicine, then it is necessary to reason with those at the point of awl or with your fingernail until they become moist and the discharge above is blocked from consolidation; and then cure those until they are consolidated.
Lahoras tu osta aquelas am razio pus vehement que la primieyra entro que mot sancno e sian excoriadas; e aprop cura aquelas entro que sian sanadas.	Then you must grasp those with reason more violent than the first, until there is much blood and they are exfoliated; and then cure those until they are healed.
De curacio de almesamir, so es clau.	The cure of Almesmir is thus, it is the key.
Sapias que alamermar, so es clau, e no es si no notz redon segon la color del cors semblant a cap de claviel, e es fayt en tot le cors e majorment en las partidas dejos les pes e als ditz, e endeve per aquels dolor deves le anament.	Know that Almesmir is thus, it is the key, and not if not noted according to the color of the skin resembling a cap of cloves, and it is made throughout the body and most especially in the parts below the feet and hands, and therefore it causes pain through those who do the amending.
E adonc cove que sia inscidit aquo que es en le circuit del clau, e sia tengut am les forfexs o am unci, e sia eradicat de la sua razit; e aprop cura aquel.	And then it is necessary to cut out that which is in the circle of the key, and to be held by forceps or awls, and to be eradicated from its root; and then cure that.
E si vols, cauteriza le segont que es precedit en le sieu capitol.	And if you wish, cauterize it according to what is preceded in its own chapter.
Mays de veruca es eminencia petita aspre fistulada redonda sobre la superficia del cos, e motas veguadas veno en las mas dels enfantz.	But verucca is a small, hard, round excrescence on the surface of the body, and many times it appears on the skin of children.
E curacio de lu es que estendas e inscidas aquela, o que estrenhas aquela am fiel o am pel entro que caja.	And the cure for it is that you stretch and cut out that excrescence, or that you strengthen it with a needle or thread until it closes.
E si vols, cauteriza aquo, segon que havem dit, am foc o am medicina acuta.	And if you wish, cauterize it, according to what we have said, with fire or acute medicine.
E ja so eradicadas enversas e no-enversas am le instrument le qual yeu diyre.	And then they are eradicated, both ways and non-ways, with the instrument which you shall use.
Mays formica es eminencia petita feutrada o fistulada grossa sobre la superficia del cos anant mot en le preon, e quan le freg atroba aquela es centit en lu semblant de mordificacio de formigua, e es fayta entorn le cos.	But formica is a small, fatty or fistulous excrescence on the surface of the body growing downwards towards the groin, and when the skin finds that excrescence it seems to be bitten by a formic worm, and it is made around the body.
E curacio de lu es que prenguas una canula de pena de auca o de pena de voltor, e sia fort, e pausa aquela sobre la formigua entro que la contengua le cercle de la canula de las partidas de lu; e aprop revolveys la tua ma am la canula entro que inscidas aquo que es en le circuit de la formigua, e pauses aquela en le preon de la carn, e que eradiques la formigua de la sua razit.	And the cure for it is that you take a reed pipe made from goose or from wolf's tail, and make it strong, and pause it on the formica until it contains the circle of the reed pipe in its parts; and then turn your hand with the reed pipe until you cut out what is in the circuit of the formica, and pause it in the groin of the flesh, and that eradicates the formica from its root.
E si vols, fay aquo am canula de eram o de ferr segon aquesta forma:	And if you wish, do this with an iron or steel reed according to this form:
Sia la partida desus de la canulha trahent a subtilitat, sorda (so es no-perforada), envolopada per so que sobre le dit la aprencio de lu sia ablaviada e la revolucio de aquela.	Be the upper part of the reed pipe drawn out to subtlety, smooth (it is not perforated), wrapped in such a way that on the said point it takes hold and turns around itself.
E si vols cauteriza la formiga segon que es denant dit en la cauterizacio de atheyl en le capitol de cauteri.	And if you wish, cauterize the formica according to what is said before in the cauterization of atheyl in the chapter on cauterization.
De forma dels instrumentz que so aministratz a dar cristeri.	The form of the instruments that are administered to give ointment.
Alcunas veguadas es fayt cristeri de argent o de lato o de eram fondut o malleat; e alcunas veguadas es fayt de aquels instrumentz petit e gran segon aquels als quals so aministratz, quar aquel que es aministrat en la curacio dels petitz enfants sia petit; e de aquel dels quals los culs son freuls o doloyrozes, les cristeris de aquels sian petitz.	Some times it is made ointment of silver or lead or melted iron or hammered; and some times it is made with small and large instruments according to those which are administered, for that which is administered in the cure of small children is small; and the ointments of those whose buttocks are sore or painful, are small.
La forma de cristeri gran e pauc:	The form of great and little ointment:
Le cap de la canula de lu desus en le qual es liada la borsa sia ampla segon aquesta manieyra; e sia a lu distinacio la on la borsa es liada ayssi cum vezes.	The head of the reed pipe above, in which the pouch is tied, should be wide according to this manner; and there should be a distinction at the point where the pouch is tied, as it sometimes happens.
E la extremitat de lu pus dejus, la qual es entromesa en le cul, sia sorda (so es no-uberta) mot leon, atrasent a subtilita; e en la un del latz de lu sian dos traucs, e en l’autre costat un trauc, e sia la amplesa del trauc segon la groseza dels rays e pus gros un petit.	And the extremity of it that is inserted into the anus should be smooth (it is not open) like a lion's back, going towards subtlety; and on one side there are two holes, and on the other side one hole, and the width of the hole should be according to the thickness of the rays and a little larger.
E sia la borsa en la qual sian pausadas las medicinas de vesica de bestia o de pel de ovelha, e la razit de lu sia un palm.	And the pouch should be made in such a way that medicines from the bladder of an animal or the wool of a sheep are placed inside it, and the root of it should be one palm.
E sia perforada per motz traucs ayssi cum es revolvuda; e si l’espazi le qual es entre les traucs la grossetut del dit.	And it should be perforated by many small holes, as if it is being turned over; and the space between the holes should be the thickness of the same.
E aprop entromet en aquels traucs fiel fort de fiel cru le qual sia de detz fiels, o enviro aquels; e ajusta am aquel la borsa; e quan es pausada en lu la borsa, sia streyt en le cap del cristeri entre dos distingentz am fort costriccio, e aprop cristeriza am aquel quascun trauc: Mays la qualitat de cristerizar am aquel es que tu omples la borsa de la medicina, que sia escalfada segon la quantitat de la tolleransa del malaute; e guarda te que no sia trop cauda ni trop freja.	And then insert the needle into those small holes, a strong and sharp needle made from the bone of ten or more needles, or one that is similar to them; and adjust the pouch (borsa) over it; and when the pouch is placed in it, be stretched at the top of the ointment between two distinct parts with strong constriction, and then cauterize each hole: But the quality of cauterizing is that you fill the pouch with medicine, which should be heated according to the quantity of tolerance of the patient; and be careful not to make it too hot or too cold.
E aprop le malaute sia resupinat sobre le sieu dos, e eleva las suas cambas en sus e pausa dejos lu un cuer sobre le qual ja so les homes o un lansol; e aprop unta la extramitat del cauteri am oli o am album de huou o am mucellage de fenugrec o de semblantz; e aprop entromet aquel en le cul am facilitat, e aprop le ministre prengua la borsa e exprema aquel am doas mas e essemps am vehemencia entro que sia evacuat en le budelh tot aquo que es en le cristeri; e aprop extra le cristeri e le malaute leva las suas cambas a la paret.	And then the patient should be placed on their back over the said spot, with their legs lifted up and their feet placed one on either side of the cauterized area; and then a cloth or a lansol should be placed over it, and a small amount of oil or albumen of hen or mucilage of fenugreek or something similar should be applied to the extremity of the cauterizer; and then insert that into the anus with ease, and the minister should take the pouch and squeeze out what is in the ointment with two hands and sometimes with vehemence until everything is evacuated from the container; and then remove the ointment and the patient should lift their legs to the wall.
E si la medicina forsa aquel a eyssiment, tengua le tant quant poyra; e si dorm am aquel per tota una nueyt, es mays derier en juvament.	And if the medicine forces him to evacuate immediately, let him do so as much as he can; and if he sleeps with that for a whole night, it is more beneficial in its effect.
Mays si tu cristerizas aquel en las malautias de solucio de ventre e l’eyssiment de lu le coyta, lahoras tu itera le cauteri entro que sia sanat.	But if you cauterize that in the illnesses of diarrhea and the evacuation of stool is slow, then you must iterate the cauterizer until he is cured.
E si en le cul so emorroydas o apostemas ledens, lahoras sia le cristeri mot subtil e leon, dels cristeris am les quals les enfantz so criterisatz.	And if there are hemorrhoids or abscesses in the anus, then it should be the cauterizer of subtlety and lion, among the cauterizers which children are accustomed to.
De curacio de las plaguas.	The cure of plagues.
Yeu ja e dit en la divisio de la curacio de las plaguas aquo que convenia al libre, e yeu dic assi la curacio de aquelas am ma e am medicinas segon le conpliment.	And I already said in the division of the cure of plagues that this is suitable for the free, and I will say thus the cure of these with me and with medicines according to the complement.
Donc dic que las plaguas son diversificadas segon aquo en que son faytas las plaguas e segon le loc sobre le qual cazo las plaquas.	Therefore I say that plagues are diversified according to this, in which the plagues are made and according to the place where one makes the plagues.
E las causas per que motas vetz son faytas las plaguas so ayssi cum getament de peyra, o inscisio d’espaza o de cotel, o percussio am lansa, o am fustz, o am sageta, o semblantz ad aquels de motas causas.	And the causes by which many times plagues are made are thus as follows: by bite of a snake, or incision with a sword or with a cotelet, or percussion with a lance, or with a club, or with an arrow, or similar to these many causes.
Mays las plaguas que so en les locz del cos so ayssi cum plagua la qual catz sobre le cap, o·l col, o·l pietz, o·l ventre, o·l fitge, e semblantz ad aquels dels membres.	But the plagues that are on the parts of the body are thus as follows: plague which afflicts the head, or the neck, or the feet, or the belly, or the thigh, and similar to those of the members.
E yeu so recomtant la curacio de alcunas plaguas per que pauses aquela ratiocinacio e regla sobre las autras plaguas.	And I am recommending the cure for some plagues, because it is rational and a rule for other plagues.
E yeu comensare de las plaguas del cap simplas, quar la rememoracio de las compostas vindra al comensament del tertz capitol.	And I will begin with the simple plagues of the head, for the recollection of the complex ones will come at the beginning of the third chapter.
Donc dic que quan accideys en le cap plagua simpla e no es fractura, lahoras considera: si es per getament de peyra o de semblant, e ja ha trinquada la codena tant solament e es gran plagla e temes sobre aquel malaute havinement de apostema caut, lahoras tu te coyta e fleubotoma la cephalica tantost, e no tardas aquo; e extrats ad aquel del sanc segon la quantitat de la vertut de lu si no mes alcuna causa prohibent de fleubotomia, majorment si·l sanc que es eyssit de la plagua es pauc.	Therefore I say that when a simple plague occurs in the head and is not a fracture, then consider: if it is due to snakebite or something similar, and you have already noticed that the patient has only just begun to swell and is now experiencing great pain and fears an abscess will form, then you should immediately take a lead bullet and apply it to the cephalic vein, and not delay; and remove the blood from the wound according to the quantity of the virtue of the medicine if there is no other cause prohibiting this, especially if the blood that has been drawn from the plague is little.
E sia la flaubotomia del contrari de la partida plaguada; e guardase le malaute de replecio e de vi e de viandas grossas.	And it should be the bleeding of the opposite side of the affected part; and beware the patient from taking in too much food, drink, and heavy nourishment.
Mays si de la minuicio prohibeys alcuna causa, lahoras sia aminorat de la vianda e no apropinque a carn ni a vi.	But if there is any other cause prohibiting it, then let the nourishment be reduced and not approach meat or wine.
E pausa sobre la plagua, si a lu accideys apostema caut, coto enfus en oli rozat solet o en vi en le qual es stipticat.	And pause over the plague, if it becomes an abscess, cut off in oil rosated or in wine that is stipticated.
Mays si est segur de apostema caut, lahoras pausa sobre la plagua, si es recent am le sieu sanc e le ayre no ha mudat aquela la polvera la qual yeu recomtare aprop petit.	But if it is certain that the abscess is not serious, then pause over the plague, if it is recent with its own blood and the air has not changed the powder which I recommend to be applied little by little.
E si le ayre ja ha mudada aquela, lahoras pausa sobre alscus enguentz entro que sia sanada.	And if the air has already changed it, then pause over another ointment until it is healed.
Mays si la plagua es gran o es per inscizio d’espaza e de semblantz, e no so ajustadas las labias de lu per puvils, lahoras ajusta aquelas am sutura segon que yeu recomtare de la sutura de lor.	But if the plague is great or is due to incision with a sword and similar things, and the lips of it are not adjusted by poultices, then adjust those with suture according to what I recommend for the suture of them.
Mays si la plagua ja es discuberta del os e pen, e no es retencio de lu sino un petit suspensori, lahoras inscideys aquela e aprop cura la plagua am medicinas e restaura la carn aprop en loc de codena, e comanda al malaute que sia pescut de viandas en las quals es groceza: caps e formen coyt e semblantz a lor, entro que sia compost.	But if the plague has been discovered from bone and flesh, and there is no retention of it except a small suspensor, then cut into that and apply cure to the plague with medicines and restore the flesh in place of coding, and command the patient to eat foods in which greasiness is gross: heads and forms coit and similar things to theirs, until they are composed.
