E si atrobas en la codena putrefaccio e no adhereys al os, lahoras tu inscideys tot aquo poyrit e geta aquo, e aprop cura aquo.	And if you find putridity in the coding and it does not adhere to the bone, then cut into all that putridity and take it away, and apply cure there.
Mays si en aquestas plaguas es arteria o vena de la qual fluxs de sanc pot evenir, e no es abscindida per medicinas, lahoras tu inquier sobre la arteria, e si atrobas aquela no-inscidida, lahoras tu inscideys aquela am spatum, o lia aquela; e si necessitat te provoca que aquo que havem dit no comfereys, lahoras tu cauteriza entro que·l sanc sia abscidit.	But if in these plagues there is an artery or vein from which blood can flow and it is not cut off by medicines, then you should inquire about the artery, and if you find that one that has not been cut off, then you should cut into it with a spatula, or ligate it; and if necessity demands that what we have said does not occur, then you should cauterize until the blood is stopped.
E si aquestas plaguas son simplas e petitas, lahoras la causa de lor es leugiere; enayssi que tu polverizas sobre aquelas aquesta polvera, quar consolidada aquela denant que l’ayre mude aquelas.	And if these plagues are simple and small, then the cause of them is light; therefore you may powderize over those this powder, which will consolidate before the air changes those.
E la manieyra de la polvera es aquesta: recipe oli de enses partida una, de sanc de drago partida doas, de caus no-extincta partidas tres; sia tot mot trissat e crivellat, e de lu sia la plagua omplida, e sia constrengida per bona constriccio entro que be sobre aquela aderesca, e sia coagulada am le sanc.	And the manner of the powder is this: take oil of dragon's blood one part, blood of dragon two parts, and unextinguished candle three parts; grind all together and crush well, and then fill the plague with it, and compress it with good constriction until it adheres well to that place, and coagulates with the blood.
E aprop strengeys aquela desus am pulvils e leyssa aquela, e no la deslias mentre esta ayssi que no es apostemada, quar no es eredicada de lu la medicina entro que sia sanada.	And apply the powder above as poultices and let it be, and do not remove it until it is thus as if there were an abscess, for then the medicine will not be absorbed into it until it is healed.
E alcuna vetz fa aquo sola cautz, quan no es a tu en present enses e sanc de drago.	And sometimes it is done alone with this powder, when there is not enough of you in person and blood of dragon.
E ja fa aquesta meteyssa operacio en las grans plaguas quan conveneys que sia pausada sobre aquelas e sian streytas, e so plaguas recentz am le lor sanc, las quals le ayre no ha alteradas.	And this same operation is done in great plagues when it is necessary to pause over those and be stretched, and new plagues with their own blood, which the air has not altered.
E si le ayre las ha alteradas, e majorment quan es en temps d’estiu, lahoras no es entencio a la posicio de aquesta polvera, mays adonc cura aquelas am aquo que havem dit, enayssi que tu pauses sobre aquelas alcus enguents degistius, o que pauses sobre aquelas pols de la farina del ordi am aygua e mel entro que getan poyredura; e aprop cura aquelas am l’autra curacio entro que sian sanadas.	And if the air has altered them, and especially in the summer, then it is not advisable to apply this powder, but rather cure those with what we have said, by suspending over those certain ointments or powders made from barley flour mixed with water and honey until they give a purging; and then apply cure to those with another remedy until they are healed.
Mays si accideys am la plagua fractura en os, e es petita, lahoras tu extratz aquo am gesti.	But if it happens with a fracture in the bone and it is small, then you should extract that with gestures.
E yeu diyre la cura de las fracturas del cap en aquo que es envenidor.	And you should say the cure for fractures of the head in what is poisonous.
De las plaguas del col.	Of the plagues of the neck.
Mays si la plagua accideys en le col, lahoras no es en lu differencia en medicacio, e entre la plagua del cap quan es simpla.	But if the plague occurs in the neck, then there is no difference in medicine between it and the plague of the head when simple.
Mays si ja le nervi del col es inscis o arteria, lahoras si es nervi, no es en lu engen sino que sia evitada curacio de lu am aquo que fa vehement stipticitat, ayssi cum ziniar e zegi que es vetriol e semblantz a lor quar nozo als nervis e contrazo aquel.	But if the nerves of the neck are cut or artery is affected, then if it is nerve, not in you but rather be avoided any cure that would cause vehement stipticitat, such as ziniar and zegi that is vetriol and similar to theirs which does not nourish the nerves and contracts them.
E no pauses sobre la plagua alcuna causa de tot freja, quar la sustancia dels nervis es freja e la continuacio de lu es am le cervel, le qual es le pus aut de totz les membres.	And do not pause over the plague any cause that is all frozen, for the substance of the nerves is frozen and its continuation is to the brain, which is the most important of all members.
E si’ aquo am que es curat de medicinas leugieras, ayssi cum es caus lavada am aygua dousa, alcuna veguada enfusa en oli rozat o no-rozat, e thucia quan es lavada am aygua dousa e las autras peyras minarantz segon aquesta manieyra, e enguentz humitz.	And if it is so with what is cured by light medicines, such as when it is washed with warm water and then infused in rose-colored or uncolored oil, and thucia when it is washed with warm water and the other parts are softened according to this manner, and ointments moist.
Mays si la plagua es gran, lahoras aministra sutura, o coarta las labias de lu, e aprop cura aquela am pulvils entro que sia sanada.	But if the plague is great, then you should administer sutures, or bind the lips of it, and apply cure to that with poultices until it is healed.
Mays si a la plagua es profunditat o accideys en lu a la pus bassa partida poyredura, lahoras perfora aquela en le loc mays depremegut.	But if the plague is deep or occurs at the lowest part of the poultice, then you should pierce it in the most depressed location.
Mays si en la plagua ja es inscisa arteria e es conseguit flux de sanc, lahoras separa o secca aquela, o lia aquela, o cauteriza aquela si necessitat te provoca ad aquo.	But if in the plague there is already incised artery and it has resulted in blood flow, then you should separate or dry that, or ligate that, or cauterize that if necessity demands it to that.
Mays si ja ha insciditz les spondils del golayro o tot, e so salvadas las venas del col, lahoras tu ajusta las labias de la codena am sutura sobre la cana del golayro e no toques aquel; abantz egala aquel e reduzeys aquel sobre la sua figura natural, e aprop strenh aquel am strectura decent, e leyssa aquela per alcus jorns; e aprop cura aquel am enguentz en les quals es stipticitat e excitacio entro que sia sanat.	But if the vertebrae of the backbone or all have been incised and the veins of the neck are saved, then you should adjust the lips of the spine with sutures over the canal of the backbone and do not touch that; beforehand equalize that and reduce it to its natural figure, and apply strength to that with decent stretching, and leave that for some days; and apply cure to that with ointments in which there is stipticitat and excitement until it is healed.
Mays si la plagua ja en le os a fayta enprecio, lahoras percuireys aquela, e lahoras si en lu ha fragmentz de hos, extratz totz aquels que podes de lor; e aquo que a tu no es apparelhat, leyssa aquo entro que la plagua se poyrisca, e sia separat e la egrecio de lu sia alleujada.	But if the plague has made a fracture in the bone, then you should pierce it, and if there are fragments of bone in it, extract all those that you can from them; and what is not properly set, leave that until the plague subsides, and be separate and the excrescence of it be alleviated.
E si la plagua es recent lahoras polveriza sobre aquela polvera la qual t’e recomtada.	And if the plague is recent, then powderize over that the powder which I recommended to you.
Mays si en la plagua es fayta fistula, lahoras cura aquela am aquo del qual la rememoracio vindra aprop en le sieu capitol.	But if the plague has made a fistula, then cure that with that of which remembrance will come to you in its own chapter.
De las plaguas del col o de semblantz quan fayta entre las spallas e es fayta am spaza o am cotel o am lansa o am semblantz.	Of the plagues of the neck or similar when it is made between the shoulders and is made with a spaza (sword), a cotel (axe), a lansa (lance), or similar.
Si es percussio de lansa o de cotel, e vezes de lu la profunditat, lahoras considera mays si de la plagua yeys ventositat quan le malaute elena; lahoras sapias que la plagua es mortal.	If it is a blow from a lance or axe, and the wound is deep, then you should consider more carefully if there is ventilation of the plague when the patient exhales; know that the plague is mortal.
E si en lu no es profunditat e la plagua es recent am le sieu sanc, lahoras tu pauses en lu de la primieyra horo polvera, e no strenhas aquel per que no sia le sanc retengut en la profunditat de lu e que retorne al cor e que aucigua le malaute, mays pausa en lu enguent atractiu, e deslia aquela doas veguadas le dia.	And if it is not deep and the plague is recent with its own blood, then you should pause over it with powder in the first hour, and do not strengthen that which might cause the blood to be retained in the depth of it and return to the heart and afflict the patient; rather, pause over it with an attractive ointment, and remove it twice a day.
E si l’enguent no es a tu present, lahoras tu pausa en le orrifici de la plagua coto viel per que sucque aquo que yeys de las humiditatz; e fay que le malaute dorma sobre la plagua per que corra aquo que es en lu ajustat.	And if the ointment is not present, then you should pause at the orifice of the plague and cut a small vein so that it sucks up the water that comes from the humidities; and make the patient sleep on top of the wound so that the water that is in it will be adjusted.
Mays si ja de la plagua son passatz tres dias o mays e no accideys al malaute spasme ni tremor de cor mal ni strictura de ale, e vezes las autras dispozicios bonas de lu, lahoras sapias que plagua es salva; e adonc cura aquela am calguas e am l’autra curacio entro que sia sanada.	But if from the plague three days or more have passed and there is no spasm nor tremor of heart nor constriction of breath, and sometimes other good dispositions are present in him, then know that the plague is saved; and therefore cure it with calmness and with another remedy until it is healed.
Mays si la sanacio de lu es excusada, e ja tot temps es uberta, lahoras sapias que ja es fayta fistula; cura donc aquela per le sieu capitol.	But if the healing of him is excluded, and already all time is open, then know that already a fistula has been made; cure therefore that according to its own chapter.
E si la plagua es per inscisio de spaza o de cotel, e es simpla en la superficia del pietz o del dos, lahoras cura aquela am aquo que es precedit de sutura, si es gran, o am polvera, si es petita.	And if the plague is from incision of spaza or cotel, and it is simple on the surface of the foot or hand, then cure that with what precedes suturing, if it is great, or with powder, if it is small.
Mays si ja ha fayta enprecio en le os, e so ja de lu inscizas pessas, lahoras tu torqua la plagua e coyta ad extrayre aquelas pessas, si so separadas.	But if there is already a fracture in the bone, and you have incised pessas (fragments) from it, then you should torque the plague and pull them out to extract those pessas, if they are separated.
Mays si no so separadas, lahoras leyssa las entro que se poyresca la plagua, que la extraccio de lor es alleujada.	But if they are not separated, then you should leave them alone until the plague subsides, for the extraction of them is alleviated.
E de las autras plaguas accidentz en les autres membres le juvament en curacio es le juvament de aquo que havem dit.	And for other plagues that occur in other members, the treatment is the same as what we have said.
De las plaguas del ventre.	Of the plagues of the belly.
L’indisposicio la qual accideys en le ventre es o gran, o pauc, o migiera.	The indisposition which occurs in the belly is either great, or small, or middling.
De la gran alcunas veguadas yeys le budel o nervi del budel, per que es fayta intromissio de lor e la sutura de lor esser pus vehement e pus subtil.	Of the great some times yes the budel or nerve of the budel, for which there is made an introduction of them and the suture of them to be more violent and more subtle.
E disrupcio petita es fayta dificil per autra manieyra, e siec se que la reduccio de lor es pus dificil, si no te coytes de la intromissio de lor al sieu loc tantost, quar se ubre e es engrossat per que le intrament de lu es fayt difficil.	And a small disruption is made difficult by another manner, and it seems that the reduction of them is more difficult, if you do not take care of the introduction of them to their place soonest, for they open up and are engrossed, so that the instrument of it is made difficult.
E donc la milhor disrupcio es migiera, quar en aquela no es dificil la reduccio del budel, ayssi cum es dificil en las doas specias denant ditas.	And therefore the best disruption is middling, for in that there is not difficult the reduction of the budel, just as it is difficult in the two species mentioned above.
E sapias que sutura del ventre es segon quatre manieyras, mays doas suturas son comunas que conveneysso en suturas de las autras plaguas del cors.	And know that the suture of the belly is according to four manners, but two sutures are common that are necessary in sutures of other plagues of the body.
E duas autras suturas proprias comunican a las autras plaguas, mays empero so mays proprias en la sutura del ventre.	And two other sutures proper communicate with other plagues, but however are more proper in the suture of the belly.
E yeu recomti a tu quascuna am exposicio e declaracio.	And you recommend to you what is exposed and declared.
Donc dic que quan la plagua es petita e es eyssit alcuna causa del budel per aquela, e es fayt dificil a reduzir aquel, lahoras aquo es en una de doas manieyras: o per parvitat de la disrupcio ayssi cum havem dit, o quan al budel es venguda inflacio per la frigiditat de l’ayre.	So I say that when the plague is small and there is some cause of the budel for it, and it is made difficult to reduce that, then this is in one of two ways: or by the smallness of the disruption just as we have said, or when the budel has come to be inflated due to the coldness of the air.
E donc quan aquo es ayssi, lahora cove que tu scalfes aquel enayssi que tu submerges una sponga ho drap humit en aygua tebeza sola, o que coguas en aygua squinant, e cyperum, e spic, e embroques am aquela le budel entro que la imflacio sia resolvuda.	And therefore when that is so, then it is necessary for you to scrape off that area with a sponge or damp cloth, or to apply water of the following mixture: cyperum, spic, and embrocation, and pour that over the budel until the inflammation is resolved.
E alcunas veguadas fa aquo vi en le qual ha stipticitat, e es milhor que la aygua sola en resolucio de la imflacio.	And some times I have seen in which there is constriction, and it is better that water alone does not resolve the inflammation.
E donc cum tu vezes la imflacio esser resolvuda, lahoras tu humecta le budel am aygua en la qual es coyta altea e malvas, quar per aquo es alleujat le intrament de lu am pauca causa.	And therefore when the inflammation is resolved, then you should moisten the budel with water in which there is high and bad humor, because of this it is alleviated the instrument of it with little cause.
Mays si es escusat le intrament de lu aprop aquesta curacio, lahoras scindeys la disrupcio un petit am strument am le qual so inscididas emorroydas.	But if the instrument of it is excused from this cure, then you should divide the disruption into small pieces with an instrument in which there are inserted bloody vessels.
E la curacio primieyra es milhor, quan es propriada que no es seccio, e no sia occupacio a seccar aprop necessitat e defaliment.	And the first cure is better when it is proper and not a section, and there is no occupation to cut too close to necessity and deficiency.
Del instrument, sec se la forma de lu:	Of the instrument, see if its shape is like this:
La una partida de lu torta aguda, e l’autra partida no-acuta, e la extremitat subtil, e no sia am la subtilitat de spatum, abantz sia obtusa un pauc.	The one part of it is bent acute, and the other part not acute, and the extremity subtle, and not sharp like a spatula, but rather obtuse by a little.
E donc cum la plagua es amplificada e yeys fora le budel, lahoras cove que la sua reduccio sia segon la forma de lu natural, en le sieu loc propri, si es possible sobre aquo, quar milhor es.	And therefore when the plague is amplified and outside the budel, then it is necessary that its reduction be according to the form of it in its natural place, if possible on top of it, because it is better.
Mays quan la disrupcio es ampla, e es en la partida pu bassa del ventre, lahoras cove que tu fassas jazer le malaute sobre le sieu dos, e pausa las suas cambas pus autas que·l sieu cap; e si es en la partida pus desus del ventre, lahoras tu pause le cap de lu e·l pietz pus autz que las partidas dejos.	But when the disruption is wide and is in the lower part of the belly, then you must make the patient lie on their back with their legs higher than their head; and if it is in the upper part of the belly, then you should place the head lower than the feet.
E semblantment si la disrupcio es en una de las doas partz del ventre, lahoras pausa la tua entencio e la tua consideracio tostemps en aysso per que la partida en la qual es la plagua sia pus auta que l’autra.	And similarly, if the disruption is in one of the two parts of the belly, then pause your intention and consideration at this point so that the part where the plague is located is higher than the other.
E ayssi cove que tu aministres aquo en las plaguas grans e en las plaguas migieras.	And thus you should administer this in great plagues and in middling plagues.
E en las plaguas petitas, pausa aquo que es a tu preparat, e aprop fay que·l ministre sia entre las tuas mas pyatados, le qual tengua la disrupcio tota am la sua ma e ajusta las labias de lu, e aprop descuebre de aquela ad aquel que siec la sutura alcuna causa aprop autra.	And in small plagues, pause on what is to your liking, and make sure that the minister is between your most pious ones, who has the entire disruption in their hand and adjusts the lips of it, and make sure to uncover from this to that which will be some cause for another suturing.
E aquesta es la manieyra de sutura comuna: una que prenguas la agula, o comte de agula segon la cantitat de la amplitut de la plagua; e aprop layssa de la extremitat de la disrupcio del dit anular, e strenh la agula una, otre que tu no metas fiel en las doas extremitatz de la codena, am doas extremitatz del ciphac que es dejos la codena de las partidas dedintz, entro que fassas aquela penetrar de aquela partida; e tu ja has agreguadas doas extremitatz de la codena e doas extremitatz del ciphac, e so faytas quatre ordes.	And this is the common method of suturing: take the needle, or count the needle according to the size of the amplitude of the plague; and make sure to leave from the extremity of the disruption of the ring finger, and strengthen the needle one time, so that you do not put faith in the two extremities of the code, with the two extremities of the ciphac that is left over the code of the parts outside, until it penetrates that part; and you have already added the two extremities of the code and the two extremities of the ciphac, and so make four orders.
E aprop strenh am fiel doble en le circuit de la agula, e alcunas veguadas de doas partz ensemps, e aprop agregua las doas labias e la plagua per agreguacio decent; e aprop layssa la grossitut del dit e fiqua una autra agulha en aquela, e aprop lia aquela am fiel ayssi cum fiest am la primieyra agulha; e no cesses far aquo si es necessitat am las agulhas entro que ajas complida tota la contriccio de la plagua.	And so strengthen with double faith in the circle of the needle, and sometimes from two parts together, and so add the two lips and the wound by decent addition; and so leave the thickness of the finger and place another needle in that one, and so link it with a thread just like the first needle; and do not cease to do this if necessary with the needles until you have completed all the contraction of the wound.
E sian las agulhas migieras entre groceza e subtilitat, quar las agulhas subtils mot leugierament insciden la carn; e las grossas so de dificil intrament en la codena, e donc per aquo cove que sian migieras en subtilitat e grosseza.	And the needles should be middling between grossness and subtlety, because the subtle needles barely touch the flesh; and the thick ones are difficult to manipulate in the code, and therefore it is necessary that they be middling in subtlety and thickness.
E no cove que la agulha sia ficada en doas extremitatz de la codena propdana mot, per so que la carn no sia inscidida leugierament e que la plagua se huebra devant la sua consolidacio.	And it is not necessary for the needle to be placed in two extremities of the code at once, so that the flesh is not cut lightly and the wound does not become inflamed before its consolidation.
E no sian prolonguadas de sutura per que la plagua no sia prohibida de consolidacio.	And it should not be prolonged in its suture, so that the wound is not prevented from consolidating.
E aprop inscideys las extremitatz de las agulhas per so que no ledescan le malaute deves le sieu dormier; e pausaras sobre la sutura pulvils expanduts de tota partida, les quals tenguan las extremitatz de las agulhas; e layssa aquelas entro que sapias que la plagua ja es consolidada.	And so insert the extremities of the needles in such a way that they do not disturb the patient's sleep; and pause over the suture, spreading out the powder all around, which has the extremities of the needles; and leave those alone until you know that the wound is already consolidated.
E aquestas specias de sutura am agulhas en cal manieyra es pus convenient en las plaguas petitas, quar habasta en la sutura de lor una agulha o doas o entorn aquelas.	And this type of suture with needles in this manner is more suitable for small wounds, because it takes only one needle or two around those.
Mays la segonda sutura es cominal: e es que tu aministres am sutura las quatre extremitatz, de la codena e doas extremitatz del ciphac, en una veguada, am agulha en la qual sia fiel envolopat engual en subtilitat e grosseza.	But the second suture is common: and it is that you administer with suture the four extremities, of the code and two extremities of the ciphac, in one go, with a needle in which is faithful enveloped in subtlety and thickness.
E aprop quan am la agulha auras penetrat aquestas quatre extremitatz, reduzeys la agulha de aquela meteyssa partida de la qual comensest, per so que le fiel retrayt caja de la pus subirana partida a la plagua, per so que la sutura sia segon sutura de drap am la qual les draps so strengutz.	And then, when the needle has penetrated these four extremities, reduce the needle to that middle part from which it began, so that the thread retracts into the most superior part of the wound, so that the suture is according to the suture of cloth with which the cloths are strengthened.
E pausa entre quascuna sutura la quantitat del gros del dit mendre.	And pause between each suture the amount of thickness of the little finger.
E aquesta sutura sabo les homes.	And this suture is known to men.
E am tal sutura yeu cozegui la plagua la qual era accidida a un home en le sieu ventre le qual era stat plaguat am un cotel, e era la disrrumpcio de la plagua major de un palm, e era eyssit dels budels entorn dos palms del budel del mieg loc e era la disrupcio en le mieg del membre; e adonc yeu reduzegui aquel depus que le budel havia stat foro la plagua per xxiiii horas.	And with such a suture, I cured the wound that had been inflicted on a man in his belly, which was caused by a cotelet, and it was the disruption of the major wound of one palm, and it was situated around two palms of the belly button, and it was the disruption in the middle of the member; and then I reduced it from there, since the belly had been for 24 hours.
E la plagua fo consolidada en le spazi de xv dias o entorn, e curegui aquel e es sanat; e aprop aquo visquec per motz ans, e es conversat en las suas disposicios.	And the wound was consolidated in the space of 15 days or around, and I cured it and he is healthy; and so he lived for many years, and is converted to his usual dispositions.
E les autres metges havian jutgat que no fora sanat; e per miracle foc, quar yeu no curegui aquel am enguent, quar era en loc en le qual enguent no era atrobat ni deguna medicina, mays pausegui sobre la plagua coto viel dos veguadas lo dia e ablucio assiduo am aygua de mel entro que foc sanat.	And the other doctors had judged that he would not be healed; and by a miracle, it was so, because you did not cure him with an ointment, since there was no ointment nor any medicine found in that place, but instead, you paused over the wound twice a day and performed constant ablutions with water of honey until he was healed.
Mays yeu diyre dos specias de sutura proprias segon narracio de Paraula.	But you will learn two species of suture proper according to the narration of Paraula.
E es que tu comenses am sutura de la codena, e entrometas agulha de la partida deforo a la partida dedintz.	And you begin with the suture of the code, and enter the needle from the outside to the inside.
E donc cum la agulha penetra en la codena e en aquel meteys lacertz segon rectetut e en longetut de tot le cos, e layssa la extremita del ciphac en le qual has entromesa la agulha; e fay penetrar en la autra extremitat la agulha de la partida dedintz a la partida deforo en l’autra extremitat del mihat.	And then, when the needle enters the code and meets with the lacertz (ligament) according to right and length throughout the entire body, and leaves the extremity of the ciphac (muscle) in which you inserted the needle; and make the needle penetrate into the other extremity from the inside to the outside in the other extremity of the muscle.
E don cum tu auras fayta aquela penetrar, lahoras tu fay aquela penetrar autra veguada en aquela meteyssa extremitat del mihat de la partida deforo a la partida dedintz; e leyssa la extramitat del ciphac que es en aquest latz, e fay penetrar la agulha en l’autra extremitat de la partida dedintz a la partida deforo.	And then, when you have made the needle penetrate once, make it penetrate again in that same extremity of the muscle from the outside to the inside; and leave the extremity of the ciphac (muscle) that is on this side, and make the needle penetrate into the other extremity from the inside to the outside.
E fay penetrar am aquela la tua penetracio am la qual fas aquela penetrar en le ciphac en la extremitat del mirat la qual es en la partida de lu entro que tot aquel penetre.	And make the needle penetrate to that point where your penetration makes it penetrate into the muscle in the extremity of the mirror which is on this side, until everything penetrates.
E aprop comensa de aquest meteys costat e cus aquel am la extremitat que es del ciphac en l’autra latz, e extratz la agulha de la codena la qual penetrec, e aprop redutz aquela en aquela codena e cos la extremitat del ciphac que es en l’autra costat am aquesta extramitat del mirat; e extratz aquela de la codena la qual es de part de lu.	And then, starting from this side of the code, and cutting that with the extremity that is of the ciphac on the other side, and extracting the needle from the code which it has penetrated, and then reducing it to that code and cosing the extremity of the ciphac that is on the other side with this same extremity of the mirror; and extracting that from the code which is of this part of lu.
E fay aquo una veguada e autra, e fay aquo una veguada aprop autre veguada entro que tu cozes tot aquo que es deforo segon aquel eysemple.	And make it so that there is one pass and another, and make it so that there is one pass and another again, until you close all this that is outside according to that example.
E la suma de aquesta manieyra de sutura es que tu cozes am sutura de pellicies am la qual cozo las pels, enayssi que tu cozes le ciphac una veguada de la part de la extremitat de la codena, e que leysses aquela autra veguada entro que la ajas complida.	And the sum of this suture method is that you close with sutura of pellicies with which you close the pels, in such a way that you close the ciphac once from the part of the extremity of the code, and then leave it open until you have completed.
Mays la segonda specia de sutura propria la qual dieys eyssament Gualia , e aquest es de sermo de lu e per lu recomtat, es que tu cozas aquela segon semilitut am la qual alcus medicantz cozo aquela, enayssi que agreguan tota partida a la sua compar partida a lu convenient per natura; e aplican la extremitat de autre de lu e la extremitat del mirat al autra extremitat de lu, e aquo es fayt segon que yeu a tu recomti.	But the second species of suture proper which is called Gualia by you, and this is according to the word of Lu and recommended for Lu, is that you close with the second semilitut with which all medicants close with it, in such a way that they add all part to their own corresponding part, as nature allows; and they apply the extremity of another from Lu and the extremity of the mirror to the other extremity of Lu, and this is done according to what you have recommended.
Cove que tu fiques la agulha en la extremitat del mirat a tu propdana de la partida deforo, e fassas aquela penetrar a la partida dedintz en aquel sol, e leysses dos extremitatz del ciphac; e aprop revolveys la agulha e fay aquela penetrar de foro a la dedintz en dos extremitatz del ciphac.	So that you put the needle in the extremity of the mirror at your own pace from the outside, and make it penetrate into the inside in that same spot, and leave two extremities of the ciphac; and then turn back the needle and make it penetrate from outside to inside through two extremities of the ciphac.
E aprop revolveys aquelas cascunas, e fay penetrar quascunas de la partida dededintz entro a la partida deforo en dos extremitatz del mirat autras que so en le latz contrari.	And then turn back those stitches, and make each one penetrate from the inside to the outside through two extremities of the mirror that are on the opposite side.
E aquesta manieyra de sutura es milhor de la sutura comuna leugiera, e es sutura de la qual precedic rememoracio.	And this manner of suture is better than the common light suture, and it is the suture which I mentioned earlier.
Aquest es le sermo de Gualia	And this is the word of Gualia.
E mays le diyssero alcus, sutura del ventre es rectificada am dos agulhas, so es que tu entrometas en aquestas a quascunas un fiel, e comensa am intromiccio de agulha de aquo que es deves tu, e fay aquela penetrar entro al autra latz segon sutura de aquels les quals cozo les cuers engualment.	And some may say that the suture of the belly is corrected with two needles, so it is that you insert a thread into each one and begin with the introduction of needle from where it should be, and make it penetrate into the other side according to the suturing method of those who sew the skin evenly.
E sapias que quan disrupcio es en le mieg loc del ventre, lahoras la sutura de lu es pus difficil que dels autres locs del ventre.	And you should know that when disruption is in the middle of the belly, the suture of Lu is more difficult than in other places of the belly.
Mays le juguament de medicacio de plagua es jutgament de las autras plaguas.	But the judgment of wound healing is a judgment of other wounds.
La qual causa es quar quan tu consieguas la plagua recent am le sieu sanc denant que l’ayre altera aquela, e reduses le budel e cozes aquela e aptas aquela decentment, lahoras pausa sobre aquela polvera encarnativa.	The reason is because when you successfully treat a recent wound with your own blood before it has time to alter that, and reduce the swelling and close the wound, and prepare it decently, then pause over that powder-like flesh.
E si le ayre ja ha alterada la plagua, lahoras pausa sobre aquela alcus enguentz les quals so a tu presens entro que fassan peyra dura e cajan les fiels, e sian consolidatz ciphac e mirat; e aprop cura aquela ayssi cum es la curacio de las autras plaguas entro que sia sanat.	And if the air has already altered the wound, then pause over that and consider the cases of those who are present before you, until they make a strong impression on your mind and cause the threads to break, and be consolidated ciphac and mirror; and then cure it in the same way as the healing of other wounds until it is well.
Mays si a tu no so presens las medicinas, lahoras pausa sobre aquela tantost, pus que comensa a getar brac, coto viel, e permuta aquel dos veguadas le dia, ayssi cum a tu e ensenhat, entro que sia sanat, quar tu no indigeysses de autra medicacio en motas disposicios quan las plaguas so simplas.	But if you are not present with the medicines, then pause over that for now, because it begins to generate a branch, coto veil, and exchange it two times a day, just as I have taught you, until it is well, since you do not need other medication in many situations when wounds are simple.
Mays si tu temes que la plagua comunique en lesio als membres principals, lahoras cove que tu submergas lana leon en oli de trempada qualiditat, o en oli rozat, e pausa aquela en le circuit dels locs que so entre les angonas e dejos las aysselas.	But if you fear that the wound may communicate with lesions in the main members, then it is necessary that you immerse a lion's fleece (lana leon) in high-quality olive oil or rose oil and pause it in the circuit of the places between the armpits and leave it as such.
E si sent dolor o putrefaccio en les sieus budels, quar motas veguadas aquo s’endeve, lahoras cristeriza aquel am vi stiptic negre tebe, e majorment si la poyredura es pervenguda en le budel e es fayta exitura penetrant entro la conquavitat de lu.	And if you feel pain or putrefaction in your own swelling (budels), since many times this happens, then pause over that with vinegar stiptic black tea, and especially if the abscess has penetrated into the cavity of the wound.
E sapias que aquela que es del budel gros es de pus leugiera sanacio que aquela que es en les budels subtils.	And you should know that the swelling that is in the large vessels (budel gros) is easier to heal than the one that is in the small vessels (budels subtils).
E es de dificil sanacio quar le budel le qual es apelat “gegunu” no recep sanacio de plagua que caja en lu de tot; e aquo es per la gran multitut de venas que so en lu e per la magnitut de lu que so en aquelas, e per subtilitat del cos de aquel, e per propinquitat de aquel a natura de nervis.	And it is difficult to heal because the swelling that is called "gegunu" does not receive healing from wound that breaks out in it; and this is because of the great multitude of veins that are in it and the magnitude of it that is in those, and because of the subtlety of the body of that, and because of its proximity to the nature of nerves.
Mays si aquo que procezeys de la plagua es la tela, e conseguas aquela recent, redutz aquela segon la tua rectetut am la qual reduzes les budels engualment.	But if what proceeds from the wound is a web (tela), and you succeed in obtaining that which is recent, then reduce it according to your rectitude with which you reduce the swellings evenly.
Mays si es passat a lu spazi e ja es feyt vert o negre, lahoras que tu strenguas aquela am fiel sobre le loc que es denigrat de lu, per so que vengua fluxs de sanc, quar en la tela so venas e arterias.	But if it has passed through the space and is already green or black, then you should strengthen that with thread (fiel) over the location that is denigrated from it, in order that the flux of blood may come, since in the web are veins and arteries.
E aprop inscideys aquo que es otra aquel liament, e pausa dos extremitatz del fiel pendentz de la partida dejos de la plagua foro lu, per que sobre tu sia alleujada la atraccio de lu deves le cazement de la tela e emissio del brac de la plagua.	And then you should inscribe (inicieys) what is another ligament, and pause the two extremities of the thread while it is pending from the left side of the wound to the outside, so that above you may be alleviated the attraction of the wound's discharge and emission of the branch of the wound.
Rememoracio de las plaguas quan accideysso en le budel.	Remembrance of wounds when they occur in the swelling (budel).
Quan accideys disrupcio en le budel e es petita, lahoras es possibla que sia resteurada en alcus homes, per aysso quar yeu vi aquel le qual era stat plaguat en le sieu ventre am percussio de lansa et era la plagua de la part dreyta del stomac, e la plagua era antiquada e fayta fistula, e eyssic de lu gestio e ventositat.	When disruption occurs in the swelling (budel) and it is small, then it is possible that it may be restored in certain people, for this reason why you see someone who was once wounded in their own belly with a lance blow and had a wound on the right side of the stomach, and the wound was old and had become a fistula, and there was great movement and venting.
Adonc yeu pansegui la curacio de lu ja sia que no era confizat en la sanacio de lu, mays cessegui subtiliar aquel entro que foc sanat e le loc es consolidat.	Then you should continue the treatment of it, whether or not it was contained in the healing of it, but rather subtly treat that until it is well and the place is consolidated.
E yeu pus que vi le loc ja consolidat, timegui sobre le malaute que endevengues sobre lu accident de mal en le sieu ventre; e no endevenc alcu per aquo mal accident e romas en las suas milhos disposicios mangant e bevent, e aprop entrec en banh e es exercitat en sos ditz.	And you should see that the place is already consolidated, then take care of the patient who has suffered from the bad accident in their own belly; and do not neglect anyone because of this bad accident and remain in their natural habits eating and drinking, and also enter into a bath and exercise in their usual ways.
E ja diysero alcus experimentados que quan endeve plagua en le budel, e es petita, lahoras cove que sia liada segon aquesta manieyra: e es que tu prenguas fromiguas de grans caps; e aprop ajusta las doas labias de la plagua e pausa una fromigua de aquelas que aja la boca uberta sobre las doas labias de la plagua; donc quan pren sobre aquelas e strenh la sua boca, abscindeys le cap de lu, quar adhereys e no es dissolvut.	And some experienced ones will say that when a wound occurs in the swelling (budel), and it is small, then it must be tied according to this manner: and that you take threads of great caps; and then adjust the two lips of the wound and place one thread from those which have an open mouth over the two lips of the wound; therefore, when you put it on them and strengthen its mouth, cut off the head (abscindeys le cap de lu), for it adheres and does not dissolve.
E aprop pausa autra formigua prop la primieyra, e no cesses aquo a far am formiguas una aprop autra segon la quantitat de tota la plagua.	And then place another thread (formigua) right next to the first one, and do not stop doing this with threads one after another according to the quantity of all the wound.
E aprop reduzeys aquela e cos la plagua; e romanguan aquels caps annexces en le budel entro que·l budel sia sanat; e no accideys al malaute degun nocument.	And then reduce (reduzeys) that and close the wound; and those attached caps remain in the swelling until the swelling is healed; and do not cause any harm to the patient.
E ja es possible que·l budel sia liat am fiel subtil lo qual es fayt del budel de bestia annexs am lu, pus que es mes en agulha; e es que tu prenguas la extremitat de aquestz fiels de budel, e sia mot descarnat, e aprop lia la extremitat de lu am fiel de li, envolopat, e aprop entromet aquel fiel en agulhas e cos am aquel le budel, e areduzeys aquel en la disrupcio.	And it is possible that the swelling (budel) be bound with a fine thread (fiel subtil) made from the swelling of an animal attached to it, since it is more in the shape of an awl; and it is that you take the end of these threads of the swelling, and it is quite bare, and then tie the end of it with another thread, enveloped, and then insert that thread into the awls and close it with the swelling, and reduce the swelling in the disruption.
E aquesta manieyra de sutura am formiguas no es sino segon via de fiducia e d’esperansa.	And this method of suture with threads is not just according to one way, but rather through faith and hope.
Mays si la plagua es gran e ampla, majorment si es en un dels budels subtils, quar lahoras no es engen sino subtiliacio, e no es sanacio de lu de tot.	But if the wound is great and wide, especially if it is in one of the subtle swellings (budels), for then it is not just a matter of subtlety (subtiliacio), but rather a complete healing of all.
De curacio de zuchem e fistula.	The chapter on the cure of abscesses (zuchem) and fistulas.
Sapias que tota plagua e apostema quan se envilheseys e se Antiqua, e es fayt ulcus, e no es consolidat e geta braç tot temps e no es abscindit, lahoras, en qualque membre sia, universalment es nompnada fistula e nos la apelam aquela azukem.	Know that every wound (plaguada) and abscess (apostema) when it becomes old and worn out, and is made into an ulcer (ulcus), and is not consolidated and keeps getting worse over time, and is not cut off, wherever it may be, universally is called a fistula (fistula) and we call it azukem.
E fistula segon veritat es nodacio feutrada, dura, blanqua am la qual no es dolor e a la qual es conquavitat ayssi cum es conquavitat de pena de ausel; e per aysso nompnat aquela alcus rizatz, id est pena.	And fistula, according to truth, is a hardened, durable, and white nodulation (nodacio feutrada) without pain (e no es dolor), which is conquered (conquavitat) in the same way that a penance (pena de ausel) is conquered; and for this reason it is called alcus rizatz, id est penalty.
E es en alcus homes humida, la qual geta brac; e fort leu la humiditat es abscidida en alcunas horas.	And in some people (alcus homes), it is watery (humida), which drips (geta brac); and the moisture (fort leu la humiditat) is drained off in a few hours.
E alcunas veguadas aquesta humiditat es mota, e es pauca, e es grossa, e es subtil.	And in some cases (alcunas veguadas), this moisture (humiditat) is abundant (mota), and is little (pauca), and is thick (grossa), and is fine (subtil).
E yeu ja he denant dit en la divisio, lahoras cum yeu diyssi las plaguas, que tot ulcus que no es sanat ni no es en lu nuda carn, no es aquo sino per una de ix causas: de las quals la una es o per pauquesa de sanc en le cos; o per malicia de lu; o quar entre lu e las labias es carn dura prohibent nativitat de carn; o quar es de mota legesa; o quar aquel ulcus en si meteys es poyrit e la materia que es a lu tramesa es de mala qualitat; o quar la medicina es enconvenient en la curacio de lu; o quan corrupcio catz en la regio, e es pestilencia; o per proprietat de regio ayssi cum endeve a Saragossa , en la qual es fayta difficil degestio de las malautias, e es tardada en aquela sanacio de apostema per natura; o quar en lu es os un, o motz osses.	And I have already said in the division (la divisio), now as you ask about the wounds (las plaguas), that any ulcer that is not healed or does not become a wound on bare flesh (ni no es sanat ni no es en lu nuda carn) is caused by one of these reasons: among which is either because there is too little blood in the body; or because it is due to malice towards the patient; or because there is hard skin between the ulcer and the lips that prevents new tissue from forming; or because it is a very deep wound; or because the pus inside the wound is putrid and the material being sent to the wound is of poor quality; or because the medicine is inconvenient in healing the wound; or when corruption creeps into the region, and there is pestilence; or because the region has its own property, such as Saragossa, where digestion of diseases is difficult and recovery from abscesses is delayed by nature; or because there is one bone, or many bones.
Ja e mostrat totas aquelas causas, e·ls senhals de aquelas e la curacio de lor am medicinas en la divisio.	And I have already shown all those causes (totas aquellas causas) and their signs (senhals), as well as the cure for them with medicines in the division.
E cove assi que yeu fassa a tu saber la curacio de fistula la qual es fayta per via de operacio am ma.	And it is necessary that you know how to cure a fistula, which is made by surgical operation with my hands.
E sapias que fistula accideys en totz les membres del cos; quar de aquelas son fistulas que perveno a las venas grantz e arterias, o als nervis, o al ciphac, o al budel, o a la vesica, o ad alcuna de las costas, o ad alcu dels spondils del dos, o ad alcuna de las juncturas compostas per composicio ayssi quo de la ma e del pe; e de aquelas so que dan a lu propinquitat del membre principal e de semblantz.	And know that fistulas can occur in all the members of the body (totz les membres del cos); for some are fistulas that penetrate to the great veins and arteries, or nerves, or to the ribs, or to the swelling (budel), or to the bladder, or to any of the costs, or to some of the vertebrae of the back, or to any of the joints composed of bone and cartilage in such a way that they are close to the main member and resemble.
E donc aquela de aquestas fistulas que es segon aquesta manieyra es de las malautias de dificil sanacio, e no recep curacio, e occupacio am aquela es trebalh e ignorancia.	And therefore that type of fistula which is according to this manner (es segon aquesta manieyra) is one of the difficult-to-cure diseases (malautias de dificil sanacio), and does not receive treatment or care, and its occupation (occupacio) with ignorance (trebalh e ignorancia).
E si es de las fistulas alcuna la profunditat de la qual no perve ad aquestz locs que e dit, e esperas e confizas en la curacio de lu, e vols pervenir a cognicio de lu, lahoras pren tenta de eram o de ferr, e si la fistula va segon rectetut, e perquireys aquela am lu.	And if some of these fistulas are so deep that they do not reach the points I have mentioned, and you wait and hope for their cure, and wish to gain understanding of them, then you take a tentative approach with iron or steel, and if the fistula follows the natural course (va segon rectetut), you will examine it with the aid of your own judgment.
Mays si la fistula es tortuissitat, lahoras investigua aquela am tenta de plom subtil, quar plom am la levitat del sieu cors es alleujat e curvat deves la tortuositat.	But if the fistula is twisted (tortuissitat), then you investigate it with a subtle lead (plom subtil) because lead with the lightness of its own body (am la levitat del sieu cors) is relieved and curved in such a way that it can straighten out the twisting.
E si la fistula es havent motz horrificis, no es a tu possible que signifiques sobre lu am tenta.	And if the fistula is full of many horrific things (havent motz horrificis), it is not possible for you to signify anything over it with a tentative approach.
Adonc cristeriza le orrifici per sos orrificis, quar la humiditat per la qual clisterizas aquela va deves las autras orrificis e corr de lor.	Then you must cleanse the orifice with its own orifices, because the moisture that you use to cleanse it flows into other orifices and comes out of them.
E aprop inquier exquisitament, segon qual manieyra a tu es possible que conoguas si aqui has os o nervi, e es la conquavitat de la fistula longinqua o propdana, o es una fistula a la qual so motz orrificis e esta sobre aquo tot am la suma de la tua fortaleza, am la tua enterroguacio, am la qual enterroguas le malaute, e la invencio de la dolor deves la tua compressio am la ma sobre le loc, e semblantz de las significacios e de las causas accidentz al apostema.	And approach this inquiry with exquisite precision, according to which manner it is possible for you to know if there are bones or nerves (os o nervi) here, and whether the conquest of the fistula is long-standing (longinqua) or recent (propdana), or whether it is a fistula with many orifices (motz orrificis) and is situated above all with the sum of your strength, with your introspection, with which you understand the illness (enterroguacio), and the invention of pain as a result of your compression with the hand on the location, and similar signs and causes that occur to the abscess.
E cum tu auras stat sobre totas aquelas causas am stacio veraya, lahoras ve a la curacio segon confidencia: e es que tu consideras lahoras si es fistula apparent propinqua o en loc sal, longinqua de junctura, o de nervi, o de arteria, o de vena, o de un dels locs les quals yeu a tu e ditz.	And when you have considered all those causes (totas aquellas causas) and have arrived at the truth (stacio veraya), then you will go to the cure according to confidence: and it is that you consider whether this fistula is an apparent one near the surface or in a place of salt, distant from a joint, nerve, artery, vein, or one of the locations which I mention to you and say.
Lahoras tu secca la fistula segon que denant es dit de la naracio de lu, e osta aquo que es en aquela filtracio e de carns corrumpudas, e aquo que es nascut en le orrifici de la carn, o de theil e de semblantz, e cura aquela entro que sia sanada.	And then you will cut open the fistula according to what is said before in the narration of it, and you will take out what is in that filtration and of corrupted flesh, and what has been born in the orifice of the flesh, or of the bone and similar things, and cure it until it is healed.
Mays si la fistula es de longinqua profunditat, e es segon rectetut, lahoras cove que inscidas aquela en le preon atant quant a tu sira possible, e aprop mondifica aquela de totas las suas carns corrompudas; e aprop administra calguas envolopadas en medicinas acutas, e intromet aquelas entro a la conquavitat de la fistula, la qual has conprenduda am ferr.	But if the fistula is of long-standing depth and follows the natural course (es segon rectetut), then you must incise it in the preon as far as it is possible for you to reach, and appropriate mondify all its corrupted flesh; and appropriate administer some enveloped medicines, and introduce those into the conquest of the fistula which has been comprehended by iron.
E fay aquo am aquela alcunas veguadas entro que la medicina acuta corroda tot aquo que es romas en la conquavitat de la fistula de la corrupcio.	And make this with that some times until the acute medicine corrodes all that remains in the conquest of the fistula from corruption.
E aprop restaura aquela am enguentz les quals engendran carn sana entro que sia sanada.	And then restore that with the substances which generate healthy flesh until it is healed.
Mays si no es sanada per aquo, lahoras tu cauteriza aquela segon que havem recomtat.	But if it is not healed through this, then you must cauterize that according to what we have recounted.
Mays si la causa de fistula es os e es deves tu certificat aquo, lahoras tu inquireys aquela e secca aquela segon que havem recomtat, si tu no prohibeys alcuna causa de vena o de nervi o de membre principal ayssi cum havem dit.	But if the cause of the fistula is bone (os) and it is necessary for you to be certain about this, then you must inquire into that and cut open that according to what we have recounted, unless you prohibit some cause from a vein or nerve or main member in the way that we have said.
Mays si le os es a tu descubert e es en lu alcuna corrupcio e negror, lahoras tu ratz aquel entro que la corrupcio sia hostada tota; e aprop cura aquel am aquo que lu encarne entro que sia sanat.	But if the bone is revealed to you and it contains some corruption and blackness (negror), then you must remove that entire corruption and blackness, and appropriate cure that with what is in that place until it is healed.
E si no es sana e gieta brac ayssi cum fazia, lahoras sapias que tu no est pervengut a la eradicacio tota de la corrupcio; e adonc tu descuebre sobre lu segondanament e exquisitament fay la razio de lu e la mundificacio de lu am la deriera fortalasa tieua, e aprop restaura aquel.	And if it is not healed and remains black like that, then you must know that you have not achieved the total eradication of corruption; and therefore, you will discover anew over it with exquisite precision and make the reason for it and the purification of it with the utmost strength and power, and appropriate restore that.
E donc si es sanat, bo es; e sino, lahoras sapias que aquela corrupcio es en la profunditat longinqua del cors, la qual no ha conseguida, e adonc a tu en aquel no es engen sino laysar aquela.	And therefore, if it is healed, then good; and otherwise, you must know that the corruption is in the deep-seated parts of the body (profunditat longinqua del cors), which has not been achieved, and accordingly, there is nothing for you to do but leave it as it is.
E si le os corromput es petit, o es a tu possible atirar aquel, lahora tu le atira am forceps subtils las quals conveno ad aquo.	And if the corrupted bone is small, it is to your advantage to attract that, then you must attract it with subtle forceps which are suitable for this.
E si so motz osses, lahoras exquisitament fay la extraccio de totz aquels, e de aquels no laysses denguna causa am la tua fortaleza.	And if there are many bones (motz osses), then you must make the extraction of all those in an exquisite manner, and leave no cause behind with your strength.
Mays si a tu fa contrarietat alcuna causa de las humiditatz, e en lor inscizio no ha temor ni error, lahoras inscideys aquelas liaments o carns si so aqui, e deliura les osses.	But if any cause of humidity arises in your favor, and there is no fear or error in them, then you must inscribe those limbs or flesh if they are here, and deliver the bones.
Mays si a tu no es preparacio de ostar les osses de la tua hora, lahoras pausa sobre la plagua aquo que poyresca la plagua aquela, e layssa aquela entro que aquo es al enviro de aquels osses de carns e de liamentz, e guarda la plagua que no sia consolidada, e sia constrengida la seccio la qual tu has inscidida en la tua operacio.	But if your preparation is not suitable for removing the bones of that hour (ostar les osses de la tua hora), then you must pause over this wound (plagua aquo) which will render that wound (plagua aquela) into a condition where it can be surrounded by those bones (osses de carns e de liamentz), and guard the wound so that it is not consolidated, and the section which you have inscribed in your operation (seccio la qual tu has inscidida en la tua operacio) must be constrained.
Habantz, si temes, pausa sobre lu coto submers en sopre trissat am oli, o coto submers en anguent egipciac, o en alcu dels enguentz vertz, quar quan poyriran aquelas liaments, e les osses son de lor seperatz la ablacio, e de aquels atraccio es alleujada.	They had said, if you fear, pause over the wound submerged in soporific oil, or the wound submerged in Egyptian anguish, or in any of the green herbs, for when those limbs will be decomposed, and the bones are separated from their ablation, and that attraction is alleviated.
Mays si es un gran os ayssi cum le os de camba o de coyssa o semblantz ad aquels, e aquo que de lu es corromput es la facia de lu tant solament, lahoras ratz aquela am resio tant solament derriera entro que sia ostada aquela negror e corrupcio, e aprop restaura la plagua.	But if it is a great bone, like the bone of camba or coyssa or similar to those, and that which is corrupted from it is only the surface, then you must remove that with a razor only as far back as necessary until the blackness and corruption are removed, and appropriate restore the wound.
Mays si aquo que de lu es corrumpyt es gran partida, e la corrupcio ja ha conseguida la medulla del os, lahoras es causa necessaria cerrar aquel e aquel tot inscidir entro al loc on es pervenguda la corrupcio, e lahoras cura aquel entro que sia consolidada.	But if that which is corrupted from it is a great part, and the corruption has already reached the marrow of the bone (la medulla del os), then you must necessarily close that and entirely inscribe it within the location where the corruption has taken place, and then cure that until it is consolidated.
E yeu recomti a tu aquo que endevenc ad un home en la sua coyssa per que pausez aquela a eyssempli e adjutori sobre la tua operacio.	And I recommend to you that you seek out a man in his couch (en la sua coyssa) so that he may pause and give you an example and assistance over your operation.
Foc un home jove per etat entorn xxx ans, al qual accideys dolor en la sua cueyssa, e de las partidas dedintz mauguda es sobre la materia dedintz le cors entro que la materia es pervenguda a la cueyssa, e es materia de apostema am gran apostema, e no foc a lu causa extrinseca.	Seek out a young man of about thirty years old, to whom it happens that he has pain in his side (cueyssa), and the parts dedintz are mauled (mauguda) is on the material dedintz within the body (entro que la materia es pervenguda a la cueyssa), and it is material of abscess with great abscess, and there is no external cause.
E adonc foc extendut le temps am aquela per la error dels metges entro que l’apostema es hubert, e acorrero de lu materias motas, e la sua curacio foc aprop pausada entro que la camba foc fistulada, e faytz son en lu motz orrificis les quals totz getavan poyredura e las humiditatz del cos.	And then the time was extended with that because of the mistake of the doctors until the abscess was ruptured, and a great many materials (materias) flowed out, and his cure was almost paused, until the camba became fistulated, and made its way through the orifices (motz orrificis) which were all pouring forth pus and fluids from the body.
E adonc le curec multitut de metges entorn dos ans, e no foc en aquels savia ma en la art, entro que yeu fu appelat.	And then I was summoned to the many doctors for about two years, and they did not know in those what they knew in the art (ma en la art), until you were called.
E vi la camba de lu e las materias que corrian de lu aquels orrificis per gran cors; e ja le cos de aquel home era tot stabozit e la color de lu era citrina.	And I saw the camba of that and the materials that were flowing from it through great holes (orrificis) for a large body (gran cors); and already the body of that man was totally stabilized, and the color of it was yellowish (citrina).
E adonc yeu intromesi la tenta ad un de aquels orrificis e pervenguec la tenta al os.	And then I introduced the probe into one of those orifices and guided it to the bone (os).
E aprop yeu e perscrutat tostz les orrificis e trobegui aquels pervenir a lor de totas partidas de la camba.	And then I examined all the orifices and found that those which were coming from the bone (os) were coming from all parts of the camba.
E adonc yeu me coytegui e inscidegui sobre un dels orrificis aquels entro que descrobegui una partida del os, e atrobegui aquel corromput, e ja era terros e corrumput e denigrat; e era ja corrumpuda una partida de la camba entro que havia penetrat entro a la mezola.	And then I cut and inscribed over one of those orifices until I uncovered a part of the bone (os), and I found that part corrupted, and it was already rotten and corrupted and denigrated; and already a part of the camba had penetrated into the medulla.
E adon yeu serregui aquo que a mi era discubert e preparat del os descubert.	And then I took out what had been discovered and prepared from the bone (os) that was uncovered.
E yeu cujegui que no fos en le os sino aquela corrupcio la qual abscidigui e serregui, e yeu ja havia derraziguada.	And I saw that it was not in the bone (os) but that corruption which abscessed and was removed, and I had already drained it.
E aprop pausegui la restauracio de la plagua am medicina consolidativas per lonc temps, e no es consolidada.	And then I paused to restore the wound with consolidative medicine for a long time, but it was not consolidated.
E aprop yeu iteregui e descubregui sobre le os segondament sobre le descubriment primier, e atrobegui continua corrupcio am le os.	And then I iterated and uncovered over the bone (os) secondarily on the first discovery, and found continuous corruption in the bone.
E serregui aquo que a mi apares de aquela corrupcio, e aprop yeu fo perforsat fayre la curacio de lu e restauracio, e no es restaurat.	And I removed what appeared to be from that corruption, and then I was forced to perform the cure and restoration, but it was not restored.
E adonc yeu descubri sobre lu autra veguada e no cessegui inscidir le os petit a petit particuladament e perforsa la restauracio de lu, e no es restaurat entro que inscidigui entorn un palm de lu, e aquel extraxi am la medula sua, e aprop restauregui aquel am medicinas, e es consolidat leugierament e sanat.	And then I discovered another way and did not cease to inscribe the small bone (os petit) little by little particularly, and forced the restoration of it, but it was not restored until I inscribed around a palm's width from it, and that extracted with its own medulla, and I re-established it with medicines, and it consolidated gradually and healed.
E no es necessaria iteracio en la operacio de lu e seccio de lu sino per la disposicio de la freulesa de lu e per la paucitat de la tollerancia de lu e paor de lu de mort, quar a lu accidia en totas horas per superfluitat de evacuacio sincopi mala.	And it is not necessary to iterate in the operation of the abscess and its section, but rather due to the disposition of the flesh (freulesa) of the patient and the scarcity of tolerance of the patient and their fear of death, for the patient is subject to constant hours of superfluous evacuation by bad syncope.

And therefore the healing is complete, and nothing remains in place of hard bone (os carn dura); and it has been done well the disposition of him in his own body and he has returned to his virtue; and it has been converted into its own dispositions and he does not make contrary movements in ambulation nor any harm in any cause.
Mays si es os eminent en loc del cors ja trauquat, lahoras cove que tu secces aquel segon aquesta manieyra: e es que tu prenguas liament e strenh aquel en la extremitat de aquel os eminent, e comanda ad alcu que extenda aquel en sus; e pausa aquel liament de lana pus gros del primier liament; e aprop lia aquel sobre la carn que es dejos le os, e exten la extramitat de lu per que atires la carn a las partidas dejos, e tu descuebras la carn sobre le loc le qual voles serrar per que la serra no leda la carn.	But if the bone is prominent in the body already traumatized, you must cut it according to this manner: take a ligament and stretch that in the extremity of that prominent bone; and command someone to extend that over there; and pause that ligament of wool thicker than the first ligament; and then tie that over the flesh that is left on the bone, and extend the extremity of it so that you can pull the flesh to the parts left, and then uncover the flesh over the place where you want to sew so that the seam does not cut the flesh.
E pausa fust o taula dejos le os decentment, quar quan tu fas aquo no es prohibida la serra que no secce la carn corrumpuda.	And pause at the fist or table left on the bone decently, for when you do this it is not prohibited to cut the seam that does not cut the corrupted flesh.
E cove que sia la serradura sobre le loc corrumput petit a petit, quar si es en la concavitat del os corrupcio e no appar en la sua apparicio al sentiment, e forssa a serratura de lu autra veguada.	And it is necessary that the suturing be done slowly and carefully over the corrupted area, little by little, because if there is corruption in the concavity of the bone and it does not appear on its surface to the sense, then you must make another incision in a different way.
E si le os es corrumput e no-eminent, abantz es la una partida continuada am la autra, e la corrupcio es al mieg loc o en partida de lu, lahoras tu descuebre la carn de totas partz tota; e aprop pausa fust dejos, e aprop serra aquel de la primiera partida la on es la corrupcio entro que sia continuada la serratura del autra partida.	And if the bone is corrupted and not prominent, it is better to remove one part and continue with the other; and if the corruption is in the middle or in a part of it, then you must uncover all parts completely; and then pause at the fist left there, and then sew that from the first part where the corruption is into the continuation of the suturing of the other part.
E sia la serradura segon le loc de la corrupcio un petit, segon que havem dit.	And let the suturing be done according to the location of the corruption, a little at a time, as we have said.
E si la corrupcio es en la junctura, inscideys aquela junctura corrumpuda, e serra le os la on es continuat del autra part.	And if the corruption is at the junction, cut out that corrupted junction and sew the bone where it continues with the other part.
E si de la corrupcio es en la continuacio de doas juncturas, lahoras no es en lu razio sino engen.	And if the corruption is in the continuation of two joints, then it is not in reason but rather by art.
E si la corrupcio es en le pecte de la ma o del pe, es mot dificil; empero cove que tu inquieras la corrupcio en qual manieyra appareys a tu, e que abradas aquela, e mondes aquela segon quascuna disposicio la qual es a tu possibla, e am cascum engen sia rectificat a tu, quan no fa a tu contrarietat vena o nervi.	And if the corruption is in the breast of the hand or foot, it is very difficult; however, you must inquire into the corruption and how it appears to you, and then cut out that which is corrupted, and shape it according to each disposition that is possible for you, and by all means rectify it to your own being, unless it contradicts your veins or nerves.
E sapias qual es inscididors e las serras a inscidir aquestz osses son motz segon le situament dels osses, e la preparacio de aquels, e la grosseza de aquels, e la subtilitat e la grandeza e la parvitat de aquels, e la duricia e la lor raritat; per que cove que tu prepares a tota specia de operacio estrument convenient ad aquela opperacio.	And you must know what instruments and how to use the scissors to cut these bones are most suitable according to the situation of the bones, their preparation, size, subtlety, grandeur, smallness, hardness, and rarity; so that it is necessary for you to prepare all kinds of surgical instruments that are convenient for each operation.
E sapias que aquela operacio significa a tu sobre la specia del strument del qual indigeysses; quan am tu es gran studi e lonc e conoyssensa de las manieyras de aquesta art, e testimoni de manieyras de malautias, quar lahoras ja tu las avias per tu meteys aquo que es convenient a lu dels sturmentz a tota malautia.	And you must know that this operation requires of you over the species of the instrument which you need; when you are great in study and long and profound knowledge of the ways of this art, and witness to the ways of diseases, for then already you have them by yourself that is convenient to all maladies.

And you should also note at the end of this chapter the number of instruments which you will pause with, as simple ones, with which you will proceed to your prohibition, which you will experience on others.
